	tenaiva snāpayitvā tu dāhaṃ kuryād yathāvidhi ||

rajasvalāmaraṇe tu |

	pañcabhiḥ snāpayitvā tu gavyaiḥ pretāṃ rajasvalām |

	vastrāntarāvṛtāṃ kṛtvā dāhayed vidhipūrvakam || iti |

atra śātātapaḥ |

	grāme tu yatra saṃspṛṣṭir yātrāyāṃ kalahādiṣu |

	grāmasaṃdūṣaṇe caiva spṛṣṭidoṣo na vidyate ||

grāme rājamārgādau | ṣaṭtriṃśanmate 'pi |

	devayātrāvivāheṣu yajñeṣu prakṛteṣu ca |

	utsaveṣu ca sarveṣu spṛṣṭvā spṛṣṭir na vidyate ||

bṛhaspatir api |

	tīrthe vivāhe yātrāyāṃ saṃgrāme deśaviplave |

	nagaragrāmadāhe ca spṛṣṭvā spṛṣṭir na duṣyati ||

etac ca vākyatrayaṃ yatrāham anena spṛṣṭa iti jñānaṃ nāsti tadviṣayam iti kecit | ucchiṣṭāśucisparśanaviṣayam ity anye | tatra āpastambaḥ: "śaktiviṣaye na muhūrtam apy aprayataḥ syāt" iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ naimittikasnāni **

**atha kāmyasnānāni**

tatra pulastyaḥ |

	puṣye ca janmanakṣatre vyatīpāte ca vaidhṛtau |

	amāyāṃ ca nadīsnānaṃ punāty āsaptamaṃ kulam ||

	ravyaṅgāraśaner vāre snānaṃ kurvanti ye dvijāḥ |

	vyādhibhis te na pīḍyante mṛgaiḥ kesariṇo yathā ||

	caitrakṛṣṇacaturdaśyāṃ yaḥ snāyāc chivasaṃnidhau |

	na pretatvam avāpnoti gaṅgāyāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ||

bhaviṣyatpurāṇe |

	śivaliṅgasamīpe tu yat toyaṃ purataḥ sthitam |

	śivagaṅgeti tajjñeyaṃ tatra snātvā divaṃ vrajet ||

yamo 'pi |

	kārtikyāṃ puṣkare snātaḥ sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate |

	māghyāṃ snātaḥ prayāge tu mucyate sarvakilbiṣaiḥ ||

	jyeṣṭhamāse site pakṣe dvādaśyāṃ hastasaṃyute |

	daśajanmāghahā gaṅgā tena pāpaharā smṛtā ||

	yamunāyāṃ tathā snātvā māghakṛṣṇacaturdaśīm |

	vaiśākhe śuklapakṣe tu tṛtīyāyāṃ tathaiva ca ||

	gaṅgātoye naraḥ snātvā mucyate sarvakilbiṣaiḥ ||

mārkaṇḍeyo 'pi |

	gavāṃ koṭisahasrasya samyag dattasya yat phalam |

	tat phalaṃ jāhnavīsnāne rāhugraste divākare ||

padmapurāṇe 'pi |

	kārtike navamī śuklā pitṝṇām utsavāya sā |

	tasyāṃ snānaṃ hutaṃ dattam anantaphaladaṃ bhavet ||

viṣṇur api |

	sūryagrahaṇatulyā tu śuklā mādhasya saptamī |

	aruṇodayavelāyāṃ tasyāṃ snānaṃ mahāphalam ||

	punarvasubudhopetā caitramāse sitāṣṭamī |

	srotaḥsu vidhivat snātvā vājapeyaphalaṃ labhet ||

śātātapo 'pi |

	amāvāsyā bhave dvāre yadā bhūmisutasya vai |

	jāhnavīsnānamātreṇa gosahasraphalaṃ bhavet ||

purāṇe 'pi |

	kārtikaṃ skalaṃ māsaṃ nityasnāyī jitendriyaḥ |

	japan haviṣyabhuk snātaḥ sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ||

	tulāmakarameṣeṣu prātaḥsnāyī sadā bhavet |

	haviṣyaṃ brahmacaryaṃ ca mahāpātakanāśanam ||

yamo 'pi |

	ya icched vipulān bhogāṃś candrasūryagrahopamān |

	prātaḥsnāyī bhaven nityaṃ māsau dvau māghaphālgunau ||

matsyapurāṇe 'pi |

	āṣāḍhādicaturmāsān prātaḥsnāyī bhaven naraḥ |

	viprebhyo bhojanaṃ datvā kārtikyāṃ goprado bhavet ||

	sa vaiṣṇavaṃ padaṃ yāti viṣṇuvratam idaṃ smṛtam ||

vṛddhavāsiṣṭho 'pi |

	ravisaṃkramaṇe puṇye na snāyād yadi mānavaḥ |

	saptajanmasu rogī syād duḥkhabhāgīha jāyate ||

	saptajanmātaraṃ (?) rogaiḥ na vimuktaḥ sadā bhavet ||

mārkaṇḍeyo 'pi |

	sarvakālaṃ tilaiḥ snānaṃ puṇyaṃ vyāso 'bravin muniḥ |

	tuṣyaty āmalakair viṣṇur ekādaśyāṃ viśeṣataḥ ||

	śrīkāmas tu sadā snānaṃ kurvītāmalakair naraḥ |

	sapatamīṃ navamīṃ caiva parvakālaṃ ca varjayet ||

atra brahmāṇḍapurāṇam |

	nityaṃ naimittikaṃ kāmyaṃ trividhaṃ snānam ucyate |

	tarpaṇaṃ tu bhavet tasya aṅgatvena prakīrtitam || iti |

gargo 'pi |

	kuryān naimittikasnānaṃ śītādbhiḥ kāmyam eva ca |

	nityaṃ yādṛcchikaṃ caiva yathāruci samācaret || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ kāmyasnānāni**

**atha māghasnānavidhiḥ**

tatra nāradīyapurāṇam |

	saṃprāpte māghamāse tu tapasvijanavallabhe |

	krośanti sarvavārīṇi samudgacchati bhāskare ||

	punīmaḥ sarvapāpāni trividhāni na saṃśayaḥ |

	brahmaghnenāpi yāni syus tīvrakarmakṛtāni ca ||

	devais tejaḥ parikṣiptaṃ māghamāse jaleṣu vai |

	ataḥ pavitraṃ hi jalamaśeṣāghaughanāśanam ||

	naḍvaleṣu tu na snāyāt kaupye bhāṇḍe sthite jale |

	na sukhāl labhyate puṇyaṃ puṇyaṃ kṛcchreṇa labhyate ||

	māghamāse varārohe śastaṃ vai nimnagājalam |

	snāto vahniṃ na seveta asnāto vā kathaṃcana ||

viṣṇur api |

	pauṣaphālgunayor madhye prātaḥsnāyī sadā bhavet |

	darśaṃ vā paurṇamāsīṃ vā prārabhya snānam ācaret (?) ||

	puṇyāny ahāni triṃśat tu makarasthe divākare |

	tatra cotthāya niyamaṃ gṛhṇīyād vidhipūrvakam ||

	māghamāsam imaṃ pūrṇaṃ snāsye 'haṃ deva mādhava |

	tīrthasyāsya jale nityam iti saṃkalpya cetasi ||

	tataḥ snātvā gṛhī tīrthe kṛtvā śirasi vai mṛdam |

	vedoktavidhinā rājan sūryasyārghyaṃ nivedayet ||

	pitṝn saṃtarpayitvā tu avatīrya tato jalāt |

	kāṣṭhā maunī namaskṛtya pūjayet puruṣottamam ||

	śaṅkhacakradharaṃ devaṃ mādhavaṃ nāma pūjayet |

	vahnau hutvā vidhānena tatas tv ekāśano bhavet ||

	bhūśayyābrahmacaryeṇa śaktaḥ snānaṃ samācaret |

	aśaktasyāṃ dhanāḍhyasya svecchā sarvatra kathyate ||

	avaśyam eva kartavyaṃ māghasnānam iti sthitiḥ |

	tilasnāyī tilodvartī tilahomī tilodakī ||

	tiladas tilabhoktā ca ṣaṭtilo nāvasīdati |

	tilā āmalakāś caiva tīrthe deyās tu nityaśaḥ ||

	tathā prajvālayed vahnim indhanārthaṃ dvijanmanām |

	evaṃ snānasyāvasāne bhojyaṃ deyam avāritam ||

	bhojayed dvijadāmpatyaṃ bhūṣayed vastrabhūṣaṇaiḥ |

	kambalājinaratnāni vāsāṃsi vividhāni ca ||

	celakāni ca deyāni pracchādanapaṭās tathā |

	upānahau tathā gulphamocakau pādamocakau ||

	anena vidhinā dadyān mādhavaḥ prīyatām iti |

atra purāṇokto viśeṣaḥ |

	savitre prasavitre ca paraṃ dhāma jale mama |

	tvattejasā paribhraṣṭaṃ pāpaṃ yātu sahasradhā ||

	divākara jagannātha prabhākara namo 'stu te |

	paripūrṇaṃ kariṣye 'haṃ māghasnānaṃ tavājñayā ||

iti saṃkalpamantraḥ |

	ahany ahani dātavyās tilāḥ śarkaryānvitāḥ |

	māghavasāne subhage viprān saṃbhojayet tathā ||

	sūryo me pīyatāṃ devo viṣṇumūrtir nirañjanaḥ |

	dampatyor vāsasī sūkṣme saptadānyasamanvite ||

	triṃśat tu modakā deyāḥ śarkarātilasaṃyutāḥ |

	bhāgatrayaṃ tilānāṃ tu caturthaḥ śarkarāṃśakaḥ ||

	anabhyaṅgī varārohe sarvaṃ māsaṃ nayed vratī ||

tatra phalaviśeṣārthino niyamaviśeṣam āha viṣṇuḥ |

	saṃyataḥ pathi gacchet tu maunī paiśunyavarjitaḥ |

	yadīcched vipulān bhogāṃś candrasūryopamām (?) śubhān ||

	aprāvṛttaśrīras tu yaḥkāmī snānam ācaret |

	pade pade 'śvamedhasya phalaṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ ||

purāṇe 'pi |

	sarittoyaṃ mahāvegaṃ navakumbhasthaṃ tathā |

	vayunā tāḍitaṃ rātrau gaṅgāsnānasamaṃ vratam || iti |

evaṃ kurvataḥ phalam āha viṣṇuḥ |

	bālās taruṇakā vṛddhā naranārīnapuṃsakāḥ |

	snātvā māghe śubhe tīrthe prāpnuvantīpsitaṃ phalam ||

	pitrā pitāmahaiḥ sārdhaṃ prapitāmahaiḥ |

	mātṛmātāmahaiḥ sārdhaṃ vṛddhamātāmahaiḥ tathā ||

	ekaviṃśatkulaiḥ sārdhaṃ bhuktvā bhogān yathepsitān |

	māghamāsy uṣasi snātvā viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati ||

purāṇe 'pi |

	evaṃ māghaplave yāti bhitvā bimbaṃ divākare || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ māghasnānavidhiḥ**

**atha malāpakarṣaṇasnāna viṣayāṇi kānicid vacanāni likhyante**

atra vṛddhamanuḥ |

	pakṣādau ca tavau ṣaṣṭhyāṃ riktāyāṃ ca tathā tithau |

	tailenābhyajyamānas tu dhanāyurbhyāṃ vihīyate ||

hārito 'pi |

	pañcamīṃ daśamīṃ caiva paurṇamāsīṃ trayodaśīm |

	ekādaśīṃ tṛtīyāṃ ca yas tailam upasevate ||

	abhyaṅgasparśanād vāpi bhakṣaṇāc ca tathaiva ca |

	ucchīrṇā tasya vṛddhiḥ syād dhanāpatyabalāyuṣām ||

bodhāyano 'pi |

	aṣṭamyāṃ ca caturdaśyāṃ daśamyāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ |

	śiro 'bhyaṅgaṃ varjayet tu parvasaṃdhau tathaiva ca ||

gargo 'pi |

	pañcadaśyāṃ caturdaśyām aṣṭamyāṃ ravisaṃkrame |

	dvādaśyāṃ saptamīṣaṣṭhyos tailasparśaṃ vivarjayet ||

	evaṃ vāraniṣedho 'pi jyotiḥśāstre pradarśitaḥ |

	saṃtāpaḥ kāntir alpāyur dhanaṃ vai nidhanaṃ tathā |

	anārogyaṃ sarvakāmā abhyaṅgād bhāskarādiṣi ||

vāmanapurāṇe 'pi |

	nābhyaṅgam arke na ca bhūmiputre kṣauraṃ ca śukre ca kuje ca māṃsam |

	budhe ca yoṣitparvarjanīyā śeṣeṣu kāryāṇi sadaiva kuryāt ||

	citrāsu haste śravaṇe ca tailaṃ kṣuraṃ viśākhāsu bhiṣakṣu varjyam |

	mūle mṛge bhādrapadāsu māṃsaṃ yoṣinmakhārtikasottarāsu ||

	tailābhyaṅgo nārkavāre na bhaume no saṃkrāntau vaidhṛtau niṣṭiṣaṣṭhyoḥ |

	parvasv aṣṭamyāṃ ca neṣṭaḥ sa iṣṭaḥ prokto muktvā vāsare sūryasūnoḥ ||

sūryasūnuḥ śanaiśvaraḥ | evaṃ cottarādiyuktāṃ dvitīyāṃ vihāyottarāsu tithiṣv abhyaṅgasnānaṃ kuryād ity uktaṃ bhavati | atra pracetāḥ |

	sārṣapaṃ gandhatailaṃ ca yat tailaṃ puṣpavāsitam |

	anyad dravyayutaṃ tailaṃ na duṣyati kadācana ||

yamo 'pi |

	ghṛtaṃ ca sārṣapaṃ tailaṃ yat tailaṃ puṣpavāsitam |

	na doṣaḥ pakvataileṣu snānābhyaṅgeṣu nityaśaḥ || iti |

ayaṃ ca tithiviśeṣaniṣedho 'bhyaṅgasnāna eva, na nityasnānādau | tathā ca gargaḥ |

	putrajanmani saṃkrāntau śrāddhe janmadine tathā |

	nityasnāne ca kartavye tithidoṣo na vidyate ||

āpastambo 'pi |

	yādṛcchikaṃ tu yat snānaṃ bhogārthaṃ kriyate dvijaiḥ |

	tan niṣiddhaṃ daśamyādau nityaṃ naimittikaṃ tv iti ||

evaṃ kāmye 'pi draṣṭavyam | ata eva jābāliḥ |

	nityaṃ na hāpayet snānaṃ kāmyaṃ naimittikaṃ ca yat |

	daśamyām api kartavyaṃ na tu yādṛcchikaṃ kvacit || iti |

yādṛcchikaṃ malāpakarṣaṇārtham,

	malavyapohanaphalaṃ snānaṃ yādṛcchikaṃ tu tat |

iti gargasmaraṇāt | evaṃ ca yad uktam āpastambena,

	vinā tu santatasnānaṃ na snāyād daśamīṣu ca |

iti, tat kāmyanaimittikayor api pradarśanārtham ity avagantavyam |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ malāpakarṣaṇasnānam**

**athānye 'pi tithiprayuktaniṣedhāḥ pradarśyante**

tatra kratuḥ |

	ṣaṣṭhīṃ ca saptamīṃ caiva navamīṃ ca trayodaśīm |

	saṃkrāntau ravivāre ca snānam āmalakais tyajet ||

yogayājñavalkyo 'pi |

	dhātrīphalair amāvāsyā saptamīnavamīṣu ca |

	na snāyāt tatra hīyante teja āyur dhanaṃ sutāḥ ||

dhātrī āmalakī | mārkaṇḍeyo 'pi |

	saptamyāṃ na spṛśet tailaṃ nīlavastraṃ na dhārayet |

	na cāpy āmalakaiḥ snāyān na kuryāt kalahaṃ naraḥ ||

vyāso 'pi |

	ṣaṣṭhy aṣṭamī pañcadaśī pakṣadvayacaturdaśī |

	atra saṃnihitaṃ pāpaṃ taile māṃse kṣure bhage ||

etad darśapūrṇamāsavyatiriktaviṣayam, tasya tatraiva vidhānāt | vyāghro 'pi |

	aṣṭamyāṃ ca caturdaśyāṃ pañcadaśyāṃ trijanmani |

	tailaṃ māṃsaṃ vyavāyaṃ ca dantakāṣṭhaṃ ca varjayet ||

vyavāyo maithunam | atrir api |

	ṣaṣṭhyāṃ tailam anāyuṣyam aṣṭamyāṃ piśitaṃ (?) tathā |

	kṣurakarma caturdaśyām amāyāṃ maithunaṃ tathā ||

	dantakāṣṭham amāvāsyāṃ maithunaṃ ca caturdaśīm |

	hanti saptakulaṃ puṃsāṃ tailagrahaṇam aṣṭamīm ||

purāṇe 'pi |

	kuhūpūrṇendusaṃkrānticaturdaśyaṣṭamīṣu ca |

	naraś caṇḍālayoniḥ syāt tailastrīmāṃsasevanāt ||

dhaumyo 'pi |

	māṃsāśane pañcadaśī tailābhyaṅge caturdaśī |

	aṣṭamīṃ grāmyadharme ca jvalantam api pātayet ||

grāmyadharmo maithunam | purāṇe 'pi |

	caturdaśy aṣṭamī ṣaṣṭhī amāvāsyā ca pūrṇimā |

	parvāṇy etāni rājendra ravisaṃkrāntir eva ca ||

	tailastrīmāṃsasaṃbhogī parvasv eteṣu yaḥ pumān |

	viṇmūtrabhojanaṃ nāma prayāti narakaṃ dhruvam ||

mārkaṇḍeyo 'pi |

	aṣṭamī ca tathā ṣaṣṭī navamī ca caturdaśī |

	kṣurakarmaṇi varjyāḥ syuḥ parvasaṃdhis tathaiva ca ||

	amāvāsyāsu sarvāsu navavastraṃ na dhārayet ||

pracetā api |

	vidhukṣaye na gaccheta prāptakālām api striyam |

	tailaṃ ca na spṛśed āmavṛkṣādīṃś ca kartayet ||

viṣṇupurāṇe 'pi |

	chinatti vīrudho yas tu vīrutsaṃsthe niśākare |

	patraṃ vā pātayaty ekaṃ brahmahatyāṃ sa vindati ||

śaṅkho 'pi |

	amāvāsyāsu na chindyāt kuśāṃs tu samidhas tathā |

	sarvatrāvasthite some hiṃsāyāṃ brahmahā bhavet ||

paiṭhīnasir api: "nāmāvāsyāyām aṅkurāṇi chindyāt" iti | evaṃ ca yad uktaṃ jābālinā,

	kuśān kāśaṃ ca puṣpāṇi gavārthaṃ ca tṛṇādikam |

	niṣedhe cāpi gṛhṇīyād amāvāsyāhani dvijaḥ ||

iti, tac chāntīyakuśādigrahaṇam ity anusaṃdheyam |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ tithiprayuktaniṣedhāḥ**

**atha kriyāsnānam**

tatra śaṅkhaḥ |

	kriyāsnānaṃ pravakṣyāmi yathāvad vidhipūrvakam |

	mṛdbhir adbhiś ca kartavyaṃ śaucam ādau yathāvidhi ||

	jale nimagnas tūnmajjya upaspṛśya yathāvidhi |

	tīrthasyāvāhanaṃ kuryāt tat pravakṣyāmy ataḥ param ||

	prapadye varuṇaṃ devam ambhasāṃ patim ūrjitam |

	yācitaṃ dehi me tīrthaṃ sarvapāpāpanuttaye ||

	tīrtham āvāhayiṣyāmi sarvapāpaniṣūdanam |

	sāṃnidhyam asmin sve toye sthīyatāṃ madanugrahāt ||

	rudrān prapadye varadān sarvān apsupadas tv aham |

	sarvān apsupadaś caiva prapadye varuṇas tv iha ||

	devam apsupadaṃ vahniṃ prapadye 'riniṣūdanam |

	apaḥ puṇyāḥ pavitrāś ca prapadye śaraṇaṃ tathā ||

	sarve rudrās tathāgniś ca varuṇaś cāpa eva ca |

	samayantv āśu me pāpaṃ rakṣantu ca sadāpsu mām ||

	ity evam uktvā kartavyaṃ tataḥ saṃmārjanaṃ kuśaiḥ |

	āpo hiṣṭheti tisṛbhir yathāvad anupūrvaśaḥ ||

                        hiraṇyavarṇā iti ca ṛgbhiś ca tisṛbhis tathā |

                        śaṃ no devīr iti tathā śaṃ na āpas tathaiva ca ||

                        idam āpaḥ pravahatety evaṃ ca samudīrayet |

                        evaṃ saṃmārjanaṃ kṛtvā chanda ārṣaṃ ca daivatam ||

                        aghamarṣaṇasūktaṃ ca saṃsmaret prayataḥ sadā |

                        tathāmbhasi nimagnas tu triḥ paṭhed aghamarṣaṇam ||

                        pradadyān mūrdhni ca tathā mahāvyāhṛtibhir jalam || iti |

 

 

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ kriyāsnānam**

** **

** **

**atha snānārhajalāni**

 

tatra manuḥ |

                        nadīṣu devakhāteṣu taṭākeṣu saraḥsu ca |

                        snānaṃ samācaren nityaṃ gartaprasravaṇeṣu ca ||

devakhātaṃ devanirmitam, na tu sthāvarakṛttrimaṃ jalam | gartas tu kātyāyanena pradarśitaḥ |

                        dhanuḥsahasrāṇy aṣṭau tu gatir yāsāṃ na vidyate |

                        na tā nadīśabdavahā gartās tāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ||

anenārthān nadīlakṣaṇam apy uktaṃ bhavati | parvatādeḥ stokajalapravāhaḥ prasravaṇam | viṣṇupurāṇe 'pi |

                        nadīnadataṭākeṣu devakhātajaleṣu ca |

                        nityaṃ kriyārthaṃ snāyīta giriprasarvaṇeṣu ca ||

	kūpeṣūdhṛtatoyena snānaṃ kurvīta vā bhuvi |

	snāyītoddhṛtatoyena atha vā bhuvy asaṃbhave ||

mārkaṇḍeyo 'pi |

	purāṇānāṃ narendrāṇām ṛṣīṇāṃ ca mahātmanām |

	snānaṃ kūpataṭākeṣu devatānāṃ samācaret || iti |

mahātmanām ity anena patitādyudapāneṣu na snāyād ity āha | ata eva vṛddhamanuḥ |

	anyāyopāttavittasya patitasya ca vārdhuṣeḥ |

	na snāyād udapāneṣu snātvā kṛcchraṃ samācaret || iti |

evam anutsṛṣṭeṣv api draṣṭavyam | yad āha vyasaḥ |

	anutsṛṣṭeṣu na snāyāt tathaivāsaṃskṛteṣv api |

asaṃskṛtam apratiṣṭhitam | anutsṛṣṭam adattaṃ parakīyam iti yāvat | ata eva jābāliḥ |

	na pārakye sadā snāyān na bhuñjīta mahāniśi |

	nārdram ekaṃ ca vasanaṃ paridadhyāt kadācana ||

manur api |

	parakīyanipāteṣu na snāyāc ca kadācana |

	nipānakartuḥ snātvā tu duṣkṛtāṃśena lipyate || iti |

yat punar vyāsenoktam,

	pañca piṇḍān samuddhṛtya pārakye snānam ācaret |

iti,tan nadyādyalābhaviṣayam | tathā ca yamaḥ |

	alābhe devakhātānāṃ sarasāṃ saritāṃ tathā |

	uddhṛtya caturaḥ piṇḍān pārakye snānam ācaret || iti |

anenaivābhiprāyeṇa śaunako 'pi |

	vāpīkūpataṭākeṣu yadi snāyāt kadācana |

	uddhṛtya mṛttikāpiṇḍān daśa pañcātha va kṣipet ||

yogayājñavalkyo 'pi |

	parakīyanipānexu yadi snāyāt kadācana |

	sapta piṇḍān tadoddhṛtya tataḥ snānaṃ samācaret || iti |

atra yathāsāmarthyaṃ vyavasthā | evam anuddhṛtya parakīye yaḥ snāti tasyaiva taddoṣabhāktvam ity uktaṃ bhavati | uktaṃ ca śaunakena |

	anuddhṛtya tu yaḥ snāyāt parakīyajalāśaye |

	vṛthā bhavati tat snānaṃ kartuḥ pāpena lipyate ||

vṛthā niṣphalam ity arthaḥ | utsṛṣṭe tu sarvārthatvāt tadabhāvād anuddharaṇe 'pi na doṣa iti bhāvaḥ | evam uṣṇodakasnāne 'pi naiṣphalyam āha śaṅkhaḥ |

	snātasya vahnitaptena tathaiva paravāriṇā |

	śarīraśuddhir vijñeyā na tu snānaphalaṃ labhet ||

yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	vṛthā tūṣṇodakasnānaṃ vṛtha japyam avaidikam |

	vṛthā tv aśrotriye dānaṃ vṛthā bhuktam asākṣikam ||

yat tu kaiścid uktam,

	āpa eva sadā pūtās tāsāṃ vahnir viśodhakaḥ |

	tasmāt sarveṣu kāleṣu uṣṇāmbhaḥ pāvanaṃ smṛtam ||

iti, yad api ṣaṭtriṃsanmate,

	āpaḥ svabhāvato medhyāḥ kiṃ punar vahnisaṃyutāḥ |

	tena santaḥ praśaṃsanti snanam uṣṇena vāriṇā ||

iti, tad āturasnānaviṣayam | tathā ca yamaḥ |

	ādityakariṇaiḥ pūtaṃ punaḥ pūtaṃ tu vahninā |

	āmnātam āturasnāne praśastaṃ tu kuśodakam || iti |

yadā tu nadyādijalaṃ na labhyate tadānāturasyāpy uṣṇodakasnānam aviruddham ity āha sa eva |

	nityaṃ naimittikaṃ caiva kriyāṅgaṃ malakarṣaṇam |

	tīrthābhāve tu kartavyam uṣṇodakaparodakaiḥ || iti |

yat tu vṛddhamanunoktam,

	mṛte janmani saṃkrāntau śrāddhe janmadine tathā |

	aspṛśyasparśane caiva na snāyād uṣṇavāriṇā ||

	saṃkrāntyāṃ bhānuvāre ca saptamyāṃ rāhudarśane |

	ārogyaputrāmitrārthī na snāyād uṣṇavāriṇā ||

	sa gohatyākṛtaṃ pāpaṃ prāpnoty eva na saṃśayaḥ |

iti, tenāpy ukteṣu maraṇādiṣu tīrthābhāve 'pi noṣṇodakaiḥ snāyāt kiṃ tu parodakair uddhṛtair ity uktam ity avirodhaḥ | uṣṇodakasnāne tu viśeṣam āha vyāsaḥ |

	śītāsv apsu nipicyoṣṇā (?) mantrasaṃbhārasaṃbhṛtāḥ |

	gehe vā śasyate snānaṃ tad dhīnam aphalaṃ bahiḥ || iti |

saṃbhārā mṛdādayaḥ | ata eva madhyandinādhikāre vivasvān |

	mantrasaṃbhārasaṃyuktam upasparsanam ucyate |

	snāne 'vagāhane caiva plāvanaṃ vidhivarjitam || iti | \
tathālpodake 'pi na snāyād ity āha śaṅkhaḥ: "nālpodake snāyān na samudrodake 'vagāheta" iti | smṛtyantare 'pi |

	nāturo nāruṇakarānākrānte ca nabhaḥsthale |

	na parāmbhasi nālpe ca nāśiraskaḥ kathaṃcana || iti |

etat prabhūtodaksaṃbhavābhiprāyam | yad āha yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	prabhūte vidyamāne tu udake sumanohare |

	nālpodake dvijaḥ snāyān nadīṃ cotsṛjya kṛttrime ||

purāṇo 'pi |

	nadyāṃ tu vidyamānāyāṃ na snāyād anyavāriṣu |

	na snāyād alpatoye tu vidyamāne bahūdake ||

puṇyodake saṃbhavati nāpuṇye snāyād ity arthaḥ | tatra puṇyodakāny āha mārkaṇḍeyaḥ |

	bhūmiṣṭam uddhṛtāt puṇaṃ (?) tataḥ prasravaṇodakam |

	tato 'pi sārasaṃ puṇyaṃ tasmān nādeyam ucyate ||

	tīrthatoyaṃ tataḥ puṇyaṃ gāṅgaṃ puṇyaṃ tu sarvataḥ ||

tīrthatoyaṃ sādhuparigṛhītaṃ jalam | viṣṇur api: "uddhṛtāt puṇyaṃ bhūmiṣṭham udakam | tasmān nādeyam | tasmād api sādhuparigṛhītam | sarvata eva gāṅgam" iti | vivasvān api |

	ekataḥ sarvatīrthāni jāhnavy ekaiva cānyataḥ |

	brahmalokeśaśirasaḥ patitā yā mahītale ||

marīcir api |

	bhūmiṣṭham uddhṛtaṃ vāpi śītam uṣṇam athāpi vā |

	gāṅgaṃ payaḥ punāty āśu pāpam āmaraṇāntikam ||

	tribhiḥ sārasvataṃ toyaṃ pañcāhena tu yāmunam |

	sadyaḥ punāti gāṅgeyaṃ darśanād eva nārmadam ||

yogayājñavalkyo 'pi |

	trirātraphaladā nadyaḥ yāḥ kāścid asamudragāḥ |

	samudragās tu pakṣasya māsasya saritāṃ patiḥ ||

saritāṃ patiḥ samudraḥ | atra vyāsaḥ |

	nadyām astam ite snānaṃ varjayet tu sadā budhaḥ |

	nadyāṃ snātvā nadīṃ cānyāṃ na praśaṃseta dharmavit || iti |

devalo 'pi |

	na nadīṣu nadīṃ brūyāt parvateṣu na parvatam |

	nānyaṃ praśaṃsayet tīrthaṃ tīrtheṣv āyataneṣu ca || iti |

jalāvagāhanaṃ prakṛtya āpastambaḥ: "saśirāvamajjanam apsu varjayet" iti | etat sthāvarodakaviṣayam | tathā ca purāṇam |

	sravannadīṣu tu snāyāt praviśyāntaḥsthito dvijaḥ |

	taṭākādiṣu toyeṣu pratyarkaṃ snānam ācaret || iti |

atra varjyodakāny āha vyāsaḥ |

	nadyā yac ca paribhraṣṭaṃ nadyā yac ca viniḥsṛtam |

	gatapratyāgataṃ yac ca tat toyaṃ parivarjayet ||

	na meheta jaladroṇyāṃ snātuṃ ca na nadīṃ taret ||

paribhraṣṭaṃ vicchinnam | yan niḥsṛtam vicchinnaṃ tad varjayet | āvartāgataṃ gatapratyāgatam | gargo 'pi |

	pratyāvarte (?) 'mbhasi snānaṃ nadyāṃ varjyaṃ dvijātibhiḥ |

bodhāyano 'pi |

	adhovarṇodake snānaṃ varjyaṃ nadyāṃ dvijātibhiḥ |

	tasyāṃ rajakatīrthe tu daśahastena varjayet ||

	snānaṃ rajakatīrthe tu bhojanaṃ gaṇikāgṛhe |

	paścimottaraśāyitvaṃ śakrād api harec chriyam ||

gaṇikā veśyā | yogayājñavalkyo 'pi |

	agrāhyās tv agrimā āpo nadyāḥ prathamavedikāḥ |

	prakṣobhitāś ca kenāpi yāś ca tīrthād viniḥsṛtāḥ ||

agrimā navāḥ | smṛtyantare |

	ajā gāvo mahiṣyaś ca brāhmaṇyaś ca prasūtikāḥ |

	daśarātreṇa śuddhyanti bhūmiṣṭhaṃ ca navodakam ||

kātyāyano 'pi |

	yāḥ śoṣam upagacchanti grīṣme kusarito bhuvi |

	tāsu prāvṛṣi na snāyād apūrṇe daśavāsare || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ snānārhajalāni **

**atha nadīrajodoṣanirṇayaḥ**

atra yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	yāvan nodeti bhagavān dakṣiṇāśāvibhūṣaṇaḥ (?) |

	tāvad retovahā nadyo varjayitvā tu jāhnavīm ||

yāvan nodety agastyas tāvan nadyo retovahā rajasvalā ity arthaḥ | udayo 'pi tasyodīcyadeśe śarady eva jyotiḥśāstre darśitaḥ | evaṃ ca varṣākāle rajasvalā ity uktaṃ bhavati | ata eva kātyāyanaḥ |

	saṃprāpte śrāvaṇe māse sarvā nadyo rajasvalāḥ |

	tāsu snānaṃ na kurvīta varjayitvā tu jāhnavīm || iti |

saṃprāpte śrāvaṇe māse yāvan māsadvayam iti śeṣaḥ | ata eva mārkaṇḍeyaḥ |

	dvimāsaṃ saritaḥ sarvā bhavanti hi rajasvalāḥ |

	apraśastaṃ tataḥ snānaṃ varṣādau navavāriṇi || iti |

etat samudraganadīvyatiriktaviṣayam | tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ |

	yavyadvayaṃ śrāvaṇādau sarvā nadyo rajasvalāḥ |

	tāsu snānaṃ na kurvīta varjayitvā samudragām || iti |

yavyo māsaḥ, "yavyā māsāt sumekaḥ saṃvatsaraḥ" iti śatapathaśruteḥ | samudragāsv api kāsucid rajodoṣam āha sa eva |

	prāvṛṭkāle mahānadyaḥ santi sadyorajasvalāḥ |

	tāsu snānaṃ na kurvīta varjayitvā tu jāhnavīm || iti |

mahānadīṣv api jāhnavīṃ varjayitvety arthaḥ | mahānadyo vāmanapurāṇe darśitāḥ |

	godāvarī bhīmarathī kṛṣṇaveṇī sarasvatī |

	tuṅgabhadrā suprayāgā veṇī kāveriketi ca ||

	dugdhodā nalinā revā vārā śītā kalasvanā |

	etā api mahānadyo sahyamūlād vinirgatāḥ ||

nṛsiṃhapurāṇe 'pi: "gaṅgā yamunā godāvarī taṅgabhadrā kāverīty etā mahānadyaḥ" iti | snānagrahaṇaṃ tarpaṇāder api pradarśanārtham | yad āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	nabhonabhasyayor madhye sarvā nadyo rajasvalāḥ |

	na snānādīni karmāṇi tāsu kurvīta mānavaḥ || iti |

karkaṭakādimāsadvayaṃ yāvat tāvad rajasvalā ity arthaḥ | yat tu kātyāyanena "prāvṛṭkāle" ity upakramya "varjayitvā tu jāhnavīm" ity uktaṃ na tat tasyāḥ sarvatra prāvṛṭkāle rajoyogābhāvapratipādanaparam | yataḥ sa evāha |

	prqavṛtte śrāvaṇe māse tryahaṃ gaṅgā rajasvalā |

	caturthe 'hani saṃprāpte śuddhā bhavati jāhnavī || iti |

etad api sauramānābhiprāyam (?) | anyathā,

	prathamaṃ karkaṭe devi tryahaṃ gaṅgā rajasvalā |

	sarvā raktā mahānadyaḥ karatoyāmbuvāhinī || 

iti yogayājñavalkyavacanavirodhaḥ syāt, śrāvaṇamāsapravṛtter arvāg eva karkaṭasaṃkrāntiniyamāt (?) | karatoyā nadī | atra yamaḥ |

	gaṅgā dharmodbhavā puṇyā yamunā ca sarasvatī |

	antargatarajoyogāḥ sarvāheṣv api cāmalāḥ ||

	pratisrotorajoyogo rathyājalaniṣevaṇam |

	gaṅgāyāṃ na praduṣyanti sā hi dharmodbhavā svayam ||

vāmanapurāṇe 'pi |

	sarasvatī nadī puṇyā tathā vaitaraṇī nadī |

	āpagā ca mahāpuṇyā gaṅgā mandākinī tathā ||

	madhusravā cāṃśunadī kauśikī pāpanāśinī |

	dṛśadvatī mahāpuṇyā tathā hairaṇyavatī nadī ||

	varṣākālavahāḥ sarvā varjayitvā sarasvatīm |

	etāsām udakaṃ puṇyaṃ varṣākāle pravarṣitam ||

	rajasvalātvam etāsāṃ vidyate na kadācana ||

kātyāyano 'pi |

	tapanasya sutā gaṅgā gomatī ca saridvarā |

	rajasā na praduṣyanti ye cānye punnadāḥ smṛtāḥ ||

tapasya sutā yamunā | mārkaṇḍeyo 'pi |

	ādityaduhitā gaṅgā plakṣajātā sarasvatī |

	rajasā nābhibhūyante ye cānye nadasaṃjñikāḥ || iti |

kurukṣetre yā sarasvatī sā plakṣajātā | tathā gomatyādiṣv api karkaṭādau trirātram āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	karkaṭādau rajoduṣṭā gomatī vāsaratrayam |

	candrabhāgā satī sindhuḥ sarayūr narmadā tathā || iti |

evamuktarajodoṣasya kvacid apavādam āha sa eva |

	upākarmaṇi cotsarge prātaḥsnāne tathaiva ca |

	candrasūryagrahe caiva rajodoṣo na vidyate ||

	svardhunyambhaḥsamāni syuḥ sarvāṇy ambhāṃsi bhūtale |

	kūpasthāṇy api somārkagrahaṇe nātra saṃśayaḥ || iti |

ataḥ kathaṃ rajodoṣa iti bhāvaḥ | svardhunī gaṅgā |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ nadīrajodoṣanirṇayaḥ**

**atha prasaṅgāt tīrthasnānamantrāḥ pradarśyante**

	viṣṇupādābjasaṃbhūte gaṅge tripathagāmini |

	dharmapradetivikhyāte pāpaṃ me hara jāhnavi ||

	śraddhayā dharmasaṃpanne śrīmātar devi jāhnavi |

	amṛtenāmbunā devi bhāgīrathi punīhi mām ||

iti gaṅgāsnānamantraḥ |

	karatoye sadānīre saricchreṣṭetiviśrute |

	āplāvayasi pautrāṇāṃ pāpaṃ hara karodbhave ||

iti karatoyāsnānamantraḥ |

	gādhirājasute devi viśvāmitramuneḥ sute |

	ṛcīkabhārye satyārye pāpaṃ me hara kauśiki ||

iti kauśikīsnānamantraḥ |

	sahyapādodbhave devi śrīśailotsaṅgagāmini |

	kṛṣṇaveṇīti vikhyāte sarvapāpapraṇāśini ||

	sahyapādodbhavā devī kṛṣṇaveṇīti viśrutā |

	sarvapāpaviśuddhyarthaṃ snāsye devi tavāmbhasi ||

	prasīda me devi sadā rasena deveśasṛṣṭā jagatāṃ vimuktyai |

	snānena yasyām avadhūtapapaḥ prāpnoti viṣṇoḥ padam eva martyaḥ ||

	brahmāmṛtānandrasena pūrṇā jalena pūrṇām iva menire janāḥ |

	tāṃ tvāvahāhāmi pibāmi kṛṣṇe devān ṛṣīṃs tarpayiṣye pitṝṃś ca || 

iti kṛṣṇaveṇīsnānamantraḥ |

	bhīmasenasamudbhūte rathanemiviniḥsṛte |

	sarvapāpapraṇāśārthaṃ snāsye devi tavāmbhasi ||

iti bhīmarathīsnānamantraḥ |

	nabho 'stu te puṇyajale namaḥ sāgaragāmini |

	narmade pāpanirmoce namo devi varānane ||

	namo 'stu te munigaṇasiddhasevite namo 'stu te śaṅkaradehaniḥsṛte |

	namo 'stu te dharmabhṛtāṃ varaprade namo 'stu te sarvapavitrapāvini ||

iti narmadāsnānamantraḥ |

	tvaṃ devi saritāṃ nāthe tvaṃ devi saritāṃ vare |

	ubhayoḥ saṅgame snātvā muñcāmi duritāni vāi ||

iti gaṅgāsāgarasaṅgamasnānamantraḥ |

	brahmaputra mahābhāga (?) śantanoḥ kulavardhana |

	amoghagarbhasaṃbhūta pāpaṃ lauhitya me hara ||

iti lauhityasnānamantraḥ |

	agnis tu te yonir iḍā ca deho reto 'pi viṣṇor amṛtasya nābhiḥ |

	etad bruvan pāṇḍava satyavākyaṃ tato 'vagāheta patiṃ nadīnām ||

iti sāgarasnānamantraḥ |

	ājanmaśatasāhasre yat pāpaṃ kurute kvacit |

	mucyate sarvapāpebhyaḥ snātvaiva lavaṇāmbhasi ||

	aśvatthaḥ sāgaraś caiva na spraṣṭavyau kadācana |

	aśvatthaṃ mandavāre tu sāgaraṃ parvaṇi spṛśet ||

	anyadā tu kuruśreṣṭha devayonir apāṃ patiḥ |

	kuśāgreṇāpi kaunteya na spraṣṭavyo mahodadhiḥ || iti |

atrodakāntareṇaivācamanaṃ kāryam, na samudrodakena, "akṣārābhir anuṣṇābhir ācāmet" iti smaraṇāt | na ca yena snānaṃ tenaivācamanam ity api niyamo 'sti | uktaṃ ca taittirīyakaśrutau: "tasmāt samudrasya na pibanti" iti | tapraṇādikaṃ tu tenaiva kāryam, niṣedhābhāvāt | evam uṣṇodakakuṇḍasnāne 'pi draṣṭavyam | atra tīrthaprasaṅgāt paiṭhīnasiḥ |

	ṣoḍaśāṃśaṃ sa labhate yaḥ parārthena gacchati |

	ardhatīrthaphalaṃ tasya yaḥ prasaṅgena gacchati ||

śaṅkho 'pi |

	tīrthaṃ prāpyānuṣaṅgeṇa yas tatra snānam ācaret |

	snānajaṃ phalam āpnoti tīrthayātrāśritaṃ na tu ||

	nṛṇāṃ pāpakṛtāṃ tīrthe pāpapraśamanaṃ bhavet |

	yathoktaphaladaṃ tīrthaṃ bhavec chuddhātmanāṃ nṛṇām ||

vyāso 'pi |

	yasya hastau ca pādau ca manaś caiva susaṃyatam |

	vidyā tapaś ca kīrtiś ca sa tīrthaphalam aśnute ||

vṛddhavasiṣṭho 'pi |

	pitaraṃ mātaraṃ vāpi bhrātaraṃ suhṛdaṃ gurum |

	majjayet tu yam uddiśya dvādaśāṃśaṃ labheta saḥ ||

paiṭhīnasir api |

	yaḥ prakṛtiṃ kuśamayīṃ tīrthavāriṇi majjayet |

	majjayet tu yam uddiśya hy aṣṭabhāgaṃ labheta saḥ ||

atrāyaṃ mantraḥ |

	kuśo 'si tvaṃ pavitro 'si brahmaṇā nirmitaḥ purā |

	tvayi snāte tu sa snāto yasyaitad granthibandhanam || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ tīrthasnānamantrāḥ **

**atha gauṇasnānāni**

tatra gargaḥ |

	divyaṃ vāyavyam āgneyaṃ brāhmaṃ sārasvataṃ tathā |

	mānasaṃ ceti vijñeyaṃ gauṇasnānaṃ tu ṣaḍvidham ||

yogayājñavalkyo 'pi |

	māntraṃ bhaumaṃ tathāgneyaṃ vāyavyaṃ divyam eva ca |

	vāruṇaṃ mānasaṃ caiva sapta sānāny anukramāt || iti |

eteṣāṃ lakṣaṇam āha sa eva |

	āpo hiṣṭhādibhir māntraṃ mṛdālambhaś ca pārthivam |

	āgneyaṃ bhasmanā snānaṃ vāyavyaṃ gorajaḥ smṛtam ||

	yat tu sātapavarṣeṇa tat snānaṃ divyam ucyate |

	vāruṇaṃ cāvagahas tu mānasaṃ viṣṇucintanam ||

	mānasaṃ pravaraṃ snānaṃ kecid icchanti sūrayaḥ |

	ātmatīrthapraśaṃsāyāṃ vyāsena paṭhitaṃ yataḥ ||

atra viśeṣaḥ kūrmapurāṇe darśitaḥ |

	āgneyaṃ bhasmanāpādamastakād dehadhūlanam |

yogayājñavalkyo 'pi |

	śaṃ na āpas tu druṣadā āpohiṣṭhāghamarṣaṇam |

	etais tu pañcabhir mantrair mantrasnānam udāhṛtam ||

bṛhaspatir api |

	vāyavyaṃ gorajaḥ proktas taṃ gacchati gopatau |

	vidvatsarasvatīprāptaṃ snānaṃ sārasvataṃ smṛtam ||

gopatau sūrye | viduṣāṃ sarasvatī vāṇī tayā prāptaṃ sārasvatam ity arthaḥ | tatsvarūpam āha vyāsaḥ |

	svayam evopapannāya vinayena dvijātaye |

	tajjñaḥ saṃpādayet snānaṃ śiṣyāya ca sutāya ca ||

	dākṣāyaṇamayaiḥ kumbhair mantravaj jāhnavījalaiḥ |

	kṛtamaṅgalapuṇyāhaiḥ snānam astu tadarthinām ||

	ādau tāvat prabhāse bahuguṇasalile madhyame puṣkare vā |

	gaṅgādvāre prayāge kanakhalasahite bhadrakarṇe gayāyām ||

	rāhugraste tu some dinakarasahite saṃnipatyā viśeṣāt |

	etair vyākhyātatīrthais tribhuvanavihitaiḥ snānam acchidram astu ||

	prāpya sārasvataṃ snānaṃ bhaven muditamānasaḥ |

	sarvatīrthābhiṣekād dhi pavitraṃ viduṣāṃ hi vāk || iti |

etāni gauṇasnāny aśaktāv eva kārayet | tad uktaṃ kūrmapurāṇe |

	aprāyatye samutpanne snānam eva samācaret |

	brāhmādīny ayathāśaktau snānāny āhur manīṣiṇaḥ ||

yogayājñavalkyo 'pi |

	kāladoṣād asāmarthyān na śaknoti yadā hy asau |

	tadā jñātvā ṛṣibhyas tu mantrair dṛṣṭaṃ tu mārjanam ||

jābālir api |

	aśiraskaṃ bhavet snānaṃ snānāśaktau tu karmiṇām |

	ārdreṇa vāsasā vāpi mārjanaṃ daivikaṃ viduḥ || iti |

etat kapilaṃ snānam | tad āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	ārdreṇa kapaṭenāṅgaśodhanaṃ kāpilaṃ smṛtam | iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ gauṇasnānāni**

**atha saṃdhyāpraśaṃsā**

tatra yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi saṃdhyopāsananirṇayam |

	ahorātrakṛtaiḥ pāpair yām upāsya pramucyate ||

	sarvāvastho 'pi yo vipraḥ saṃdhyopāsanatatparaḥ |

	brāhmaṇyāc ca na hīyeta anyajanmagato 'pi saḥ ||

	yāvanto 'syāṃ pṛthivyāṃ tu vikarmasthā dvijātayaḥ |

	teṣāṃ hi pāvanārthāya sṛṣṭā saṃdhyā svayaṃbhuvā ||

	triṃśatkoṭyas tu vikhyātā mandehā nāma rākṣasāḥ |

	pradravanti sahasrāṃśum udyantaṃ dine dine ||

	ahany ahani te sarve sūryam icchanti khāditum |

	ataḥ sūryasya teṣāṃ ca yuddham āsīt sudāruṇam ||

	tato devagaṇāḥ sarve ṛṣayaś ca tapodhanāḥ |

	saṃdhyāṃ tu samupāsīnā yat kṣipanty anvahaṃ jalam ||

	brahmavyāhṛtisaṃyuktaṃ gāyatryā cābhimantritam |

	dahyante tena te daityā vajrībhūtena vāriṇā ||

	etad viditvā yaḥ saṃdhyām upāste saṃśitavrataḥ |

	dīrgham āyuḥ sa vindeta sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ||

	yas tu tāṃ kevalāṃ saṃdhyām upāsīta sa puṇyabhāk |

	tām parityajya karmāṇi kurvann āpnoti kilbiṣam ||

	brahmaṇopāsitā saṃdhyā viṣṇunā śaṅkareṇa ca |

	kas tāṃ nopāsayed devīṃ siddhikāmo dvijottamaḥ ||

kaśyapo 'pi |

	brahmaṇo hṛdayaṃ viṣṇur viṣṇor api śivaḥ smṛtaḥ |

	śivasya hṛdayaṃ saṃdhyā tenopāsyā dvijottamaiḥ || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ saṃdhyāpraśaṃsā **

**atha saṃdhyāśabdārthanirṇayaḥ **

tatra dakṣaḥ |

	ahorātrasya yaḥ saṃdhiḥ sūryanakṣatravarjitaḥ |

	sā tu saṃdhyā samākhyātā munibhis tattvadarśibhiḥ || iti |

sā saṃdhyā upāsyeti śeṣaḥ | ata eva yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	saṃdhau saṃdhyām upāsīta nāstage nodgate ravau |

chandogaśrutir api: "brahmavādino vadanti: kasmād brāhmaṇo 'horātrasaṃyoge saṃdhyām upāste | kasmād brāhmaṇaḥ sāyam āsīnaḥ saṃdhyām upāste | kasmāt prātas tiṣṭhan | kā ca saṃdhyā | kaś ca saṃdhyākālaḥ | kiṃ ca saṃdhyāyāḥ saṃdhyātvam | daivāś cāsurāś cāspardhanta | te asurā ādityam abhidravan | sa ādityo 'bibhet | tasya hṛdayaṃ kūrmarūpeṇātiṣṭhat sa prajāpatim upādhāvat tasya prajāpatir etad bheṣajam apaśyat | ṛtaṃ ca satyaṃ ca brahma coṃkāraṃ ca tripadāṃ gāyatrīṃ brahmaṇo mukham apaśyat | tasmād brahmaṇo 'horātrasaṃyoge saṃdhyām upāste | sajyotiṣy ā jyotiṣo darśanāt so 'sya saṃdhyākālaḥ | sā saṃdhyā | tat saṃdhyāyāḥ saṃdhyatvam | yat sāyam āsīnaḥ saṃdhyām upāste tayā vīrasthānaṃ jayati | yat prātas tiṣṭhan tayā svargalokaṃ jayati | atha yad apaḥ prayuṅkte tā vipruṣo vajrībhūtvā asurān apāghnanti" iti | anenāpi yā upāsyā sā saṃdhyā ity uktaṃ bhavati | "sajyotiṣi" sasūrye kāle prārabhya "ā jyotiṣo darśanāt" ā nakṣatradarśanāt upāsītety arthaḥ | tathā ca nārasiṃhapurāṇam |

	upāsya paścimāṃ saṃdhyāṃ sādityāṃ vai yathāvidhi |

	gāyatrīm abhyaset tāvad yāvad ṛkṣāṇi paśyati ||

	pūrvāṃ saṃdhyāṃ sanakṣatrām upakramya yathāvidhi |

	gāyatrīm abhyaset tāvad yāvad ādityadarśanam ||

sanakṣatrām ity anenāniyame prāpte niyamārtham āha dakṣaḥ |

	rātryantayāmanāḍī dve saṃdhyāyāḥ kala ucyate |

	darsanād ravirekhāyās tadanto sumibhiḥ smṛtaḥ ||

ravirekhāyā darsanād upalakṣitaḥ kālaḥ saṃdhyānta ity arthaḥ | sā ca saṃdhyā yogayājñavalkyena darsitā |

	pūrvā saṃdhyā tu gāyatrī sāvitrī madhyamā smṛtā |

	yā bhavet paścimā saṃdhyā sā vijñeyā sarasvatī ||

vyāso 'pi |

	gāyatrī nāma pūrvāhṇe sāvitrī madhyame dine |

	sarasvatī ca sāyāhne saiva saṃdhyā triṣu smṛtā ||

	pratigrahād annadoṣāt pātakād upapātakāt |

	gāyatrī procyate tasmād gāyantaṃ trāyate yataḥ ||

	savitṛdyotanāc caiva sāvitrī parikīrtitā |

	jagataḥ prasavitrī yā vāgnūpatvāt (?) sarasvatī ||

	upāste saṃdhivelāyāṃ niśāyā divasasya ca |

	tām eva saṃdhyāṃ tasmāc ca pravadanti manīṣiṇaḥ || iti |

atra svādhiṣṭhitamantradvārā tatpratipādyasyāspi sāvitrītvam aviruddham iti bhāvaḥ | ato gāyatryādināmatrayapratipādyaḥ savitaiva saṃdhyetu anusaṃdheyam | uktaṃ ca smṛtyantare |

	prātaḥkāle tu gāyatrī sāyaṃkāle sarasvatī |

	madhandine ca sāvitrī upāsyā nāmabhedataḥ ||

	gāyatrīha bhaved raktā sāvitrī śuklavarṇikā |

	sarasvatī tathā kṛṣṇā upāsyā varṇabhedataḥ ||

	gāyatrī brahmarūpā tu sāvitrī rudrarūpiṇī |

	sarasvatī viṣṇurūpā upāsyā rūpabhedataḥ ||

	udaye brahmarūpaṃ tu madhyāhne tu maheśvaram |

	sāyāhne viṣṇurūpaṃ tu trirūpaṃ vai divākaram ||

	upāsane tu saṃdhyāyāṃ niśāyā divasasya ca |

	tām eva saṃdhyāṃ tasmāc ca pravadanti manīṣiṇaḥ || iti |

upāsanaṃ cātra dhyānam, "vācaṃ brahmety upāsīta | mano brahmety upāsīta" ityādiṣu tathā darśanāt | taittirīyaśrutir api: "udyantam astaṃ yantam ādityam abhidhyāyan kurvan brāhmaṇo vidvāṃt sakalaṃ bhadram aśnute 'sāv ādityo brahmeti brahmaivaṃ san brahmāpyeti ya evaṃ veda" iti | uktagāyatyādināmatrayopetaṃ varṇatrayānvitaṃ rūpatrayātmakaṃ saṃdhyāśabdābhilakṣyam ādityaṃ brahmeti kālatraye 'pi yathā krameṇa dhyāyan brahmāpyeti prāpnotīty arthaḥ | ata eva vyāsaḥ |

	nābhinnāṃ pratipadyeta gāyatrīṃ brahmaṇā saha |

	so 'ham asmīty upāsīta vidhinā yena kenacit ||

kūrmapurāṇe 'pi |

	prākkūleṣu tataḥ sthitvā darbheṣu susamāhitaḥ |

	prāṇāyāmatraṃ kṛtvā dhyāyet saṃdhyām iti śrutiḥ ||

	yā saṃdhyā sā jagatsūtir māyātītā hi niṣkalā |

	īśvaro kevalā śaktis tattvatrayasamanvitā ||

	dhyātvārkamaṇḍalagatāṃ sāvitrīṃ vai japed budhaḥ ||

atra dhyānadeśo 'pi smṛtyantare darśitaḥ |

	gāyatrīṃ cintayed yas tu hṛtpadme samupasthitām |

	dharmādharmavinirmuktaḥ sa yāti paramāṃ gatim || iti |

evaṃ ca saṃdhyām upāsītety anena saṃdhyām uktarūpām arkamaṇḍalāntargatām ādityākhyāṃ brahmātmikāṃ devatāṃ hṛdi so 'ham asmīty upāsīta dhyāyed ity uktaṃ bhavati | tenātropāsanam eva pradhānam anyat sarvaṃ mārjanādikam aṅgam ity anusaṃdheyam | ata eva yudhiṣṭhirādibhir yuddhodyataiḥ sāṅgānuṣṭhānāsamarthaiḥ sakalāṅgaparityāgenādityopāsanamātram anuṣṭhitam | tad uktaṃ vyāsena |

	te tathaiva mahārāja saṃśitā raṇamūrdhani |

	saṃdhyāgataṃ sahasrāṃśum ādityam upatasthire || iti |

daṃśitāḥ saṃnaddhāḥ | saṃdhim āgataṃ saṃdhyāgatam astaṃgatam iti yāvat | evaṃ ca yad uktaṃ yogayājñavalkyena,

	oṃkāro vyāhṛtīḥ saptagāyatrī śirasā saha |

	āpo hiṣṭhety ṛcas tisro drupadā cāghamarṣaṇam ||

	ud u tyaṃ citraṃ tac cakṣus tejo 'sīti yathākramam |

	gāyatryāś ca turīyaṃ tu saṃdhyām etaiḥ samācaret || 

iti, tatrāpy etair mantrair ātmaśuddhidvārā saṃdhyā samācared upāsīteti saṃdhyāśabdasya devatāparatvād avirodha iti ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ saṃdhyāśabdārthanirṇayaḥ**

**atha prāthaḥsaṃdhyā**

tatra dakṣaḥ |

	brāhme muhūrta utthāya kṛtaśaucavidhir dvijaḥ |

	prātaḥsaṃdhyām upāsīta dantadhāvanapūrvakam || iti |

śaucagrahaṇaṃ snānasyāpi pradarśanārtham, anyathā saṃdhyādyanadhikārāt | tad āha sa eva |

	asnātvā nācaret karma japahomādi kiṃcana |

	lālāsvedasamākīrṇaḥ śayanād utthitaḥ pumān ||

kūrmapurāṇe 'pi |

	na ca snānaṃ vinā puṃsāṃ prāśastyaṃ karmasu smṛtam |

	home japye viśeṣeṇa tasmāt snānaṃ smācaret || iti |

**atrāyaṃ saṃdhyāprayogaḥ**

kṛtasnānas tv ācānto yathāvidhi prāṇān āyamya prātaḥsaṃdhyām upāsiṣye iti saṃkalpya "āpo hiṣṭhā mayobhuvaḥ" iti tṛceta mārjayet | tad uktaṃ yājñavalkyena |

	prāṇān āyamya saṃprokṣya tṛcenābdaivatena tu | iti |

atra vyāsaḥ |

	sindhudvīpa ṛṣiḥ chando gāyatry āpo hi devatāḥ |

	mārjane viniyogaś ca abdaivatye prakīrtitaḥ ||

āvaśyakaṃ caitad ārṣādijānam anyathā doṣaśravaṇāt | tad āha sa eva |

	aviditvā muniṃ chando daivataṃ yogam eva ca |

	yo 'dhyāpayej japed vāpi pāpīyān jāyate tu saḥ ||

yogayājñavalkyo 'pi |

	brāhmaṇaṃ viniyogaṃ ca chanda ārṣaṃ ca daivatam |

	ājñātā pañca yo mantre na sa tatphalam aśnute || iti |

mārjane tu viśeṣam āha brahmā |

	ṛgante mārjanaṃ kuryāt pādānte vā samāhitaḥ |

	tṛcasyānte 'tha vā kuryāc chiṣṭānāṃ matam īdṛśam || iti |

yogayājñavalkyo 'pi |

	āpo hiṣṭheti tisṛbhiḥ ṛgbhiḥ saṃprayataḥ śuciḥ |

	navapraṇavayuktābhir jalaṃ śirasi nikṣipet || iti |

atra phalaviśeṣam āha śaunakaḥ |

	navapraṇavayuktena āpohiṣṭhātṛcena ca |

	saṃvatsarakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ mārjanānte vinaśyati ||

vyāso 'pi |

	āpohiṣṭhātṛce kuryān mārjanaṃ tu kuśodakaiḥ |

	praṇavena tu saṃyuktaṃ kṣiped vāri pade pade ||

	vipruṣo 'ṣṭau kṣiped ūrdhvam adho yasya kṣayāya jit |

	rajastamomohajātān jāgratsvapnasuṣuptijān |

	vāṅmanaḥkarmajān doṣān navaitān navabhir dahet || iti |

atra pratipādaṃ mārjane kartavye nava vipruṣo bhavanti | tatra "yasya kṣayāya jinvatha" ity anena vipruṣam adho vikṣiped ity arthaḥ | atra hārītaḥ: "mārjanārcanabalikarmabhojanāni daivena tīrthena kuryāt" iti | daivam aṅgulyagram | tac ca mārjanaṃ dhārācyutena na kāryam | tathā ca brahmā |

	dhārācyutena toyena saṃdhyopāstir vigarhitā |

	pitaro na praśaṃsanti na praśaṃsanti devatāḥ || iti |

atra hetum āha sa eva |

	mantrapūtaṃ jalaṃ yasmād āpohiṣṭhābhimantritam |

	pataty aśucideśe tu tasmāt tat parivarjayet || iti |

kathaṃ tarhi mārjanam ity apekṣite sa evāha |

	nadyās tīrthe hrade vāpi bhājane mṛṇmaye 'pi vā |

	audumbare 'tha sauvarṇe rājate dārudaṃbhave ||

	kṛtvā tu vāmahate vā saṃdhyopāstiṃ samācaret | iti |

audumbare tāmramaye kṛtvodakam iti śeṣaḥ | evaṃ ca yad uktam,

	vāmahaste jalaṃ kṛtvā ye tu saṃdhyām upāsate |

	sā saṃdhyā vṛṣalī jñeyā asurās tais tu tarpitāḥ ||

iti, tan mṛṇmayādipātrasadbhāvaviṣayam ity anusaṃdheyam | evam uktena vidhinā mārjayitvā "sūryaś ca" ity apaḥ pibet | tad āha bodhāyanaḥ: "athātaḥ saṃdhyopāsanavidhiṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ | tīrthaṃ gatvā prayato 'bhiṣiktaḥ prakṣālitapāṇipādo 'pa ācamya 'agniś ca mā manyuś ca" iti sāyam apaḥ pītvā "sūryas ca mā manyuś ca" iti prātaḥ sapavitreṇa pāṇinā surabhimatyābliṅgabhir vāruṇībhir hiraṇyavarṇābhiḥ pāvamānībhir vyāhṛtibhir anyaiś ca pavitrair ātmānaṃ prokṣya prayato bhavati" iti | "agniś ca" "sūryaś ca" it yajurvedapaṭhitau mantrau | sūryaś cety asya mantrasya prakṛtiś chandaḥ, agniṛṣiḥ, sūryamanyumanyupatirātrayo (?) devatāḥ, prātaḥsaṃdhyācamane viniyogaḥ | surabhimatī "dadhikrāvṇaḥ" iti | tasyā vāmadeva ṛṣiḥ, anuṣṭup chandaḥ, dadhikrāvā devatā, mārjane viniyogaḥ | abliṅgābhir āpohiṣṭhādibhiḥ | "hiraṇyavarṇābhiḥ" — "hiraṇyavarṇāḥ", "yāsāṃ rājā", "yāsāṃ devāḥ", "śivena mā", iti catasṛbhiḥ | tāsāṃ triṣṭup chandaḥ, agniḥ ṛṣiḥ, āpo devatā, mārjane viniyogaḥ | chandogānāṃ tu ācamanamantrau gautamenoktau: "ahaś ca mādityaś ca punātu ity prātaḥ, rātris ca mā varuṇaḥ punātu iti sāyam" iti | ime yajuṣī prajāpatir apaśyat | liṅgokte devate | saṃdhyācamane tu viseṣam āha viṣṇuḥ |

	jānubhyām upariṣṭāt tu śuṣkavāsāḥ sthito jale |

	sāṃdhyam ācamanaṃ kurvan śuciḥ syād asuciḥ smṛtaḥ ||

saṃdhyacamanānantaraṃ nārāyaṇaḥ |

	spṛṣṭvā cābhiṣṭuta toyaṃ mūrdhni brahmamukhena tu |

	āpo hiṣṭheti sūktena darbhari mārjanam ācaret || iti |

abhiṣṭud oṃkāraḥ | brahmamukham api manunoktam |

	oṃkārapūrvikās tisro mahāvyāhṛtayo 'vyvyāḥ |

	tripadā caiva gāyatrī vijñeyaṃ brahmaṇo mukham || iti |

tena toyaṃ spṛṣṭvā tena toyena āpo hiṣṭheti sūktena darbhair mārjanam ācared ity arthaḥ | tac ca sūktaṃ navarcam | tatra bhṛguḥ |

	āpohiṣṭhā navasv ṛkṣu sindhudvīpa ṛṣiḥ smṛtaḥ 

	abdaivatyās tu saptarco gāyatryo dve anuṣṭubhau ||

mārjanaṃ prakṛtya kātyāyano 'pi |

	śiraso mārjanaṃ kuryāt kuśaiḥ sodakabindubhiḥ |

	praṇavo bhūr bhuvaḥ svaś ca gāyatrī ca tṛtīyakā ||

	abdaivataṃ tṛcaṃ caiva caturtham iti mārjanam ||

mārjanānantaraṃ brahmā |

	jalapūrṇaṃ tathā hastaṃ nāsikāgre samarpayet |

	ṛtaṃ ceti paṭhitvā tu taj jalaṃ tu kṣitau kṣipet ||

yamo 'pi |

	gṛhītvā pāṇinā vāri svaśākhoktām ṛcaṃ japet |

	bibhṛyān nāsikāgre tu niruddhaprāṇamārutaḥ ||

	ya evaṃ drupadāṃ nityaṃ trir ahnaḥ prayato japet |

	na paryuṣanti pāpāni tasya dehe dvijanmanaḥ || iti |

tataḥ sūryārghyaṃ nivedayet | tathā ca vyāsaḥ |

	karābhyāṃ toyam ādāya gāyatryā cābhimantritam |

	ādityābhimukhas tiṣṭhaṃs trir ūrdhvam atha cotkṣipet ||

atra viśeṣam āha hārītaḥ: "sāvitryābhimantritam udakaṃ puṣpamiśritam" | añjalinā kṣiped iti śeṣaḥ | nārāyaṇas tv arghyadāne mantrāntaram āha |

	karābhyām añjaliṃ kṛtvā jalapūrṇaṃ samāhitaḥ |

	ud u tyam ity mantreṇa tat toyaṃ ca kṣiped bhuvi ||

tataḥ pradakṣiṇam āvṛtyodakaṃ spṛśet | tad uktaṃ vāmanapurāṇe |

	sāyaṃ mantravad ācamya prokṣya sūryasya cāñjalim (?) |

śrutir api: "yat pradakṣiṇaṃ prakramanti tena pāpmānam avadhūnvanti" iti | 

	utthāyārkaṃ pratiprāsya trikenāñjalināmbhasaḥ |

	uccitram ṛggdvayenainam upatiṣṭhed anantaram ||

	saṃdhyādvaye 'py upasthānam etad āhur manīṣiṇaḥ |

	praṇavo vyāhṛtayas tisraḥ sāvitrī ceti tu trikam ||

smṛtyantare 'pi |

	ud u tyaṃ citraṃ tac cakṣur upasthāya tribhiḥ sadā |

	saṃdhyayor ubhayoḥ sūryaṃ gāyatrījapam ācaret || iti |

eteṣāṃ gāyatrī triṣṭub uṣṇig (?) iti krameṇa chandāṃsi; praskaṇvakutsavasiṣṭhāḥ krameṇa ṛṣayaḥ; sūryo devatā; sūryopasthāne (?) viniyogaḥ | tataḥ kṛtaprāṇāyāmaḥ saṃdhyāṃ dhyātvā gāyatrījapānantaram ādityam upatiṣṭheta | tad uktaṃ kūrmapurāṇe |

	ācamya mantravan nityaṃ punar ācamya vāgyataḥ |

	saṃmārjya mantrair ātmānaṃ kuśaiḥ sodakabindubhiḥ ||

	āpohiṣṭhāvyāhṛtibhiḥ sāvitryā vāruṇaiḥ śubhaiḥ |

	oṃkāravyāhṛtiyutāṃ gāyatrīṃ vedamātaram ||

	japtvā jalāñjaliṃ dadyād bhāskaraṃ prati tanmanāḥ |

	prākkūleṣu tataḥ sthitvā darbheṣu susamāhitaḥ ||

	prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ kṛtvā dhyāyet saṃdhyām iti śrutiḥ |

	yā saṃdhyā sā jagatsūtir māyātītā hi nirmalā ||

	īśvaro kevalā śaktis tattvatrayasamudbhavā |

	dhyātvārkamaṇḍalagatāṃ sāvitrīṃ vai japed budhaḥ ||

	sahasraparamāṃ nityaṃ śatamadhyāṃ daśāvarām |

	sāvitrīṃ vai japed vidvān prāṅmukhaḥ prayataḥ sthitaḥ ||

	athopatiṣṭhed ādityam udayantaṃ samāhitaḥ |

	mantrais tu vividhaiḥ sauraiḥ ṛgyajuḥsāmasaṃbhavaiḥ ||

iti svaśākhādhītamantrābhiprāyam, "upasthānaṃ svakair mantrair ādityasya tu kārayet" iti vasiṣṭhasmaraṇāt | ato yajuḥśākhināṃ "mitrasya", "mitro janān", "prasmitra", ity tribhir upasthānam | tāsāṃ prathamā gāyatrī, uttare triṣṭubhau, viśvedevā ṛṣayaḥ, mitro devatā, sūryopasthāne viniyogaḥ | evam anyeṣām api draṣṭavyam | bodhāyanas tu japānte 'har ahar upasthānam āha: "evam eva prātaḥ prāṅmukhas tiṣṭhan maitrībhyām ahar upatiṣṭhate mitrasya carṣaṇīdhṛtaḥ, mitro janān yātayantīti dvābhyām" iti | atra purāṇam |

	ātmapādau tathā bhūmiṃ saṃdhyākāle 'bhivādayet |

	āyur vidyāṃ tathārogyaṃ prāpnoti putuṣaḥ sadā || iti |

evaṃ kurvataḥ phalam āha yamaḥ |

	saṃdhyām upāsate ye tu satataṃ saṃśitavratāḥ |

	vidhūtapāpās te yānti brahmaloke sanātanam ||

atrir api |

	yas tu saṃdhyām upāsīta śraddhayā vidhivad dvijaḥ |

	na tasya kiṃcid aprāpyaṃ triṣu lokeṣu vidyate ||

kūrmapurāṇe 'pi |

	ananyacetasaḥ śāntā brāhmaṇā vedapāragāḥ |

	upāsya vidhivat saṃdhyāṃ prāptāḥ pūrve parām gatim ||

athākaraṇe doṣo 'pi dakṣeṇa darsitaḥ |

	saṃdhyāhīno 'śucir nityam anarhaḥ sarvakarmasu |

	yad anyat kurute karma na tasya phalabhāg bhavet ||

gobilo 'pi |

	saṃdhyā yena na vijñātā saṃdhyā naiva hy upāsitā |

	jīvamāno bhavec chūdro mṛtaḥ śvā cābhijāyate ||

manur api |

	na tiṣṭhati tu yaḥ pūrvāṃ nopāste yaś ca paścimām |

	sa śūdravad bahiṣkāryaḥ sarvasmād dvijakarmaṇaḥ ||

viṣṇupurāṇe 'pi |

	upatiṣṭhanti ye saṃdhyāṃ ye na pūrvāṃ na paścimām |

	vrajanti te durātmānas tāmisraṃ narakaṃ nṛpa ||

kūrmapurāṇe 'pi |

	yo 'nyatra kurute yatraṃ dharmakārye dvijottama |

	vihāya saṃdhyāpraṇatiṃ sa yāti narakāyutam ||

viṣṇupurāṇe 'pi |

	tasmān no laṅghanaṃ kāryaṃ saṃdhyopāsanakarmaṇaḥ |

	sa hanti sūryaṃ saṃdhyāyā nopastiṃ kurute tu yaḥ || iti |

etat sarvam anārtaviṣayam | ata eva yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	anārtaś cotsṛjed yas tu sa vipraḥ śūdrasaṃmitaḥ |

	prāyaścittī bhavec caiva loke bhavati ninditaḥ ||

atrir api |

	nopatiṣṭhanti ye saṃdhyāṃ svasthāvasthās tu vai dvijāḥ |

	hiṃsanti te sadā pāpā bhagavantaṃ divākaram ||

	ye hiṃsanti dvijāḥ sūryaṃ mokṣadvāram anuttamam |

	kathaṃ mokṣasya saṃprāptir bhavet teṣāṃ dvijanmanām ||

viṣṇupurāṇe 'pi |

	sarvakālam upasthānaṃ saṃdhyayoḥ pārthiveṣyate |

	anyatra sūtakāśaucavibhramāturabhītitaḥ || iti |

vibhramo bhrāntiḥ | tadādiṣv asāmarthyena saṃdhyāyā akaraṇe 'pi doṣo nastīty arthaḥ | sūtakādau tu saty api sāmarthye na saṃdhyopāsanaṃ kāryam ity āha marīciḥ |

	sūtake karmaṇāṃ tyāgaḥ saṃdhyādīnāṃ vidhīyate | iti |

yat tu pulastyenoktam,

	saṃdhyām iṣṭiṃ caruṃ homaṃ yāvajīvaṃ samācaret |

	na tyajet sūtake vāpi tyajan gacchaty adhogatim ||

iti, tan mānasasaṃdhyābhiprāyam | yataḥ sa evāha |

	sūtake mṛtake caiva saṃdhyākarma na saṃtyajet |

	manadoccārayen mantrān prāṇāyāmam ṛte dvijaḥ || iti |

evaṃ ca yāni sūtakādau saṃdhyākarmaniṣedhaparāṇi tāni vācikamantraprayoganiṣedhaparāṇīti mantavyam | yad api paiṭhīnasinoktam: "sūtake sāvitryāñjaliṃ prakṣipya pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā sūryaṃ dhyāyan namaskuryāt" iti, tad api sakalasaṃdhyākarmopalakṣaṇārtham iti "saṃdhyām iṣṭim" ity anena samānārtham | yad vā: yad atra saṃdhyākarmaṇi śrautam añjalidānādi, tad evānuṣṭheyaṃ nānyad ity abhiprāya ity anusaṃdheyam | yad atra uktaṃ tad grāhyam | atra śātātapaḥ |

	darbhahīnā tu yā saṃdhyā yac ca dānaṃ vinodakam |

	asaṃkhyātaṃ tu yaj japyaṃ tat sarvaṃ syān nirarthakam ||

kūrmapurāṇe 'pi |

	prāṅmukaḥ sapavitaḥ san saṃdhopāsanam ācaret |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ prātaḥsaṃdhyā**

**atha prāṇāyāmamahimā **

tatra manuḥ |

	prāṇāyāmā brāhmaṇasya trayo 'pi vidhivat kṛtāḥ |

	vyāhṛtipraṇavair yuktā vijñeyaṃ paramaṃ tapaḥ ||

	dahyante dhmāyamānānāṃ dhātūnāṃ hi yathā malāḥ |

	tathendriyāṇāṃ dahyante doṣāḥ prāṇasya nigrahāt ||

	savyāhṛtipraṇavakāḥ prāṇāyāmās tu ṣoḍasa |

	api bhrūṇahanaṃ māsāt punanty ahar ahaḥ kṛtāḥ ||

yamo 'pi |

	daśapraṇavasaṃyuktaiḥ prāṇāyāmaiś caturdaśaiḥ |

	mucyate brahmahatyāyāḥ kiṃ punaḥ śeṣapātakaiḥ ||

vyāsaḥ |

	savyāhṛtiṃ sapraṇavāṃ gāyatrīṃ śirasā saha |

	ye japanti sadā teṣāṃ na bhayaṃ vidyate kvacit ||

yogayājñavalkyo 'pi |

	ya etā vyāhṛtīḥ sapta saṃsmaret prāṇasaṃyame |

	upāsitaṃ bhavet tena viśvaṃ bhuvanasaptakam ||

	sarveṣu caiva lokeṣu kāmacāraś ca jāyate ||

vyāso 'pi |

	ṣoḍaśākṣarakaṃ brahma gāyatryās tu śiraḥ smṛtam |

	sakṛd āvartayan vipraḥ saṃsārāt sa vimucyate || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ prāṇāyāmamahimā**

**atha prāṇāyāmavidhiḥ**

tatra yogayājñavalkyaḥ|

	evaṃ saṃmarjanaṃ kṛtvā bāhyaśuddhyarthakārakam |

	athābhyantarśuddhyarthaṃ prāṇāyāmaṃ samācaret ||

saṃvarto 'pi |

	prāṇāyāmais tribhiḥ pūto gāyatrīṃ tu tato japet | iti |

prāṇasya vāyor āyāmo nirodhaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥ | sa kiṃlakṣaṇa ity apekṣite manur āha |

	savyāhṛtiṃ sapraṇavāṃ gāyatrīṃ śirasā saha |

	triḥ paṭhed āyataprāṇaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥ sa ucyate || iti |

vyāhṛtayo bhūrādyāḥ sapta satyāntāḥ,

	sapta vyāhṛtayaḥ proktāḥ prāṇāyāme tu nityaśaḥ |

	bhūr bhuvaḥ svar mahar janas tapaḥ satyaṃ tathaiva ca ||

iti yogayājñavalkyasmaraṇāt | śiraś cātra "om āpo jyotiḥ" iti yājurvediko mantraḥ,

	om āpo jyotir ity eṣa mantro vai taittirīyakaḥ |

iti vyāsasmaraṇāt | "sapraṇavām" ity anena bhūrādiṣu navasv api praṇavayogam āha | tathā ca yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	bhūr bhuvaḥ svar mahar janas tapaḥ satyaṃ tathaiva ca |

	pratyoṃkārasamāyuktaṃ tathā tat savituḥ padam ||

	om āpo jyotir ity etac chiraḥ paścāt prayojayet |

	trir āvartanayogāt tu prāṇāyāmas tu śabdyate || iti |

oṃkāro 'py atra mantrādau draṣṭavyaḥ | tathā ca yamaḥ |

	oṃkārapūrvikāḥ sapta japet tu vyāhṛtīs tathā |

	śirasā saha gāyatrīṃ prāṇāyāmaḥ paraṃtapa ||

japen manaseti śeṣaḥ | tathā ca saṃvartaḥ |

	praṇavena tu saṃyuktā vyāhṛtīḥ sapta nityaśaḥ |

	sāvitrīṃ śirasā sārdhaṃ manasā triḥ paṭhed dvijaḥ || iti |

atra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	badhvāsanaṃ niyamāsūn smṛtvā cārṣādikaṃ tathā |

	saṃnimīlitadṛṅ maunī prāṇāyāmaṃ samabhyaset || iti |

āsanaṃ cātra savastikādyanyatamaṃ veditavyam | ārṣādikaṃ cātra vyāsenoktam |

	praṇavasya ṛṣir brahmā gāyatraṃ chanda eva ca |

	devo 'gniḥ sarvakarmādau viniyogaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ||

yogayājñavalkyo 'pi |

	vyāhṛtīnāṃ tu sarvāsām ārṣaṃ caiva prajāpatiḥ |

	gāyatryuṣṇiganuṣṭup ca bṛhatī paṅktir eva ca ||

	triṣṭup ca jagatī caiva chandāṃsy etāni sapta vai |

	agnir vāyus tathādityo bṛhaspaty āpa eva ca ||

	indraś ca viśvedevāś ca devatāḥ samudāhṛtāḥ |

	prāṇāyāmaprayoge ca viniyoga udāhṛtaḥ ||

	savitā devatā yasyā mukham agnis tripāc ca yā |

	viśvāmitra ṛṣiś chando yāyatrī sā viśiṣyate ||

	viniyogas tupanaye prāṇāyāme tathaiva ca |

	om āpo jyotir ity eṣa mantro yas tu prakīrtyate ||

	tasya prajāpatiś cārṣaṃ yajuśchandovivarjitam ||

	brahmā vāyuś ca sūryaś ca devatāḥ samudāhṛtāḥ|

	prāṇasyāyamane caiva viniyoga udāhṛtaḥ || iti |

brahmā tu vyāhṛtīnām ṛṣibhedam āha |

	viśvāmitro jamadagnir bharadvājo 'tha gautamaḥ |

	ṛṣir atrir vasiṣṭhaś ca kaśyapaś ca yathākramam || iti |

sa ca prāṇāyāmaḥ pūrakakumbhakarecakais trilakṣaṇo jñeyaḥ | tathā ca yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

                        pūrakaḥ kumbhako recyaḥ prāṇāyāmas trilakṣaṇaḥ |

eteṣāṃ lakṣaṇam āha sa eva |

                        nāsikākṛṣṭa ucchvāso dhmātaḥ pūraka ucyate |

                        kumbhako niścalaśvāso ricyamānas tu recakaḥ || iti |

kumbhake tu viśeṣam āha atriḥ |

                        ā keśāgrān nakhāgrāc ca nirodhaḥ śakyate budhaiḥ |

                        nirodhāj jāyate vāyur vāyor agniś ca jāyate |

                        agner āpaś ca jāyante tato 'ntaḥ śudhyate tribhiḥ || iti |

yogayājñavalkyas tu pūrakarecakayor viśeṣam āha |

                        bāhyasthitaṃ ghrāṇapuṭena vāyuṃ ākṛṣya yatnena śaniḥ samastam |

                        nāḍyaś ca sarvāḥ paripūraṇīyāḥ sa pūrako nāma mahānirodhaḥ ||

                        śanair nāsāpuṭe vāyum utsṛjen na tu vegataḥ |

                        na kampayec charīraṃ tu sa yogī paramo mataḥ || iti |

tatra vyāsaḥ |

                        nābhipadmasthitaṃ dhyāyet kaṃ raktaṃ pūraṇena tu |

                        nīlotpalābhaṃ hṛtpadme kumbhakena janārdanam ||

	lalāṭasthaṃ śivaṃ śvetaṃ recakenāpi cintayet |

	śuddhasphaṭikasaṅkāśaṃ nirmalaṃ pāpanāśanam ||

atra phalam āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	raktaṃ prajāpatiṃ dhyāyed viṣṇuṃ nīlotpalaprabham |

	śaṃkaraṃ tryambakaṃ śvetaṃ dhyāyan mucyeta bandhanāt ||

yogayājñavalkyo 'pi |

	kumbhake viṣṇusāyujyaṃ pūrake brahmaṇo 'ntikam |

	recakena tṛtīyena prāpnuyād aiśvaraṃ padam || iti |

atra brahmā |

	pādayoś ca tathā jānvor jaṅghayor jaṭhare 'pi ca |

	kaṇṭhe mukhe tathā mūrdhni krameṇa vyāhṛtīr nyaset ||

	bhūr aṅguṣṭhadvaye nyasya bhuvas tarjanikādvaye |

	jyeṣṭhāṅgulidvaye dhīmān svaḥpadaṃ viniyojayet ||

	karanyāsavidhiṃ kṛtvā aṅganyāsaṃ samārabhet |

	bhūḥpadaṃ hṛdi vinyasya bhuvaḥ śirasi vinyaset ||

	śikhāyāṃ svaḥpadaṃ nyasya kavace tat padaṃ nyaset |

	akṣṇor bhargapadaṃ nyasya digvidikṣu dhiyaḥpadam || iti |

tata om āpo jyotir iti sarvāṅganyasaḥ,

	śiras tasyās tu sarvāṅge prāṇāyāme paraṃ nyaset |

iti vyāsasmaraṇāt | evaṃ kurvataḥ phalam āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ kṛtvā sūrasyodayaṃ prati |

	nirmalāḥ svargam āyānti santaḥ sukṛtino yathā ||

saṃvarto 'pi |

	mānasaṃ vācikaṃ pāpaṃ kāyenaiva tu tat kṛtam |

	tat sarvaṃ naśyati kṣipraṃ prāṇāyāmatraye kṛte || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ prāṇāyāmavidhiḥ **

**dhyeyasvarūpam**

uktaṃ prāṇāyāmānantaram eva saṃdhyāṃ dhyāyed iti | tatra dhyeyasvarūpam āha gobilaḥ: "prātar gāyatrī ravisthitā raktavarṇā kumāryakṣamālāhastā haṃsāsanam ārūḍhā brahmadaivatyā ṛgvedam udāharantī; madhandine sāvitrī ravimadhye sthitā śvetavarṇā yauvanasthā trinetrā triśūlahastā vṛṣabhāsanam ārūḍhā rudradaivatyā yajurvedam udāharantī; sāyaṃ sarasvatī ravimadhye sthitā śyāmavarṇā vṛddhā caturbhujā cakrahastā suparṇāsanam ārūḍhā viṣṇudaivatyā sāmavedam udāharantI" | evaṃvidhā krameṇa kālatraye 'py āvāhyeti śeṣaḥ | tad uktaṃ gāyatrīnirṇaye |

	bālāṃ tv avṛddhāṃ gāyatrīṃ tryakṣarāṃ caturānanām |

	śaktāṃ raktāmbaropetām akṣasūtradharāṃ tathā ||

	kamaṇḍaludharāṃ devīṃ haṃsavāhanasaṃsthitām |

	brahmāṇīṃ brahmadaivatyāṃ brahmalokanivāsinīm ||

	āvāhayet tu mantreṇa āyāntīṃ sūryamaṇḍalāt |

	evaṃ madhyamasaṃdhyāyāṃ sāvitrīṃ yuvatīṃ tathā ||

	śuklāṅgīṃ śuklavastrāṃ ca vṛṣārūḍhāṃ trilocanām |

	triśūlaḍamarūhastāṃ rudrāṇīṃ rudradevatām ||

	kailāsanilayāṃ devīm āyāntīṃ sūryamaṇḍalāt |

	evaṃ paścimasaṃdhyāyāṃ vṛddhāvasthāṃ sarasvatīm ||

	varṇataḥ kṛṣṇavarṇāṃ ca cārurūpāṃ caturbhujām |

	śaṅkhacakragadāpadmadhāriṇīṃ viṣṇudevatām ||

	badaryāśramavāsāṃ tām āyāntīṃ sūryamaṇḍalāt || iti |

yogayājñavalkyas tu varṇaviparyāsam āha |

	śvetā bhavati gāyatrī sāvitrī śuklavarṇikā |

	kṛṣṇā sarasvatī jñeyā saṃdhyātrayam udāhṛtam || iti |

evaṃ ca ravimaṇḍalāntaḥsthāṃ brahmalokavāsinīṃ vā saṃdhyāṃ dhyāyed ity uktaṃ bhavati | uktaṃ ca yogayājñavalkyena |

	ādityamaṇḍalāntaḥsthāṃ brahmalokagatāṃ tathā |

	akṣasūtradharāṃ devīṃ padmāsanagatāṃ śubhām |

	āvāhya yajuṣānena tejo 'sīti vidhānataḥ || iti |

tejo 'sīti vājasaneyiko mantraḥ | vyāsas tu mantrāntaram āha |

	āvāhayec ca gāyatrīṃ sarvapāpapraṇāśinīm |

	āgaccha varade devi japye me saṃnidhau bhava ||

	gāyantaṃ trāyase yasmād gāyatrī tvam udāhṛtā ||

gobilo 'pi |

	āyāhi varade devi tryakṣare brahmavādini |

	gāyatrī chandasāṃ mātar brahmayone namo 'stu te ||

śaunako 'pi |

	āvāhanaṃ taittirīye uktaṃ cāpi visarjanam | iti |

tatrāvāhanmantraḥ: "āyātu varadā devī" iti | tasya gāyatrī chandaḥ; viśvedevā ṛṣayaḥ; śukro devatā; gāyatryāvāhane viniyogaḥ | evam āvāhyoktanāmādiyuktāṃ saṃdhyāśabdābhilipyām ādityākhyāṃ brahmātmikāṃ devīṃ hṛdi sāham asmīti dhyāyet | tad uktaṃ vyāsena |

	na bhinnāṃ pratipadyeta gāyatrīṃ brahmaṇā saha |

	sāham asmīty upāsīta vidhinā yena kenacit || iti |

etat sarvaṃ saṃdhyāśabdārthanirṇaye darśitam | tatas tāṃ gāyatryās turīyeṇa pādenopasthāya japet | tad api tenaivaoktam |

	turīyaṃ tu padaṃ tasyāḥ śivabrahmapade sthitam |

	upasthāya turīyeṇa japet tāṃ tu samāhitaḥ ||

turīyaṃ pādaṃ "paro rajasi. sāvad om" ity aṣṭākṣaram | tasya vimala ṛṣiḥ; turīyaṃ chandaḥ; paramātmā devatā; mokṣe viniyogaḥ | 

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ dhyeyasvarūpanirṇayaḥ**

**atha gāyatrīmahimā**

tatra yamaḥ |

	gāyatrīṃ caiva vedāṃś ca tulayāyolayat prabhuḥ |

	ekataś caturo vedān sāṅgāṃś ca sapadakramān |

	ekataś caiva gāyatrīṃ tulyarūpā tu sā smṛtā ||

manur api |

	akāraṃ cāpy ukāraṃ ca makāraṃ ca prajāpatiḥ |

	vedatrayān niraduhad bhūr bhuvaḥ svar itīti ca ||

	tribhya eva tu vedebhyaḥ pādaṃ pādam adūduhat |

	tad ity ṛco 'syāḥ sāvitryāḥ parameṣṭhī prajāpatiḥ ||

śaṅkho 'pi: "nāghamarṣaṇāt param antarjale na vyāhṛtibhyaḥ paraṃ home na sāvitryāḥ paraṃ japye" iti | brahmāpi |

	gāyatryā na paraṃ japyaṃ gayatryā na paraṃ tapaḥ |

	gāyatryā na paraṃ dhyānaṃ gāyatryā na paraṃ hutam ||

vyāso 'pi |

	daśakṛtvaḥ prajaptā sā tryahāt pāpaṃ tu yat kṛtam |

	tat pāpaṃ praṇudaty āśu nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ||

	śataṃ japtvā tu sā devī pāpaughaśamanā smṛtā |

	sahasrajaptā sā devī upapātakanāśinī ||

	lakṣajāpena ca tathā mahāpātakanāśinī |

	koṭijāpena rājendra yad icchati tad āpnuyāt ||

	yakṣavidyādharatvaṃ vā gandharvatvam athāpi vā |

	devatvam athavā rājyaṃ bhūlokaṃ hatakaṇṭakam ||

manur api |

	yo 'dhīte 'hany ahany etāṃ trīṇi varṣāṇy atandritaḥ |

	sa brahmapadam apyeti vāyubhūtaḥ svamūrtimān ||

vyāso 'pi |

	daśabhir janmajanitaṃ śatena tu purākṛtam |

	triguṇaṃ tu sahasreṇa gāyatrī hanti kilbiṣam || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ gayatrīmahimā**

**athāsyā ārṣādikam ucyate**

tatra brahmā |

	chando gāyatrī gāyatryāḥ savitā devatā smṛtā |

	śuklo varṇo mukhaṃ cāgnir viśvāmitra ṛṣis tathā ||

	trayī śiraḥ śikhā rudro viṣṇur hṛdayam eva ca |

	upāsane viniyogaḥ sāṅkhyāyanasagotratā ||

	trailokyaṃ caraṇaṃ jñeyaṃ pṛthivī kukṣir eva ca |

	evaṃdhyatvā tu gāyatrīṃ japed dvādaśalakṣaṇām || iti |

gāyatrīkalpe tu pratipādam asyā ārṣādikam uktam: "tat savituḥ ity asya gāyatrī chandaḥ; viśvāmitra ṛṣiḥ; brahmā devatā | bhargo devasya ity asya gāyatrī chandaḥ; viśvāmitra ṛṣiḥ; viṣṇur devatā | dhiyo yo naḥ ity asya gāyatrī chandaḥ; viśvāmitra ṛṣiḥ; rudro devatā | akṣarāṇāṃ tu sarveṣāṃ prajāpatiḥ ṛṣiḥ; gāyatrī chandaḥ; viniyogo 'ṅganyāse; devatās tu brahmoktā veditavyāḥ:

	āgneyaṃ prathamaṃ tasyā vāyavyaṃ tu dvitīyakam |

	tṛtīyaṃ sūryadaivatyaṃ caturthaṃ vaidyutaṃ tathā ||

	pañcamaṃ yamadaivatyaṃ vāruṇaṃ ṣaṣṭham ucyate |

	bārhaspatyaṃ saptamaṃ ca pārjanyaṃ cāṣṭamaṃ viduḥ ||

	aindraṃ tu navamaṃ proktaṃ gāndharvaṃ daśamaṃ smṛtam |

	pauṣṇam ekādaśe proktaṃ śaivaṃ dvādaśakaṃ tathā ||

	tvāṣṭraṃ trayodaśaṃ proktaṃ vāsavaṃ tu caturdaśam |

	mārutaṃ pañcadaśakaṃ saumyaṃ ṣoḍaśakaṃ smṛtam ||

	saptadaśaṃ tv āṅgirasaṃ vaiśvadevam ataḥ param |

	āśvinaṃ caikonaviṃśaṃ prājāpatyaṃ ca viṃśakam ||

	sarvadevamayaṃ proktam ekaviṃśakam akṣaram |

	raudraṃ dvāviṃśakaṃ jñeyaṃ brāhmaṃ caiva tataḥ param ||

	vaiṣṇavaṃ ca caturviṃśam etā akṣaradevatāḥ |

	japakāle tu saṃcintya tāsu sāyujyam āpnuyāt || iti |

athākṣaratatvāni |

	atah tattvāni vakṣyāmi akṣarāṇāṃ viśeṣataḥ |

	pṛthivī hy udakaṃ tejo vāyur ambaram eva ca ||

	gandho raso 'tha rūpaṃ ca sparśaḥ śabdo 'tha vāg iti |

	hastāv upasthaḥ pāyuś ca pacchrotraṃ tvak ca cakṣuṣī ||

	jihvā ghrāṇo manastattvam ahaṃkāro mahat tathā |

	guṇatrayaṃ ca sattattvaṃ kramaśas tattvanirṇayaḥ || iti |

athākṣaraśaktayo 'pi: "sahā nityā viśvahṛdayā vilāsinī prabhāvatī lolā śāntā kāntiḥ durgā sarasvatī viṣṇurūpā viśālā īśā āpyāyinī vimalā tamo'pahāriṇī hiraṇyarūpā sūkṣmā viśvayoniḥ jayāvahā padmālayā varā śobhā gadārūpā — iti śaktayaḥ" |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ ārṣādinirṇayaḥ**

**atha nyāsavidhiḥ**

tatrādāv astramantreṇa karaśuddhiḥ | tato gāyatryā vyāpakaṃ kṛtvā karanyāsapūrvakam aṅganyāsaṃ kuryāt, tasya sarvamantrasādhāraṇatvāt | tatrāṅganyāso vyāsena darśitaḥ |

	hṛdi tatsavitur nyasya nyasyet kaṇṭhe vareṇiyam |

	bhargo devasyeti khaṇḍaṃ śikhāyāṃ ca tato nyaset ||

	dhīmahīti nyased vaktre dhiyo yo naś ca netrayoḥ |

	pracodayād iti padam astrārthe viniyojayet ||

	anāmikādvaye dhīmān nyaset tatpadam agrataḥ |

	kaniṣṭhikādvaye bhargaḥ pāṇyor madhye dhiyaḥpadam ||

	oṃ bhūr vinyasya hṛdaye oṃbhuvaḥ śirasi nyaset |

	oṃ svaḥ śikhāyāṃ vinyasya gāyatryāḥ prathamaṃ padam ||

	vinyaset kavace dhīmān dvitīyaṃ netrayor nyaset |

	tṛtīyenāstravinyāsaṃ caturthaṃ sarvato nyaset ||

atra brahmā |

	tat kāraṃ vinyaset svāṅge pādāṅguṣṭhadvaye dvijaḥ |

	sakāraṃ gulphadeśe tu vikāraṃ jaṅghayor nyaset ||

	jānvos tu viddhi tuḥkāraṃ vakāraṃ corudeśataḥ |

	rekāraṃ vinyased guhye ṇikāraṃ vṛṣaṇe nyaset ||

	kaṭideśe tu yaṅkāraṃ bhakāraṃ nābhimaṇḍale |

	rgokāraṃ jaṭhare dhīmān dekāraṃ stanayor nyaset ||

	vakāraṃ hṛdi vinyasya syakāraṃ kaṇṭha eva tu |

	dhīkāram āsye vinyasya makāraṃ tālumadhyataḥ ||

	hikāraṃ nāsikāgre tu dhikāraṃ nayanadvaye |

	bhruvor madhye tu yokāraṃ lalāṭe tu dvitīyakam ||

	pūrvānane tu naḥkāraṃ prakāraṃ dakṣiṇānane |

	uttarāsye tu cokāraṃ dakāraṃ pāscimanane ||

	vinyasen mūrdhni yātkāraṃ sarvavyāpinam īśvaram || iti |

atra sarve mantrāḥ praṇavānt namo'ntāś ca | tathā ca bhṛguḥ |

	oṃkāram ādāv uccārya mantrabījam anantaram |

	nāma grāhyaṃ namo'ntaṃ tu japanyāsaḥ prakīrtitaḥ || iti |

tato varṇadhyānaṃ kuryāt | tad āha brahmā |

	kṛtvā caivedṛśaṃ nyāsam aśeṣaṃ pāpanāśanam |

	paścāt samācared dhyānaṃ varṇarūpasamanvitam || iti |

tad api tenaivoktam |

	tatkāraṃ campakāpītaṃ brahmaviṣṇuśivātmakam |

	śāntaṃ padmāsanārūḍhaṃ dhyāyet svasthānasaṃsthitam ||

	sakāraṃ cintayec chyāmam atasīpuṣpasaṃnibham |

	padmamadhyasthitaṃ saumyam upapātakanāśanam ||

	vikāraṃ piṅgalaṃ nityaṃ kamalāsanasaṃsthitam |

	dhyāyec chāntaṃ dvijaśeṣṭho mahāpātakanāśanam ||

	tuḥkāraṃ cintayet prājña indranīlasamaprabham |

	nirdahet sarvaduḥkhaṃ tu grahatārasamudbhavam ||

	vakāraṃ vahnidīptyābhaṃ cintayet tu vicakṣaṇaḥ |

	bhrūṇahatyākṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tatkṣaṇād eva naśyati ||

	rekāraṃ vimalaṃ dhyāyec chuddhasphaṭikasaṃnibham |

	pāpaṃ naśyati tat kṣipram agamyāgamanodbhavam ||

	ṇikāraṃ cintayed yogī vidyutsphuritasaprabham |

	abhakṣyabhakṣajaṃ pāpaṃ tatkṣaṇād eva naśyati ||

	yaṅkāraṃ tārakāvarṇam induśekharabhūṣaṇam |

	yogināṃ varadaṃ dhyāyed brahmahatyāvināśanam ||

	bhakāraṃ kṛṣṇavarṇaṃ tu nīlameghasamaprabham |

	dhyātvā puruṣahatyādi pāpaṃ nāśayati dvijaḥ ||

	rgokāraṃ raktavarṇaṃ tu kamalāsanasaṃsthitam |

	gohatyādikṛtaṃ pāpaṃ nāśayantaṃ vicintayet ||

	dekāraṃ marakataśyāmaṃ kamalāsanasaṃsthitam |

	cintayet satataṃ yogī strīhatyā dahyate param ||

	vakāraṃ śuklavarṇaṃ tu jātīpuṣpasamaprabham |

	guruhatyākṛtaṃ pāpaṃ dhyātvā dahati tatkṣaṇāt ||

	syakāraṃ ca tathā pītaṃ suvarṇasadṛśaprabham |

	manasā cintitaṃ pāpaṃ dhyātvā dahati mānavaḥ ||

	dhīkāraṃ cintayec chuklaṃ kundapuṣpasamaprabham |

	pitṛmātṛvadhāt pāpān mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ||

	makāraṃ padmarāgābhaṃ cintayed dīptatejasam |

	pūrvajanmārjitaṃ pāpaṃ tatkṣaṇād eva naśyati ||

	hikāraṃ śaṅkhavarṇaṃ tu pūrṇacandrasamaprabham |

	aśeṣapāpadahanaṃ dhyāyen nityaṃ vicakṣaṇaḥ ||

	dhikāraṃ pāṇḍuraṃ dhyāyet padmasyopari saṃsthitam |

	pratigrahakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ smaraṇād eva naśyati ||

	yokāraṃ raktavarṇaṃ tu indragopakasaṃnibham |

	dhyātvā prāṇivadhe pāpaṃ nirdahen munipuṅgava |

	dvitīyaś caiva yaḥ prokto yokāro rukmasaṃnibhaḥ ||

	nirdahet sarvapāpāni nānyaiḥ pāpais ca lipyate |

	naḥkāraṃ tu mukhaṃ pūrvam ādityodayasaṃnibham ||

	sakṛd dhyātvā dvijaśreṣṭhaḥ (?) sa gacched daivataṃ padam |

	nīlotpaladalaśyāmaṃ prakāraṃ dakṣiṇānanam ||

	sakṛd dhyātvā dvijaśreṣṭhaḥ sa gacched aiśvaraṃ padam |

	saumyaṃ gorocanapītaṃ cokāraṃ cottarānanam ||

	sakṛd dhyātvā dvijaśreṣṭhaḥ sa gacched vaiṣṇavaṃ padam |

	śaṅkhakundendusaṅkāśaṃ dakāraṃ paścimānanam ||

	sakṛd dhyātvā dvijaśrṣṭhaḥ sa gaccched brahmaṇaḥ padam |

	yātkāras tu śiraḥ proktaś caturvadanasaṃnibhaḥ ||

	pratyakṣaphalado brahmā viṣṇū rudra iti sthitiḥ |

	etaj jñātvā tu medhāvī japahomaṃ karoti yaḥ ||

	na bhavet sūtakaṃ tasya mṛtakaṃ ca na vidyate |

	sākṣād bhavaty asau brahmā svayaṃbhūḥ parameśvaraḥ ||

	yas tv evaṃ na vijānāti gāyatrīṃ tu yathāvidhi |

	kalpitaṃ sūtakaṃ tasya mṛtakaṃ ca mayānagha ||

	naiva dānaphalaṃ tasya naiva yajñaphalaṃ labhet |

	na ca tīrthaphalaṃ proktaṃ tasyaivaṃ sūtake sati ||

atha mudrāḥ | tā api tenaiva darśitāḥ |

	athāto darśayen mudrāṃs samukhaṃ saṃpuṭaṃ tathā |

	tato vitatavistīrṇe dvimukhatrimukhe tathā ||

	caturmukhaṃ pañcamukhaṃ ṣaṇmukhādhomukhe tathā |

	vyāpakāñjalikākhyaṃ ca śakaṭaṃ tadanantaram ||

	yamapāśaṃ ca grathitaṃ tataḥ syāt sanmukhonmukham |

	vilambo muṣṭiko mīnas tataḥ kūrmavarāhakau ||

	siṃhākrāntaṃ mahākrāntaṃ tato mudgarapallavau ||

etāsāṃ lakṣaṇam āha sa eva |

	saṃmukhaṃ saṃhatau hastau uttānau kuñcitāṅgulī |

kuñcitā vakrā aṅgulayo yayor uktalakṣaṇayor hastayos tau saṃmukhaṃ nāma mudrā,

	saṃpuṭaṃ padmakośābhau karāv anyonyasaṃhatau |

saṃhatau padmamukulābhau karau saṃpuṭaṃ nāma mudrā,

	vitataṃ saṃhatau hastāv uttānāv āyatāṅgulī |

āyātāḥ prasāritā aṅgulayo yayor uktalakṣaṇayoḥ hastayos tau vitataṃ nāma mudā,

	vistīrṇaṃ saṃhatau pāṇī mitho muktāṅgulidvayau |

muktam aṅgulidvayaṃ yābhyāṃ pāṇibhyāṃ tau mithaḥ saṃyutau vistīrṇaṃ nāma mudrā,

	saṃmukhāsaktayoḥ pāṇyoḥ kaniṣṭhādvayayogataḥ |

	śeṣāṅgulīnāṃ vairalye dvimukhatrimukhādayaḥ ||

mithaḥ saṃmukhāsaktayoḥ pāṇyoḥ kaniṣṭhādvayayogena śeṣāṅgulivairalye aṅguṣṭhadvayam ārabhyānāmikāntaṃ yāvat dvimukhatrimukhacaturmukhapañcamukhā nāma mudrā bhavanti | tatra vakāre dvimukhm, rekāre trimukham, ṇikāre caturmukham, yakāre pañcamukham |

	śeṣāṅgulīnāṃ saṃyogāt pūrvayogavināśanam |

	tiryaksaṃyujyamānāgrau saṃyuktāṅgulimaṇḍalau |

	hastau ṣaṇmukham ity uktā mudrā mudrāviśāradaiḥ ||

pūvayogaḥ kaṇiṣṭhādvayasaṃyogaḥ | tadvināśenetarāṅgulīnāṃ saṃyogāt tiryaksaṃyujyamānam agraṃ yayos tathā saṃyuktam aṅgulimaṇḍalaṃ ca yayos tau hastau ṣaṇmukhaṃ nāma mudrā,

	ākuñcitāgrau saṃyuktau nyubjau hastāv adhomukham |

īṣadvakrāgrau arvākkṛtau saṃyuktau hastau adhomukhaṃ nāma mudrā,

	uttānau tādṛśāv eva vyāpakāñjalikaṃ karau ||

tādṛśau saṃyutau uktalakṣaṇau karau vyāpakāñjalikaṃ nāma mudrā,

	adhomukhau baddhamuṣṭimuktāṅguṣṭhakau karau |

	śakaṭaṃ nāma kathitaṃ

muktāgrāṅguṣṭhau yayor uktalakṣaṇayoḥ karayos tau śakaṭaṃ nāma mudrā,

	yamapāśam ataḥ param |

	baddhamuṣṭikayoḥ pāṇyor uttānā vāmatarjanī ||

	kuñcitāgrānyayā yuktā tarjanyā nyubjavakrayā |

baddhamuṣṭikayor upary adhobhāvenāvasthitayoḥ pāṇyoḥ ya uttānā kuñcitāgrā vāmatarjanī sānyayā dakṣiṇatarjanyā nyubjavakrayā yuktā yamapāśaṃ nāma mudrā,

	uttānasaṃdhisaṃlīnabaddhāṅgulitalau karau |

	saṃmukhau ghaṭitau dīrghāv aṅguṣṭhau grathitaṃ matam ||

uttānāni saṃdhisaṃlīnāni baddhāny aṅgulitalāni yayoḥ karayos tau tathoktau | tāv anyonyam upaghāṭitau dīrghau vakrāṅguṣṭhau yayos tau grathitaṃ nama mudrā,

	saṃcitordhvāṅgulir vāmas tādṛśo dakṣiṇena tu |

	adhomukhena saṃyuktaḥ sanmukhonmukham ucyate ||

saṃcitāḥ saṃbaddhā ūrdhvāṅgulayo yasya sa tathoktaḥ | tādṛśo dakṣiṇenādhomukhena kareṇa saṃyuktaḥ sanmukhonmukhaṃ nāma mudrā,

	uttāne hy unnate koṭī vilambaḥ kathitaḥ karau |

uttāne unnate koṭī yayos tau vilambo nāma mudrā,

	muṣṭī cānyonyasaṃyukāv uttānau muṣṭiko bhavet |

anyonyasaṃyuktāv uttānau muṣṭiko nāma mudrā,

	mīnas tu saṃmukhībhūtau yuktānām aniṣṭhikau |

	ūrdhvasaṃyuktavakrāgrau śeṣāṅgulitalau karau ||

yukte saṃbaddhe anāmikākaniṣṭhike yayos tau yathoktau tathoktau tāv anyonyasaṃmukhībhūtau tathā ūrdhvaṃ saṃyuktāni vakrāṇi śeṣāṅgulitalāni yayoḥ karayos tau mīno nāma mudrā,

	adhomukhaḥ karo vāmas tādṛśo dakṣiṇena tu |

	pṛṣṭhadeśe samākrāntaḥ kūrmo nāmābhidhīyate ||

adhomukho nyubjo vāmas tādṛśena dakṣiṇena (?) pṛṣṭhadeśe yuktaḥ nāma mudrā,

	ūrdhvamdhyo vāmabhujaḥ kakṣābhyāśāśraye kare |

	varāhaḥ kathyate

kakṣasamīpāśraye kare sati uktalakṣaṇo vāmabhujo vārāho mudrā,

	siṃhākrāntaṃ karṇāśritau karau ||

karṇadvayāśritāv āyatāṅgulikau karau siṃhākrāntaṃ nāma mudrā,

	kiṃcidākuñcitāgrau cen mahākrāntaṃ tataḥ param |

tāv eva kuñcitāgrau mahākrāntaṃ nāma mudrā,

	ūrdhvaṃ kiṃcidgatau pāṇī mudgaro nāma tarjanī |

	grastā dakṣiṇahastena

kiṃcidūrdhvaṃ gatayoḥ pāṇyor yā vāmatarjanī dakṣiṇahastena gṛhītā sā mudgato nāma mudrā,

	pallavo dakṣiṇaḥ karaḥ |

	adhomukhastho mūrdhni mudrāṇām iti lakṣaṇam ||

ity uktalakṣaṇo mūrdhni nihitaḥ karaḥ pallavo nāma mudrā | atra mahāsaṃhitokto viśeṣaḥ |

	na jātu darśayen mudrā mahājanasamāgame |

	kṣubhyanti devās tasya viphalaṃ ca kṛtaṃ bhavet || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ nyāsavidhiḥ**

**atha gāyatrīkavacam**


        om iti hṛdaye bhūr iti mukhe bhuva iti śirasi suvar iti sarvāṅge; tato yathāvidhi gāyatrīm abhyaset

evaṃ kurvataḥ phalam āha vyāsaḥ |

	vinyasyaiva japed yas tu gāyatrīṃ vedamātaram |

	brahmalokam avāpnoti vyasasya vacanaṃ yathā ||

	svarūpaṃ yaḥ punas tasyā jñātvopāste yathāvidhi |

	gṛhṇan doṣair na lipyeta ratnapūrṇāṃ vasundharām ||

	yathākathaṃcij japtā sā devī paramapāvanī |

	sarvakāmapradā proktā kiṃ punar vidhinā nṛpa || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ gāyatrīkavacam**

**atha gayatrījapavidhiḥ**

tatra manuḥ |

	ācamya prayato nityam ubhe saṃdhyā samāhitaḥ |

	śucau deśe japañ japyam upāsīta yathāvidhi ||

yathāśāstram ity arthaḥ | tat katham ity apekṣite śaṅkha āha: "kuśabrusyāṃ samāsīnaḥ kuśottarāyāṃ vā kuśapavitrapāṇir udaṅmukhaḥ sūryābhimukho vākṣamālām ādāya devatāṃ dhyāyan japaṃ kuryāt" iti | brusī āsanam | kuśottarā kusacchadā | devatā cātra gāyatrīpratipādyā, "maunaṃ mantrārthacintanam" iti bṛhaspatismaraṇāt | tasyāś cāyam arthaḥ | devasya dyotamānasya savitur ādityasya saṃbandhibhūtaṃ tat brahma bhargas tejorūpaṃ vareṇyaṃ dhīmahi dhyāyemahīti saṃbandhaḥ, tacchabdasya brahmavācakatvāt | tad uktaṃ bhagavadgītāu |

	oṃ tat sad iti nirdeśo brahmaṇas trividhaḥ smṛtaḥ | iti |

ya evaṃvidhaḥ paramātmā sa no 'smākaṃ dhiyo buddhiḥ dṛṣṭādṛṣṭārthaphaleṣu karmasu pracodayāt prerayet iti | evaṃ ca savitṛmaṇḍalāntaḥsthaṃ hiraṇmayaṃ puruṣaṃ dhyāyan japed ity uktaṃ bhavati | uktaṃ ca gāyatrījapadhikāre tu markaṇḍeyena |

	kuśabrusyāṃ niviṣṭas tu kuśapāṇir jitendriyaḥ |

	arkamadhyagataṃ dhyāyet puruṣaṃ tu mahādyutim || iti |

atra śaṅkhaḥ |

	svaravarṇapadair vākyaṃ suddham āvartayej japan |

	na kampayec chirogrīvaṃ dantān naiva pradarśayet || iti |

tac ca vākyaṃ manunoktam |

	etad akṣaram etāṃ ca japan vyāhṛtipūrvikām |

	saṃdhyayor vedavid vipro vedapuṇyena yujyate || iti |

etad akṣaraṃ praṇavaḥ | etāṃ gāyatrīm | ata eva vyāsaḥ |

	praṇavavyāhṛtiyutāṃ gāyatrīṃ tu japet tataḥ |

praṇavo 'py atra mantrādau draṣṭavyaḥ | tathā ca saṃvartaḥ |

	praṇavādyāṃ tu saṃdhyāyāṃ japed vyāhṛtibhiḥ saha | iti |

vyāhṛtayo 'py atra bhūrādyās tisra eva | yogayājñavalkyas tv anye 'pi praṇavayogam āha |

	oṃkāraṃ pūrvam ucchārya bhūr bhuvaḥ svas tathaiva ca |

	gāyatrīṃ praṇavaṃ cānte japa evam udāhṛtaḥ || iti |

eṣā saṃpuṭagāyatrī | atra viśeṣam āha bodhāyanaḥ: "ubhayataḥ praṇavām savyāhṛtikām" iti | gāyatrīm āvartayed ity anuvartate | vṛddhamanur api |

	ṣaḍoṃkārāṃ japan vipro gāyatrīṃ manasā śuciḥ |

	anekajanmajaiḥ pāpair mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ || iti |

sā ca kiṃlakṣaṇety apekṣite sa evāha |

	tisro vyāhṛtayaḥ pūrvaṃ ṣaḍoṃkarasamanvitāḥ |

	punaḥ saṃhṛtya coṃkāraṃ mantrasyādyantayos tathā ||

	soṃkārā caturāvṛttyā vijñeyā sā śatākṣarā |

	śatākṣarāṃ samāvartya sarvavedaphalaṃ labhet |

	etayā jñātaya nityaṃ vāṅmayaṃ viditaṃ bhavet ||

	upāsitaṃ bhavet tena viśvaṃ bhuvanasaptakam | iti |

asyārthaḥ: soṃkārety anena vyāhṛtīnāṃ saṅkhyānanupraveśam āha | evaṃ coṃkāreṇa saha pañcaviṃśatyakṣarā caturāvṛttyā śatākṣarā saṃpadyata iti | atra japayajñaṃ prakṛtya nṛsiṃhapurāṇam |

	trividho japayajñaḥ syāt tasya bhedaṃ nibodhata |

	vācikākhya upāṃśuś ca mānasas trividhaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

	trayāṇāṃ japayajñānāṃ śreyān syād uttatottaraḥ || iti |

atra hārītaḥ |

	uccais tv ekaguṇah prokto dyāno (?) daśaguṇaḥ smṛtaḥ |

	upāṃśuḥ syāc chataguṇaḥ sāhasro mānasaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

uccopāṃśutvayor lakṣaṇaṃ purāṇe darśitam |

	yad uccanīcasvaritaiḥ spaṣṭaiḥ spaṣṭapadākṣaraiḥ |

	mantram uccārayed vācā japayajñaḥ sa vācikaḥ ||

	śanair udīrayen mantram īṣad oṣṭhau pracālayet |

	kiṃcic chabdaṃ svayaṃ vidyād upāṃśuḥ sa japaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

mānasasya tu lakṣaṇaṃ vaiyāghrapādenoktam |

	yo bhaved acalacjihvād aśanāvaraṇo japaḥ |

	sa mānasaḥ samākhyāto japaḥ śrutiparāyaṇaiḥ || iti |

varṇānupalabdhyā svaramātropalabdher dhvānaḥ (?) | yat punar vyāsenoktam,

	noccair japyaṃ budhaḥ kuryāt savitryās tu viśeṣataḥ |

iti, tan mānasādijapaprasaṃsābhiprāyam, na punar uccais tv apratiṣedhārtham | tathātve,

	upāṃśujapayuktasya saṃsyāc chataguṇaṃ bhavet |

iti vacanavirodhaḥ syāt | śaṃsya uccair japaḥ | atra japaniyamaprakāram āha śaunakaḥ |

	kṛtvottānau karau prātaḥ sāyaṃ cādhomukhau tataḥ |

	madhye stabdhakarābhyāṃ tu japa evam udāhṛtaḥ ||

bṛhaspatir api |

	manaḥsaṃharaṇaṃ śaucaṃ maunaṃ mantrārthacintanam |

	avyagratvam anirvedo japasaṃpattihetavaḥ ||

vyāso 'pi |

	na caṅkraman na ca hasan na pārśvān avalokayan |

	nāpāśrito na jalpaṃś ca na prāvṛtaśirās tathā ||

	na padā padam ākramya na caiva hi tathā karau |

	na cāsamāhitamanā na ca saṃśrāvayañ japet ||

	homā praigraho dānaṃ bhojanācamane japaḥ |

	na bahirjānu kāryāṇi sāṅguṣṭhāni sadācaret ||

sumantur api |

	nādhoratnir nānyamanā na ca vyatyastapatkaraḥ |

	apavitrakaro nagnaḥ śirasi prāvṛto 'pi vā ||

	pralapan vā japed yāvat tāvan niṣphalam ucyate |

śātātapo 'pi |

	darbhahīnā ca yā saṃdhyā yac ca dānaṃ vinodakam |

	asaṅkhyātaṃ ca yaj japyaṃ tat sarvaṃ syān nirarthakam ||

bodhāyano 'pi: "nābher adhaḥ sparsanaṃ karmasaṃyukto varjayet" iti | yamo 'pi |

	nābher adhastyakāyaṃ tu spṛṣṭvā prakṣālayet karau |

	dakṣiṇaṃ vā spṛśet karṇaṃ smared vā viṣṇum avyayam ||

śaunako 'pi |

	pūrvāṃ saṃdhyāṃ japan tiṣṭhed upāsīnas tu paścimām |

	na cāntarā vyāharet tu viramed vā kathaṃcana || iti |

atra kvacid apavādam āha sa eva |

	viramed brāhmaṇe prāpte kāmaṃ tena ca saṃvadet |

	śūdraṃ dṛṣṭvā tu saṃprāptaṃ nadhīyīta kathaṃcana ||

śūdraṃ dṛṣṭvā viramed eva na saṃvaded ity arthaḥ | vyāso 'pi |

	japakāle na bhāṣeta vratahomādikeṣu ca |

	eteṣv evāvasaktaṃ tu yady āgacched dvijottamaḥ ||

	abhivādya tato vipraṃ yogakṣemaṃ ca kīrtayet | iti |

avasakto 'vahitaḥ | pramādakṛte tu vāgyamalope yogayājñavalkyoktaṃ draṣṭavyam |

	yadi vāgyamalopaḥ syāj japādiṣu kathaṃcana |

	vyāhared vaiṣṇavaṃ mantraṃ smared vā viṣṇum avyayam || iti |

tathā deśaniyamo 'pi tenaiva darśitaḥ |

	agnyagāre jalānte vā japed devālaye 'pi vā |

	puṇyatīrthe gavāṃ goṣṭhe dvijakṣetre 'tha vā gṛhe ||

atra śaṅkhaḥ |

	gṛhe tv ekaguṇaṃ japyaṃ nadyadau dviguṇaṃ smṛtam |

	gavāṃ goṣṭhe daśaguṇam agnyagāre  śatādhikam ||

	siddhakṣetreṣu tīrtheṣu devatānāṃ ca saṃnidhau |

	sahasraśatakoṭiḥ syād anantaṃ viṣṇusaṃnidhau ||

atrāpi viśeṣaḥ kūrmapurāṇe darsitaḥ |

	guhyakā rākṣasāḥ siddhā haranti prasabhaṃ yataḥ |

	ekānte śudddhadeśe ca tasmāj japyaṃ samācaret ||

aṅgirā api |

	prachannāni ca dānāni jñānaṃ ca nirahaṃkṛtam |

	japyāni ca suguptāni teṣāṃ phalam anantakam || iti |

atra japasaṃkhyām āha yamaḥ |

	sahasraparamāṃ devīṃ śatamadhyāṃ daśāvarām |

	gāyatrīṃ tu japen nityaṃ sarvapāpapraṇāśinīm || iti |

daśāvarām ity āpadviṣayam | bodhāyano 'pi: "darbheṣv āsīno darbhān dhārayamāṇaḥ sodakena pāṇinā prāṅmukhaḥ sāvitrīṃ sahasrakṛtva āvartayec chatakṛtvo 'parimitakṛtvo vā" iti | sahasrakṛtva iti vānaprasthādiviṣayam | tathā ca yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	brahmacāry āhitāgniś ca śatam aṣṭottaraṃ japet |

	vānaprastho yatis caiva sahasrād adhikaṃ japet || iti |

tayor anagnikatvena homakālānatipatter iti bhāvaḥ | śatam aṣṭottaram ity anuditahomaviṣayam | brahmacāriṇo 'pi "saṃdhyayor agnikarma ca" iti prāg udayād agnikāryasmaraṇād avirodhaḥ | uditahominas tu manūktaṃ draṣṭavyam |

	pūrvāṃ saṃdhyāṃ japet tiṣṭhan sāvitrīm ārkadarsanāt |

	paścimāṃ tu samāsīnaḥ samyag ārkṣavibhāvanāt || iti |

ṛkṣaṃ nakṣatram | atra tiṣṭhan japed iti vyatyayenānvayaḥ, japasyaiva pradhānatvāt | ata eva śaṅkhaḥ |

	pūrvāṃ saṃdhyāṃ japet tiṣṭhann āsīnaḥ paścimāṃ tathā | iti |

nanu ca "nāntarā viramet" iti japamadhye viramaṇaniṣedhād anuitahomina āhitāgner  viramaṇāsaṃbhava eva | maivam, tasya śrutilakṣaṇatvena madhye 'pi viramaṇe 'virodhāt | ata eva āpastambaḥ: "vipratiṣedhe śrutilakṣaṇam balīyaḥ" iti | atra japāntaraṃ gobilaḥ |

	maheśvaramukhotpannā viṣṇor hṛdayasaṃbhavā |

	brahmaṇā samanujñātā gaccha devi yathecchayā ||

iti gāyatrīvisarjanamantraḥ | śaunako 'pi |

	āvāhanaṃ taittirīya uktaṃ cāpi visarjanam | iti |

atra, "uttame śikhare devi" iti visarjanamantraḥ | atra gobilaḥ |

	na kadācid api prājño gāyatrīm udake japet |

	gāyatry agnimukhā proktā tasmād utthāya tāṃ japet || iti |

śrutir api: "agnimukhā gāyatrī, tasmān nāpsu japet" iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ gāyatrījapīvidhiḥ (?)**

**gāyatrījapaviṣayāḥ**

athānyāny api gāyatrījapaviṣayāṇy eva kānicid vacanāni likhyante | tatra manuḥ |

	sahasrakṛtvas tv abhyasya bahir etat trikaṃ dvijaḥ |

	mahato 'py enaso māsāt tvacevāhir vimucyate ||

praṇavo vyāhṛtayaḥ sāvitrī ceti trikam | saṃvarto 'pi |

	brahmacārī mitāhāraḥ sarvabhūtānukampanaḥ |

	gāyatrīlakṣajāpena sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ||

	ayājyayājanaṃ kṛtvā bhuktvā cānnaṃ vigarhitam |

	gāyatry aṣṭasahasraṃ tu japaṃ kṛtvā viśuddhyati ||

	aihitāmuṣmikaṃ pāpaṃ sarvaṃ niravaśeṣataḥ |

	pañcarātreṇa gāyatrīṃ japamāno vyapohati ||

caturviṃśatimate 'pi |

	gāyatryās tu japet koṭiṃ brahmahatyāṃ vyapohati |

vasiṣṭho 'pi |

	gāyatryaṣṭasahasraṃ tu japaṃ kṛtvotthite ravau |

	mucyate pātakaiḥ sarvair yadi na bhrūṇahā bhavet ||

	lakṣāśītiṃ japed yas tu surāpānād vimucyate |

	punāti hemahartāraṃ gāyatrīlakṣasaptatiḥ ||

	gāyatryāḥ ṣaṣṭibhir lakṣair mucyate gurutalpagaḥ ||

yogayājñavalkyo 'pi |

	yatra yatra ca saṃkīrṇam ātmānaṃ manyate dvijaḥ |

	tatra tatra tilair homo gāyatryā japa eva vā ||

yamo 'pi |

	ghṛtayuktais tilair vahniṃ hutvā tu susamāhitaḥ |

	gāyatryāḥ prayataḥ śuddhaḥ sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ||

	snāyāc chatena gāyatryāḥ śatam antarjale japet |

	apaḥ śatena pītvā tu sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ||

vyāso 'pi |

	saṃvatsaraṃ vā ṣaṇmāsān yo japed vidhivad dvijaḥ |

	so 'cirāt sarvakāmāṃs tu prāpnuyān nātra saṃśayaḥ ||

mārkaṇḍeyo 'pi |

	sarveṣām eva pāpānāṃ saṃkare samupasthite |

	daśasāhasram abhyastā gāyatrī śodhanaṃ param || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ gāyatrīviṣayāḥ**

**atha japamālā **

tatra yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	sphoṭikendrākṣarudrākṣaiḥ putrajīvasamudbhavaiḥ |

	akṣamālā tu kartavyā uttamā hy uttarottarā ||

purāṇe 'pi |

	akṣasūtraṃ tu kartavyaṃ muktāmaṇimayaṃ śubham |

	sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ tāmraṃ sphoṭikaṃ vātha kārayet ||

hārīto 'pi |

	śaṅkharūpyamayī mālā kāñcanī nimbajaiḥ phalaiḥ |

	padmākṣakais ca rudrākṣair virdrumair (?) maṇimauktikaiḥ ||

	rajatendrākṣakair mālā tathaivāṅguliparvabhiḥ |

	putrajīvimayī mālā śastā vai japakarmaṇi ||

atra vyāsaḥ |

	hiraṇyaratnamaṇibhir japyaṃ śataguṇaṃ bhavet |

	sahasraguṇam indrākṣai rudrākṣair ayutaṃ bhavet ||

	niyataṃ prayutaṃ vā syāt padmākṣais tu na saṃśayaḥ |

	putrajīvikajapyasya parisaṃkhyā na vidyate ||

smṛtyantare 'pi |

	hastasaṃkhyākṛtāj japyād ariṣṭair aṣṭadhā phalam |

	putrajīvena daśadhā phalaṃ syān mantrajāpinām ||

	śatadhā śaṅkhapadmābhyāṃ maṇibhis tu sahasradhā |

	kuśagranthyā ca rudrākṣaiḥ phalaṃ lakṣaguṇaṃ bhavet ||

hārīto 'pi |

	japyaṃ śataguṇaṃ proktaṃ nimbāriṣṭakamālayā |

	rudrākṣair lakṣaguṇitaṃ vidrumair daśalakṣakam ||

	mauktikaiḥ sphoṭikaiś caiva koṭikoṭiguṇottaram |

	parisaṃkhyā na vijñeyā rudrākṣāṅguliparvabhiḥ ||

	padmākṣaiḥ putrajīvaiś ca parisaṃkhyā na vidyate |

brahmāpi |

	rudrākṣair dviguṇaṃ hemnaḥ padmabījais tathārbudam |

	kuśagranthyā dvijaśreṣṭha koṭikoṭir viśiṣyate ||

rudrākṣaṃ prakṛtya skandapurāṇe |

	lakṣakoṭisahasrasya lakṣakoṭiśatasya ca |

	jape ca labhate puṇyaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ||

	ucchiṣṭo vā vikarmasthaḥ saṃliptaḥ sarvapātakaiḥ |

	mucyate sarvapāpena rudrakṣasya tu dhāraṇāt ||

	rudrākṣaṃ kaṇṭha ādhāya śvāpīha mriyate yadi |

	so 'pi rudrapadaṃ yāti kiṃ punar mānuṣādayaḥ || iti |

atra purāṇam |

	sphāṭikaṃ tv akṣasūtraṃ tu śāntipuṣṭikaraṃ hi tat |

	sarvasiddhikaraṃ svarṇaṃ mauktaṃ rājatam eva ca ||

	bhuktimuktipradaṃ śaṅkhaṃ padmendrākṣau ca darbhajam |

	sarvakāmapradaṃ dhanyam āyuṣyaṃ sarvasiddhidam |

	putrajīvākṣasūtraṃ tu śāntipuṣṭipradāyakam ||

hārīto 'pi |

	śaṅkhahemamayī raupyā mālā vai śāntikarmaṇi |

	padmākṣair indrarudrākṣair mṛnmayaiḥ puṣṭikarmaṇi ||

	putrajīvāṅgulīparvamālā syān muktisiddhidā |

	sphaṭikai racitā mālā muktidā vittadā tathā || iti |

atra saṃkhyāniyamam āha brahmā |

	aṣṭottaraśatāṃ kuryāc catuḥpañcāśikāṃ tathā |

	saptaviṃśatikā kāryā tato naivādhikā matā ||

	aṣṭottaraśatā mālā uttamā sā prakīrtitā |

	catuḥpañcāśikā yā tu madhyamā sā prakīrtitā ||

	adhamāpy ucyate nityaṃ mālā dvātriṃśasaṃbhavā |

	uttameṣu ca sādhyeṣu bhogamokṣapradeṣu ca ||

	aṣṭottaraśatāyāṃ tu mālāyāṃ japam ācaret |

	catuḥpañcāśikāyāṃ vā nādhamāyāṃ kadācana ||

	vaśyādikṣudrakarmāṇi māranoccāṭanāni ca |

	vidveṣonmādamohāni japed dvātriṃśakair dvijaḥ ||

	adhamenādhamāny eva hy akṣasūtreṇa yojayet |

	adhame cādhamāṃ mālām uttamāṃ tu visarjayet || iti |

atra skandapurāṇam |

	tarjanyā na spṛśet sūtraṃ kampayen na ca dhūnayet |

	aṅguṣṭhasya tu madhyasthe parivartaṃ samācaret ||

	ullaṅghite tathā merau patite cākṣasūtrake |

	prāṇāyāmaśataṃ kṛtvā ghṛtaprāśanam ācaret ||

aṅguṣṭhākarṣaṇam |

	madhyamākarṣaṇaṃ tasya sarvasiddhipradāyakam |

	nānyāṅgulibhir ākarṣen na nakhaiś ca tathā spṛśet || iti 

**iti śrīsakalavidyāviśāradaśrīkeśavādityabhaṭṭopādhyāyasūnunā **

**yājñikadevaṇabhaṭṭopādhyāyena viracitāyāṃ smṛticandrikāyāṃ**

**prātaḥsaṃdhyākāṇḍaṃ saṃpūrṇam**

**athābhyukṣaṇāharaṇam**

tatra śāṭyāyaniḥ |

	tataḥ sūryam upasthāya samyag ācamya ca svayam |

	abhyukṣaṇaṃ samādāya saṃyatātmā gṛhaṃ vrajet || iti |

ācamya dvir iti śeṣaḥ | tayā ca vṛddhaśātātapaḥ |

	tataḥ samyag dvir ācamya abhyukṣaṇam athāharet |

	na vinābhyukṣaṇaṃ jātu vidhijñaḥ kiṃcid ācaret ||

āharaṇe viśeṣam āha śāṭyāyaniḥ |

	sopānatkaḥ sadarbhaś ca pātrasthaṃ sadaśottaraḥ || iti |

abhyukṣaṇm āhared iti śeṣaḥ | sadaśm uttarīyaṃ yasyāsau sadaśottaraḥ | pracetā api |

	anuguptā apo gṛhya pracārārthaṃ gṛhaṃ vrajet |

	savane prokṣaṇaṃ kuryād gṛhī tena sadā śuciḥ || iti |

anuguptāḥ kenāpy adṛṣṭāḥ | savane prātarādau | ata eva gargaḥ |

	trisaṃdhyaṃ vāgyato vāri guptam āhṛtya śodhayet |

śodhayet samyak parīkṣet | atra kālaniyamam āha gobilaḥ: "purā prāduṣkaraṇavelāyāḥ sāyaṃ prātar anuguptā apa āharet paricaraṇīyāḥ" iti | prāduṣkaraṇaṃ viharaṇam | atra pātraniyamam āha yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ tāmraṃ mukhyaṃ pātraṃ prakīrtitam |

	tadalābhe tu mṛtpātraṃ sravate yan na dhāritam ||

śāṭhyāyanir api |

	āśmaṃ hiraṇmayaṃ raupyaṃ dāravaṃ mṛnmayaṃ dṛḍham |

	tāmram patrapuṭaṃ puṇyaṃ pātram abhyukṣaṇāya vai ||

patrapuṭaṃ pātrāntarālābhaviṣayam | yad āha āpastambaḥ |

	sarvālābhe tu pātrāṇāṃ parṇapātraṃ vidhīyate |

	pātraṃ tad api vijñeyaṃ sravate yan na dhāritam ||

tathā varjyāny api sa evāha |

	śailālavālukādūrvātṛṇaparṇāyasair api |

	abhyukṣaṇaṃ na gṛhṇīyād āpastambo 'bravīn muniḥ || iti |

	nālikābhinnapātreṇa kāṃsyapātreṇa caiva hi |

	prāṇyaṅgaphalajenāpi kuryān nābhyukṣaṇaṃ dvijaḥ || iti |

nālikā veṇumayī | prāṇyaṅgaṃ śaṅkhaśuktyādi | phalajaṃ nārikelabilvādimayam | vṛddhaśātātapo 'pi |

	śaivālatṛṇaparṇādyair asaṃskārāmbubhājanaiḥ |
