	sikatāvastralepaiś ca na kuryāt prokṣaṇaṃ budhaḥ ||

asaṃskārāmbubhājanaiḥ uktasaṃmārjanādisaṃskārarahitair iti yāvat | yamo 'pi |

	pātrād virahitaṃ toyam uddhṛtaṃ savyapāṇinā |

	na tena prokṣaṇaṃ kuryād vastraniṣpīḍanena ca || iti |

pātrād virahitaṃ pāṇyādināhṛtam | ata eva śāṭhyāyaniḥ |

	nāhared ekapātras tu nāvrato na ca kanyakā |

	na pāṇinā na vastreṇa toyam abhyukṣaṇāya vai ||

ekapātraḥ pidhānarahitaḥ | avrato 'nupanītaḥ | ata eva pracetāḥ |

	nāhared ekajātis tu na baṭur na ca kanyakā |

	nānupeto naikavastras toyam abhyukṣaṇāya vai ||

ekajātiḥ śūdraḥ | tathā ca manuḥ |

	brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo vaiśyas trayo varṇā dvijātayaḥ |

	caturtha ekajātis tu śūdro nāsti tu pañcamaḥ || iti |

abhyukṣaṇānantaraṃ pracetāḥ |

	abhyukṣaṇodapātraṃ tu na tāvat sthāpyate kvacit |

	yāvan nācamanaṃ dattaṃ prokṣitā na galanti yāḥ ||

anenāhṛtābhyukṣaṇam anidhāyaivācamya prokṣya nidadhyād ity uktaṃ bhavati | śāṭhyāyanir api |

	prokṣaṇagrahaṇaṃ pātraṃ nidadhad gṛham āgataḥ |

	akṛtvācamanaṃ bhūmāv ācāntaḥ prayato bhavet || iti |

ācamanam akṛtvā prokṣaṇapātraṃ bhūmāv anidadhad ācāntaḥ prayato bhaved ity arthaḥ | ācamanānantaraṃ pulastyaḥ |

	tena dravyāṇy aśeṣāṇi prokṣyācamya punar gṛhe |

	tataḥ karmāṇi kurvīta satkriyāś ca dvijottamaḥ || iti |

atra gṛhe punar ācamya tena dravyāṇi prokṣayed ity anvayaḥ | dravyāṇy api gargeṇa darśitāni |

	trisaṃdhyaṃ vāgyato vāri guptam āhṛtya śodhayet |

	homopahārabhūgehadravyātmaparicārakān ||

yamo 'pi |

	abhyukṣet tu prayatnena prātaḥ paryuṣitaṃ gṛham |

	madhyāhne caiva saṃdhyāyāṃ na cānabhyukṣite yajet ||

atra gargaḥ |

	gocarmamātram abbindur gāṃ śodhayati pātitaḥ |

	samūḍhām asamūḍhāṃ vā yatra lepo na vidyate ||

uktābhyukṣaṇāsamarthaṃ prakṛtya śāṭhyāyaniḥ |

	nadyādau samyag ācāntaḥ saṃyato gṛham āgataḥ |

	uddhṛtya maṇikāt toyam athābhyukṣaṇam ācaret ||

	gṛhe vā samupaspṛśya kṛtvā svarṇakuśodakam |

	kṛtvācamanam ācāntaḥ punaḥ prokṣaṇam ācaret ||

maṇikam udapātram | pracetā api |

	vaiśvānareṇa yat kiṃcit kurute prokṣaṇaṃ dvijaḥ |

	gaṅgātoyasamaṃ sarvaṃ vadanti brahmavādinaḥ || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyām abhyukṣaṇāharaṇam**

**athāgnihotramahimā**

tatra prajāpatiḥ |

	agnihotraphalā vedāḥ saṣaḍaṅgapadakramāḥ |

	agnihotrasamo dharmo na bhūto na bhaviṣyati ||

hārīto 'pi |

	nāgnihotrāt paro dharmo nāgnihotrāt paraṃ tapaḥ |

	nāgnihotrāt paraṃ śreyo nāgnihotrāt paraṃ yasaḥ ||

	nāgnihotrāt parā siddhir nāgnihotrāt parā gatiḥ |

	nāgnihotrāt paraṃ snānaṃ nāgnihotrāt paraṃ vratam ||

	nirdvandvā nirmanaskā vā yam upāyan manīṣiṇaḥ |

	so 'yaṃ sūkṣmo 'gnohotreṣu gūḍho 'gnir iva dāruṣu ||

	śukriyeṣu rahasyeṣu niṣatsūpaniṣatsu ca |

	yaṃ paṭhanti mahātmānaḥ so 'gnihotre prakāśate ||

	suhutāny agnihotrāṇi nayanti paramāṃ gatim |

	atra svargaś ca mokṣaś ca yo yathā gantum icchati ||

	ādyā vyāhṛtayas tisraḥ svadhā svāhā namo vaṣaṭ |

	yasyaite veśmani sadā brahmalokasya eva saḥ ||

aṅgirā api |

	yo dadyāt kāñcanaṃ meruṃ pṛthivīṃ ca sasāgarām |

	tat sāyaṃprātar homasya tulyaṃ bhavati vā na vā ||

satyavrato 'pi |

	śiloñchināṃ tu yad dharmyam ahany ahani yat phalam |

	tad darsapūrṇamāsābhyāṃ samyag āpnoti vai dvijaḥ ||

vāyupurāṇe |

	darśaṃ ca pūrṇamāsaṃ ca ye yajanti dvijātayaḥ |

	na teṣāṃ punarāvṛttir brahmalokāt kadācana ||

paiṭhīnasir api |

	hutāgnihotrasya kṛtāgnikriyasya samāptajapyasya pathi sthitasya |

	yad brāhmaṇasyātmani brahmavīryaṃ tat kāṅkṣante ṛṣayo vai samastāḥ ||

hārīto 'pi |

	nāsty ajajñasya loko vai nāyajño vindate śubham |

	aniṣṭayajño 'pūtātmā bhraśyati chinnaparṇavat ||

	yajñena lokā vimalā vibhānti yajñena devā amṛtatvam āpuḥ |

	yajñena pāpair bahubhir vimuktaḥ prāpnoti lokān paramasya viṣṇoḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyām agnihotramahimā**

**atha karmāṇi**

tatra manuḥ |

	vedoditaṃ svakaṃ karma nityaṃ kuryād atandritaḥ |

	tad dhi kurvan yathāśakti prāpnoti paramāṃ gatim ||

etat smārtasyāpi pradarśanārtham | ata eva viṣṇuḥ |

	śrautaṃ smārtaṃ ca yat kiṃcid vidhānaṃ sarvam ādarāt |

	gṛhe nivasatā kāryam anyathā doṣam ṛcchati ||

smārtaṃ gṛhyoktam aupāsanādi | tad vaivāhikāgnau kāryam | tathā ca yājñavalkyaḥ |

	karma smārtaṃ vivahāgnau kurvīta pratyahaṃ gṛhī |

	dāyakālāhṛte vāpi śrautaṃ vaitānikāgniṣu ||

śrautam agnihotrādi | vaitānikā gārhapatyādayaḥ | gautamo 'pi: "bhāryādir agnir dāyādir vā tasmin gṛhyāṇi" iti | dāyaṃ pitṛdhanam | atra bhāryāditve dāyāditve ca yathā svagṛhyaṃ vyavasthā | evaṃ ca yad uktaṃ gārgyeṇa,

	kṛtvā dārān na vai tiṣṭhet kṣaṇam apy agninā vinā |

	tiṣṭheta ced dvijo vrātyas tathā ca patito bhavet ||

	yathā snānaṃ yathā bhāryā vedasvādhyayanaṃ yathā |

	tathaivopāsanaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ na sthitis tadviyogataḥ ||

iti, yad ap vasiṣṭhena "aśrotriyā ananuvākyā anagnayaḥ śūdradharmāṇo bhavanti" iti, yad api vyāsena,

	yo 'gṛhītavivāhāgnir gṛhastha iti manyate |

	annaṃ tasya na bhoktavyaṃ vṛthāpāko hi sa smṛtaḥ ||

iti, tad adhikāraprāptau satyāṃ veditavyam | aśrotriyā vedarahitāḥ | anuvākyam anuvacanaṃ tadvihīnā ananuvākyā jñānarahitā ity arthaḥ | atra gargaḥ |

	yo vaidikam anādṛtya karma smārtaitihāsikam |

	mohāt samācared vipro na sa puṇyena yujyate ||

	pradhānaṃ vaidikaṃ karma guṇabhūtaṃ tatherarat |

	guṇaniṣṭhaḥ pradhānaṃ tu hitvā gacchaty aghogatim || iti |

etad vidyamānavaidikasāmarthyaviṣayam | ata eva vyāsaḥ |

	śrautaṃ karma na cec chaktaḥ kartuṃ smārtaṃ samācaret |

	atrāpy aśaktaḥ karaṇe sadācāro bhaved budhaḥ ||

anena sati sāmarthye bhavitavyaṃ vaidikenety uktaṃ bhavati | uktaṃ ca vasiṣṭhena: "alam agnyādheyāya nānāhitāgniḥ syāt, alaṃ ca somāya nāsomayājī" iti | alaṃ samartha ity arthaḥ | sāmarthyaṃ cānāhitāgnipitṛrāhityādi | evaṃ ca yasyādhānādisāmarthyam asti tasyaiva "anāhitāgnitāsteyam" ityādidoṣo nānyasyety anusaṃdheyam | atra vasiṣṭhaḥ: "avaśyaṃ brāhmaṇo 'gnīn ādadhīta | darśapūrṇamāsāgrayaṇeṣṭicāturmāsyapaśusomaiś ca yajeta" iti | hārīto 'pi |

	pākayajñān yajen nityaṃ haviryajñāṃś ca nityaśaḥ |

	saumyāṃś ca vidhipūrveṇa ya icched dharmam avyayam || iti |

te ca gautamena darśitāḥ: "aṣṭakā pārvaṇaṃ śrāddhaṃ śrāvaṇyāgrayaṇī caitry āśvayujī ceti sapta pākayajñasaṃsthāḥ | agnyādheyam agnihotraṃ darśapūrṇamāsau cāturmāsyāny āgrayaneṣṭir nirūḍhapaśubandhaḥ sautrāmaṇir iti sapt haviryajñasaṃsthāḥ | agniṣṭomo 'tyagniṣṭoma ukthyaḥ ṣoḍaśī vājapeyo 'tirātro 'ptoryāma iti sapta somasaṃsthāḥ" iti | pārvaṇaṃ parvaṇi kriyagāṇaṃ (?) sthālīpākalakṣaṇam | śrāddhaṃ māsisrāddham | śrāvaṇī sarpabaliḥ | āgrayāny āgrayaṇam | caitrī holakākhyaṃ karma | āśvayujī indradvajahomākhyaṃ karma | anye prasiddhāḥ | kecit "aupāsanahomo vaiśvadevaṃ pārvaṇam aṣṭakā māsiśrāddhaṃ sarpabalir īśānabaliḥ" iti sapta pākayajñān āhuḥ | evam ekaviṃśatisaṃsthaṃ yajñam abhidhāya devalaḥ: "vājapeyāśvamedharājasūyapauṇḍarīkagosavādayo mahāyajñakratavaḥ" iti | atra kālaniyamam āha manuḥ |

	agnihotraṃ tu juhuyād ādyante dyuniśoḥ sadā |

	darśena cārdhamāsānte pūrṇamāsena caiva hi ||

	sasyānte navasasyeṣṭyā tathartvante dvijo 'dhvaraiḥ |

	paśunā tva ayanasyānte samānte saumikair makhaiḥ || iti |

ādyante dyuniśoḥ sāyaṃ prātaḥ saṃdhyayor ity arthaḥ | adhvaraiś caturmāsyaiḥ,

	sasyayukto naveṣṭyā tu cāturmāsyaiḥ smṛto makhaḥ |

iti jābālismaraṇāt | atrānukalpam āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	pratisaṃvatsaraṃ somaḥ paśuḥ pratyayanaṃ tathā |

	kartavyāgrayaneṣṭiś ca cāturmāsyāni caiva hi ||

	eṣām asaṃbhave kuryād iṣṭiṃ vaiśvānarīṃ dvijaḥ || iti |

eṣāṃ somādīnāṃ kathaṃcid asaṃbhave pratinidhitvena tattatkāla eva pṛthak pṛthag etām iṣṭiṃ nirvaped ity arthaḥ | tattatkāryakaratvena tatatdharmalābhāt, "pratinidhis taddharmā ca syāt" ity āpastambasmaraṇāt | nanv evaṃ tarhi saumikādividhyantaraprāptiḥ syāt | maivam, agnihotrādiśabdasya tattadaṅgavargaprāptyarthatvāt | yat punar manunoktam,

	iṣṭiṃ vaiśvānarīṃ nityaṃ nirvaped abdaparyaye |

	kḷptānāṃ paśusomānāṃ niṣkṛtyartham asaṃbhave || iti |

tad api paśvādikārya eveṣṭividhānaparaṃ na punas tadakaraṇe prāyaścittavidhānārtham | niṣkṛtiḥ somādikāryaniṣpattiḥ | yady evaṃ vaiśvānaryaivālaṃ kim anyair ity āśaṅkyānantaram āha sa eva |

	āpatkalpena yo dharmaṃ kurute 'nāpadi dvijaḥ |

	sa nāpnoti phalaṃ tasya paratreti vicāritam ||

	viśvaiś ca devaiḥ sādhyaiś ca brāhmaṇaiś ca maharṣibhiḥ |

	āpatsu maraṇād bhītair vadheḥ pratinidhiḥ kṛtaḥ || iti |

vidher mukhyasyety arthaḥ | ato niṣkṛtigrahaṇe 'pi vaiśvānareṣṭiḥ pratinidhir eva na prāyaścittam ity anusaṃdheyam | etenaiteṣāṃ nityatvam ity uktaṃ bhavati | uktaṃ ca prajāpatinā akaraṇe prāyaścittavidhānāt | \
	kāle tv ādhāya karmāṇi apravāsī viśeṣataḥ |

	tapaḥ kurvaṃs trirātreṇa māsi māsi viśuddhyati ||

	darśaṃ vā paurṇamāsīṃ vā luptvā cobhayam eva vā |

	ekasmin kṛcchrapādena dvayor ardhena śodhanam ||

	havir yajñeṣv aśaktasya luptam apy ekam āditaḥ |

	prājāpatyena śuddhyeta pākasaṃsthāsu caiva hi ||

	saṃdhyopāsanahānau tu nityasnānaṃ vilopya ca |

	homaṃ ca naityakaṃ śuddhyet sāvitryaṣṭasahasrakṛt ||

	samānte somayāgānāṃ hānau cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret |

	akṛtvānyatamaṃ yajñaṃ yajñānām adhikārataḥ ||

	upavāsena suddhyeta pākasaṃsthāsu caiva hi ||

kātyāyano 'pi |

	pitṛyajñātyaye caiva vaiśvadevadvayasya ca |

	aniṣṭvā navayajñena navānnaprāśane tathā ||

	bhojane patitānnasya carur vaiśvānaro bhavet || iti |

manur apy akṛtanavayajñasya navāśananiṣedham āha |

	nāniṣṭvā navasasyeṣṭyā paśunā cāgnimān dvijaḥ |

	navānnam adyān māṃsaṃ ca dīrgham āyur jijīviṣuḥ ||

ayaṃ ca navānnaniṣedho vakṣyamāṇavrīhyādyabhiprāyeṇa | tathā ca āpastambaḥ: "yad akṛtvāgrayaṇaṃ navasyāśnīyād devebhyo bhāgaṃ pratikḷptam adyād ārtim ārcchet" iti | viṣṇur api |

	navayajñādhikārasthāḥ śyāmākā vrīhayo yavāḥ |

	akṛtāgrayaṇo nadyād anyeṣv aniyamaḥ smṛtaḥ || iti |

atra kālaniyamam āha āpastambaḥ: "varṣāsu śyāmākair yajeta śaradi vrīhibhir vasante yavair yathartu veṇuyavair iti vijñāyate" iti | śrutir api: "gṛhamedhī vrīhiyavābhyāṃ śaradvasantayor jayeta śyāmākair nīvārair vā varṣāsv āpatkalpo 'nyonyena purāṇair vā" iti | atra kūrmapurāṇe |

	nāstikyād atha vālasyād yo 'gnīn nādhātum icchati |

	yajeta vā na yajñena sa yāti narakān bahūn ||

	tasmāt sarvaprayatnena brāhmaṇo 'pi viśeṣataḥ |

	ādhāyāgniṃ viśuddhātmā yajeta parameśvaram || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyām agnihotrādikarmāṇi**

**adhikārinirūpaṇam**

uktāny ādhānādīni karmāṇi | adhunā tatra tatrādhikārī nirūpyate | tatra vasiṣṭhaḥ: "alam agnyādheyāya nānāhitāgiḥ syād alaṃ ca somāya nāsomayājī" iti | alaṃ samartha ity arthaḥ| tac ca sāmarthyaṃ yājñavalkyena darśitam |

	traivārṣikādhikānno yaḥ sa hi somaṃ pibed dvijaḥ || iti |

varṣatrayaṃ yāvad bhṛtyabharaṇaparyāptam annam adhikaṃ vā yasyāsti sa somaṃ pibet somena yajetety arthaḥ | tathā ca manuḥ |

	yasya traivārṣikaṃ bhaktaṃ paryāptaṃ bhṛtyavṛttaye |

	adhikaṃ vāpi vidyeta sa somaṃ pātum arhati ||

etat kāmyasomābhiprāyam, ṛṇaśruter nityasyāvaśyakartavyatvāt, akaraṇe pratyavāyavidhānāc ca | uktaṃ cānantaram eva manunā |

	ataḥ svalpīyasi dravye yaḥ somaṃ pibati dvijaḥ |

	apītasomapūrvo 'pi sa na prāpnoti tatphalam || iti |

ataḥ uktād alpīyasi dravye yaḥ pūrvam akṛtasomayāgaḥ so 'pi tasya nityasya phalaṃ na prāpnoti | kim uta kāmyasyety arthaḥ | ato nāpadhanaḥ kamyasomayāgaṃ kuryāt | anenaivābhiprāyeṇa śaṅkho 'pi |

	traivārṣikādhikānnas tu pibet somam atandritaḥ |

	iṣṭiṃ vaiśvānarīṃ kuryāt tathaivālpadhano dvijaḥ || iti |

iṣṭigrahaṇaṃ somayāgāt prācīnāgnihotrādikarmopalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva yājñavalkyaḥ |

	prāksaumikīḥ kriyāḥ kuryād yasyānnaṃ vārṣikaṃ bhavet | iti |

prāksomodbhavāḥ prāksomikyaḥ | manur api |

	puṇyāny anyāni kurvīta śraddadhāno jitendriyaḥ |

	na tv alpadakṣiṇair yajñair yajeteha kathaṃcana ||

	indriyāṇi yaśaḥ svargam āyuḥ kīrtiṃ prajāḥ paśūn |

	hanty alpadakṣiṇo yajñaḥ tasmān nālpadhano yajet ||

matsyapurāṇe 'pi |

	annahīno dahed rāṣṭraṃ mantrahīna tathartvijaḥ |

	yajantaṃ dakṣiṇāhīno nasti yajñasamo ripuḥ || iti |

annaparimāṇam api śaṅkhenoktam |

	sahasraṃ bhojayet some brāhmaṇānāṃ śataṃ paśau |

	cāturmāsyeṣu sarveṣu śataṃ parvaṇi parvaṇi || iti |

yat tu śrutau: "dātavyaiva yajñe dakṣiṇā bhavaty alpikāpi" iti, tan nityābhiprāyam | ata eva bodhāyanaḥ |

	yasya luptāni nityāni tathaivājasrakāṇi ca |

	vipathastho hi na svargaṃ gacchet tu patito hi saḥ ||

	tasmāt skandaiḥ phalair mūlair madhunātha rasena vā |

	nityaṃ nityāni kurvīta na ca nityāni lopayet || iti |

tenālpadhanasyāpi nityasome 'dhikārasiddhiḥ | evam ādhāne 'pi draṣṭavyam | tathā ca prajāpatiḥ |

	sarvasaṃsthādhikārī syād āhitāgnir dhane sati |

	ādadhyān nirdhano 'py agniṃna tu pāpabhayād dvijaḥ ||

na pāpabhayād āhitāgniḥ saṃsthādhikārī, kiṃ tu dhane saty eva, tāsāṃ kāmyatvāt | nirdhano 'lapadhana ity arthaḥ | manur api |

	prājāpatyam adatvāśvam agnyādheyasya dakṣiṇāṃ |

	anāhitāgnir bhavati brāhmaṇo vibhave sati ||

avibhave tu brāhmaṇo 'śvam adatvāpy āhitāgnir bhavatīti bhāvaḥ | ata eva āpastambaḥ: "yady anāḍhyo 'gnīn ādadhīta kāmam evaikāṃ gāṃ dadyāt" iti | atra kālaniyamam āha viṣṇuḥ: "yady ahar evainaṃ śraddhopanam etat tad ahar evādadhīta" iti | kārṣṇājinir api |

	putram utpādya karmaitat kuryād vaitānikaṃ budhaḥ |

	yathākathaṃcid ādadhyāt prāptaṃ cet sādhuto dhanam || iti |

sādhugrahaṇaṃ śūdrādivyudāsārtham | ata eva manuḥ |

	ye śūdrād adhigamyārtham agnihotram upāsate |

	ṛtvijas te hi śūdrāṇāṃ brahmavādiṣu garhitāḥ ||

	teṣāṃ satatam ajñānāṃ vṛṣalāgnyupasevināṃ |

	padā mastakam ākramya dātā durgāṇi saṃtaret || iti |

anenādhānapūrvakam aghinotraṃ niṣiddhyate nāgnihotramātram, "vṛṣaḷāgnyupasevinām" iti śūdrāgnitvavacanāt | yamo 'pi |

	upādāya dhanaṃ śūdrād yo 'gnihotram upāvaset |

	śūdrāgnihotrī sa bhaved brahmavādiṣu garhitaḥ ||

	parakarmakaro nityaṃ śūdrāgneḥ paryupāsanāt |

	ātmānaṃ samadhaḥ (?) kṛtvā parāṃs tārayate hi saḥ ||

chāgaleyo 'pi |

	yaḥ śūdrād adhigamyārthān agnihotram upāvaset |

	dātā tatphalam āpnoti kartā ca narakaṃ vrajet ||

evaṃ yajñārthe 'pi dhane draṣṭavyam, tatrāpi doṣaśravaṇāt | tathā ca yamaḥ |

	dharmavid brāhmaṇaḥ śūdrād yajñārthaṃ nāhared dhanam |

	jāyate pretya caṇḍālaḥ śūdrārtheneṣṭavedataḥ ||

manur api |

	na yajñārthaṃ dhanaṃ śūdrād vipro bhikṣeta dharmavit |

	yajamānas tu bhikṣitvā caṇḍālaḥ pretya jāyate ||

yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	caṇḍālo jāyate yajñakaraṇāc chūdrabhikṣitāt |

śaṅkho 'pi |

	na śūdrāt tu dhanaṃ bhikṣet sarvaṃ dadyāt tu bhikṣitam |

anenārthād asarvadānaṃ niṣiddham ity uktaṃ bhavati | ata eva manuḥ |

	yajñārtham arthaṃ bhikṣitvā yo na sarvaṃ prayacchati |

	sa yāti bhāsatāṃ vipraḥ kākatāṃ ca śataṃ samāḥ ||

yamo 'pi |

	yajñārthaṃ bhikṣitaṃ dravyaṃ yaḥ sarvaṃ nopayojayet |

	śvapākayonau jāyeta sa tad bhuktvā tu durmatiḥ || iti |

yadā tu prakrāntayajñasya madhye kathaṃcit paśvādyasaṃbhavena pratiruddhaḥ tadā śūdrādes tad grāhyam ity āha manuḥ |

	yajñaś cet pratiruddhaḥ syād ekenāṅgena yajvanaḥ |

	brāhmaṇasya viśeṣeṇa dhārmike sati rājani ||

	yo vaiśyaḥ syād bahupaśur hīnakratur asomapaḥ |

	kuṭumbāt tasya tad dravyam āhared yajñasiddhaye ||

	āharet trīṇi vā dve vā kāmaṃ śūdrasya veśmanaḥ |

	na hi śūdrasya yajñeṣu kaścid asti parigrahaḥ ||

	na hi śūdrasya yajñeṣu kaścid asti parigrahaḥ |

	yo 'nāhitāgniḥ śatagur ayajvā ca sahasraguḥ |

	tayor api kuṭumbābhyām āhared avicārayan || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyām adhikārinirūpaṇam**

**atha homavidhiḥ**

tatra dakṣaḥ |

	saṃdhyākarmāvasāne tu svayaṃhomo vidhīyate |

	svayaṃ homaphalaṃ yat syāt tad anyena na labhyate ||

kiṃ tarhy anyahome phalam ity apekṣite sa evāha |

	home yat phalam uddiṣṭaṃ juhvataḥ svayam eva tu |

	hūyamāne tad anyena phalam ardhaṃ prapadyate || iti |

atra kartṛniyamam āha śaunakaḥ: "pāṇigrahaṇād avigṛhyaṃ (?) paricaret svayaṃ patny api vā putraḥ kumāry antevāsī" iti | antevāsī śiṣyaḥ | dakṣo 'pi |

	ṛtvik putro gurur bhrātā bhāgineyo 'tha viṭpatiḥ |

	etair api hutaṃ yat syāt tad dhutaṃ svayam eva tu ||

viṭpatir jāmātā | āpastambo 'pi: "ahar ahar yajamānaḥ svayam agnihotraṃ juhuyāt parvaṇi vā brahmacārī vā juhuyād brahmaṇā his a parikrīto bhavati | kṣīrahotā vā juhuyād dhanena hi sa parikrīto bhavatīti bahvṛcabrāhmaṇam" iti | atra viśeṣam āha viṣṇuḥ: "svayam ahutvā na paraṃ yājayet" iti | viṣṇupurāṇe 'pi |

	ṛtvak putro 'tha patnī vā śiṣyo vāpi sahodaraḥ |

	prāpyānujñāṃ viśeṣeṇa juhuyād vā yathāvidhi ||

etat sarvaṃ svayaṃhomālābhaviṣayam, tasyaiva praśastatvāt | tathā ca śrutiḥ |

	anyaiḥ śatahutād dhomād ekaḥ śiṣyahuto varaḥ |

	śiṣyaiḥ śatahutād dhomād ekaḥ putrahuto varaḥ |

	putraiḥ śatahutād dhomād eko hy ātmahuto varaḥ || iti |

yat punar manunoktam,

	naiva kanyā na yuvatir nālpavidyo na bāliśaḥ |

	hotā syād agnihotrasya nārto nāsaṃskṛtas tathā ||

	narake hi patanty ete juhvantaḥ sa yasya tat |

	tasmād vaitānakuśalo hotā syād vedapāragaḥ ||

iti, tac chrautāgniviṣayam, agnihotragrahaṇāt | etena na śaunakoktivirodhaḥ | kanyāgrahaṇaṃ patnyā ap pradarśanārtham | ata eva gobilaḥ: "kāmaṃ gṛhyāgnau patnī juhuyāt sāyaṃprātar homau" iti | ṛtvigādihome 'pi yajamānasaṃnidhānena bhavitavyam ity uktaṃ kātyāyanena |

	asamakṣaṃ tu dampatyor hotavyaṃ nartvigādinā |

	dvayor apy samakṣaṃ tu bhaved dhutam anarthakam || iti |

atrāpiśabdāt kathaṃcid anyatarābhāve 'pi na doṣa ity uktaṃ bhavati | ata eva kvacit pravāsānugrahas tenaiva darśitaḥ |

	nikṣiptāgniṃ svadāreṣu parikalpyartvijaṃ tathā |

	pravaset kāryavān vipro vṛthaiva na ciraṃ vaset || iti |

atra yajñapārśvaḥ |

	duhitrā snuṣayā vāpi vihāro na virudhyate |

	nirlepanaṃ ca pātrāṇām upalepanam arcanam || iti |

vihāro viharaṇam | atra kālaniyamam āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	sūrye 'staśailam aprāpte ṣaṭtriṃśadbhir ihāṅgulaiḥ |

	prāduṣkaraṇam agnīnāṃ prātar bhāsāṃ ca darśane ||

prāduṣkaraṇaṃ viharaṇam | tathā homakālo 'pi tenaiva darśitaḥ |

	yāvat samyaṅ na bhāvyante nabhasy ṛkṣāṇi sarvaśaḥ |

	na ca lauhityam āyānti tāvat sāyaṃ tu hūyate ||

marīcir api |

	niraśmivatyāṃ saṃdhyāyāṃ sūryanakṣatraraśmibhiḥ |

	homakālaḥ sa vijñeyo hy agnigarbhā tathā mahī ||

āpastambo 'pi: "samudro vā eṣa yad ahorātras tasyaite gādhe tīrthe yat sandhī | tasmāt sandhau hotavyam iti śailālibrāhmaṇaṃ bhavati | nakṣatraṃ dṛṣṭvā pradoṣe niśāyāṃ vā sāyam" iti | hotavyam iti sarvatrānuvartate | yatra śakyam upasthātuṃ tad gādham | nakṣatram ekam ap dṛṣṭvā pradoṣe, sarveṣūditeṣu niśāyāṃ yasyāṃ daśāyāṃ śerate bhūtāni | ata evoktam "kālātipattir navanāḍikordham" iti | ete catvāraḥ sāyaṃ homakālāḥ | tathā prātar homakālā api tenaiva darśitāḥ: "uṣasy upodayaṃ samayāviṣita (?) udite prātaḥ" | samayāviṣite ardhodite | tathā manur api |

	udite 'nudite caiva samayādhyuṣite tathā |

	sarvathā vartate yajñaḥ itīyaṃ vaidikī śrutiḥ || iti |

eteṣāṃ lakṣaṇam āha vyāsaḥ |

	rātreḥ ṣoḍaśake bhāge grahanakṣatrabhūṣite |

	kāle tv anudite prātar homaṃ kuryād vicakṣaṇaḥ ||

	tathā prabhātasamaye naṣṭanakṣatramaṇḍale |

	ravir yāvan na dṛśyeta raśmibhis tu samanvitaḥ ||

	uditaṃ taṃ vijānīyāt tatra homaṃ prakalpayet || iti |

anena rekhādarśanād ārambhya tṛtīyo homakālaḥ ity uktaṃ bhavati | ata eva kātyāyanaḥ |

	hastād ūrdhvaṃ ravir yāvad bhuvaṃ hitvā na gacchati |

	tāvad dhomavidhiḥ puṇyo nānyo hy uditahominām ||

āśvalāyano 'pi: "saṅgavāntaḥ prātaḥ" iti | akāle anāgate kāle kṛte punaḥ kāle kartavyam | atīte tu kāle kṛte tasyānupādeyatvāt kṛtam apy akṛtam evety arthaḥ | yadā tu kathaṃcin mukhyakālātikramaḥ tadā gobiloktaṃ draṣṭavyam: "atha yadi gṛhye 'gnau sāyaṃprātarhomayor darśapūrṇamāsayor vā havyaṃ hotāraṃ vā nādhigacchet kathaṃ kuryād iti | ā sāyamāhuteḥ prātarāhutir nātyeti ā prātarāhuteḥ sāyamāhutir āmāvāsyāyāḥ paurṇamāsī nātyety ā paurṇamāsyā amāvāsyā" iti | ataḥ gauṇe 'pi kāle 'tipannaṃ karma kuryād iti bhavaḥ | tac ca prāyaścittānantaram eva kāryam, "yadi sāyamagnihotrkālo 'tipadyeta" ity āpastambena mukhyakālātipāttau prāyaścittābhidhānāt | āśvalāyano 'pi: "saṅgavāntaḥ prātas tam atinīya caturgṛhītam ājyaṃ juhuyāt" iti | etac ca gauṇakālānuṣṭhānam āpadviṣayam, homakālān prakṛtya, "sarveṣv eteṣu kāleṣu hotavyam āpadi hutam ity eva pratīyāt" ity āpastambasmaraṇāt | uktaṃ ca gobilena: "yadi havyaṃ hotāraṃ vā nādhigacchet kathaṃ kuryāt" iti | gauṇakālābhiprāyeṇa kātyāyano 'pi |

	paurṇamāsyatyaye havyaṃ hotā vā yad ahar bhavet |

	tad ahar juhuyād evam amāvāsyātyaye 'pi ca ||

havyaṃ haviḥ | hotā ṛtvik | atrāpi kṛtvā pāthikṛtaṃ vaiśvānaraṃ vātipannaṃ kāryam: "agnaye pathikēte puroḍāśam aṣṭākapālaṃ nirvaped yo darśapūrṇamāsayājī sann amāvāsyāṃ vā paurṇamāsīṃ vātipādayed vaiśvānaraṃ dvādaśakapālaṃ nirvaped avāvāsyāṃ vā paurṇamāsīṃ vātipadya" iti śruteḥ | etad ap yāvad anyasya parvaṇo na kālaḥ | tatprāptau tu prāyaścittam eva na punar atipannānuṣṭhānam adhikārāntarāvarodhena pūrvādhikāranivṛtteḥ | uktaṃ ca bhāṣyakāreṇa: "tato darśo vā pūrṇamāso vā yāvad anyo na parvakālaḥ" iti | eṣa eva nyāyaḥ sāyaṃprātarhomayor api | evaṃ paśvāgrayaṇādyatipattāv api kṛtvā pāthikṛtaṃ vaiśvānaraṃ cātipannānuṣṭanaṃ (?) tayor api tadvikāratvāt | atra vaijāvāpaḥ (?) |

	eke hy uditahomāḥ syur anye 'nuditahominaḥ |

	anye bhojanahomāś ca pakṣahomās tathaiva ca ||

bhojanahomāḥ syur ity āpadviṣayam | evaṃ pakṣahomo 'pi draṣṭavyaḥ | tathā ca marīciḥ |

	śarīrāpad bhaved yatra bhayād vārtaḥ prajāyate |

	tathānyāsv api cāpatsu pakṣahomo vidhīyate ||

"yāyāvarā ha vai purā nāma ṛṣaya āsaṃste 'dhany āśramyaṃste 'rdhamāsāyārdhamāsāya agnihotraṃ juhuvuḥ | tasyād yāyāvaradharmeṇa āmayāvyārto vā jananamaraṇayor adhvani vāpatsu vārdhamāsāyārdhamāsāyāgnihotraṃ juhuyāt pratipadi sāyaṃ caturdaśa caturgṛhītāny unnayaty ekā samit sakṛd dhomaḥ sakṛt pāṇinirmārjanaṃ sakṛd upasthānam evaṃ prātaḥ" iti | pakṣahome tu madhye tv āpannivṛttau punar homo na doṣāyety aha marīciḥ |

	pakṣahomān atho kṛtvā madhye tasmān nivartitaḥ |

	homaṃ punaḥ parkuryāt tu na cāsau doṣabhāg bhavet ||

tathā samasyahomo 'pi tenaiva darsitaḥ |

	pravāse vāgnihotrī yas tripakṣāhaṃ ca sapta vā |

	dātavyo homa ekāhe sāyaṃ prātaḥ pṛthak pṛthak || iti |

atra dravyaniyamam āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	kṛtamodanasaktvādi taṇḍulādi kṛtākṛtam |

	vrīhyādi cākṛtaṃ proktam iti havyaṃ tridhā budhaiḥ ||

smṛtyantare 'pi |

	tailaṃ dadhi payas somo yavāgūr odano ghṛtam |

	taṇḍulā māṃsam āpaś ca daśa dravyāṇy akāmataḥ ||

kātyāyano 'pi |

	haviṣyeṣu yavā mukhyās tad anu vrīhayaḥ smṛtāḥ |

	abhāve vrīhiyavayor dadhnā vā payasāpi vā |

	tadabhāve yavāgvā vā juhuyād udakena vā ||

śaunako 'pi: "kāmaṃ tu vrīhiyavatilaiḥ" iti | mukhyadravyālābhe tu kātyāyanoktaṃ draṣṭavyam |

	yathoktas tv asampattau grāhyaṃ tadanusāri ca |

	yavānām itv godhūmā vrīhīṇām (?) iva taṇḍulāḥ || iti |

yatra punar dravyādiviśeṣānupādānaṃ tatrāpi sa evāha |

	ājyaṃ havyam anādeśe juhotiṣu vidhīyate |

	mantrasya devatāyās tu prajāpatir iti sthitiḥ || iti |

atrāhutiparimāṇam āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	prathadhānyaṃ catuḥṣaṣṭir āhuteḥ parikīrtitam |

	tilānāṃ tu tadardhaṃ syāt tadardhaṃ syād ghṛtasya tu ||

bodhāyano 'pi |

	vrīhīṇāṃ vā yavānāṃ vā śatam āhutir iṣyate | iti |

homas tu gṛhyoktavidhinā tad uktaṃ gṛhyapariśiṣṭe |

	svasvagṛhyoktavidhinā homaṃ kuryād yathāvidhi | iti |

yathāvidhi yathāśastram ity arthaḥ | tat katham ity apekṣite,

	tīrthāyatanasaṃpūrṇaṃ prātar uttānapāṇinā |

	dvayaṅgule samidho 'tītya sarvatra juhuyād dhaviḥ ||

viṣṇur api |

	aprabuddhe sadhūme vā juhuyād yo hutāśane |

	yajamāno bhaved andhaḥ so 'mutreti hi naḥ śrutam ||

	yo 'narciṣi juhoty agnau vyaṅgāre caiva mānavaḥ |

	mandāgnir āmayāvī ca daridraś copajāyate ||

	ataś ca bahuśuṣkendhasusamiddhe hutāśane |

	vidhūme lelihāne ca hotavyaṃ karmasiddhaye ||

āpastambo 'pi: "yad aṅgāreṣu vyavaśānteṣu lelāyad vibhāti tad devānām āsyam | tasmāt tathā hotavyaṃ yathāsye 'pidadhāty evaṃ tad iti vijñāyate" iti | vyavaśānteṣv arcirvirahiteṣu jvālā yad vibhāti dīpyamānaṃ vibhāti vety arthaḥ | yasya punaḥ śrautāgniḥ smārthāgniś ca tasyānuṣṭhāne viśeṣam āha bharadvājaḥ |

	homaṃ vaitānike kṛtvā smārtaṃ kuryād vicakṣaṇaḥ |

	smṛtīnāṃ vedamūlatvāt smārtaṃ kecit purā viduḥ ||

śātātapo 'pi |

	śrautaṃ yatnāt svayaṃ kuryād anyo 'pi smārtam ācaret |

	aśaktau śrautam apy anyaḥ kuryād ācāram antataḥ || iti |

etac ca jñātvaivānuṣṭheyam anyathā doṣaśravaṇāt | tathā ca aṅgirāḥ |

	svābhiprāyakṛtaṃ karma yat kiṃcij jñānavarjitam |

	krīḍākarmeva bālānāṃ tat sarvaṃ niṣprayojanam ||

caturviṃśatimate 'pi |

	hutaṃ jñānakriyāhīnaṃ hutās tv ajñānataḥ kriyāḥ |

	apaśyann andhako dagdhaḥ pasyann api ca paṅgukaḥ || iti |

yadā tu pramādāt karmapracyutiḥ tadā prajāpatinoktaṃ draṣṭavyam |

	pramādāt kurvatāṃ karma pracyavetādhvareṣu yat |

	smaraṇād eva tad viṣṇoḥ saṃpūrṇaṃ syād iti śrutiḥ ||

adhvareṣu yajñeṣu | atra kūrmapurāṇam |

	brahmaṇy ādhāya karmāṇi niḥsaṅgaḥ kāmavarjitaḥ |

	prasannenaiva manasā kurvāṇo yāti tat padam || iti |

brahmaṇyādhānaṃ brahmārpaṇam | tad api tatraivoktam |

	brahmaṇā dīyate deyaṃ brahmaṇe saṃpradīyate |

	brahmaiva dīyate ceti brahmārpaṇam idaṃ param ||

	nāhaṃ kartā sarvam etad brahmaiva kurute tadā |

	etad brahmārpaṇam proktam ṛṣibhis tattvadarśibhiḥ ||

	prīṇātu bhavagān īśaḥ karmaṇānena śāśvataḥ |

	karoti satataṃ buddhyā brahmārpaṇam idaṃ param ||

	yad vā phalānāṃ saṃnyāsaṃ prakuryāt parameśvare |

	karmaṇām etad ity āhuḥ brahmārpaṇam anuttamam ||

	tasmāt seveta satataṃ karmayogaṃ prasannadhīḥ |

	tṛpyate parameśasya tat padaṃ yāti śāśvatam || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ homavidhiḥ**

**athaupavasthyaniyamāḥ **

tatra pulastyaḥ |

	sakṛt parvaṇi sarpīṃṣi haviṣyaṃ laghubhojanam |

	na sāyaṃ nopavāsaḥ syāt tailāmiṣavivarjitam ||

atra viśeṣam āha āpastambaḥ: "tṛptiś cānnasya | yac cainayoḥ priyaṃ syāt tad etasminn ahani bhuñjīyātām" iti | atra varyāny āha hārītaḥ: "māṣamasūramadhumāṃsaparānnamaithunāni vratye 'hani varjayet" iti | vratyāham anvādhānadinam | bharadvājo 'pi |

	varjayet parvakāleṣu strītailāmiṣabhojanam ||

sāṅkhyāyano 'pi |

	kalahaṃ krītavikrītaṃ prahāsaṃ bahubhāṣaṇam |

	tauryatrikaṃ vṛthā śayyāṃ yakṣyamāṇo vivarjayet ||

jābālir api |

	kaidārakān kulutthāṃś ca varjayet kodravāṃs tathā |

	anṛtaṃ bahuvādaṃ ca krayavikrayam eva ca ||

	dantaśaucaṃ ca pūrvedhyur yāgasyaitāni varjayet |

	masūrān lavaṇān kṣārāṃś caṇakān koradūṣakān |

	māṣān madhu parānnaṃ ca varjayet varvaṇi dvijaḥ |

gṛhyapariśiṣṭe 'pi |

	śākaṃ māṃsaṃ masūrāṃś ca caṇakaṃ koradūṣakān |

	māṣān madhu parānnaṃ ca varjayed aupavastake (?) ||

bodhāyano 'pi: "sarvam evaitad ahaḥ kośidhānyaṃ varjayed anyatra tilebhyaḥ" iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyām aupavasathyaniyamāḥ**

**atha punarādhānanimittāni**

tatra kātyāyanaḥ |

	vihāyāgniṃ sabhāryaś cet sīmām ullaṅghya gacchati |

	homakālātyaye tasya punar ādhānam iṣyate ||

śaunako 'pi |

	agnāv anugate yatra homakaladvayaṃ vrajet |

	ubhayor vipravāse vā laukikāgnir vidhīyate ||

	proṣite tu yadā patnī yadi grāmāntraṃ vrajet |

	homakāle tu saṃprāpte na sā doṣeṇa yujyate ||

	atha tatraiva vasati homakālavyatikramaḥ |

	laukiko 'gnir vidhīyīta kāṭhakaśrutidarśanāt ||

	yajamānaś ca patnī ca ubhau pravasato yadi |

	ā homān na nivartetāṃ punar ādhānam arhati ||

āpastambo 'pi: "yadi patnī sīmāntare ādityo 'stam iyād abhyudiyād vā punar ādheyaṃ tasya prāyaścittiḥ | nāsati yajamāne grāmamaryādām agnīn atihareyur yady atihareyur agnayo laukikāḥ saṃpadyerann iti | yadā yāvatyo grāmamaryādā nadyas tāvatīr atikrāmantau anvārabheyātāṃ yadi nānvārabheyātāṃ laukikāḥ saṃpadyeran" iti | śaunako 'pi |

	homadvayātyaye darśapūrṇamāsātyaye tathā |

	punar evāgnim ādadhyād iti bhārgavaśāsanam || iti |

dhāryamāṇe 'gnau caturahād ūrdhvam api homavicchittau punarādhānam ity āpastambamatiḥ | āśvalāyano 'pi: "sarvāṃś cānugatān ādityo 'bhyudiyād vāstam iyād vāgnyādheyaṃ punarādheyaṃ vā samārūḍheṣu cāraṇināśaḥ" iti | etad vihṛtāgniviṣayam iti kaiścid vyākhyātam | āpastambo 'pi: "yasya vobhāv anugatāv abhinimroced abhyudiyād vā punarādheyaṃ tasya prāyaścittiḥ" iti | ubhau gārhapatyāhavanīyau | tathā yadi pakṣahome pakṣatrayam atīyāt punarādheyaṃ tasya prāyaścittir iti | śaunako 'pi |

	daiviko bhautikaś caiva svedārthaṃ yo 'gnir uddhṛtaḥ |

	sarve te laukikā jñeyā ekāgau vigate sati ||

etat pramādoddhṛtāgniviṣayam | paiṭhīnasir api |

	praskhalīkṛtadharmasya pīḍyamānasya śatrubhiḥ |

	māsadvayaṃ pravāso 'sti parato 'nāhitāgnivat || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ punarādhānanimittāni**

**agnyādheyaviṣayam**

athāgnihotraprasaṅgād anyad apy agnyādheyaviṣayaṃ kiṃcid ucyate | tatra yājñavalkyaḥ |

	dāhayitvāgnihotreṇa striyaṃ vṛttavatīṃ patiḥ |

	āhared vidhivad dārān agnīṃś caivāvilambayan || iti |

vṛttavatīm ācāravatīm | sā ca yadi savarṇā | tathā ca manuḥ |

	evaṃvṛttāṃ savarṇāṃ strīṃ dvijātiḥ pūrvamāriṇīm |

	dāhayed agnihotreṇa yajñapātrais ca dharmavit || iti |

evaṃvṛttām uktācārām | anenaikāntato 'savarṇāyā agnihotreṇa dahanaṃ na niṣiddhyate kiṃ tu satyām eva savarṇāyāṃ tasyā adhikārāsaṃbhavāt | tathā ca yājñavalkyaḥ |

	satyām anyāṃ savarṇāyāṃ dharmakāryaṃ na kārayet | iti |

satyāṃ sarvarṇāyām asavarṇāṃ dharmakāryaṃ kārayet, tayā saha dharmān nācared ity arthaḥ | anenāsatyāṃ savarṇāyām asavarṇāyā apy adhikāra ity uktaṃ bhavati | ata eva vasiṣṭho 'pi śūdrayaiva saha dharmānuṣṭhānaniṣedham āha: "kṛṣṇavarṇā vai rāmā ramaṇāyaiva na dharmāya" iti | kṛṣṇavarṇā śūdrā | savarṇānekatve tu vinā jyeṣṭhayā itarābhiḥ saha na dharmān ācaret | kiṃ tu sahaiva jyeṣṭhayā | tathā ca yājñavalkyaḥ |

	savarṇāsu vidhau dharmye jyeṣṭhaya na vinetarā | iti |

dharmye vidhau jyeṣṭhayā vinā itarā madhyamā kaniṣṭhā vā na niyoktavyā kiṃ tu sahaiva jyeṣṭhayety arthaḥ | na ca jyeṣṭhāṃ muktvā itarā sahadharmacāriṇīti vyākhyānaṃ śaṃkanīyam, yat āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	naikayāpi vinā kāryam ādhānaṃ bhāryayā dvijaiḥ |

	akṛtaṃ tad vijānīyāt sarvān anvārabhanti yat ||

yady asmāt sarvāḥ striya ādhīyamānān agnīn anvārabhantīty arthaḥ | āpastambo 'pi: "ādhāne hi satī karmabhiḥ saṃbadhyate" | bodhāyano 'pi: "ekaikām eva sannayet" iti | ato jyeṣṭhayā sahaivetarāsām adhikāro (?) na vinā jyeṣṭhayeti siddham | etad api jyeṣṭhāyām aduṣṭāyām | ata eva kātyāyanaḥ |

	jyeṣṭhāyāṃ doṣahīnāyāṃ kanīyasyā yad agnimān |

	brahmahatyā bhaved asya pratiparva hi sarvadā || iti |

doṣaduṣṭāyāṃ tu tāṃ prityajya anyayā saha dharmam ācared iti bhāvaḥ | tathā ca dakṣaḥ |

	dharmapatnī samākhyātā nirdoṣā yadi sā bhavet |

	doṣe sati na doṣaḥ syād anyā kāryā guṇānvitā || iti |

yat tu viṣṇunoktam,

	agnihotrādiyajñeṣu dvitīyā na sahācaret |

	anyathā niṣphalaṃ tasya sviṣṭaiḥ kratuśatair api ||

iti, tad asavarṇadvitīyāviṣayam | jyeṣṭhāyām aduṣṭāyāṃ kevalaṃ dvitīyāviṣayaṃ vā satv agniṣu yā pariṇītā tadviṣayaṃ vā | anyathā pūrvoktavacanavirodhaḥ syāt | yad api kātyāyanenoktam,

	prathamā dharmapatnī syād dvitīyā rativardhinī |

	dṛṣṭam eva phalaṃ tatra nādṛṣṭam upapadyate ||

iti, tad api vaiṣṇavena samānaviṣayam | nanv āhitāgneḥ punar udvāho niṣiddha eva | yad āha āpastambaḥ: "dharmaprajāsaṃpanne dāre nānyāṃ kurvīta | anyatarābhāve kāryā prāg agnyādheyāt" iti | maivam, yathā prāg agnyādheyāt tathordhvam api sati nimitte punar udvāhaḥ kārya iti tasyārthaḥ | ata eva kātyāyanaḥ |

	sadāro 'nyān punar dārān kathaṃcit kāraṇāntare |

	yadīcched agnimān kartuṃ kva homo 'sya vidhīyate ||

	agnāv eva bhaved dhomo laukike na kadācana |

	na hy āhitāgneḥ svaṃ karma laukike 'gnau vidhīyate ||

etat pūrvasyām anadhikāriṇyāṃ yāvad anyāvivāhaḥ tadviṣayam | ūrdhvaṃ vivāhād utsargeṣṭyāgnīn utsṛjyānyayā saha punar ādadhyād iti bhāvaḥ | nanu ca punaḥpariṇītāyām apy agnihotrādikāras tarhi kathaṃ dvitīyayā saha nācared ity asya tadviṣayatvam | ucyate, satyaṃ na tadviṣayatṃ brūmaḥ kiṃ tu yasyāḥ punar aprajastvādinā punar udvāhe 'pi doṣābhāvān nādhikākranāśas tadviṣayam iti brūmaḥ | ata eva smṛtyantaram |

	vyādhitāṃ strīprajāṃ vandhyām unmattāṃ vigatārtavām |

	aduṣṭāṃ labhate tyaktuṃ tīrthato na tu dharmataḥ || iti |

tīrthataḥ yonita ity arthaḥ | ato nātra punaḥ dvitīyayā sahādhānam agniparityāgakāraṇābhāvāt | evaṃ ca pūrvamāriṇīṃ bhāryām agnihotreṇa dāhayitvā yogyabhāryārahitaś cet punaḥ pariṇīya tayā bhāryayā sahādhānaṃ kuryāt, itaras tv ādhānamātram eveti mantavyam | yat tu kātyāyanenoktm,

	mṛtāyāṃ ceha bhāryāyāṃ dvitīyāyāṃ kathaṃcana |

	samutsṛjed agnihotraṃ mohito 'jñānacakṣuṣā |

	brahmojjhitaṃ vijānīyād yaś ca kāmāt samutsṛjaet || 

viṣṇur api |

	dvitīyāṃ caiva yo bhāryāṃ dahed vaitānikāgnibhiḥ |

	tiṣṭhantyāṃ prathāyāṃ tu surāpānasamaṃ hit tat || i

iti, tad ādhāne 'nanupraviṣṭadvitīyabhāryāviṣayam | anyathā "āhitāgnibhir dahanti" iti śrutir viruddhapramāṇaṃ syāt | nanv eṣā śrutir dvitīyetaraviṣayāpi ghaṭata eva | maivaṃ smṛtivaśāc chruteḥ saṅkhocasyāyuktatvāt | pratyuta smṛter viṣayāntarasaṃbhavena tatsaṃkoca eva yuktaḥ | yatra punar viṣayāntarāsaṃbhavas tatra tadvaśāt saṅkoco bhavaty eva | yathoktaṃ kātyāyanena |

	strī dharmacāriṇī sādhvī mṛtā dāhyā tadāgnibhiḥ |

	viparītā na dāhyā tu punar dārakriyā tathā ||

yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	dāhayitvāgnihotreṇa striyaṃ vṛttavatīṃ patiḥ |

vṛttavatīm ācāravatīm ity arthaḥ | atreyam agnivyavasthā: sarvādhāne tv ekabhāryasya pūrvaṃ bhāyāmaraṇe tatrāgnihotram utsṛjya punaḥ pariṇīya tayā sahādhānam | punar āharaṇāsāmarthye ātmārtham agnyādheyaṃ kuryāt, "dārakarmaṇi yady aśaktaḥ ātmārtham agnyādheyaṃ kurvīta | agnotraṃ darśapūrṇamāsau āgrayaṇaṃ ca śeṣāṇi karmāṇi na bhavanti" iti āpastambasmaraṇāt | bahvṛcabrāhmaṇam api: "tasmād apatnīko 'gnim āharet" iti | evaṃ ca yad uktam anyaiḥ: "patnyāṃ rajasvalāyām etad vacanam" iti, tad apy apāstam | yad vātra viṣṇūktaṃ draṣṭavyam |

	mṛtāyām api bhāryāyāṃ vaidikāgniṃ na hi tyajet |

	upādhināpi tat karma yāvajjīvaṃ samācaret | iti |

upādhiś cātra kuśamayī patnī |

	anye kuśamayīṃpatnīṃ kṛtvā tu gṛhamedhinaḥ |

	agnihotram upāsante yāvajjīvam atandritāḥ ||

anyatrāpi |

	rāmas tu kṛtvā sauvarṇīṃ sītāṃ patnīṃ yaśasvinīm |

	īje bahuvidhair yajñaiḥ saha bhrātṛbhir acyutaḥ ||

yat tu satyāṣāḍhenoktam: "na svāmitvasya bhāryāyāḥ putrasya deśasya kālasyāgner devatāyāḥ karmaṇaḥ śabdasya ca pratinidhir vidyate" iti, tan mānuṣādipatnīviṣayaṃ kuśādimayyāḥ patnyāḥ pratidhitvasya vācanikatvāt | ato yat kaiścid uktam "kuśādimayyāḥ patnyāḥ kāryakaratvāsaṃbhavena pratinidhitvāsaṃbhavāt, 'anye kuśamayīm' ity agnihotrastutyartham" iti tad apy apāstam | evaṃ vidhānād upari yajamānamaraṇe tasyāgitretāyāṃ pitṛmedhaḥ kāryaḥ | ādhāne 'py asāmarthye tasya pretādhānam eva | tad apy āpastambenoktam: "yady āhitāgnir utsṛṣṭāgnir vicchinnāgnir vidhurāgnir vā pramīyeta na tam anyena tretāgnibhyo dahanti tasya prācīnāvīty agnyāyatanāny uddhṛtyāvokṣya yajamānāyatane pretaṃ nidhāya gārhapatyāyatane araṇiṃ saṃnidhāya manthati — 'ye 'syāgnayo juhvato māṃsakāmāḥ saṃkalpayante yajamānamāṃsaṃ jānantu te 'smai haviṣe svāditāya svargalokam imaṃ pretaṃ nayantu' iti tūṣṇīṃ vihṛtya dvādaśagṛhītena srucaṃ pūrayitvā tūṣṇīṃ hutvā prete ''mātyā ity etadādi karma pratipadyate" iti | atraiva pūrvaṃ yajamānamaraṇe tasyāgnitretāyāṃ pitṛmedhaḥ | patnyās tu pretādhānam eva | sarvādhāne vānekabhāryasya pūrvaṃ jyeṣṭhāmaraṇe tatrāgnīn utsṛjya punar dvitīyayā sahādhānam | punas tanmaraṇe tatrāpy agnihotram utsṛjya patnyantarābhāve punaḥ pariṇīya tayā sahādhānādi | pariṇayanāsāmarthye tu ātmārtham agnyādhānādi pūrvavat | atraiva pūrvaṃ yajamānamaraṇe tasyāgnitretāyāṃ pitṛmedhaḥ patnyās tv aupāsane, "tayor yaḥ pūrvaḥ mriyeta yajamānaḥ patnī vā tasyāgnihotreṇāyaṃ pitṛmedhaḥ saṃpadyate yaḥ paścāt tasyaupasanena" ity āpastambasmaraṇāt | atraiva pūrvaṃ patnīmaraṇe tatrāgnihotram aupāsaṃ cotsṛjya punaḥ pariṇīya tayā sahādhānam, "athainam upoṣati" ity ārabhya "purastāt sabhyāvasathyābhyām aupāsanena ca" ity āpastambenaiva aupāsanasyāpi pratipattividhānāt | punas tanmaraṇe tatrāpy eṣa eva nyāyaḥ | punardārāharaṇāsāmarthye ātmārtham agnyādhānādi | tatrāpy asāmarthyaniścaye patnyās tretāyām eva pitṛmedhaḥ yajamānasya tv aupāsanena tasyāgnyantarābhāvāt, "yaḥ paścāt tasyāpāsanena"(?) iti smaraṇāc ca | 

	nanu cātrārdhādhānapakṣe 'pi "tayor yaḥ pūrvaḥ" iti smaraṇāt, agnitretāyām eva patnyāḥ pitṛmedhaḥ yajamānasyaupāsana evādhānādi kiṃ na syāt |

	maivam, "śavāgnayo vā ete patnyāṃ mṛtāyāṃ dhāryante" iti kāṭhakaśrutyā teṣāṃ pitṛmedhaikārthatvaśravaṇāt | ataḥ pūrvoktaiva jyāyasī | ardhādhāna evānekabhāryasya yasya pūrvaṃ maraṇaṃ tasyāgnitretāyām eva pitṛmedhaḥ patnīnāṃ tu svaiḥ svair aupāsanasyāgner amśaiḥ | tad uktaṃ kalpabhāṣye: "svaiḥ svair aupāsanasyāgner aṃśair vā syād upoṣaṇam" iti | atraiva pūrvaṃ patnīmaraṇe tatrāgihotram aupasanaṃ cotsṛjya punar dvitīyayā sahādhānādi | yadā tu yugapad eva jāyāpatyor maraṇaṃ tadā tayoḥ sahaiva pitṛmedhaḥ | tad uktam āpastambena: "sahaiva prete sahaiva pitṛmedhaḥ" iti | dvivacanaliṅgān mantrān saṃgamayati | anāhitāgnes tu aupāsanena pitṛmedhaḥ | tad api tenaivoktam: "aupāsanāgninānāhitāgniṃ dahanti nirmanthena patnīm uttapanenetarān" iti | itarān brahmacāriprabhṛtīn | ātmādisamārūḍheṣv agniṣu yajamānamaraṇe 'pi tenaivoktam: "yady ātmany araṇyor vā samārūḍheṣv agniṣu yajamāno mriyeta pūrvavad agnyāyatanāni kalpayitvā yajamānāyatane pretaṃ nidhāya gārhapatyāyatane laukikāgnim upasamādhāya pretasya dakṣiṇaṃ pāṇim upasaṃgṛhya tatputro bhrātānyo vā pratyāsannabudhuḥ 'upāvaroha jātaveda imaṃ taṃ svargāya lokāya naya prajānan | āyuḥ prajāṃ rayim asmāsu dhehi | pretāhutiṃ casya juṣasva' iti laukikāgnim upāvarohaty araṇyor vopāvarohya manthed araṇyoḥ samārūḍhasyānirvartyamāne 'pretam anvārambhe' ity etaṃ mantraṃ japet | viharaṇādi samānam" iti ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ homakāṇḍam**

**athādarśāvekṣaṇādi**

tatra dakṣaḥ |

	devakaryaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā guruṃ maṅgalavīkṣaṇam | iti |

maṅgalavīkṣaṇam ādarśādyavekṣaṇam | purāṇe 'pi |

	rocane candanaṃ hema mṛdaṅgaṃ darpaṇaṃ maṇim |

	gurūn agnīṃś ca sūryaṃ ca prātaḥ paśyet sadā budhaḥ || iti |

nārado 'pi |

	loke 'smin maṅgalāny aṣṭau brāhmaṇo gaur hutāśanaḥ |

	hiraṇyaṃ sarpir ādityaḥ āpo rājā tathāṣṭamaḥ ||

	etāni satataṃ paśyen namasyed arcayec ca yaḥ |

	pradakṣiṇaṃ ca kurvīta tathāsyāyur na hīyate ||

manur api |

	angicit kapilā satrī rājā bhikṣur mahodadhiḥ |

	dṛṣṭamātrāḥ punanty ete tasmāt paśyeta nityaśaḥ ||

kātyāyano 'pi |

	śrotriyaṃ subhagām agniṃ gām agnicitam eva ca |

	prātar utthāya yaḥ pasyed āpadbhiḥ sa pramucyate ||

	pāpiṣṭhaṃ durbhagām antyaṃ nagnam utkṛttanāsikām |

	prātar utthāya yaḥ paśyet tat kaler upalakṣaṇam ||

vāmapurāṇe 'pi |

	homaṃ ca kṛtvālabhanaṃ (?) śubhānāṃ tato bahir nirgamanaṃ praśastam |

	dūrvāṃ ca sarpir dadhi sodakumbham dhenuṃ savatsām ṛṣabhaṃ suvarṇam ||

	mṛd gomayaṃ svastikam akṣatāṃś ca tailaṃ madhu brāhmaṇakanyakāś ca |

	śvetāni puṣpāṇi tathā śamīṃ ca hutāśanaṃ candanam arkabimbam ||

	aśvatthavṛkṣaṃ ca samālabheta tataś ca kuryān nijajātidharmam |

brahmapurāṇe 'pi |

	svam ātmānaṃ ghṛte paśyed yadīcchec cirajīvitam |

bharadvājo 'pi |

	kaṇḍūyan pṛṣṭhato gāṃ tu kṛtvā cāśvatthavandanam |

	upagamya gurūn sarvān viprāṃś caivābhivādayet || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikayām ādarśāvekṣaṇādi**

**atha vedābhyāsaḥ**

tatra dakṣaḥ |

	dvitīye ca tathā bhāge vedābhyāso vidhīyate |

	vedasvīkaraṇaṃ pūrvaṃ vicāro 'bhyasanaṃ japaḥ ||

	taddānaṃ caiva śiṣyebhyo vedābhyāsso hi pañcadhā |

	samitpuṣpakuśādīnāṃ sa kālaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ||

aṣṭadhā vibhaktasyāhno dvitīyabhāge | kūrmapurāṇe 'pi |

	vedābhyāsaṃ tataḥ kuryāt prayatnāc chaktito dvijaḥ |

	japed adhyāpayec chiṣyān dhārayed vai vicārayet ||

	avekṣeta ca śāstrāṇi dharmādīni dvijottamaḥ || iti |

manur api |

	buddhivṛddhikarāṇy āśu darmyāṇi ca hitāni ca |

	nityaṃ śāstrāṇy avekṣeta nigamāṃś caiva vaidikān || iti |

yad atra vaktavyaṃ tat sarvaṃ saṃskārakāṇḍa evoktam | 

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ vedābhyāsaḥ**

**atha dhanārjanam**

tatra dakṣaḥ |

	tṛtīye ca tathā bhāge poṣyavargārthasādhanam | iti |

aṣṭadhā vibhaktasyāhnas tṛtīye bhāge | caturviṃśatāv api |

	poṣyavargārthasiddhyarthaṃ dhanam iccheta buddhimān | iti |

poṣyavargo 'pi dakṣeṇa darśitaḥ |

	mātā pitā gurur bhāryā prajā dīnāḥ samāśritāḥ |

	abhyāgato 'tithiś cāgniḥ poṣyavarga udāhṛtaḥ || iti |

etad api yathāvṛtti kāryam | tathā ca manuḥ |

	yātrāmātraprasiddhyarthaṃ svaiḥ karmabhir agarhitaiḥ |

	akleśena śarīrasya kurvīta dhanasaṃcayam || iti |

yātrā prāṇavṛttiḥ | svaiḥ karmabhiḥ yasya yāni vṛttyarthāni tair ity arthaḥ | tāny api tenaiva darśitāni |

	adhyāpanaṃ cādhyayanaṃ yajanaṃ yājanaṃ tathā |

	dānaṃ pratigrahaś caiva ṣaṭkarmāṇy agrajanmanaḥ || iti |

agrajanmā brāhmaṇaḥ | tatra trīṇi vṛttyarthāni | trīṇi dharmārthāni | yad āha sa eva |

	ṣaṇṇāṃ tu karmaṇām asya trīṇi karmāṇi jīvikā |

	yajanādhyāpane caiva viśiṣṭāc ca parigrahaḥ ||

anenādhyayanādīni trīṇy eva avaśyakartavyāni na yājanādīnity uktaṃ bhavati | uktaṃ ca gautamena: "dvijātīnām adhyayanam ijyā dānaṃ brāhmaṇasyādhikaḥ (?) pravacanayājanapratigrahāḥ pūrveṣv aniyamāḥ" iti | brāhmaṇagrahaṇaṃ kṣatriyavyudāsārtham | ata eva manuḥ |

	trayo dharmā nivartante brāhmaṇāt kṣatriyaṃ prati |

	adhyāpanaṃ yājanaṃ ca tṛtīyaś ca pratigrahaḥ ||

	vaiśyaṃ prati tathaiveti nivarterann iti sthitiḥ | iti |

evaṃ ca yad uktaṃ manunā,

	abrāhmaṇād adhyayan āpatkāle vidhīyate |

iti, tad avṛttyarthādhyāpanābhiprāyam | anyathā pūrvoktavacanavirodhāt | kāni tarhy anayor vṛttyarthānīty apekṣite manur āha |

	śastrāstrabhṛttvaṃ kṣatrasya vaṇikpaśukṛṣir viśaḥ |

	ājīvanārthaṃ dharmas tu dānam adhyayanaṃ yajiḥ || iti |

śastrāstrabhṛttvaṃ prajāpālanadvāreṇa jīvanārtham | vaṇikchabdena tatkarma vāṇijyaṃ lakṣyate | paśuśabdena tatpālanam | ata eva yājñavalkyaḥ |

	pradhānaṃ kṣatriye karma prajānāṃ paripālanam |

	kusīdakṛṣivāṇijyapāśupālyaṃ viśaḥ smṛtam || iti |

pradhānaṃ mukhyaṃ yato dharmārthaṃ vṛttyarthaṃ ca,

	kṣatriyasya paro dharmaḥ prajānāṃ paripālanam|

iti manusmaraṇāt | kusīdaṃ vṛddhyarthaṃ dhanaprayogaḥ | lābhārthaṃ krayavikrayau vāṇijyam | pāśupālyaṃ paśurakṣaṇam | atra viśeṣam āhatuḥ śaṅkhalikhitau: "gā rakṣeta tāsv apītāsu na piben na tiṣṭhantīṣūpaviśen na svayam utthāpayec chanair ārdraśākhayā pṛṣṭhato hanyān nātīrthena viṣamenālpodakenāvatārayed bālavṛddharogārthaśrāntā upāsīta śaktitaḥ pratīkāraṃ kuryād gavām eṣa dharmo 'nyathā viplavaḥ" iti | atra vṛttyantarṇy āha manuḥ |

	sapta vittāgamā dharmyā dāyo lābhaḥ krayo jayaḥ |

	proyogaḥ karmayogaś ca satpratigraha eva ca ||

dāyo 'nvayāgataṃ dhanam | lābho nidheḥ, "nidhiṃ brāhmaṇo labdhvā sarvam ādadyāt | kṣatriyaś caturtham aṃśaṃ rājñe datvā caturtham aṃśaṃ brāhamaṇebhyo dadyāt | svayam ardham ādadyāt | vaiśyaś caturtham aṃśaṃ rājñe datvā svayaṃ caturtham aṃśaṃ gṛhītvā brāhmaṇebhyo 'rdhaṃ dadyāt | śūdraś cāvāptaṃ dvādaśadhā vibhajya pañcāṃśān brāhmaṇebhyo rājñe pañcāṃśān svayam aṃśadvayam ādadyāt" iti viṣṇusmaraṇāt | krayaḥ prasiddhaḥ | ete trayaś caturṇām api varṇānāṃ dharmyāḥ | jayo yuddhena kṣatriyasyaiva | prayogo vṛddhyarthaṃ dhanaprayogaḥ | karmayogaḥ kṛṣivāṇijyam | ete vaiśyasyaiva | satpratigraho brāhmaṇasyaiveti |

	ṛtām ṛtābhyāṃ jīvet tu mṛtena pramṛtena vā |

	satyānṛtābhyām api vā na śvavṛttyā kadācana ||

	ṛtam uñchaśilaṃ jñeyam amṛtaṃ syād ayācitam |

	mṛtaṃ tu yācitaṃ bhaikṣaṃ pramṛtaṃ karpaṇaṃ smṛtam |

	satyānṛtaṃ ca vāṇijyaṃ tena caivāpi jīvyate |

	sevā śvavṛttir ākhyātā tasmāt tāṃ parivarjayet || iti |

patitaparityaktaikaikakaṇopādānam uñchaḥ | śālyāder nipatitaparityaktavallarīgrahaṇaṃ śilam | yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	kusūlakumbhidhānyo vā tryāhiko 'śvastano 'pi vā |

	jīved vāpi śiloñchena śreyān eṣāṃ paraḥ paraḥ || iti |

kusūlaṃ koṣṭhakam | tatparimitadhānyasaṃcitā kusūladhānyaḥ | sa vā syāt | kumbhidhānyaḥ kumbhaparimitadhānyasaṃcetā | sa vā syāt,

	kusūladhānyako vā syāt kumbhīdhānyaka eva vā |

iti manusmaraṇāt | tryahaparyāptadhanasaṃcetā tryāhikaḥ sa vā syāt | na svastanasaṃcayam asyāstīty aśvastanaḥ | sadyaḥ prakṣālaka ity arthaḥ | sa vā syād iti | teṣāṃ aśvastanāntānāṃ vṛttayo manunoktā veditavyāḥ | 

	ṣaṭkarmaiko bhavaty eṣāṃ tribhir anyaḥ pravartate |

	dvābhyām ekaś caturthas tu brahmasūtreṇa jīvati || iti |

asyārthaḥ: ekaḥ kusūladhānyo yajanādiṣaṭkarmā bhavet | anyo dvitīyaḥ tribhir yājanādhyāpanapratigrahair vartate | ekas tṛtīyaḥ dvābhyāṃ pratigrahetarābhyām | caturthas tu brahmasūtreṇādhyāpaneneti | ete ca kusūladhānyatvādayo brāhmaṇasyaiva, itarasya pratigrahāder asaṃbhavāt | śiloñche tu varṇatrayasādhāraṇe | tathā ca āpastambaḥ: "svakarma brāhmaṇasyādhyayanam adhyāpanaṃ yajño yājanaṃ dānaṃ pratigrahaṇaṃ dāyādyaṃ śiloñchaḥ | anyac cāparigṛhītam | etāny eva kṣatriyasyādhyāpanayājanapratigrahaṇānīti parihāpya daṇḍayuddhādhikāni | kṣatriyavaiśyasya daṇḍayuddhavarjaṃ kṛṣigorakṣyavāṇijyādhikam" iti | parāśaras tu kalāv aviśeṣeṇa caturṇām api kṛṣyanugraham āha |

	ataḥ paraṃ gṛhasthasya karmācāraṃ kalau yuge |

	dharmaṃ sādhāraṇaṃ śaktyā cāturvarṇyāśramāgatam ||

	taṃ pravakṣyāmy ahaṃ pūrvaṃ parāśaravaco yathā |

	ṣaṭkarmasahito vipraḥ kṛṣikarma ca kārayet ||

	svayaṃ kṛṣṭe tathā kṣetre dhānyaiś ca svayam ārjitaiḥ |

	nirvapet pañcayajñāṃś ca kratudīkṣāṃ ca kārayet ||

	kṣatriyo 'pi kṛṣiṃ kṛtvā devān viprāṃś ca pūjayet |

	vaiśyaḥ śūdras tathā kuryāt kṛṣivāṇijyaśilpakam ||

	caturṇām api varṇānām eṣa dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ ||

atra viśeṣam āha hārītaḥ |

	na parvasu saṃdhivekayor vāhayet |

	aṣṭagavaṃ dharmyahalaṃ ṣaḍgavaṃ jīvitārthinām |

	caturgavaṃ nṛśaṃsānāṃ dvigavaṃ brahmaghātinām ||

	bālānāṃ damanaṃ caiva vāhanaṃ ca na śasyate |

	vṛddhānāṃ durbalānāṃ ca prajāpativaco yathā ||

parāśaro 'pi |

	kṣudhitaṃ tūṣitaṃ śrāntaṃ balīvardaṃ na yojayet |

	hīnāṅgaṃ vyathitaṃ klībaṃ vṛṣaṃ vipro na vāhayet ||

	vāhayed divasasyārdhaṃ paścāt snānaṃ samācaret |

sānam atra balīvardānām | ata eva hārītaḥ |

	snāpayitvānaḍuho 'laṃkṛtya brāhmaṇān bhojayet | iti |

atra kūrmapurāṇam |

	labdhalābhaḥ pitṝn devān brāhmaṇāṃś cāpi pūjayet |

	te tṛptās tasya tad doṣaṃ śamayanti na saṃśayaḥ ||

	devebhyaś ca pitṛbhyaś ca dadyād bhāgaṃ tu viṃśakam |

	triṃśadbhāgaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ kṛṣiṃ kurvan na duṣyati ||

bṛhaspatir api |

	rājño dadyāt tu ṣaḍbhāgaṃ devatānāṃ ca viṃśakam |

	triṃśadbhāgaṃ tu viprāṇāṃ kṛṣiṃ kurvan na duṣyati ||

hārīto 'pi |

	yūpo 'yaṃ nihito madhye medhinām iha karṣakaiḥ |

	tasmād atandrito dadyād atra dhānyārthadakṣiṇāḥ||

	bhūmiṃ bhitvauṣadhīś chitvā hatvā kīṭapipīlikāḥ |

	punanti khalayajñena karṣakā nātra saṃśayaḥ ||

ata eva tasyākaraṇe doṣaḥ parāśareṇa darśitaḥ |

	yo na dadyā dvijātibhyo rāśimulam upāgate |

	sa coraḥ sa ca pāpiṣṭhaḥ brahmaghanaṃ taṃ vinirdiśet ||

purāṇe śaṅkaro 'pi |

	adatvā karṣako devi yas tu dhānyaṃ praveśayet |

	tasya tṛṣṇābhibhūtasya yat pāpaṃ tad bravīmy aham ||

	divyaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu durātmā kṛṣikārakaḥ |

	marudeśe bhaved vṛkṣaḥ sa puṣpaphalavarjitaḥ ||

	tasyānte mānuṣo bhūtvā kadācit kalaparyayāt |

	daridro vyādhito mūrkhaḥ kulahīnaś ca jāyate ||

kūrmapurāṇe tu gṛhasthabhedena vṛttivyavasthā darśitā |

	dvividhas tu gṛhī jñeyaḥ sādhakaś cāpy asādhakaḥ |

	adhyāpanaṃ yājanaṃ ca pūrvasyāhuḥ pratigraham ||

	śiloñchenāpy upādadyād gṛhasthaḥ sādhakaḥ punaḥ |

	asādhakas tu yaḥ prokto gṛhasthāśramasaṃsthitaḥ ||

	śiloñche tasya kathite dve vṛttī paramarṣibhiḥ |

	amṛtenātha vā jīven mṛtenāpy atha vā yadi ||

	ayācitaṃ syād amṛtaṃ mṛtaṃ bhakṣaṃ tu yācitam || iti |

śūdravṛttayas tu uśanasā darśitāḥ |

	śūdrasya dvijaśuśrūṣā sarvaśilpāni vāpy atha |

	vikrayaḥ sarvapaṇyānāṃ śūdrakarma udāhṛtaḥ || iti |

śilpāni vicitrakarmāṇi | vipraśuśrūṣā dharmārthā,

	viprasevaiva śūdrasya viśiṣṭaṃ karma kīrtyate |

iti manusmaraṇāt | viśiṣṭam utkṛṣṭam, tasya dharmavṛttihetutvāt | sarvalilpānīty āpadviṣayam | yad āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	śūdrasya dvijaśuśrūṣā tayā jīvan vaṇig bhavet |

	śilpair vā vividhair jīved dvijātihitam ācaret ||

yaiḥ śilpair dvijātayaḥ śuśrūṣyante tair ity arthaḥ | tathā ca manuḥ |

	yaiḥ karmabhiḥ pracaritaiḥ śusrūṣyante dvijātayaḥ |

	tāni kārukakarmāṇi śilpāni vividhāni ca ||

tāni ca devalena darśitāni: "śūdradharmo dvijātiśuśrūṣā pāpavarjanaṃ kalatrādipoṣaṇaṃ karṣaṇaṃ paśupālanaṃ bhārodvahanapaṇyāpaṇyavyavahāracitrakarmanṛttagītaveṇuvīṇāmuraja-mṛdaṅgavadanāni" iti | tasya cocchiṣṭādi deyam | tathā ca manuḥ |

	ucchiṣṭam annaṃ dātavyaṃ jīrṇāni vasanāni ca |

	pulakāś caiva dhānyānāṃ jīrnāś caiva paricchadāḥ ||

asamyak kṛṣṭāḥ pulakāḥ | paricchadā upānatprabhṛtayaḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ dhanārjanam**

**pratigrahādinirūpaṇam**

uktaṃ brāhmaṇasy pratigrahādiṣu sāmānyenādhikāra iti | adhujā viśeṣato 'dhikāro nirūpyate | tatra yājñavalkyaḥ |

	rājāntevāsiyājyebhyaḥ sīdann icched dhanaṃ kṣudhā| iti |

kṣudhā sīdan pīḍyamātno rājapratigrahādiṣv adhikriyata ity arthaḥ | manur api |

	rājato dhanam anvicchet saṃsīdan snātakaḥ kṣudhā |

	yājyāntevāsinor vāpi na tv anyata iti sthitiḥ ||

etac ca sati saṃbhave anyato dhanagrahaṇaniṣedhaparaṃ na punar atyantaniṣedhāya,

	sarvataḥ pratigṛhṇīyād brāhmaṇas tv anayaṃ gataḥ |

iti tenaivoktatvāt | ata eva nārado 'pi rājādipratigraha eva śreyān ity āha |

	śreyān pratigraho rājñāṃ nānyeṣāṃ brāhmaṇād ṛte |

	brāhmaṇaś caiva rājā ca dvāv apy etau dhṛtavratau ||

	naitayor antaraṃ kiṃcit prajādharmābhirakṣaṇāt |

	śucīnām aśucīnāṃ ca saṃnipāto yathāmbhasām |

	samudre samatāṃ yāti tadvad rājñāṃ dhanāgamaḥ ||

	yathāgnau saṃsthitaṃ caiva śuddhim eti hi kāñcanam |

	evaṃ dhanāgamāḥ sarve śuddhim āyānti rājani || iti |

atra sati vibhave rājādibhyo dhanaṃ lipsed iti bhavaḥ | ata eva manuḥ |

	na sīdet snātako vipraḥ kṣudhā saktaḥ kathaṃcana |

	na jīrṇamalavadvāsā bhavec ca vibhave sati ||

kṣudhā na sīded ity anena asatyāṃ kṣudhi na pratigrahādi kāryam ity uktaṃ bhavati |

	vidyamāne dhane yas tu pratigraharucir dvijaḥ |

	narakaṃ rauravaṃ prāpya tataiva paripacyate ||

yamo 'pi |

	yas tu yācaniko martyo na sa svargasy bhājanam |

	udvejayati bhūtāni yathā coras tathaiva saḥ ||

	saktāḥ pratigrahe ye tu na tu dāne kadācana |

	teṣāṃ vaivasvataḥ prāha na tūrdhagamanaṃ kvacit || iti |

śātātapo 'pi |

	vedākṣarāṇi yāvanti niyuñjītārthakāraṇāt |

	tāvanti bhrūṇahatyā vai vedavikrayy avāpnuyāt ||

dhanārthaṃ vedākṣarāṇāṃ viniyogo vedavikrayaḥ | tadvā vedavikrayī | sa bhrūṇahatyām avāpnotīty arthaḥ | vedavikrayaś chāgalena ṣaḍvidho darśitaḥ |

	prakhyāpanaṃ pralapanaṃ praśnapūrvapratigrahaḥ |

	yājanādhyāpane vādaḥ ṣaḍvidho vedavikrayaḥ || iti |

evaṃ praśnapūrvadāne 'pi doṣo draṣṭavyaḥ | tad āha śātātapaḥ |

	praśnapūrvaṃ tu yo dadyād brāhmaṇāya pratigraham |

	sa pūrvaṃ narakaṃ yāti brāhmaṇas tadanantaram ||

nanu yadi sadhanasyaiva pratigrahaniṣedhas tarhi nirdhanasya prāguktadoṣābhāvaḥ syāt | satyaṃ kiṃ tu tatrāpy asti vyāsokadoṣaḥ |

	pratigraharucir na syād vṛttyarthaṃ tu samācaret |

	vṛttyarthād adhikaṃ gṛhṇan brāhmaṇo yāty adhogatim ||

	vṛttisaṅkocam anvicchen neheta dhanasaṃcayam |

	dhanalābhe pravṛttas tu brāhmaṇyād eva hīyate ||

vṛttir vartanam | manur api |

	saṃtoṣaṃ param āsthāya sukhārthī saṃyato bhavet |

	saṃtoṣamūlaṃ hi sukhaṃ duḥkhamūlaṃ viparyayaḥ ||

saṃyataḥ pratyāhṛtendriyaḥ | vyāso 'pi |

	saṃtuṣṭaḥ ko na śaknoti phalair mūlaiś ca vartitum |

	sarvas tv indriyalaulyena saṅkaṭāny avagāhate ||

	daridro 'rthaṃ tato rājyaṃ tathendratvaṃ tato 'kṣayam |

	padaṃ vāñchati nānto 'sti tastāt tṛṣṇāṃ parityajet || iti |

tato dharmasaṃcaya evāvaśyako na dhanasaṃcaya ity abhiprāyaḥ | tathā ca manuḥ |

	nāmutra hi sahāyārthaṃ pitā mātā ca tiṣṭhataḥ |

	na putradādā na jñātiḥ dharmas tiṣṭhati kevalaḥ ||

	ekaḥ prajāyate jantur eka eva pralīyate |

	eko 'nubhuṅkte sukṛtam eka eva ca duṣkṛtam ||

	mṛtaṃ śarīram utsṛjya kāṣṭhaloṣṭasamaṃ kṣitau |

	vimukhā bāndhavā yānti dharmas tam anugacchati ||

	tasmād dharmaṃ sahāyārthaṃ nityaṃ dharmas tam anugacchati || iti |

evaṃ cāsati dhane rājādibhyaḥ sthitimātraparyāptaṃ dhanaṃ gṛhṇīyād anyathā neti siddham | yat tu yamenoktam,

	rājakilbiṣadagdhānāṃ viprāṇām akṛtātmanām |

	svinnānām (?) iva bījānāṃ punar janma na vidyate || 

iti, yad api hārītena,

	daśasūnāsahasrāṇi ahnā rājā karoti vai |

	tāny eva kurute rātrau ghoras tasya pratigrahaḥ || iti |

yad api caturviṃśatau,

	rājapratigraho ghoro madhvāsvādo viṣopamaḥ |

	putramāṃsaṃ varaṃ bhoktuṃ na tu rājapratigrahaḥ || iti |

tad ucchāstravartirājapratigrahaviṣayam | ata eva manuḥ |

	yo rājñaḥ pratigṛhṇāti lubdhasyocchāstravartinaḥ |

	sa paryāyeṇa yātīmān narakān ekaviṃśatim ||

	tāmisram andhatāmisraṃ mahārauravarauravau |

	narakaṃ kālasūtraṃ ca mahānarakam eva ca ||

	saṃjīvanaṃ mahāvīciṃ tapanaṃ saṃpratāpanam |

	sahātaṃ ca sakākolaṃ kuḍmalaṃ pratimūrtikam ||

	lohaśaṅkum ṛjīṣaṃ ca panthānaṃ śālmalīṃ nadīm |

	asipatravanaṃ caiva lohadārakam eva ca ||

	etad vidanto vidvāṃso brāhmaṇā brahmavādinaḥ |

	na rājñaḥ pratigṛhṇanti pretya śreyo 'bhikāṅkṣiṇaḥ || iti |

yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	na rājñaḥ pratigṛhṇīyāl lubdhasyocchāstravartinaḥ |

	pratigrahe sūnicakridhvajiveśyānarādhipāḥ ||

	duṣṭā daśaguṇaṃ pūrvāt pūrvād ete yathākramam |

sūnī hiṃsakaḥ | cakrī tailikaḥ | dvajī madyavikretā | yamo pi |

	arājanyaprasūtasya rājñaḥ svacchandavartinaḥ |

	ghoraḥ pratigrahas tasya madhvāsvādo viṣopamaḥ ||

	tathaiva rājamahiṣī rājāmātyāḥ purohitāḥ |

	pāpenārthena saṃyuktāḥ sarve te rājadharmiṇaḥ || iti |

arajanaprasūtaḥ akṣatriyaprasūtaḥ | tathā patitayājane 'pi doṣam āha hārītaḥ: "patitayājanāt patitasaṃkariyājanāt saṃkaritvam upaiti | saṃkīrṇayājanāt saṃkaraiḥ saṃkīryate | śūdrayājanāj jātataś cyavate" iti |

	yājanaṃ yonisaṃbandhaṃ svādhyāyaṃ sahabhojanam |

	kṛtvā sadyaḥ pataty eva patitena na saṃśayaḥ || iti |

patitapratigrahe tu śuddhau viśeṣam āha uśanā |

	patitād dravyam ādāya bhuṅkte vā brāhmaṇo yadi |

	kṛtvā tasya samutsargaṃ hy atikṛcchraṃ cared dvijaḥ || iti |

evaṃ śūdrayājane 'pi draṣṭavyam | tathā ca sumantuḥ: "śūdrayājakaḥ sarvadravyaparityāgāt pūto bhavati" iti | parityāge viśeṣam āha hārītaḥ: "śūdrayājako garhitaṃ dravyaṃ nāgahrade prakṣipya brāhmaṇān upetya brūyāt trāyantu māṃ bhavanto varṇasāmyam" iti | nāgahrado 'akṣobhyahradaḥ | atra manuḥ |

	āhṛtābhyudyatāṃ bhikṣāṃ purastād apracoditām |

	mene prajāpatir grāhyām api duṣkṛtakarmaṇaḥ || iti |

āhṛtāṃ saṃpradānadeśam ānītāṃ deyatvenodyatāṃ saṃkalpitāṃ purastād apracoditāṃ pūrvaṃ "tubhyaṃ dadāmi" ity akathitāṃ bhikṣāṃ prajāpatir grāhyāṃ manyata ity arthaḥ | tathā ca āpastambaḥ |

	udyatām āhṛtāṃ bhikṣāṃ purastād apraveditām |

	bhojyāṃ mene prajāpatir api duṣkṛtakāriṇaḥ || iti |

bhikṣāgrahaṇam anyeṣāṃ śayyādīnām upalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva manuḥ |

	śayyāṃ gṛhaṃ kuśān gandhān apaḥ puṣpaṃ maṇin dadhi |

	dhānāmatsyān payo māṃsaṃ śākaṃ caiva na nirnudet ||

yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	kuśāḥ śākaṃ payo matsyā gandhāḥ puṣpaṃ dadhi kṣitiḥ |

	māṃsaṃ śayyāsanā dhānāḥ pratyākhyeyaṃ na vāri ca ||

gautamo 'pi: "edhodakayavasamūlaphalamadhvabhayābhyudyataśayyāsanāvasathayānapayo-dadhidānāśapharipriyaṅgusraṅmārgaśākāny apraṇodyāni sarveṣām" iti | śapharyaḥ sūkṣmamatsyāḥ | apraṇodyāny aprtyākhyeyāni | tatra hetum āha bharadvājaḥ |

	ayācitopapanne hi nāsti doṣaḥ pratigrahe |

	amṛtaṃ tad vidur devās tasmāt tan naiva nirnudet || iti |

pratyākhyāne 'pi doṣam āha manuḥ |

	na tasya pitaro 'śnanti daśavarṣāṇi pañca ca |

	na ca havyaṃ vahaty agniḥ yas tām abhyavamanyate || iti |

atra yamokto viśeṣaḥ |

	rakṣasāṃ gacchate yoniṃ yas tām abhyavamanyate |

iti etad apy anāpatprakaraṇāt patitādivarjaṃ veditavyam | ata eva yājñavalkyaḥ |

	ayācitāhṛtaṃ grāhyam api duṣkṛtakarmaṇaḥ |

	anyatra kulaṭāṣaṇḍapatitebhyas tathā dviṣaḥ || iti |

kulāt kulam aṭatīti kulaṭā svairiṇī | yamo 'pi |

	cikitsakasya mṛgayor veśyāyāḥ kitavasya ca |

	ṣaṇḍasūtikayor eva udyatāṃ parivarjayet ||

mṛgayuḥ vyādhaḥ | kitavo dyūtakṛt | sūniko hiṃsraḥ | hārīto 'pi |

	cikitsakakṛtaghnānāṃ śalyakartuś ca vārdhuṣeḥ |

	ṣaṇḍasya kulaṭāyāś ca udyatām api varjayet ||

vārdhuṣet lakṣaṇaṃ vasiṣṭhenoktam |

	samarghaṃ dhanam āhṛtya mahārghaṃ yaḥ prayacchati |

	sa vai vārdhuṣiko nāma brahmavādiṣu garhitaḥ ||

yasya punar uktapraśastapratigrahādyasaṃbhavo viśuddhatvena vaiśyādivṛttyanāśrayaṇaṃ ca tasya garhitapratigrahādy api na doṣāyety āha manuḥ |

	vaiśyavṛttim anātiṣṭhan brāhmaṇaḥ sve pathi sthitaḥ |

	avṛttikarśitaḥ sīdann imaṃ dharmaṃ samācaret ||

avṛttikarśito vṛttyabhāvapīḍitaḥ | imaṃ vakṣyamāṇam ity arthaḥ |

	nādhyāpanād yājanād vā garhitād vā pratigrahāt |

	doṣo bhavati viprāṇāṃ jvalanāmbusamā hi te ||

	pavitraṃ duṣyatīty etad dharmato nopapadyate |

	jīvitātyayam āpanno yo 'nnam atti yatas tataḥ ||

	sarvataḥ pratigṛhṇīyād brāhmaṇas tv anayaṃ gataḥ |

	ākāśam iva pāpena na sa pāpena lipyate ||

yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	āpadgataḥ saṃpragṛhṇan bhuñjāno vā yatas tataḥ |

	na lipyetainasā vipro jvalanārkasamo hi saḥ ||

bṛhaspatir api |

	vṛddhau ca mātāpitarau sādhvī bhāryā sutaḥ śiśuḥ |

	apy akāryaśataṃ kṛtvā bhartavyā manur abravīt ||

atra purāvṛttam āha manuḥ |

	ajīgartaḥ sutaṃ hantum upāsarpad bubhukṣitaḥ |

	na cālipyata pāpena kṣutpratīkāram ācaran ||

	śvamāṃsam icchann ārto 'ttuṃ dharmādharmavicakṣaṇaḥ |

	prāṇānāṃ parirakṣārthaṃ vāmadevo na liptavān ||

	bharadvājaḥ kṣudhārtas tu saputro vijane vane |

	bahvīr gāḥ pratijagrāha pṛthos takṣno mahātapāḥ ||

	kṣudhārtaś cāttum abhyāgād viśvāmitraḥ śvajāghanīm |

	caṇḍālahastād ādāya dharmādharmavicakṣaṇaḥ ||

śvajāghanīṃ śvapuccham | ato mukhyavṛttiyasaṃbhave paravṛttyāśrayaṇād viguṇāpi svakīyaiva vṛttir jyāyasīti mantavyam | uktaṃ ca manunā |

	varaṃ svadharmo viguṇo na pārakyaḥ svanuṣṭhitaḥ |

	paradharmeṇa jīvan hi sadyaḥ patati jātitaḥ ||

anenaivābhiprāyeṇa vyāso 'pi |

	dvujātibhyo dhanaṃ lipset praśastebhyo dvijottamaḥ |

	api vā jātimātrebhyo na tu śūdrāt kathaṃcana || iti |

yadā tu garhitadvijātipratigrahādy api na saṃbhavati tadā śūdrād api pratigṛhṇīyād ity uktaṃ bhavati | uktaṃ caturviṃsatau |

	sīdaṃś cet pratigṛhṇīyād brāhmaṇebhyas tato nṛpāt |

	tatas tu vaiśyaśūdrebhyaḥ śaṅkhasya vacanaṃ yathā || iti |

śūdrapratigrahe tu viśeṣam āha aṅgirāḥ |

	yat tu rāśīkṛtaṃ dhānyaṃ khale kṣetre 'tha vā bhavet |

	śūdrād api grahītavyam ity āṅgirasabhāṣitam ||

yadā tu śūdrād api pratigrahāsaṃbhavaḥ kṣatriyādivṛttyasaṃbhavaś ca tadā stainyaṃ vihitam ity āha vyāsaḥ |

	āpatsu vihitaṃ stainyaṃ viśiṣṭasamahīnataḥ |

	hīnād ādeyam ādau syāt samād vā tad anantaram ||

	asaṃbhave tv ādadīta viśiṣṭād api dhārmikāt | iti |

atra kālaniyamam āha manuḥ |

	tathaiva saptame bhakte bhaktāni ṣaḍanaśnatā |

	aśvastanavidhānena hartavyaṃ hīnakarmaṇaḥ ||

	khalāt kṣetrād agārād vā yato vāpy upalabhyate |

	ākhyātavyaṃ tu tat tasmai pṛcchate yadi pṛcchati ||

	brāhmaṇasvaṃ na hartavyaṃ kṣatriyeṇa kadācana |

	dasyuniṣkriyayos tu svam ajīvan hartum arhati || iti |

saptame bhakte caturthe 'hni prātaḥkāle | hīnakarmaṇa abrāhmaṇād ity arthaḥ | ata eva yājñavalkyaḥ |

	bubhukṣitas tryahaṃ sthitvā dhānyam abrāhmaṇād dharet |

atra manuḥ |

	vānaspatyaṃ mūlaphalaṃ dārvagnyarthaṃ tathaiva ca |

	tṛṇaṃ ca gobhyo grāsārtham asteyaṃ manur abravīt || iti |

yamo 'pi |

	tṛṇaṃ kāṣṭhaṃ phalaṃ mūlaṃ prakāśaṃ vai hared dvijaḥ |

	gobrāhmaṇārthe gṛhṇan vai na sa pāpena lipyate || iti |

nārado 'pi |

	śālivrīhitilānāṃ tu muṣṭir grāhyā vidhīyate |

	yavagodhūmayor vāpi yadi vā mudgamāṣayoḥ ||

	eteṣāṃ mānavair muṣṭir grahītavyāpadi sthitaiḥ |

	śākaṃ śākapramāṇena gṛhyamāṇaṃ na duṣyati ||

	grahītavyāni puṣpāṇi devatārcanakāraṇāt |

	adattadāyinaṃ vidyād yady abhyadhikam icchati ||

āpadi sthitair adhikam ity arthaḥ, "tilamudgamāṣayavagodhūmādīnāṃ sasyamuṣṭigrahaṇeṣu na doṣaḥ pathikānām" iti smaraṇāt | yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	dvijaḥ spṛtau (?) tu puṣpāṇi sarvataḥ svavad āharet |

svavat aviśaṅkam ity arthaḥ | etat sarvam āpadi parigrahaviṣayam | anyathāsteyam ityāder avivakṣitārthatvaprasaṅgāt | anāpadi tu gautamenoktam: "go'gnyarthe tṛṇamedhān vīrudvanaspatīnāṃ ca puṣpāṇi svavad ādadīta phalāni cāparivṛtānām" iti | svavat yathā teṣāṃ pīḍā na bhavati tathāhartavyam ity arthaḥ,

	patraṃ puṣpaṃ pracinvāno mūlacchedaṃ tu varjayet |

	mālākāra ivārāme na yathāṅgārakārakaḥ ||

iti vyāsasmaraṇāt | aparivṛtānām adattavṛttīnām aparirakṣitānām iti yāvat | ata eva parigṛhīte daṇḍam āha manuḥ |

	tṛṇaṃ vā yadi vā kāṣṭhaṃ puṣpaṃ vā yadi vā phalam |

	anāpṛṣṭas tu gṛhṇāno hastacchedanam arhati ||

atra yājñavalkyaḥ |

	vidyātapobhyāṃ hīnena naiva grāhyaḥ pratigrahaḥ |

	gṛhṇan pradātāram adho nayaty ātmānam eva ca ||

	[āmapātre yathā nyastaṃ kṣīraṃ dadhi ghṛtaṃ madhu |

	naśyeyuḥ pātradaurbalyāt te rasās tac ca bhājanam ||

	evaṃ hiraṇyaṃ gām aśvaṃ vastraṃ chatraṃ tilādikam |

	apṛṣṭvā pratigṛhṇāno bhasmībhavati kāṣṭhavat || ] iti |

evaṃ ca vidyāvato 'rthasyaiva pragrahadhikāro nānyasyeti siddham | yaḥ punaruktapratigrahādhikāre saty api na pratigṛhṇāti tasya phalam āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	pratigrahasamartho 'pi nādatte yaḥ pratigraham |

	ye lokā dānaśīlānāṃ tān sa prāpnoti puṣkalān ||

yamo 'pi |

	pratigrahasamarthasya nivṛttasya pratigrahāt |

	ya eva dadato dharmasya evāpratigṛhṇataḥ ||

	sarvavedādhigamanāt sarvadevaniṣevaṇāt |

	gavāṃ koṭipradānāc ca śreyāṃs tasyāparigrahaḥ || 

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ pratigrahādinirūpaṇam**

**athāpadvṛttayaḥ**

atra manuḥ:

	ajīvaṃs tu yathoktena brāhamaṇḥ svena karmaṇā |

	jīvet kṣatriyadharmeṇa sa hy asya pratyantaraḥ ||

	ubhābhyām apy ajīvaṃs tu kathaṃ syād iti ced bhavet |

	kṛṣigorakṣyam āsthāya jīved vaiśyasaya jīvikām ||

pratyanantaraḥ saṃnikṛṣṭaḥ | ubhābhyāṃ brāhmaṇakṣatriyavṛttibhyām apy ajīvan vaiśyavṛttikām āsthāya jīven na śūdrasyety arthaḥ | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	ajīvan karmaṇā svena vipraḥ kṣatraṃ samāśrayet |

	vaiśyakarmātha vā kuryād vārpalaṃ (?) parivarjayet ||

vṛṣalaḥ śūdraḥ | vaiśyakarmaṇi viśeṣam āha gautamaḥ: "kṛṣivāṇijye cāsvayaṃkṛte kusīdaṃ ca" iti | kusīdaṃ vṛddhyarthaṃ dhanaprayogaḥ | kūrmapurāṇe 'pi |

	kusīdakṛṣivāṇijyaṃ prakurvītāsvayaṃkṛtam |

	kṛṣet abhāve vāṇijyaṃ tadabhāve kusīdakam || iti |

yat punar manunoktam,

	vaiśyavṛttyāpi jīvaṃs tu brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo 'pi vā |

	hiṃsāprāyāṃ parādhīnāṃ kṛṣiṃ yatnena varjayet ||

	kṛṣiṃ sādv iti manyante sā vṛttiḥ sadvigarhitā |

	bhūmiṃ bhūmiśayāṃś caiva hanti kāṣṭham ayomukham ||

iti, tat svayaṃkṛtābhiprāyam, anyathā pūrvoktavacanavirodhāt parādhīnām balīvardāyattām | parakṛtakṛṣyādyasaṃbhave tu svayaṃ kṛtam api kṛṣyādi bhavaty eva | yathoktaṃ bṛhaspatinā |

	kusīdakṛṣivāṇijyaṃ prakurvīta svayaṃ kṛtam |

	āpatkāle svayaṃ kuryān nainasā yujyate dvijaḥ || iti |

kūrmapurāṇe 'pi |

	svayaṃ vā karṣaṇaṃ kuryād vāṇijyaṃ vā kusīdakam |

	kaṣṭā pāpīsasī vṛttiḥ kusīdaṃ tāṃ vivarjayet || iti |

tathā nārado 'pi vṛddhyapajīvanaṃ niṣiddham ity āha |

	āpatsv api hi kaṣṭāsu brāhmaṇasya na vārdhuṣam | iti |

vasiṣṭho 'pi: "brāḥmaṇarājanyau vārdhuṣaṃ na dadyātām" iti | vārdhuṣaṃ vṛddhyarthaṃ dhanaprayogaṃ na kuryātām ity arthaḥ | etat sarvam anyahastād ādāya prayoganiṣedhaparam | yato 'nantaram āha sa eva |

	samārghaṃ dhanam uddhṛtya mahārghaṃ yaḥ prayacchati |

	sa vai vārddhuṣiko nāma brahmavādiṣu garhitaḥ || iti |

anyahastād alpikayā vṛddhyā dhanaṃ gṛhītvā anyasmai mahatyā vṛddhyā yo dadāti sa vārdhuṣiko brahmavādiṣu garhita ity artha | atrānantaraṃ doṣo 'pi tenaiva darśitaḥ |

	bhrūṇahatyāṃ ca vṛddhiṃ ca tulayā samatolayat |

	atiṣṭhad bhrūṇahā koṭyāṃ vārddhuṣiḥ samakampata ||

hārīto 'pi |

	brahmaghnaṃ vṛddhijīvaṃ ca tulayā samatolayet |

	atiṣṭhad brahmahā koṭhyāṃ vṛddhijīvas (?) tv akampata || 

evaṃ dhānyādivikraye 'pi draṣṭavyam | tathā ca manuḥ |

	samārghaṃ paṇyam āhṛtya mahārghaṃ yaḥ prayacchati |

	sa vai vārdhuṣiko nāma yaś ca vṛddhyā prayojayet || iti |

atra,

	yaḥ samārgham ṛṇaṃ gṛhya mahārghaṃ saṃprayojayet |

	sa vai vārdhuṣiko nāma brahmavādiṣu garhitiaḥ ||

	vṛddhiṃ ca brahmahatyāṃ ca tulayā samatolayat |

	atiṣṭhad brahmahā koṭhyāṃ vārdhuṣiḥ samakampata ||

iti bodhāyanokto viśeṣaḥ | etac ca viśiṣṭasyaiva niṣedhāt kathaṃcit svakīyasvavṛddhyarthaṃ dhanaprayogo na niṣddhyate iti gamyate | ata eva manuḥ |

	brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo vāpi vṛddhiṃ naiva prayojayet |

	kāmaṃ tu khalu dharmārthe dadyāt pāpīyase 'lpikām || iti |

pāpīyase nikṛṣṭakarmaṇe dharmārtham alpikayā dadyād ity arthaḥ | tathā ca paiṭhīnasiḥ: "kāmaṃ tu pāpīyase dadyān na jyāyasīṃ vṛddhim upādadīta" iti | sā ca bṛddhir manunā darśitā |

	vasiṣṭhavihitāṃ vṛddhiṃ sṛjed vittavivardhinīm |

	aśītibhāgaṃ gṛhṇīyān māsād vārdhuṣikaḥ śate || iti |

yat tu bṛhaspatinoktam,

	bahavo vardhnopāyā ṛṣibhiḥ parikīrtitāḥ |

	sarveṣām api caiteṣāṃ kusīdam adhikaṃ viduḥ ||

iti, tad vittavṛddhau ādhikyapratipādanaparaṃ na punaḥ śraiṣṭhyābhidhānāya | yato 'nantaram āha sa eva |

	anāvṛṣṭyā rajabhāyān mūṣakādyair upaplavaiḥ |

	kṛṣyādike bhaved dhāniḥ sā kusīde na vidyate ||

	śuklapakṣe tathā kṛṣṇe rajanyāṃ divase 'pi vā |

	uṣṇe varṣati śīte vā vardhate na nivartate ||

	deśaṃ gatānāṃ yā vṛddhir nānāpaṇyopajīvinām |

	kusīdaṃ kurvataḥ samyak sā sthitasyaiva jāyate || iti |

evaṃ ca brāhmaṇaḥ sīdan kṣātradharmeṇa jīved alābhe viśāṃ vā na śaudreṇeti siddham | evaṃ kṣatriyavaiśayor api svānantarā vṛttir veditavyā | tathā ca manuḥ |

	jīved etena rājanyaḥ sarveṇāpy anayaṃ gataḥ |

	na tv eva jyāyasīṃ vṛttim abhimanyeta karhicit || iti |

etena vaiśyavartanena | anayaṃ gataḥ āpadaṃ prāpta ity arthaḥ |

	vaiśyo 'jīvan svadharmeṇa śūdravṛttyāpi vartayet |

	anācārann akāryāṇi nivarteta ca śaktimān ||

akāryāṇy ucchiṣṭabhojanādīni | śaktimān nistīrṇāpatkaḥ | śūdravṛttyā nivartetety arthaḥ | vasiṣṭho 'pi: "ajīvan svadharmeṇānantarāṃ papīyasīṃ vṛttiṃ tiṣṭhen na kadācij jyāyasīm" iti | pāpīyasīṃ hīnavarṇaviṣayām | jyāyasīm uparitanavarṇaviṣayām | śūdrasya tūparitanavarṇavixayo 'pi bhavaty eva | tad āha nāradaḥ |

	utkṛṣṭaṃ cāpakṛṣṭaṃ ca tayoḥ karma na vidyate |

	madhyame karmaṇī hitvā sarvasādhāraṇe hi te || iti |

tayor brāhmaṇaśūdrayor madhye brāhmaṇasyāpakṛṣṭaṃ śaudraṃ karma nāsti | tathā śūdrasyotkṛṣṭaṃ brāhmaṇakarma nāstīty arthaḥ | kecid atyantāpadi śaudram api karmecchanti | tad āha gautamaḥ: "aśaudreṇa | tad apy eke prāṇasaṃśaye" iti | aśaudreṇa karmaṇā jīvet | prāṇasaṃdehe tad api jīvanārtham ity arthaḥ | śūdrāpadvṛttayas tu yājñavalkyena darsitāḥ |

	śūdrasya dvijaśuśrūṣā tayājīvan vaṇig bhavet |

	śilpair vā vividhair jīvet dvijātihitam ācaret || iti |

yaiḥ karmabhir dvijātayaḥ śuśrūṣyante tair ity arthaḥ | tathā ca manuḥ |

	yaiḥ karmabhiḥ pracaritaiḥ śuśrūṣyante dvijātayaḥ |

	tāni kārukakarmāṇi śilpāni vividhāni ca || iti |

tatra vṛttyantarāṇy āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	kṛṣiḥ śilpaṃ bhṛtir vidyā kusīdaṃ śakaṭaṃ giriḥ |

	sevānūpo nṛpo baikṣam āpattau jīvanāni tu ||

śilpaṃ sūpakaraṇādi | bhṛtiḥ preṣyatvam | vidyā bhṛtakādhyāpanādi | kusīdaṃ vṛddhyarthaṃ dhanaprayogaḥ | sakaṭaṃ dhānyādivahanadvāreṇa jīvanārtham | giriḥ svagatatṛṇādidvāreṇa | sevā paracittānuvartanam | anūpo bahuvṛkṣajalo deśaḥ | nṛpo rājā | etāny āpattau jīvanānīti vacanād āpadavasthāyāṃ yasya yā vṛttiḥ pratiṣiddhā sā tasyābhyanujñāyate | manur api |

	vidyā śilpaṃ bhṛtiḥ sevā gorakṣyaṃ vipaṇiḥ kṛṣiḥ |

	dhṛtir bhaikṣaṃ kusīdaṃ ca daś jīvanahetavaḥ || iti |

dhṛtiḥ saṃtoṣaḥ | yasminn atisvalpenāpi jīvyante | tatr aṅgirāḥ |

	vyādhitasya daridrasya kuṭumbāt pracyutasya ca |

	adhvānaṃ vā pravṛttasya bhikṣācaryaṃ vidhīyate || iti |

etad api paravṛttyāśrayaṇaṃ viguṇāyā api svavṛtter alābhaviṣayam | tathā ca manuḥ |

	varaṃ svadharmo viguṇaḥ na pārakyaḥ svanuṣṭhitaḥ |

	paradharmeṇa jīvan hi sadyaḥ patati jātitaḥ ||

gautamo 'p: "yājanādhyāpanapratigrahāḥ sarveṣāṃ pūrvaḥ pūrvo guruḥ | tadalābhe kṣatravṛttiḥ" iti | sarveṣāṃ brāhmaṇādīnāṃ ca kāryā iti śeṣaḥ | tatrāpatkalpa ity anuvartate | ataḥ sarvagrahaṇenāpraśastā gṛhyante | praśastānām anāpadi vidhānāt | anena yājanādhyapanābhyāṃ pratigrahaḥ praśasta ity uktaṃ bhavati | yamo 'pi |

	pratigrahādhyapanayājanānāṃ pratigrahaṃ śreṣṭhatamaṃ vadanti |

	pratigrahāc chuddhyati japyahomaiḥ yājyaṃ tu pāpair na punanti vedāḥ ||

yājyaṃ yājakam ity arthaḥ | etad dvijātipratigrahābhiprāyam | śūdraviṣayasaiva manunā yājanādhyāpanābhyāṃ nikṛṣṭatvābhidhānāt |

	pratigrahād yājanād vā tathaivādhyapanād api |

	pratigrahaḥ pratyavaraḥ sa tu viprasya garhitaḥ || iti |

pratyavaro nikṛṣṭaḥ | atra hetum āha sa eva |

	yājanādhyāpane nityaṃ kriyete saṃskṛtātmanām |

	pratigrahas tu kriyate śūdrād apy antyajanmanaḥ ||

	japahomair apaity eno yājanādhyāpanaiḥ kṛtam |

	pratigrahanimittaṃ tu tyāgena tapasaiva ca || iti |

saṃskṛtātmanāṃ dvijātīnām iti yāvat | ato yājanādhyapanābhyāṃ dvijāteḥ pratigraha eva śreyān iti mantavyam | pratigrahe 'pi viśeṣam āha manuḥ |

	akṛtaṃ ca kṛtāt kṣetrād gor ajāvikam eva ca |

	hiraṇyaṃ dhānyam annaṃ ca pūrvaṃ pūrvam adoṣavat || iti |

akṛtam akṛṣṭam | vaiśavṛttyā jīvato yad apaṇyaṃ tad āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	phalophalakṣaumasomamanuṣyāpūpavīrudhaḥ |

	tilaudanarasakṣaudradadhikṣīraghṛtaṃ jalam ||

	śastrāsavamadhūcchiṣṭamadhulākṣāḥ sabarhiṣaḥ |

	mṛccarmapuṣpakutapakeśatakraviṣakṣitīḥ ||

	kauśeyanīlīlavaṇamāṃsaikaśaphasīsakān |

	śākārdrauṣadhipiṇyākapaśugandhāṃs tathaiva ca ||

	vaiśyavṛttyāpi jīvan no vikrīṇīta kadācana || iti |

phalāni badareṅgudavyatiriktāni | upalaṃ māṇikyādi | kṣaumam atasīsūtranirmitam | apūpaṃ maṇṭkādi | vīrul latā | rasā ikṣurasādayaḥ | āsavo madyam | madhūcchiṣṭaṃ sikthakam | madhu kṣaudram | lākṣā jatu | barhiḥ kuśādi | kutapaḥ kambalaviseṣaḥ | keśāś camaryādisaṃbandhāḥ | ekaśaphāḥ aśvādayaḥ | paśava āraṇyā grāmyāś ca, "paśūnām ekaśaphāḥ keśinaś ca sarve cāraṇyāḥ paśavo vasāṃsi daṃṣṭriṇaś ca" iti vasiṣṭhasmaraṇāt | keśino manuṣyāḥ | gautamo 'pi: "tasyāpaṇyaṃ gandharasakṛtānnatilaśāṇakṣaumājināni raktanirṇikte vāsasī kṣīraṃ savikāraṃ mūlaphalapuṣpauṣadhamadhumāṃsatṛṇodakapathyāni paśavaś ca hiṃsā saṃyoge purīṣavaśākumārivehataś ca nityaṃ bhūmivrīhiyavājāvyaśvarṣabhadhenvanaḍuhaś caike" iti | kṛtānnaṃ pakvānnam | raktaṃ tāntavam, "raktaṃ śāṇakṣaumavikāni ca" iti manusmaraṇāt | nirṇiktaṃ prakṣālitam | mūlaṃ haridrādi | phalaṃ kramukādi | apathyaṃ viṣam | hiṃsāsaṃyoge saṃjñapte paśavo na vikreyāḥ | vaśā vandhyā | vehad garbhaghātinī | bhūmyādayo 'pi nityam avikreyā ity eke manyante | ekagrahaṇān na gautama iti vyākyātaṃ tadbhāṣye | avikreyam ity anuvṛttau nārado 'pi |

	kusumbhaṃ nārikelaṃ ca vṛntākaṃ pūtikaṃ tathā |

	somaḥ śleṣmāntako yajñas toyaṃ sarpiś ca sarvathā ||

manur api |

	kṣīraṃ kṣaudraṃ dadhi ghṛtaṃ tailaṃ madhu guḍaṃ kuśān | iti |

kṣaudraṃ mākṣikam | ayaṃ cāpaṇyaniṣedho brāhmaṇasyaiva | yad āha nāradaḥ |

	vaiśyavṛttyāpy avikreyaṃ brāhmaṇasya payo dadhi | iti |

āpastambo 'pi: "avihitā brāhmaṇasya vaṇijyā | āpadi vyavahareta paṇyānām apaṇyāni vyudasyan" iti | apaṇyāni vyudadyan paṇyair vyavaharetety arthaḥ | atrāpi viśeṣam āha sa eva: "akrītapaṇyair vyavaharate" iti | akrītapaṇyaiḥ krayetaropaāyalabdhair ity arthaḥ | anenāpdy akrītapaṇyair api na vyavahared ity uktaṃ bhavati | evam uktaniṣedhātikramaṇe doṣam āhatuḥ śaṅkhalikhitau: "tiladadhikṣaudralavaṇalākṣāmadyamāṃsakṛtānnastrīpuruṣahastyaśvavṛṣabhagandharasakṛṣṇā-jinasomodakāt sadyaḥ patati brāhmaṇaḥ" iti | yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	lākṣālavaṇamāṃsāni patanīyāni vikraye |

	payo dadhi ca madyaṃ ca hīnavarṇakarāni tu ||

hīnavarṇaḥ śūdraḥ | manur api |

	sadyaḥ patati māṃsena lākṣayā lavanena ca |

	tryaheṇa śudro bhavati brāhmaṇaḥ kṣīravikrayāt ||

	itareṣāṃ tu paṇyānāṃ vikrayād iha kamataḥ |

	brāhmaṇaḥ saptarātreṇa vaiśyabhāvaṃ nigacchati ||

yamo 'pi |

	snehadravyarasānāṃ ca satvānāṃ jīvatām api |

	vikretā dānapaṇyānāṃ procyate brahmahā budhaiḥ ||

	gavāṃ vikrayakārī tu gavi romāṇi yāni tu |

	tāvad varṣasahasrāṇi gavāṃ goṣṭhe krimir bhavet ||

	dānābhyañjanabhogebhyo yad anyat kurute tilaiḥ |

	krimir bhavati viṣṭhāyāṃ karmaṇā tena pāpakṛt ||

manur api |

	bhojanābhyañjanād dānād yad anyat kurute tilaiḥ |

	krimir bhūtvā sa viṣṭhāyāṃ pitṛbhiḥ saha majjati || iti |

yat tu tenaivoktam,

	kāmam utpādya kṛṣyāṃ tu svayam eva kṛṣīvalaḥ |

	vikrīṇīta tilāñ chuddhān dharmārtham acirasthitān || 

iti — śuddhān dravyāntareṇāmiśrān — yad api vasiṣṭhena: "kāmaṃ vā svayaṃ kṛṣyotpādya tilān vikrīnīran" iti, tad vinimayalakṣaṇavikrayābhiprāyam | yad āha nāradaḥ |

	aśaktau bheṣajasyārthe yajñahetos tathaiva ca |

	yady avaśyaṃ tu vikreyās tilā dhānyena tatsamāḥ || iti |

dhānyenaiva tu tulyamānās tilā vikreyāḥ na rūpakādinety arthaḥ | yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	dharmārthaṃ vikrayaṃ neyās tilā dhānyena tatsamāḥ |

manur api |

	rasā rasair nimātavyā na tv eva lavaṇaṃ rasaiḥ |

	kṛtānnaṃ cākṛtānnena tilā dhānyena tatsamāḥ ||

kṛtānnaṃ pakvānnam | nimātavyāḥ parivartanīyā ity arthaḥ | evaṃ manuṣyādiṣv api draṣṭavyam | ata eva āpastambaḥ: "annena cānnasya manuṣyāṇāṃ ca manuṣyaiḥ rasānāṃ ca rasaiḥ gandhānāṃ ca gandhaiḥ vidyayā ca vidyānām" iti | atra vinimaya ity anuvartate | raseṣu viśeṣam āha vasiṣṭhaḥ: "rasā rasaiḥ samato hīnato vā nimātavyāḥ" iti | samastas tulyamānatvena | hīnato 'lpaparimāṇatvena | gautamas tv annaviṣaye viśeṣam āha: "samenāmena tu pakvasya" iti | pakvasamenāmena pakvavinimayo bhavatīty arthaḥ | atra hārītaḥ |

	vinimayas tu rasādīnāṃ vikrayo naiva duṣyati |

	yajñārthe dakṣiṇādīnāṃ prajāpativaco yathā ||

nārado 'pi |

	brāhmaṇasya tu vikreyaṃ śuṣkaṃ dārutṛṇāni ca | iti |

evaṃ paravṛttyāśrayaṇena āpadaṃ nistīrya prāyaścittena pāvayitvātmānaṃ svavṛttāv eva nyaset | tathā ca yājñavalkyaḥ |

	kṣātreṇa karmaṇā jīved viśāṃ vāpy āpadi dvijaḥ |

	nistīrya tām athātmānaṃ pāvayitvā nyaset pathi || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyām āpatkāṇḍam**

**tato mādhyandinasnānam**

tatra bodhāyanaḥ |

	tato madhyāhnasamaye punaḥ snānaṃ samācaret |

	sūryasya cāpy upasthānaṃ japahomādikaṃ tataḥ ||

kūrmapurāṇe |

	tato madhyāhnasamaye snānārthaṃ mṛdam āharet |

madhyāhnasamaye aṣṭadhā vibhaktasyāhnaḥ caturthabhāge | ata eva dakṣaḥ |

	caturthe 'hnas tathā bhāge snānārthaṃ mṛdam āharet |

	tilapuṣpakuśādīni snānaṃ cākṛttrime jale ||

vasiṣṭhahārītāv api |

	pavitrapāṇir ekāgraḥ pārśvān anavalokayan |

	arug divācaret snānaṃ madhyāhnāt prāg viśeṣataḥ ||

arug arogī | anenārthān na rogī snāyād ity uktaṃ bhavati | uktaṃ ca vyāsena |

	snānaṃ madhyandine kuryāt sujīrṇe 'nne nirāmayaḥ |

	na bhuktvālaṃkṛto rogī nājñātāmbhasi nākulaḥ || iti |

etac ca snānaṃ gṛhasthavanasthayor veditavyam | tathā ca dakṣaḥ |

	prātar madhyāhnayoḥ snānaṃ vānaprasthagṛhasthayoḥ |

	yates triṣavaṇaṃ snānaṃ sakṛc c brahmacāriṇaḥ || iti |

atra vyāsaḥ |

	mantrapūtair jalaiḥ snānaṃ prāhuḥ snānaṃ phalapradam |

	na vṛthā vārimagnānāṃ yādasām iva tatphalam ||

yādasāṃ jalajantūnām ity arthaḥ | yogayājñavalkyo 'pi |

	matsyakacchapamaṇḍūkās toye magnā divāniśam |

	vasanti caiva te snānān nāpnuvanti phalaṃ kvacit || iti |

ato mantravad eva kāryam ity abhiprāyaḥ | ata eva tadakaraṇe doṣam āha vivasvān |

	aviditvaiva yaḥ snānavidhānaṃ snānam ācaret |

	ya yāti narakaṃ ghoram iti dharmasya dhāraṇā || iti |

etad api dvijātiviṣayam | tad āha viṣṇuḥ |

	brahmakṣatraviśāṃ caiva mantravat snānam iṣyate |

	tūṣṇīm eva hi śūdrasya strīṇāṃ ca kurunandana ||

atra snānadravyāṇy āha yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	mṛt tilān gomayaṃ darbhān puṣpāṇi surabhīṇi ca |

	āharet snānakāle tu snānārthaṃ prayataḥ śuciḥ || iti |

śātātapo mṛtsvarūpam āha |

	valmīkākhūtkarāl lepāj jalāc ca pathivṛkṣayoḥ |

	kṛtaśaucāvaśiṣṭāc ca na grāhyāḥ sapta mṛttikāḥ ||

	śucideśāt tu saṃgrāhyāḥ śarkarāśmādivarjitāḥ |

	raktā gaurā tathā śvetā mṛttikā trividhā smṛtā |

	mṛttikāṃ gomayaṃ vāpi na niśāyāṃ samāharet ||

	na gomūtraṃ pradoṣeṣu gṛhṇīyād buddhimān naraḥ || iti |

mṛdādyāharaṇāntaraṃ yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	gatvodakāntaṃ vidhivat sthāpayet tatpṛthak kṣitau |

	tridhā kṛtvā mṛdaṃ tāṃ tu gomayaṃ ca vicakṣaṇaḥ ||

	adhamottamamadhyānām aṅgānāṃ kṣālanaṃ tu taiḥ |

	bhāgaiḥ pṛthak pṛthak kuryāt kṣālane mṛdasaṃkaraḥ ||

	adbhir mṛdbhiś ca caraṇau prakṣālyācamya vai śuciḥ | iti |

atra malasnānaṃ prakṛtya vyāsaḥ |

	ṣaḍbhiḥ pādau caturbhis tu jaṅghe nābhikaṭī tribhiḥ |

	mṛdaikayā siraḥ kṣālyaṃ dvabhyāṃ nābhes tathopari ||

	adhaś ca tisṛbhiḥ kāryaḥ pādau ṣaḍbhis tathaiva ca |

	prakṣālya sarvakāyaṃ tad dvir ācamya yathāvidhi || iti |

atra yathāsvaśākhaṃ vyavasthā | mṛdadiparimāṇaṃ kūrmapurāṇe darśitam |

	snānārthaṃ mṛttikā grāhyā hy ārdrāmalakamātrikā |

	gomayasya pramāṇaṃ tat tenāṅgaṃ lepayet tataḥ || iti |

etac ca malapakarṣaṇaṃ snānaṃ taṭe kāryam | tathā ca nṛsiṃhapurāṇe |

	śucau deśe samabhyukṣya sthāpayet kuśamṛttikāḥ |

	mṛttoyena svakaṃ dehaṃ bahiḥ saṃśodhya yatnataḥ ||

dakṣo 'pi |

	nityaṃ naimittikaṃ kāmyaṃ trividhaṃ snānam ucyate |

	teṣāṃ madhye tu yan nityaṃ tat punar bhidyate tridhā ||

	malāpakarṣaṇaṃ pārśve mantravat tu jale smṛtam |

	saṃdhyāsnānam ubhābhyāṃ tu snānadeśāḥ prakīrtitāḥ || iti |

pārśve taṭe | saṃdhyasnānaṃ mārjanam | tad ubhābhyāṃ jalasthalābhyāṃ kāryam ity arthaḥ | atra malasnāne 'pi nityagrahaṇam anuktaśākhinām api tasya nityatvaṃ yathā syād iti | malasnānānantaraṃ yamaḥ |

	pādaprakṣālanaṃ kṛtvā ācamya prāṅmukhaḥ sthitaḥ |

	prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ kuryāt tato dhyatvā divākaram || iti |

tatas tīrthaparikalpanādi kuryāt | tathā ca matsyapurāṇam |

	darbhapāṇis tu vidhinā svācāntaḥ prayataḥ suciḥ |

	tīrthaṃ tu kalpayed vidvān mūlamantreṇa mantravit ||

	oṃ namo nārāyaṇāyeti mūlamantra udāhṛtaḥ |

	caturhastasamāyuktaṃ caturaśraṃ samantataḥ ||

	prakalpyāvāhayed gaṅgām ebhir mantrair vicakṣaṇaḥ |

	viṣṇupādaprasūtāsi vaiṣṇavī viṣṇudevatā ||

	trāhi nas tv enasas tasmād ājanmamaraṇāntikāt |

	tisraḥ koṭyo 'rdhakoṭī ca tīrthānāṃ vāyur abravīt ||

	divi bhuvy antarikṣe ca tāni me santu jāhnavi |

	nandinīty eva te nāma deveṣu nalinīti ca ||

	dakṣā pṛthvī ca vihagā visvarāyā śivāmṛtā |

	vidyādharī suprasannā tathā lokaprasādinī ||

	kṣamā ca jāhnavī caiva śāntā śāntipradāyinī |

	etāni puṇyanāmāni snānakāle prakīrtayet ||

	bhavet saṃnihitā tatra gaṅgā tripathagāminī |

tathā gaṅgāvākyam api |

	nandinī nalinī sītā mālatī ca mahāpagā |

	viṣṇupādābjasaṃbhūtā gaṅgā tripathagāminī |

	bhāgīrathī bhogavatī jāhnavī tridaśeśvarī |

	dvādaśaitāni nāmāni yatra yatra jalāśaye ||

	snānodyataḥ smaren nityaṃ tatra tatra bhavāmy aham |

vyāso 'pi |

	kurukṣetra gayā gaṅgā prabhāsaṃ naimisaṃ tathā |

	tīrthāny etāni sarvāṇi snānakāle bhavantu me || iti |

etat sarvaṃ kṛtrimodakaviṣayam,

	gaṅgādisarvatīrthāni kṛtrimādiṣu saṃsmaret  |

iti yogayājñavalkyasmaraṇāt | devalo 'pi |

	na nadīṣu nadīṃ brūyāt parvateṣu na parvatam |

	nānyat praśaṃset tatrasthas tīrtheṣv āyataneṣu ca || iti |

evam āvāhya svaśākhoktena vidhinā snāyāt | ata eva śaucānantaraṃ matyapurāṇe |

	snānaṃ kuryān mṛdā tadvad āmantrya ca vidhānataḥ |

	aśvakrānte rathakrānte viṣṇukrānte vasundhare || iti |

atra jamadagniḥ |

	atha snānaṃ pravakṣyāmi sarvapāpapraṇāśanam |

	nālpodake dvijaḥ snāyān nadīṃ cotsṛjya kṛtrime ||

	prāgagram udagagraṃ vā dhautavastraṃ prasārayet |

	aśvakrānta iti śuddhāṃ mṛttikām āharec chuciḥ ||

	namo mitrasyety ādityāya datvā prakṣālayet karau |

	gandhadvārām iti japtvā svāny evāṅgāni lepayet ||

	hiraṇyaśṛṅgaṃ varuṇam ity apo 'bhiprapadyate |

	sumitrā na ity apaḥ kṣiptvā durmitrās tu bahiḥ kṣipet ||

	yad apāṃ krūram ity apas trir āloḍya tu pāṇinā |

	ādityābhimukho majjed āpo asmān iti dvyṛcā ||

	madhyandine 'pa ācāmen mantreṇāpaḥ punantv iti |

	agniś ca meti sāyaṃ ca prātaḥ sūryaś ca meti ca ||

	surabhimatyābliṅgābhḥ prokṣayet kuśapāṇinā |

	hiraṇyavarṇīyābhiś ca pāvamānībhir eva ca ||

	ṛtaṃ cety etad apsv antas triḥ paṭhed aghamarṣaṇam |

	yathāsvamedhe 'vabhṛthaṃ tathā snāne 'ghamarṣaṇam || iti |

anyaj jalatarpaṇādi sarvaṃ prātaḥsnānoktaṃ veditavyam | ādityābhimukho majjed iti sthāvarodakaviṣayam | tathā ca nṛsiṃhapurāṇam |

	nadyāṃ sravatsu ca snāyāt pratisrotaḥ sthito dvijaḥ |

	taṭākādiṣu toyeṣu pratyarkaṃ snānam ācaret || iti |

atra drupadāṃ prakṛtya kūrmapurāṇaṃ |

	apaḥ pāṇau samādāya jalair vai mārjane kṛte |

	vinyasya mūrdhni tat toyaṃ mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ || iti |

atra viśeṣam āha yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	apaḥ pāṇau samādāya triḥ paṭhed drupadām ṛcam |

	tat toyaṃ mūrdhni vinyasya sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ||

antarjalajapaṃ prakṛtyāpi sa evāha |

	hatvā lokān apīmāṃs trīṃs triḥ paṭhed aghamarṣaṇam |

	yathāśvamedhāvabhṛtha evaṃ vai manur abravīt ||

	drupadā nāma sā devī yajurvede pratiṣṭhitā |

	antarjale trir āvṛtya mucyate brahmahatyayā ||

vyāso 'pi |

	drupadā nāma gāyatrī brāhmī vājasaneyake |

	sakṛd antarjale japtur brahmahatyāṃ vyapohati ||

	antarjale trir āvṛtya sāvitrīṃ prayatas tataḥ |

	mucyate pātakaiḥ sarvair yadi na brahmahā bhavet ||

hārīto 'pi |

	jumbukā nāma gāyatrī vede vājasaneyake |

	antarjale sakṛj japtvā brahmahatyāṃ vyapohati ||

sumantur api: "mātaraṃ bhaginīṃ hatvā mātṛṣvasāraṃ pitṛṣvasāraṃ snuṣāṃ sakhīṃ cānyad vāgamyāgamanaṃ kṛtvāghamarṣaṇasūktam antarjale trir āvṛtya tad etasmāt pūto bhavati" iti | hārīto 'pi: "āyaṃ (?) gauḥ pṛśnir akramīd ity etām ṛcaṃ trir antarjale japan sarvasmāt pāpāt pramucyate | api vā vyāhṛtīs trir antarjale japan sarvasmāt pāpāt pramucyate" iti | gautamo 'pi: "api vā gāyatrīṃ paccho 'rdharcaśaḥ samastām iti trir antarjale japan sarvasmāt pāpāt pramucyate (?) | api vā praṇavaṃ trir antarjale japan sarvasmāt pāpāt pramucyate" iti | atra vasiṣṭhaḥ snānavidhānam āha |

	atha snānavidhiṃ kṛtsnaṃ pravakṣyāmy anupūrvaśaḥ |

	yena snatvā divaṃ yānti śraddadhānā dvijottamāḥ ||

	prayato mṛdam ādāya dūrvām ārdrāṃ ca gomayam |

	sthāpayitvā tathācamya tataḥ snānaṃ samācaret ||

	mṛdaikayā śiraḥ kṣālyaṃ dvābhyāṃ nābhes tathopari |

	adhaś ca tisṛbhiḥ kāyaṃ pādau ṣaḍbhis tathaiva ca ||

	prakṣālya sarvam aṅgaṃ tu dvir ācamya yathāvidhi |

	tataḥ saṃmārjanaṃ kuryān mṛdā pūrvaṃ tu mantravit ||

	aśvakrānte rathakrānte viṣṇukrānte vasundhare |

	uddhṛtāsi varaheṇa kṛṣṇena śatabāhunā ||

	mṛttike tvāṃ ca gṛhṇāmi prajayā ca dhanena ca |

	mṛttike brahmadattāsi kāśyapenābhimantritā ||

	mṛttike hana me pāpaṃ yan mayā duṣkṛtaṃ kṛtam |

	mṛttike dehi me puṣṭiṃ tvayi sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam ||

	punaś ca gomayenaiva agram agram iti bruvan |

	agram agraṃ carantīnām oṣadhīnāṃ vane vane ||

	tāsām ṛṣabhapatnīnāṃ pavitraṃ kāyaśodhanam |

	tvaṃ me rogāṃś ca śokāṃś ca pāpaṃ me nuda gomaya ||
