	kāṇḍat kāṇḍād iti dvābhyām aṅgam aṅgam iti spṛśet || 

dūrvayeti śeṣaḥ | yājurvedikāv etau mantrau |

	kṛtvaivaṃ mārjanaṃ mantrair aśvakrāntadibhis tataḥ |

	ihaiva devīm amṛtāṃ pārāvata purādiṣu ||

	etāḥ śatam iti dhyātvā tīrthāny āvāhayed budhaḥ |

	kurukṣetraṃ gayāṃ gaṅgāṃ prabhāsaṃ puṣkarāṇi ca ||

	tato mahāvyāhṛtibhir gāyatryā cābhimantrayet |

	āpo hiṣṭhedam āpaś ca drupadād iva ity api ||

	tathā hiraṇyavarṇābhiḥ pāvamānībhir eva ca |

	tato 'rkam īkṣya soṃkāraṃ nimajjyāntarjale budhaḥ |||

	prāṇāyāmāṃś ca kurvīta gāyatrīṃ cāghamarṣaṇam |

	yathoktaiḥ kṣobhitas tais tu majjet trir daṇḍavat tataḥ ||

yathoktair vāyor ādhmānanirodhotsargarūpaiḥ,

	snātvā saṃgṛhya vāso 'nyad ūrū saṃśodhayen mṛdā |

	apavitre kṛte te tu kaupīnasrāvavāriṇā |

	nottarīyam adhaḥ kuryān nopary ādhastyam ambaram |

	nāntarvāso vinā jātu nivased vasanaṃ budhaḥ ||

	prāg vodag vā śucau deśe upaviśya dvir ācamet |

	yo 'nena vidhinā snāti yatra yatrāmbhasi dvijaḥ ||

	sa tīrthaphalam āpnoti tīrthe tu dviguṇaṃ phalam |

	manovākkarmabhiś cāpi yat pāpaṃ kurute tu saḥ ||

	nāśam āpnoti tat sarvam āmapātram ivāmbhasi || iti |

mṛttoyaiḥ kṛtamalāpakarṣaṇo nimajjyāpa upaspṛśya āpo hiṣṭheti tisṛbhir hiraṇyavarṇā iti catasṛbhiḥ idam āpaḥ pravahateti ca tīrtham abhimantrayet | tato 'psu nimagnaḥ trir aghamarṣaṇaṃ japet | tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam iti, drupadāṃ vā sāvirtīm, yujyate mana ity anuvākaṃ vā puruṣasūktaṃ vā | snātaś cārdravāsā devarṣipitṛtarpaṇam ambhaḥstha eva kurvīteti | āpastambo 'pi: "śanair apo 'bhyaveyād abhighnann abhimukham ādityam udakam upaspṛśed iti sarvatrodakasparśanavidhiḥ" iti | atrodakasparśanam ity etad vanasthaviṣayaṃ tatprakaraṇe pāṭhād iti vyākhyātaṃ tadbhāṣye | atrānukalpam āha yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	ya eṣa vistaraḥ proktaḥ snānasya vidhir uttamaḥ |

	asāmarthyān na kuryāc cet tatrāyaṃ vidhir ucyate ||

	snanam antarjale caiva mārjanācamane tathā |

	jalābhimantraṇaṃ caiva tīrthasya parikalpanam ||

	aghamarṣaṇasūktena trirāvṛttena nityaśaḥ |

	snānācaraṇam ity etat samuddiṣṭaṃ maharṣibhiḥ || iti |

etat tīrthaparikalpanaṃ jalābhimantraṇācamanamārjanāntarjalasnāneṣu trirāvṛttāghamarṣaṇasūktavidhiparam it kaiścid vyākhyātam |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ madhyandinasnānam**

**atha madhyāhnasaṃdhyā**

tatra śaṅkhaḥ |

	prātaḥ saṃdhyāṃ madhyamāṃ snānakarmaṇi |

	sādityāṃ paścimāṃ saṃdhyām upāsīta yathavidhi ||

snānakarmaṇi mādhyandinasnānānantaram ity arthaḥ | atrāyaṃ prayogaḥ | kṛtasnanas tv ācānto yathāvidhi prāṇān āyamya madhyāhnasaṃdhyām upāsiṣye iti saṃkalpya pūrvavad apo hiṣṭheti tṛcena yājayitvāpaḥ punantv ity apaḥ pibet | tasyānuṣṭub chandaḥ | viṣṇuḥ ṛṣiḥ, apo devatā, madhyāhnasaṃdhyācamane viniyogaḥ | tato mārjanādi sarvaṃ prātaḥsaṃdhyāvad ā sāvitrījapāt | atra viśeṣaḥ kūrmapurāṇe darśitaḥ |

	tato madhyāhnasaṃdhyāyām asīnaḥ prāṅmukho japet |

	sthito japet sadādālam ādityābhimukho dvijaḥ || iti |

sthitaś ced ādityābhimukho japed ity arthaḥ | ata eva yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	tiṣṭhaṃś ced vīkṣamāṇo 'rkam āsīnaḥ prāṅmukho japet |

atrāpi svaśākhoditair mantrair ādityam upatiṣṭhet, 

	upasthānaṃ svakair karmair ādityasya tu kārayet |

iti vasiṣṭhasmaraṇāt | etat sarvaṃ nārāyaṇoktam |

	upavītī baddhaśikhaḥ samācamya yathāgamam |

	pavitrapāṇiḥ soṃkaraṃ yajñeśaṃ manasā smaret ||

	prātaḥsaṃdhyāvidhānena chanda ārṣaṃ ca daivatam |

	smṛtvā cācamya ca prāṇān āyamed darbhapāṇinā ||

	āpaḥ punantu mantreṇa āpo tiṣṭheti mārjanam |

	prakṣipya cāñjaliṃ samyag ud u tyaṃ citram ity api ||

	tac cakṣur devahitaṃ ca haṃsaḥ śuciṣad ity api |

	etaj japed ūrdhavāhuḥ sūryaṃ paśyan samāhitaḥ ||

	gāyatryā tu yathāśakti upasthāya divākaram |

	noccair japyaṃ budhaḥ kuryāt sāvitryā ca viseṣataḥ || iti |

kūrmapurāṇe tatsnānamadhya eva saṃdhyācamanādy uktam |

	tato madhyāhnasamaye snānārthaṃ mṛdam āharet |

	puṣpākṣatān kuśatilān gomayaṃ śuddham eva ca ||

	mṛdaikayā śiraḥ kṣālyaṃ dvābhyāṃ nābes tathopari |

	adhaś ca tisṛbhiḥ kāyaṃ pādau ṣaḍbhis tathaiva ca ||

	mṛttikā ca samuddiṣṭā tv ārdrāmalakamatrikā |

	gomayasya pramāṇaṃ tat tenāṅgaṃ lepayet tataḥ ||

	prakṣālyācamya vidhivat tataḥ snāyāt samāhitaḥ |

	abhimantrya jalaṃ mantrair abliṅgair vāruṇaiḥ śubhaiḥ ||

	bhāvapūtas tad avyaktaṃ dhārayed viṣṇum avyayam |

	āpo nārā iti proktās tā evāsyāyanaṃ punaḥ ||

	tasmān nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ snānakāle smared budhaḥ |

	prekṣya soṃkāram ādityaṃ trir nimajjya jalāśaye ||

	ācāntaḥ punar ācāmen mantreṇānena mantravit |

	antaś carasi bhūteṣu guhāyāṃ viśvatomukhaḥ ||

	tvaṃ yajñas tvaṃ vaṣaṭkāra āpo jyotī raso 'mṛtam |

	tataḥ saṃmārjanaṃ kuryād āp hiṣṭhā manobhuvaḥ ||

	idam āpaḥ pravahata vyāhṛtībhis tathaiva ca |

	tato 'bhimantrya tat toyam āp hiṣṭādimantrakaiḥ ||

	antarjalagato magno japet trir aghamarṣaṇam |

	athopatiṣṭhed adityam ūrdhvaṃ puṣpānvitaṃ jalam ||

	prakṣipyālokayed devam ud vayaṃ tamasaḥ pari |

	ud u tyaṃ citram ity etat tac cakṣur iti mantrataḥ ||

	haṃaḥ śuciṣid ity eva sāvitryā ca viśeṣataḥ |

	anyaiś ca vaidikair mantraiḥ sauraiḥ pāpapraṇāśanaiḥ ||

	sāvitrīṃ vai japet paścāj japayajñaḥ sa vai smṛtaḥ | iti |

bodhāyano 'pi: 


        atha hastau prakṣālya kamaṇḍuluṃ mṛtpiṇḍaṃ ca parigṛhya tīrthe gatvā triḥ padau prakṣālayet trir ātmānam | athāpo 'bhipratipadyate hiraṇyaśṛṅgaṃ varuṇam iti | athāñjalinā apa upahanti sumitrā na āpa oṣadhayaḥ santv iti | tāṃ diśaṃ nirukṣati yasyām asya diśi dveṣyo bhavati durmitrās tasmai bhūyāsur iti | athāpa upaspṛśya triḥ pradakṣiṇam udakam āvartayati yad apāṃ krūram iti | apsu nimajjya uttīrya cācāntaḥ punar ācāmet āpaḥ punantu iti | pavitre kṛtvādbhir mārjayitvāpo hiṣṭheti tisṛbhir hiraṇyavarṇāṃ iti catasṛbhiḥ pavamānaḥ suvarjana ityāntenānuvākenāmārjayitvāntarjalagato 'ghamarṣaṇena trīn prāṇāyāmān dhārayitvā uttīrya vāsaḥ pīḍayitvā prakṣālitopavātākliṣṭāni vāsāṃsi paridhāyācamya darbheṣv āsīno dharbhān dhārayamāṇaḥ prāṅmukhaḥ sāvitrīṃ sahasrakṛtva āvartayet | iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ mādhyandinasaṃdhyānirṇayaḥ**

**atha japayajñapraśaṃsā**

tatra vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	ye pākayajñāś catvāro vidhiyajñasamanvitāḥ |

	sarve te japayajñasya kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm ||

pākayajñā devayajñādayaḥ | vidhiyajño jyotiṣṭomādiḥ | manur api |

	vidhiyajñāj japayajño viśiṣṭo daśabhir guṇaiḥ |

	japyenaiva tu saṃsiddhyed brāhmaṇo nātra saṃśayaḥ ||

yamo 'pi |

	vṛttīnāṃ karṣaṇaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ dharmāṇāṃ svāgatakriyā |

	japayajñas tu yajñānāṃ sarveṣām uttamaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

purāṇe 'pi |

	yakṣarakṣaḥpiśācāś ca grahāḥ sarve vibhīṣaṇāḥ |

	japinaṃ nopasarpanti dūrād evāpayānti te ||

vasiṣṭho 'pi |

	yathāgnir vāyunoddhūto haviṣā caiva dīpyate |

	evaṃ japyaparo nityaṃ mantrayuktaḥ sadā dvijaḥ || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ japayajñapraśaṃsā**

**atha japyāni**

tatra yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	japayajño hi kartavyaḥ sarvavedapraṇītakaiḥ |

	pavitrair vividhaiś canyair gṛhyopaniṣadāṃ tathā ||

	adhyātmavidyā vividhā japyās tu japasiddayet |

anyair devatāstavanādibhiḥ | viṣṇur api: "snātaḥ pavitrapāṇiḥ yathāśakti japed viśeṣataḥ sāvitrīm puruṣasūktaṃ vā naitābhyāṃ adhikam asti" iti | tāni ca pavitrāṇi vasiṣṭhena darśitāni |

	sarvavedapavitrāṇi vakṣyāmy aham ataḥ param |

	yeṣāṃ japaiś ca homaiś ca pūyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ||

	aghamarṣaṇaṃ devakṛtaṃ śuddhavatyas taratsamāḥ |

	kūśmāṇḍyaḥ pāvamānyaś ca durgā sāvitry athaiva ca ||

	abhiṣaṅgāḥ padastobhāḥ sāmāni vyāhṛtis tathā |

	vāruṇāni ca sāmāni gāyatraṃ raivataṃ tathā ||

	abliṅgā bārhaspatyaṃ ca vāksūktaṃ madhvṛcas tathā |

	śatarudram atharvaśiras trisuparṇaṃ mahāvratam ||

	gosūktam aśvasūktaṃ ca indraśuddhe ca sāmanī |

	trīṇy ājyadohāni rathantaraṃ ca agnivrataṃ vāsudevyaṃ bṛhac ca |

	etāni japyāni punanti jantūn jātismaratvaṃ labhate ya icchet ||

aghamarṣaṇm ṛtaṃ cetyādyās tisraḥ | devakṛtaṃ devakṛtsyainasa ityādayaḥ | śuddhavatya eto 'nvindraṃ stavāmetyādyās tisraḥ | taratsamās taratsamandī dhāvatītyadyās tisraḥ | kūśmāṇḍyo yad devā devaheḷanam ity anuvākatrayam | pāvamānyaḥ svādiṣṭhaya madiṣṭhayety evamādyāḥ | durgā jātavedase sunavāma somam ity ekā ṛk | sāvitrī tat savitur iti | abhiṣaṅgādayo raivatāntāḥ sāmaviśeṣāḥ | abliṅgā āpo hiṣṭhetyādyāḥ | bārhaspatyaṃ yas tastambha sahasety ekādaśarcam | vāksūktam ahaṃ rudrebhir ity aṣṭarcam | madhvṛcaḥ madhu vātā ṛtāyate ityādyās tisraḥ | śatarudrīyaṃ namas te rudra manyave ity ekādaśānuvākāḥ | trisuparṇaṃ brahma metu (?) mām ity anuvākatrayam | mahāvrataṃ rājanaṃ (?) nama sāma | gosūktaṃ ā gāvo agmann (?) ity aṣṭarcam | aśvasūktaṃ mā no mitro varuṇa iti dvāviṃśarcam | indraśuddhādayo bṛhadantāḥ sāmaviśeṣāḥ | etāni pavitrāṇi aghamarṣaṇānīty arthaḥ | caturviṃśatāv api |

	devavratājyadohāni āgnīdhraṃ ca rathantaram |

	gharmasāmāni raudrāṇi japtvā pāpaiḥ pramucyate ||

	yajñāyajñiyam ādityaṃ jyeṣṭhasāma ca rājanam |

	gāruḍāni ca sāmāni japtvā mucyeta kilbiṣāt ||

manur api |

	vedam evābhasen nityaṃ yathākalam atandritaḥ |

	na hy asyāhuḥ paraṃ dharmam upadharmo 'sya ucyate ||

	vedābhyāsena satataṃ śaucena tapasaiva ca |

	adroheṇa ca bhūtānāṃ jātiṃ smarati paurvikīm ||

	paurvikīṃ saṃsmaran jātiṃ brahmaivabhasate dvijaḥ |

	brahmābhāsena cājasram anantaṃ sukham aśnute ||

yamo 'pi |

	japed vāpy asya vāmīyaṃ pāvamānīr athāpi vā |

	kuntāpaṃ vālakhilyāṃś ca nivit praiṣaṃ vṛṣākapim ||

	hotṝn rudrān pitṝñ japtvā mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ ||

asya vāmīyam "asya vāmasya palitasya hotuḥ" iti dvipañcāśadṛcam | hotṝn cittiḥ srug ityādi | rudrān kadrudrāyeti pañca rudrasūktāni | pitṝn pareyuvāṃsam ityādīn | caturviṃśatāv api |

	agner manve 'nuvākaṃ tu japed enam anuttamam |

	siṃhe me manyur ity etam anuvākaṃ japed dvijaḥ ||

	japtvā pāpaiḥ pramucyeta bodhāyanavaco yathā |

	trimadhu trisuparṇaṃ ca nāciketatrayaṃ tathā ||

	nārāyaṇaṃ japet sarvaṃ mucyate  brahmahatyayā |

	yat kiṃcit pātakaṃ kuryād yat kiṃcedam ṛcaṃ japet ||

	haṃsaḥ śuciṣad ity etāṃ japed vāpi triyambakam |

	brāhmaṇāni ca kalpāṃś ca ṣaḍaṅgāni tathaiva ca ||

	ākhyātāni tathānyāni japtvā pāpaiḥ pramucyate |

	itihāsapurāṇāni devatāstavanāni ca ||

	japtvā pāpaiḥ pramucyeta dharmākhyānais tathā paraiḥ |

yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	śukriyāraṇyakajapo gāyatryāś ca viśeṣataḥ |

	sarvapāpaharā hy ete rudraikādaśinī tathā ||

śukriyaṃ viśvāni deva savitar iti | āraṇyakaṃ priyaṃ śukriyaṃ viśvāni deva savitar iti | āraṇyakaṃ priyaṃ vācaṃ prapadyata iti | etad dvayam api vājasaneyake paṭhyate | rudrā ekādaśakṛtvo 'bhyasyante yasyāṃ japakriyāyāṃ sā rudraikādaśinīty ucyate | atrir api |

	ekādaśaguṇān vāpi rudrān āvṛtya dharmavit |

	mahāpāpair api spṛṣṭo mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ||

purāṇe 'pi |

	pṛthivīṃ sasāgarāṃ yo hi kṛtsnāṃ śailavanānvitām |

	dadyāt kāñcanasaṃpūrṇāṃ haimīm oṣadhisaṃyutām ||

	tasyādhikaphalaṃ nūnaṃ rudrajāpī sakṛd dvijaḥ |

	tapas tapyati cātyarthaṃ sahasrābdāni saṃyamī ||

	na sa tatphalam āpnoti yaḥ sakṛd rudrajāpakaḥ |

	gavāṃ koṭipradānaṃ yaḥ karoti vidhivad gurau ||

	na sa tatphalam āpnoti yaḥ sakṛd rudrajāpakaḥ |

	yajñas tapaś ca dānāni tīrthāni vividhāni ca ||

	etāni rudrajāpasya kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm ||

atra saṃvartaḥ |

	svaramātrāvihīnaṃ tu pādākṣaravivarjitam |

	nyūnādhikaṃ vā kṛtvā tu ābhir gīrbhir itīrayet || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ japyāni**

**atha japyaprasaṅgād anyad api japyantaram ucyate**

tatra pulastyaḥ |

	kāmaḥ kāmapradaḥ kāntaḥ kāmapālas tathā hariḥ |

	ānando mādhavaś caiva kāmasaṃsiddhaye japet ||

	rāmaḥ paraśurāmaś ca nṛsiṃho viṣṇur eva ca |

	trivikramaś cetyādīni jpayāny arijigīṣubhiḥ ||

	vidyām abhyasyatāṃ nityaṃ japtavyaḥ puruṣottamaḥ |

	dāmodaraṃ bandhagato nityam eva japen naraḥ ||

	keśavaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣam aniśaṃ hi tathā japet |

	netrabādhāsu sarvāsu hṛṣīkeśaṃ bhayeṣu ca ||

	acyutaṃ cāmṛtaṃ caiva smared auṣadhakarmaṇi |

	saṅgrāmābhimukho gacchan saṃsmared aparājitam ||

	cakriṇaṃ gadinaṃ caiva śārṅgiṇaṃ khaḍginaṃ tathā |

	kṣemārthī pravasan nityaṃ dikṣu prācyādiṣu smaret ||

	ajitaṃ cādhipaṃ caiva sarvaṃ sarveśvaraṃ tathā |

	saṃsmaret puruṣo bhaktyā vyavahāreṣu sarvadā ||

	nārāyaṇaṃ sarvakālaṃ kṣutapraskhalanādiṣu |

	grahanakṣatrapīḍāsu devabādhāsu sarvadā ||

	dasyuvairinirodheṣu siṃhavyāghrādisaṅkaṭe |

	andhakāre tamisre ca narasiṃham anusmaret ||

	taraty akhiladurgāṇi tāpārto jalaśāyinam |

	garuḍadhvajānusmaraṇād viṣavīryaṃ praśāmyati ||

	snāne devārcane home praṇipāte pradakṣiṇe |

	kīrtayed bhagavannāma vāsudeveti tatparaḥ ||

	sthāpane vittadhānyāder apathyānne ca duṣṭaje |

	kurvīta tanmanā bhūtvā anantācyutakīrtanam ||

	nārāyaṇaṃ śārṅgadharaṃ śrīdharaṃ puruṣottamam |

	vāmanaṃ khaḍginaṃ caiva durḥsvapneṣu sadā smaret ||

	ekārṇavādau paryaṅkaśāyinaṃ ca naraḥ smaret |

	balabhadraṃ samṛddhyarthaṃ vīrakarmaṇi saṃsmaret ||

	jagatsūtim apatyārthīstuvan bhaktyā na sīdati |

	śrīśaṃ sarvābhyudayike karmaṇy āśu prakīrtayet ||

	ariṣṭeṣv apy aśeṣeṣu viśokaṃ ca sadā japet |

	marutprapatanāgnyambubandhanādiṣu mṛtyuṣu ||

	svatantraparatantreṣu vāsudevaṃ japed budhaḥ |

	svārthaśaktiyuktasya devadevasya cakriṇaḥ ||

	yad vābhirocate nāma tat sarvārtheṣu kīrtayet |

	sarvārthasiddhim āpnoti nāmnām ekārthatā yataḥ ||

	sarvāṇy etāni nāmāni parasya brahmaṇo 'nagha ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ japyāntaranirṇayaḥ **

**atha brahmayajñaḥ**

tatra manuḥ |

	apāṃ samīpe niyato naityakaṃ vidhim āsthitaḥ |

	sāvitrīm apy adhīyīta gatvāraṇyaṃ samāhitaḥ || iti |

yathā chadīṃṣi (?) na dṛśyante tathāraṇyaṃ gatvety arthaḥ | tathā ca śrutiḥ:"brahmayajñena yakṣyamāṇaḥ prācyāṃ diśi grāmād achadirdarśa (?) udīcyāṃ prāgudīcyāṃ vodita āditye" iti | ādityodayād ūrdhaṃ noditamātra ity arthaḥ | ata eva bṛhaspatiḥ |

	sa cārvāk tarpaṇāt kāryaḥ paścād vā prātar āhuteḥ |

	vaiśvadevavasāne vā nānyad arte nimittitaḥ || iti |

vaiśvadevaśabdenātra manuṣyayajñāntaṃ karma lakṣyate, na vaiśvadevamātraṃ tatraiva tasya vidhānāt | tathā ca śrutiḥ: "pañca vā ete mahāyajñāḥ satati pratāyante satati saṃtiṣṭhante devayajñaḥ pitṛyajño bhutayajño manuṣyayajño grahayajñaḥ" iti | satati saṃtatam anvaham ity arthaḥ | kūrmapurāṇe 'pi |

	yadi syāt tarpaṇād arvāg brahmayajñaḥ kṛto na hi |

	kṛtvā manuṣyayajñṃ vai tataḥ svādhyāyam ārabhet || iti |

"ṛte nimittitaḥ" ity anena sati nimitte kālāntare 'py aviruddha ity uktaṃ bhavati | ata eva śrutiḥ: "grāme manasā svādhyayam adhīyīta divā naktaṃ veti ha smāha śauca āhneya utāraṇye bala uta vācota tiṣṭhann uta vrajaṇṇ utāsīna uta śayāno 'dhīyītaiva svādhyāyaṃ taspasvī puṇyo bhavati" iti atrāhneyaḥ śauca ity āha smeti saṃbandhaḥ | adhyayane tu viśeṣam āha yogayājñavalkyaḥ | 

	pradakṣiṇaṃ samāvṛtya namaskṛtyopaviśya ca |

	darbheṣu darbhapāṇibhyāṃ saṃhatābhyāṃ kṛtāñjaliḥ ||

	svādhyāyaṃ tu yathāśakti brahmayajñārtham ācaret ||

śaunako 'pi |

	prāṇāyāmair dagdhadoṣaḥ śuklāmbaradharaḥ śuciḥ |

	yathāvidhy apa ācamya āhared darbhasaṃstaram ||

	pavitrapāṇiḥ kṛtvā tu upasthaṃ dakṣiṇottaram | iti |

adhīyīteti śeṣaḥ | tac cācamanaṃ taittirīyakaśrutau darśitam: "udita āditye dakṣiṇata upavīyopaviśya hastāv avinijya trir ācāmed dviḥ parimṛjya sakṛd upaspṛśya śiraś cakṣuṣī nāsike śrotre hṛdayam ālabhya yat trir ācāmati tena ṛcaḥ prīṇāti yad dviḥ parimṛjati tena yajūṃṣi yat sakṛd upaspṛśati tena sāmāni yat savyaṃ pāṇiṃ pādau prokṣati yac chiraś cakṣuṣī nāsike śrotre hṛdayam ālabhate tenātharvāṅgiraso brāhmaṇānītihāsān purāṇāni kalpān gāthā nārāśaṃsī prīṇāti darbhāṇāṃ mahad upastīryopasthaṃ kṛtvā prāṅāsīnaḥ svādhyāyam adhīyītāpāṃ vā eṣa oṣadhīnāṃ raso yad darbhāḥ sarasam eva brahma kurute dakṣiṇottarau pāṇī pādau kṛtvā sapavirāv om iti pratipadyate" iti | tato vyāhṛtīr anūcya sāvitrīṃ paccho 'rdharcaśaḥ sarvām iti brūyāt | tad āha śaunakaḥ: "oṃpūrvā vyāhṛtayaḥ savitrīm anvāha paccho 'rdharcaśaḥ sarvām" iti | tisra eva vyāhṛtayaḥ | tathā ca śrutiḥ: "trīn eva prāyuṅkta bhūr bhuvaḥ svar ity āhaitad vai vācaḥ satyaṃ yad eva vācaḥ satyaṃ tat prāyuṅktātha sāvitrīṃ gāyatrīṃ trir anvāha paccho 'rdharcaśo 'navānaṃ savitā śriyaḥ prasavitā śriyam evāpnoty atho prajñātayaiva pratipadā chandāṃsi pratipadyate" iti | pratipadārambhaḥ | anena vedādim ārabhya kramād uparyupary evādhīyītety uktaṃ bhavati | uktaṃ ca yogayājñavalkyena |

	ādāv ārabhya vedaṃ tu snātvopary upari kramāt |

	yad adhīte 'nvahaṃ śaktyā sa svādhyāya iti smṛtaḥ || iti |

svādhyāyo brahmayajñaḥ, "atha brahmayajñaḥ svādhyāyo brahmayajñaḥ" iti vajasaneyakaśruteḥ | atra viśeṣam āha śaunakaḥ |

	mandram eva bhavet prātar uccair mandhyandine sthite |

	uccair evāparāhṇe tu saṃdhyākāla upārabet ||

aurasaṃ mandram | gṛhyaśaunako 'pi: "dvyāvāpṛthivyoḥ saṃdhim īkṣamānaḥ saṃmīlya vā yathā yuktam ātmānaṃ manyeta tathā yukto 'dhīyīta" iti | viṣṇur api |

	oṃkāraṃ vyāhṛtīs tisraḥ sāvitrīṃ ca tad ity ṛcam |

	manasaitān anusmṛtya vedādīn samupakramet || iti |

atrādiśabdena purāṇādīnāṃ grahaṇam | ata eva yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	vedārtharvapurāṇāni seihāsāni śaktitaḥ |

	japayajñaprasiddhyarthaṃ vidyāṃ cādhyātmikīṃ japet ||

japayajño brahmayajñaḥ | śrutir api: "yad ṛco 'dhīte paya āhutibhir eva tad devāṃs tarpayati yd yajūṃṣi ghṛtāhutibhir yat sāmāni somāhutibhir yad atharvāṅgiraso madhvāhutibhir yad brāhmaṇānītihāsān purāṇāni kalpān gāthā nārāśaṃsīr medāhutibhir eva tad devāṃs tarpayati ta enaṃ tṛptā āyuṣā tejasā varcasā śriyā yaśasā brahmavarcasenānnādyena ca tarpayanti" iti | atra liṅgaguprāṇe viśeṣo darśitaḥ |

	svaśākhādhyayanaṃ vipra brahmayajña iti smṛtaḥ | iti |

yat tu śrutau: "yat svādhyāyam adhīyītaikām apy ṛcaṃ yajuḥ sāma vā tad brahmayajñaḥ saṃtiṣṭhate" iti, tad anadhyāyaviṣayam | ata eva āpastambaḥ: "atha yadi vāto vā vāyāt stanayed vā vidyoteta vāvasphūrjed vā ekāṃ varcam ekaṃ vā yajur ekaṃ vā sāvābhivyāharet bhūr bhuvaḥ suvaḥ satyaṃ tapaḥ śraddhāyāṃ juhomīti vaitat tenorhavāsyaitad (?) ahaḥ svādhyāya upātto bhavati" iti | etad apy anadhyāyamātropalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva manuḥ |

	naityake nāsty anadhyāyo brahmasatraṃ hi tat smṛtam |

	brahmāhutihutaṃ puṇyam anadhyāyavaṣaṭkṛtam ||

naityake nityasvādhyāye brahmayajña ity arthaḥ | śrutir api: "tasya vā etasya yajñasya dvāv anadhyāyau yad ātmāśucir yad deśaḥ" iti | dvāv evānadhyāyau nānya ity arthaḥ | evam adhītya "namo brahmaṇe" ity paridhānīyāṃ trir brūyāt | tathā ca śrutiḥ: "sa vā eṣa yajñaḥ sadyaḥ pratāyate sadyaḥ saṃtiṣṭhate tasya prāk sāyam avabhṛtho namo brahmaṇa iti parīdhānīyāṃ trir anvāhāya upaspṛśya gṛhāṇeti tato yat kiṃca dadāti sā dakṣiṇā" iti | evaṃ kurvataḥ phalam āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	yaṃ yaṃ kratum adhīyīta tasya tasyāpnuyāt phalam |

	trivṛttapūrṇapṛthivīdānasya phalam aśnute ||

śrutir api: "yāvantaṃ ha vā imāṃ vittasya pūrṇāṃ dadat svargaṃ lokaṃ jayati tāvantaṃ lokaṃ jayati bhūyāṃsaṃ cākṣayyaṃ cāpapunarmṛtyuṃ jayati brahmaṇaḥ sāyujyaṃ gacchati" iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ brahmayajñaḥ**

**atha tarpaṇam**

tatra śātātapaḥ |

	tarpaṇaṃ tu tataḥ kuryāt pratyahaṃ snātako dvijaḥ |

	devebhyaś ca ṛṣibhyaś ca pitṛbhyaś ca yathākramam || iti |

etac ca japānantaraṃ kāryam | tathā ca vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	ṛksāmātharvavedoktān japen mantrān yajūṃṣi ca |

	japitvaivaṃ tataḥ kuryād devarṣipitṛtarpaṇam || iti |

yat tu yogayājñavalkyen,

	japed vedādim ekāgras taṭe baddhāñjaliḥ śanaiḥ |

	brahmayajñaprasiddhyarthaṃ brahmavidyām athāpi vā ||

	japtvā vā praṇavaṃ śaktyā tatas tarpaṇam ācaret ||

iti brahmayajñānantaraṃ tarpaṇam uktam, tat prātarāhuter anantaraṃ brahmayajñakaraṇavixayam, tatrāpi tasya vidhānāt | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	sa cārvāk tarpaṇāt kāryaḥ paścād vā prātarāhuteḥ |

	vaiśvadevāvasāne vā nānayad arte (?) nimittataḥ || iti |

vaiśvadevāvasāne manuṣyayajñānte | tathā ca kūrmapurāṇe |

	yadi syāt tarpaṇād arvāg brahmayajñaḥ kṛto na hi |

	kṛtvā manuṣyayajñaṃ vai tataḥ svādhyāyam ācaret || iti |

tarpaṇaṃ prakṛtya śātātapaḥ |

	devarṣipitṛmanuṣyādīn svaśākhāvidhicoditān |

	ekaikāñjalinā tṛptiṃ prathamāntena vācayet || iti |

śrīviṣṇupurāṇe 'pi |

	śucir vastradharaḥ snāto devarṣipitṛtarpaṇam |

	teṣām eva tu tīrthena kurvīta susamāhitaḥ ||

	trir apaḥ prīṇanārthāya devānām apavarjayet |

	atharṣīṇāṃ yathānyāyyaṃ sakṛc cāpi prajāpateḥ ||

	pitṝṇāṃ prīṇanārthāya trir apaḥ pṛthivīpate |

vyāso 'pi |

	ekaikam añjaliṃ devā dvau dvau tu sanakādayaḥ |

	aśnanti pitaraḥ trīṃs triyas tv ekaikam añjalikam || iti |

atra yathāsvaśākhaṃ vyavasthā | yeṣāṃ tu śākhināmanāmnā taṃ teṣāṃ vikalpa eva | yat tu kūrmapurāṇe,

	anvārabdhena savyena pāṇinā dakṣiṇena tu |

	devarṣīṃs tarpayed dhīmān udakāñjalibhiḥ pitṝn || 

iti, tat pūrvokāñjalikaraṇena vikalpārtham | ata eva yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	ubhābhyām api hastābhyām aparājitadiṅmukhaḥ |

	saṃpṛktāṅguṣṭhakābhyāṃ tu savyopakramam eva vā ||

	tṛpyantv iti samuccārya tṛpyantām apy athāpi vā |

	vidhijñaḥ prakṣipet toyaṃ devādīnāṃ aśeṣataḥ || iti |

aparājitā dig aiśānī | yat tu vyāghreṇoktam,

	ubhābhyām api hastābhyām udakaṃ yaḥ prayacchati |

	sa mūḍho narakaṃ yāti kālasūram avākchirāḥ ||

iti, tac chrāddhādiviṣayam | ata eva kārṣṇājaniḥ |

	śrāddhe vivāhakāle ca pāṇinaikena dīyate |

	tarpaṇe tūbhayenaiva vidhir eva purātanaḥ || iti |

etac ca tarpaṇam udakādau ca kāryam | tathā ca gobilaḥ |

	nodakeṣu na pātreṣu na kruddho naikapāṇinā |

	nopatiṣṭhati tat toyaṃ yan na bhūmau pradīyate ||

ato bhūmāv eva deyam ity abhiprāyaḥ | śaṅkho 'pi |

	udake nodakaṃ kuryāt pitṛbhyas tu kadācana |

	uttīrya ca śucau deśe kuryād udakatarpaṇam || iti |

atra viśeṣam āha hārītaḥ |

	vasitvā vasanaṃ śuṣkaṃ sthale vistīrṇabarhiṣi |

	vidhijñas tarpaṇaṃ kuryān na pātreṣu kadācana ||

	pātrād vā jalam ādāya śubhe pātrāntare kṣipet |

	jalapūrṇe 'tha vā garte na sthale tu vivarhiṣi || iti |

pātraṃ cātra pitāmahenoktam |

	hemarūpyamayaṃ pātraṃ tāmraṃ kāṃsyasamudbhavam |

	ptṝṇāṃ tarpaṇe cātra mṛnmayaṃ tu parityajet ||

āstaraṇe tu viśeṣo yogayājñavalkyena darśitaḥ |

	āvāhya pūrvavan mantrair āstīrya ca kuśān bahūn |

	prāgagreṣu surān samyag dakṣiṇāgreṣu vai pitṝn ||

tarpayed iti śeṣaḥ | yatra punar aśuci sthalaṃ tatra jale dadyād ity āha viṣṇuḥ |

	sthale sthitvā jale yas tu prayacched udakaṃ naraḥ |

	nopatiṣṭhati tad vāri pitṝṇāṃ tan nirarthakam ||

	yatrāśucisthale vā syād udake devatāḥ pitṝn |

	tarpayet tu yathākāmam apsu sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam || iti |

anenaivābhiprāyeṇa kārṣṇājanir api |

	devatānāṃ pitṝṇāṃ ca jale dadyāj jalāñjalim |

	asaṃskṛtapramītānāṃ sthale dadyāj jalaṃ punaḥ || iti |

atrāñjaliniyamam āha bodhāyanaḥ |

	jalāñjalitrayaṃ dadyād ye cānye saṃskṛtā bhuvi |

	asaṃskṛtapramītānām ekam eva taṭe kṣipet ||

atrāyaṃ mantraḥ |

	agnidagdhāś ca ye jīvā ye 'py adagdhāḥ kule mama |

	bhūmau dattena tṛpyantu tṛptā yāntu parāṃ gatim || iti |

atrādhikāribhedena sthānaniyamo 'pi hārītena darśitaḥ |

	ārdravāsā jale kuryāt tarpaṇācamanaṃ japam |

	śuṣkavāsāḥ sthale kuryāt tarpaṇācamanaṃ japam ||

jale sthitveti śeṣaḥ | ata eva sumantuḥ |

	jalārdravāsāḥ sthalago yaḥ prayacchej jalāñjalim |

	vastraniścyotitaṃ pretā apavārya pibanti te ||

apavārya tadbhāginaṃ vārayitvety arthaḥ | likhito 'pi |

	śuṣkeṇāntarjale caiva bahir apy ārdravāsasā |

	snānaṃ dānaṃ japo homo niṣphalaṃ pitṛtarpaṇam ||

snānaṃ brāhmam | ata eva hārītaḥ |

	brāhmaṃ snānaṃ tathā dānaṃ devatāpitṛtarpaṇam |

	jalamadhye tu kurvāṇaḥ śuṣkavastro 'pi duṣyati ||

atra smṛtyantaram |

	khaḍgamauktikahastena kartavyaṃ pitṛtarpaṇam |

	maṇikāñcanadarbhair vā nāśuddhena kadācana ||

yogayājñavalkyo 'pi |

	anāmikādhṛtaṃ hema tarjanyāṃ rūpyam eva ca |

	kaniṣṭhikādhṛtaṃ khaḍgaṃ tena pūto bhaven naraḥ ||

marīcir api |

	vinā rūpyasuvarṇena vinā tāmratilais tathā |

	vinā mantraiś ca darbhaiś ca pitṝṇāṃ nopatiṣṭhati || iti |

naitad rajatādisamuccayārthaṃ vacanam | yat āhatur marīciyogayājñavalkyau |

	tilānām apy abhāve tu suvarṇaṃ rajatānvitam |

	tadabhāve niṣiñcet tu darbhair mantreṇa vā punaḥ || iti |

anena pitṛtarpaṇe tilānām āvaśyakatvam uktaṃ bhavati | ata eva vṛddhamanuḥ |

	yathā yodhasahasrebhyaḥ rājā gacchati dhārmikaḥ |

	evaṃ tilasamāyuktaṃ jalaṃ preteṣu gacchati ||

yat tu rāmāyaṇe,

	pādaśaucam anabhyaṅgaṃ tilahīnaṃ tu tarpaṇam |

	sarvaṃ tat trijaṭe tubhyaṃ yac ca śrāddham adakṣiṇam ||

iti, tat tilalābhe 'pi tadvihīnatarpaṇābhiprāyam, anyathā marīcivacanavirodhāt | tilagrahaṇe viseṣam āha marīciḥ |

	muktahastena dātavyaṃ na mudrāṃ tatra darśayet |

	vāmahaste tilā grāhyā muktahastas tu dakṣiṇaḥ || iti |

mudrā predeśinyaṅguṣṭhayoḥ saṃyogaḥ | etad anuddhṛtodakatarpaṇābhiprāyam uddhṛte viśeṣābhidhānāt | tathā ca yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	yady uddhṛtaṃ niṣiñcet tu tilān saṃmiśrayej jale |

	ato 'nyathā tu savyena tilā grāhyā vicakṣaṇaiḥ || iti |

anyathānuddhṛte | etad apy alomakāṅgābhiprāyam, anyathā doṣaśravaṇāt | tathā ca gobilaḥ |

	romasaṃsthāṃs tilān kṛtvā yas tu tarpayate pitṝn |

	pitaras tarpitās tena rudhireṇa jalena ca ||

	śuklais tu tarpayed devān manuṣyān śabalais tilaiḥ |

	pitṝṃs tu tarpayet  kṛṣṇais tarpayan sarvadā dvijaḥ || iti |

kūrmapurāṇe devarṣipitṛtarpaṇe viśeṣo darśitaḥ |

	devān brahmaṛṣīṃś caiva tarpayed akṣatodakaiḥ |

	pitṝn bhaktyā tilaiḥ kṛṣṇaiḥ svasūtroktavidhānataḥ || iti |

uktatilatarpaṇasya kvacid apavādam āha marīciḥ |

	saptamyāṃ ravivāre ca gṛhe janmadine sadā |

	bhṛtyaputrakalatrārthī na kuryāt tilatarpaṇam ||

purāṇe 'pi |

	pakṣayor ubhayo rājan saptamyāṃ niśi saṃdhyayoḥ |

	vidyāputrakalatrārthī tilān pañcasu varjayet ||

	nimbasya bhakṣaṇaṃ tailaṃ tilais tarpaṇam añjanam |

	saptamyāṃ naiva kurvīta tāmrapātre ca bhojanam || iti |

atra tarpaṇīyān āha satyavrataḥ |

	kṛtopavītī devebhyo nivītī ca bhavet tataḥ |

	manuṣyāṃs tarpayed bhaktyā brahmaputrān ṛṣīṃs tathā ||

	apasavyaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā savyaṃ jānv ācya bhūtale |

	darbhapāṇis tu vidhinā pretān saṃtarpayet tataḥ ||

purāṇe 'pi |

	devān devagaṇāṃś caiva sunīn munigaṇān api |

	pitṝn pitṛgaṇāṃś caiva nityaṃ saṃtarpayet tataḥ ||

matsyapurāṇe 'pi |

	devā yakṣās tathā nāgā gandharvāpsaraso 'surāḥ |

	sarpāḥ krūrāḥ suparṇāś ca taravo jambhakāḥ khagāḥ ||

	vāyvādhārā jalādhārās tathaivākāśagāminaḥ |

	nirādhārāś ca ye jīvā ye ca dharmaratās tathā ||

	teṣām āpyāyanāyaitad dīyate salilaṃ mayā |

	kṛtopavīti devebhyo nivītī ca bhavet tataḥ |

	manuṣyāṃs tarpayed bhaktyā brahmaputrān ṛṣīṃs tathā ||

	sanakaś ca sanandaś ca tṛtīyaś ca sanātanaḥ |

	kapilaś cāsuriś caiva voḍhaḥ pañcaśikhas tathā ||

	sarve te tṛptim āyāntu maddattenāmbunākhilāḥ |

	marīcim atrim aṅgirasaṃ pulastyaṃ pulahaṃ kratum ||

	pracetasaṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ ca bhṛguṃ nāradam eva ca |

	devabrahmaṛṣīn sarvāṃs tarpayed akṣatodakaiḥ ||

	apasavyaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā savyaṃ jānv ācya bhūtale |

	agniṣv āttās tathā saumyā haviṣmantas tathoṣmapāḥ ||

	pinākino barhiṣadas tathānye kāmacāriṇaḥ |

	tarpayet tān pitṝn bhaktyā satilodakacandanaiḥ ||

	darbhapāṇis tu vidhinā pretān saṃtarpayet tataḥ | iti |

yogayājñavalkyo 'pi |

	brahmāṇaṃ tarpayet pūrvaṃ viṣṇuṃ rudraṃ prajāpatim |

	devān chandāṃsi vedāṃś ca ṛṣīṃś caiva tapodhanān ||

	ācāryāṃś caiva gandharvān ācāryatanayāṃs tathā |

	saṃvatsaraṃ sāvayavaṃ devīr apsarasas tathā ||

	tathā devānugān nāgān sāgarān parvatān api |

	sarito 'tha manuṣyāṃś ca yakṣān rakṣāṃsi caiva hi ||

	piśācāṃś ca suparṇāṃś ca bhūtāny atha paśūṃs tathā |

	vanaspatīn auṣadhīś ca bhūtagrāmaṃ caturvidham ||

	savyaṃ jānu tato 'nvācya pāṇibhyāṃ dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ |

	talliṅgais tarpayen mantraiḥ sarvān pitṛgaṇāṃs tathā ||

	mātāmahāṃś ca satataṃ śraddhayā tarpayed budhaḥ || iti |

atra brahmā tṛpyatām iti prayogaḥ,

	anvārabdhena savyena pāṇinā dakṣiṇena tu |

	tṛpyatām iti sektavyaṃ nāmnā tu praṇavādinā || 

iti tenaiva devatātarpaṇānantaram abhidhānāt | śaunako 'pi |


        agnir viṣṇuḥ prajāpatiḥ brahmā vedā devā ṛṣayaḥ chandāṃsi oṃkāro 'tha vaṣṭkāro vyāhṛtayaḥ sāvitrī yajñā dyāvāpṛthivī anatrikṣam ahorātrāṇi sāṃkhyāḥ siddhāḥ samudrā nadyo girayaḥ kṣetrauṣadhivanaspatigandharvāpsaraso nāgā vayāṃsi gāvaḥ sādhyā viprā yakṣā rakṣāṃsi bhūtāny evamantāni | atha ṛṣayaḥ: śatarcino madhyamā gṛtsamado viśvāmitro vāmadevo 'trir bharadvājo vasiṣṭhaḥ pragādhāḥ pāvamānyaḥ kṣudrasūktā mahāsūktā iti | prācīnāvītī: sumantujaimini-vaiśampāyanapailasūtrabhāṣyabhāratamahābhāratadharmācāryāḥ, jānantivāhavigārgyagautamaśākalyavābhravyamāṇḍavyamāṇḍūkeyāḥ, gargī vācaknavī vaḍavā prācitheyī sulabhā maitreyī kaholaṃ kauṣītakaṃ mahākauṣītakaṃ bharadvājaṃ paiṅgaṃ suyajñaṃ saṅkhyāyanaṃ aitareyaṃ mahaitareyaṃ bāṣkalaṃ gārgyaṃ sujātavaktram audavāhiṃ mahaudavāhiṃ saujāmiṃ śaunakam āśvalāyanaṃ ye cānye ācāryās te sarve tṛpyantv iti pratipūruṣaṃ pitrṝṃs tarpayitvā | iti |

atrāpi pūrvavad agnis tṛpyatām iti prayogaḥ | atha vā kūrmapurānoktam |

	tataḥ saṃtarpayed devān ṛṣīn pitṛgaṇāṃs tathā |

	ādāv oṃkāram uccārya nāmno 'nte tarpayāmi ca || iti |

atha vā smṛtyantaroktam |

	tṛpyantv iti samuccārya tṛpyatām ity athāpi vā |

	vidhijñaḥ prakṣipet toyaṃ devādīnām aśeṣataḥ || iti |

atra tarpaṇīyeṣu yathāsvaśākhaṃ vyavasthā | ata eva satyavrataḥ |

	japtvānena vidhānena devarṣipitṛtarpaṇam |

	svaśākhāvihitaṃ kuryāt snānāṅgaṃ pṛthag eva hi ||

yajuḥśākhināṃ tu kāṇḍānukramaṇyāṃ kāṇḍarṣitarpaṇam uktam |

	atha kāṇḍaṛṣīn etān udkāñjalibhiḥ śuciḥ |

	avyagras tarpayen nityaṃ mantraiḥ parvāṣṭamīṣu ca || iti |

pitṛtarpaṇaṃ prakṛtya paiṭhīnasiḥ |

	apasavyaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā sthitvā ca pitṛdiṅmukhaḥ |

	pitṝn divyān adivyāṃś ca pitṛtīrthena tarpayet || iti |

divyā vasvādayaḥ | adivyāḥ svapitrādayaḥ | te ca dvivyās tenaiva darśitāḥ |

	dhruvo dharaś ca somaś ca āpaś caivānilo 'nalaḥ |

	pratyūṣaś ca prabhāsaś ca vasavo 'ṣṭau prakīrtitāḥ ||

	ajaikapād ahirbudhnyo virūpākṣaś ca raivataḥ |

	haraś ca bahurūpaś ca tryambakaś ca sureśvaraḥ ||

	sāvitraś ca jayantaś ca pitnākī cāparājitaḥ |

	ete rudrāḥ samākhyātā ekādaśa surottamāḥ ||

	indro dhātā bhagaḥ pūṣā mitro 'tha varuṇo 'ryamā |

	arcir vivasvān tvaṣṭā ca savitā viṣṇur eva ca ||

	ete ca dvādaśādityā devānāṃ pravarā matāḥ |

	ete 'tha divyāḥ pitaraḥ pūjyāḥ sarve prayatnataḥ || iti |

atra dhruvāya nama ity evaṃ prayogaḥ | ata eva yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	vasūn rudrāṃs tathādityān namaskārasamanvitān |

tarpayed iti śeṣaḥ | tataḥ svapitrādīṃs tarpayet | tatra viśeṣam āha satyavrataḥ |

	apasavyaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā savyaṃ jānv ācya bhūtale |

	darbhapāṇis tu vidhinā pretān saṃtarpayet tataḥ ||

kātyāyano 'pi |

	athādbhis tarpayed devān satilābhiḥ ptṝn api |

	namo 'nte tarpayāmīti ādāv om iti ca bruvan ||

paiṭhīnasir api |

	sanāmagotragrahaṇaṃ puruṣaṃ puruṣaṃ prati |

	tilodakāñjalīṃs trīṃs trīn uccair uccair vinikṣipet ||

yogayājñavalkyo 'pi |

	dakṣiṇe pitṛtīrthena jalaṃ siñced yathāvidhi |

	dakṣiṇenaiva gṛhṇīyāt pitṛtīrthaṃ samāhitaḥ ||

	savarṇebhyo 'ñjalir deyo vāsavarṇebhya eva ca |

	nāmagotrasvadhakārais tarpayed anupūrvaśaḥ || iti |

nāmādigrahaṇe viśeṣam āha bodhāyanaḥ |

	śarmāntaṃ brāhmaṇasyoktaṃ varmāntaṃ kṣatriyasya tu |

	guptāntaṃ caiva vaiśyasya dāsāntaṃ śūdrajanmanaḥ ||

	caturṇām api varṇānāṃ pitṝṇāṃ pitṛgotrataḥ |

	pitṛgotraṃ kumārīṇām ūḍhānāṃ bhartṛgorataḥ ||

evaṃ caivaṃ prayogo bhavati — om pitṝn śrīvatsagorān viṣṇuśarmanaḥ svadhā namas tarpayāmīti | evaṃ pitāmahādīṃś ca tarpayet | evam ekaikasyāñjalitrayaprasekaḥ | tato mātṝś śrīvatsagotrā gaṅgā dāyīḥ svadhā namas tarpayāmīti | evaṃ pitāmahīprapitāmahyau | tato mātāmahādīnām | tad uktaṃ satyavratena |

	pitṛbhyaḥ pratyahaṃ dadyāt tato mātṛbhya eva ca |

	tato mātāmahādīnāṃ pitṛvyasya sutasya ca ||

bodhāyano 'pi |


        prācīnāvītī — om pitṝn svadhā namas tarpayāmi | pitāmahān svadhā namas ta- | mātṝḥ svadhā namas ta- | pitāmahīḥ svadhā namas ta- | prapitāmahīḥ svadhā namas ta- | mātāmahān svadhā namas ta- | mātuḥ pitāmahān svadhā namas ta- | mātuḥ prapitāmahān svadhā namas ta- | mātāmahīḥ svadhā namas ta- | mātuḥ pitāmahīḥ svadhā namas ta- | mātuḥ prapitāmahīḥ svadhā namas ta- | om ācāryān svadhā namas ta- | ācāryapatnīḥ svadhā namas ta- | gurūn svadhā namas ta- | gurupatnīḥ svadhā namas ta- | sakhīn svadhā namas ta- | sakhipatnīḥ svadhā namas ta- | jñātīn svadhā namas ta- | jñātipatnīḥ svadhā namas ta- | amātyān svadhā namas ta- | amātyapatnīḥ svadhā namas ta- | sarvān svadhā namas tarpayāmi |

atra sarvatra nāmagotrādyanusaṃdheyam | uktam atra yogayājñavalkyena |

	talliṅgais tarpayen mantraiḥ sarvān pitṛgaṇāṃs tathā |

te ca mantrā tenaiva darśitāḥ |

	udīratām aṅgirasa āyantv ity ūrjam ity api |

	pitṛbhya iti ye ceha madhu vātā iti tṛcam ||

	pitṝn dhyāyan prasiñced vai japen mantrān yathākramam |

	tṛpyadhvam iti ca trir vai tataḥ prāñjalir ānataḥ ||

	namo va ity uktvā vai tato mātāmahān api |

	tarpayed ānṛśaṃsyārthaṃ dharmaṃ paramam āsthitaḥ || iti |

asyārthaḥ: udīratām iti mantrānte pitaro 'mukagotrā amukaśarmāṇas tṛpyadhvaṃ svadheti prathamaṃ tilodakāñjaliṃ ninayet | evam aṅgirasa āyantu na iti dvitīyatṛtīyamantrānte 'pi | tata ūrjaṃ vahantīḥ, pitṛbhyaḥ svadhāvibhyo, ye ceha pitaraḥ ity ekaikamantrānte pitāmahā anukagotrā amukaśarmāṇas tṛpyadhvaṃ svadheti pṛthak pṛthag añjaliṃ dadyāt | tata evam "madhu vātāḥ" ity ekaikamantrānte prapitāmahasya | evaṃ mātāmahādiṣv api | mantras tu "namo vaḥ" ity eka eva punaḥ punar āvartate | mātṛprabhṛtīnāṃ tu nāmādibhir eva dadyād ity evaṃ kaiścid vyākhyātam | jīvapitṛkasya tu viśeṣam āha yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	kavyavāho 'nalaḥ somo yamaś caivāryamā tathā |

	agniṣvāttāḥ somapāś ca tathā barhiṣado 'pi ca ||

	yadi syāj jīvapitṛka etān vidyāt tataḥ pitṝn |

	yebhyo vāpi pitā dadyāt tebhyo vāpi pradāpayet |

	etāṃś caiva pramītāṃś ca pramītapitṛko dvijaḥ ||

atra kavyavāhaṃ atpayāmīti prayogaḥ, "nāmānte tarpayāmi ca" iti smaraṇāt | atra purāṇam |

	pretebhyaś ca pṛthag dadyān manasā tatpadaṃ smaran |

	ātmano 'pi jalaṃ dadyād iti dvaipāyano 'bravīt ||

atrāvasānāñjalim āha kātyāyanaḥ: "pitṛvaṃśyā mātṛvaṃśyā ye cānye matta udakam arhanti tāṃs tarpayāmīty avasānāñjaliḥ" iti | tata kāmyodakaṃ dadyāt | viṣṇupurāṇe |

	idaṃ vāpi japed apsu dadyād ātmecchayā nṛpa |

	upakārāya bhūtānāṃ kṛtadevāditarpaṇaḥ ||

	devāsurās tathā yakṣā gandharvoragarākṣasāḥ |

	piśācā guhyakāḥ siddhāḥ kūśmāṇḍās taravaḥ khagāḥ ||

	jalecarā bhūnilayā vāyvādhārāś ca jantavaḥ |

	tṛptim etena yāntv āśu maddattenāmbunākhilāḥ ||

	narakeṣu samasteṣu yātanāsu ca ye sthitāḥ |

	teṣām āpyāyanāyaitad dīyate salilaṃ mayā ||

	ye 'vāndhavā vāndhavā ye ye 'nyajanmani bāndhavāḥ |

	te tṛptim akhilā yāntu ye cāsmatto 'mbukāṅkṣiṇaḥ ||

purāṇe 'pi |

	yatra kvacana saṃsthanāṃ (?) kṣuttṛṣṇopahatātmanām |

	teṣāṃ hi dattam akṣayyam idam astu tilodakam ||

	ye matkule luptapiṇḍāḥ putradāravivarjitāḥ |

	teṣāṃ hi dattam akṣayyam idam astu tilodakam ||

	mātṛvaṃśyā mṛtā ye ca pitṛvaṃśyās tathaiva ca |

	teṣāṃ hi dattam akṣayyam idam astu tilodakam || iti |

śrīviṣṇupurāṇe tu vistārāsamarthasya saṃkṣepatarpaṇam uktam |

	ābrahmastambaparyantaṃ jagat tṛpyatv iti bruvan |

	kṣipet payo 'ñjalīṃs trīṃs tu kurvan saṃkṣepatarpaṇam ||

evaṃ kurvataḥ phalam āha śaṅkhaḥ |

	snātaḥ saṃtarpaṇaṃ kṛtvā pitṝṇāṃ tu tilāmbhasā |

	pitṛlokam avāpnoti prīṇāti ca tathā pitṝn ||

purāṇe 'pi |

	evaṃ yaḥ sarvabhūtāni tarpayed anvahaṃ dvijaḥ |

	sa gacchet paramaṃ sthānaṃ tejomūrtim anāmayam || iti |

tathākaraṇe 'pi doṣas tatraiva darśitaḥ |

	devatāś ca munīṃś caiva pitṝn vai yo na tarpayet |

	devādīnām ṛṇī bhūtvā narakaṃ sa vrajaty adhaḥ ||

yogayājñavalkyo 'pi |

	nāstikyabhāvādyas tāṃs tu na tarpayati vai pitṝn |

	pibanti dehaniḥsrāvaṃ pitaro 'sya jalārthinaḥ || iti |

dehaniḥsrāvaṃ rudhiram | kātyāyano 'pi |

	chāyāṃ yatheccheccharadātapārtaḥ payaḥ pipāsuḥkṣudhito 'lam annam |

	bālo janitrīṃ jananī ca bālaṃ yoṣit pumāṃsaṃ puruṣaś ca yoṣām ||

	tathā sarvāṇi bhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca |

	viprād udakam icchanti sarve 'bhyudayakāṅkṣiṇaḥ ||

	tasmāt sadaiva kartavyam akurvan mahatainasā |

	yujyate brāhmaṇaḥ kurvan viśvam etad bibharti hi ||

tatra pitṛgādhām āha yamaḥ |

	api naskhakule (?) bhūyād yo no dadyāj jalāñjalim |

	nadīṣu bahutoyāsu śītalāsu viśeṣataḥ || iti |

viṣṇur api |

	kule 'smākaṃ sa jantuḥ syād yo no dadyāj jalāñjalim |

	nadīṣu bahutoyāsu śītalāsu viśeṣataḥ || iti |

ata eva hārītaḥ na sravantīr vṛthātikrāmed evaṃ hy āha |

	devāś ca pitaraś caiva kāṅkṣanti salilāñjalim |

	adatte tu nirāśāste prayānti hi yamālayam ||

atra yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	yāvad devān ṛṣīṃś caiva pitṝṃś cāpi na tarpayet |

	tāvan na pīḍayed vastraṃ yo na snāto bhaved dvijaḥ ||

	niṣpīḍayati yo vastraṃ snānavastram atarpite |

	nirāśāḥ pitaro yānti śāpaṃ datvā sudāruṇam || iti |

atas tarpaṇānantaraṃ niṣpīṣayed iti bhāvaḥ | atra viśeṣaḥ smṛtyantare darśitaḥ |

	vastraniṣpīḍitaṃ toyaṃ śrāddhe cocchiṣṭabhojanam |

	bhāgadheyaṃ śrutiḥ prāha tasmān niṣpīḍayet sthale || iti |

niṣpīḍanānantaraṃ yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	niṣpīḍya snānavastraṃ tu ācamya prayataḥ śuciḥ |

	devānām arcanaṃ kuryād brahmādīnām amatsaraḥ || iti |

ācamya sūryāyārghyaṃ datveti śeṣaḥ | tathā ca viṣṇupurāṇam |

	datvā kāmyodakaṃ samyag etebhyaḥ śraddhayānvitaḥ |

	ācamya ca tato dadyāt sūryāya salilāñjalim || iti |

atra viśeṣo nṛsiṃhapurāṇe darśitaḥ |

	tato 'rghyaṃ bhānave dadyāt tilapuṣpajalānvitam |

	utthāpya mūrdhaparyantaṃ haṃsaḥ śuciṣad uccaran ||

	jale devaṃ namaskṛtya tato gacched gṛhaṃ budhaḥ |

	pauruṣeṇa ca sūktena tato viṣṇuṃ samarcayet || iti |

gṛhaṃ gacched abhyukṣaṇam ādāyeti śeṣaḥ,

	trisaṃdhyaṃ vāgyato vāri guptam āhṛtya śodhayet |

	homopahārabhūgeha (?) dravyātmaparicārakān ||

iti gargasmaraṇāt ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ tarpaṇanirṇayaḥ**

**atha yamatarpaṇam**

tatra skandapurāṇe |

	kṛṣṇapakṣacaturdaśyām aṅgārakadinaṃ yadā |

	tadā snātvā śubhe toye tarpayed yamanāmabhiḥ || iti |

tāni nāmāni vṛddhamanunā darsitāni |

	yāṃ kāṃcit saritaṃ prāpya kṛṣṇapakṣe caturdaśīm |

	yamunāṃ ca viśeṣeṇa niyato niyatendriyaḥ ||

	yamāya dharmarājāya mṛtyave cāntakāya ca |

	vaivasvatāya kālāya sarvabhūtakṣayāya ca ||

	audumbarāya dadhnāya nīlāya parameṣṭhine |

	vṛkodarāya citrāya citraguptāya te namaḥ || iti |

tarpayed iti śeṣaḥ | atra yamāya nama ity evaṃ prayogaḥ | kṛṣṇatrayodaśyāṃ caturdaśyāṃ vā,

	"yamāya dharmarājāya mṛtyave cāntakāya ca |

	vaivasvatāya kālāya sarvabhūtakṣayāya ca |

ebhiḥ saptabhir namaskāramantraiḥ saptodakāñjalīn dadyāt sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate" iti gadyavyāsasmaraṇāt | atra viśeṣam āha vṛddhamanuḥ |

	ekaikasya tilair miśrāṃs trīṃs trīn kṛtvā jalāñjalīn |

	yāvajjanmakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tatkṣaṇād eva naśyati ||

skandapurāṇe |

	dakṣiṇābhimukho bhūtvā nilaiḥ svayaṃ samāhitaḥ |

	devatīrthena devatvāt tilaiḥ pretādhipāya ca ||

evaṃ kurvataḥ phalam āha vṛddhamanuḥ |

	ihajanmakṛtaṃ pāpam anyajanmakṛtaṃ ca yat |

	aṅgārakacaturdaśyāṃ tarpayaṃs tad vyapohati ||

yamo 'pi |

	yatra kvacana nadyāṃ hi snātvā kṛṣṇacaturdaśīm |

	saṃtarpya dharmarājaṃ ca mucyate sarvakilbiṣaiḥ || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ yamatarpaṇam**

**bhīṣmatarpaṇam**

atha mādhaśuklāṣṭamyāṃ bhīṣmatarpaṇaṃ smaranti | tathā ca purāṇam |

	śuklāṣṭamyāṃ tu māghasya dadyād bhīṣmāya yo 'ñjalim |

	saṃvatsarakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tatkṣaṇād eva naśyati ||

tatrāyaṃ mantraḥ |

	vaiyāghrapādagotrāya saṅkṛtipravarāya ca |

	gaṅgāputrāya bhīṣmāya pradāsye 'haṃ tilodakam |

	aputrāya dadāmy etat salilaṃ bhīṣmavarmaṇe || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ bhīṣmatarpaṇavidhiḥ**

**atha devatārcanam**

tatra hārītaḥ |

	kurvīta devatāpūjāṃ japayajñād anantaram |

	sthaṇḍile pratimāyāṃ vā jale 'gnau hṛdaye 'pi vā ||

japayajño brahmayajñaḥ | atra brahmayajñaṃ prakṛtya,

	japayajñasya siddhyarthaṃ vidyām ādhyātmikīṃ japet |

iti yājñavalkyasmaraṇāt | marīcir api |

	vidhāya devatāpūjāṃ prātarhomād anantaram |

	sthaṇḍile pratimāyāṃ vā vahnau vā hṛdayāmbuje ||

nṛsiṃhapurāṇe 'pi |

	jale devaṃ namaskṛtya tato gacched gṛhaṃ budhaḥ |

	pauruṣeṇa tu sūktena tato viṣṇuṃ samarcayet || iti |

atraiṣāṃ vikalpo veditavyaḥ | atra yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	aṅguṣṭhe caiva govindaṃ tu mahīdharam |

	madhyamāyāṃ hṛṣīkeśam anāmikāyāṃ trivikramam ||

	kaniṣṭhāyāṃ nyased viṣṇuṃ hastamadhye ca mādhavam |

	agnau hutaṃ ca dattaṃ ca devatārcanam eva ca ||

	hastanyāsaprabhāvena sarvaṃ bhavati cākṣayam || iti |

tac cārcanaṃ nāradenoktam |

	imam arthaṃ purā pṛṣṭo nārado bhagavān ṛṣiḥ |

	naranārāyaṇābhyāṃ ca tair munīndraś ca saṃgataiḥ ||

	nārāyaṇārcanavidhiṃ śrotuṃ no vaktum arhasi |

	dharmārthakāmāpavargān yena prāpnoti puṣkalān ||

	śrutvaitat sa ciraṃ dhyātvā sasmāra ca purātanam |

	kṣīrābdhau yac chrutaṃ pūrvaṃ puṣkarākṣamukhāc cyutam ||

	śṛṇvantu munayaḥ samyak puruṣottamapūjanam |

	yat kṛtvā munayaḥ sarve brahma nirvāṇam āpnuyuḥ ||

	snātvā yathoktavidhinā prāṅmukhaḥ śuddhamānasaḥ |

	svaśākhoktakriyāṃ kṛtvā hutvā caivādihotrakam ||

	kuryād ārādhanaṃ viṣṇor devadevasya cakriṇaḥ |

	apsv agnau hṛdaye sūrye sthaṇḍile pratimāsu ca ||

	ṣaṭsv eteṣu hareḥ samyag arcanaṃ munibhiḥ smṛtam |

	agnau kriyāvatāṃ devo divi devo manīṣiṇām ||

	pratimāsv alpabuddhīnāṃ yogināṃ hṛdaye hariḥ |

	āpo hy āyatanaṃ tasya tasmāt tāsu sadā hariḥ ||

	āpo hy āyatanaṃ tasya tasmāt tāsu sadā hariḥ |

	tasya sarvagatatvāc ca sthaṇḍile bhāvitātmanām ||

	ṛgvede pauruṣaṃ sūktam arcitaṃ guhyam uttamam |

	ānuṣṭubhasya sūktasya triṣṭubantasya devatā ||

	puruṣo yo jagadbījam ṛṣir nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ |

	prathamāṃ vinyased vāme dvitīyāṃ dakṣiṇe kare ||

	tṛtīyāṃ vāmapāde tu caturthī dakṣiṇe tathā |

	pañcamīṃ vāmajaṅghāyāṃ dakṣiṇasyāṃ tathottarām ||

	saptamīṃ vāmakaṭyāṃ tu dakṣiṇasyāṃ tathāṣṭamīm |

	navamīṃ nābhimadhye tu daśamīṃ hṛdi vinyaset ||

	ekādaśīṃ kaṇṭhadeśe dvādaśīṃ vāmabāhuke |

	trayodaśīṃ dakṣiṇe tu āsyadeśe caturdaśīm ||

	akṣṇoḥ pañcadaśīṃ nyasya ṣoḍaśīṃ mūrdhni vinyaset |

	yathātmani tathā deve nyāsakarma samācaret ||

	evaṃ nyāsaṃ tu kṛtvādau paścād devasya pūjanam |

	gandhamālyaiḥ surabhibhir ātmānaṃ cārcayed budhaḥ ||

	tataḥ pītaṃ samārādhya gandhapuṣpākṣataiḥ śubhaiḥ |

	ādyayāvahayed devam ṛcā tu puruṣottamam ||

	dvitīyayāsanaṃ dadyāt pādyaṃ caiva tṛtīyayā |

	caturthyārghyaṃ pradātavyaṃ pañcamyācamanīyakam ||

	ṣaṣṭhyā snānaṃ prakurvīta saptamyā vastram eva ca |

	yajñopavītam aṣṭamyā navamyā gandham eva ca ||

	daśamyā puṣpadānaṃ syād ekādaśyā tu dhūpakam |

	dvādaśyā ca tathā dīpaṃ trayodaśyā caruṃ tathā ||

	caturdaśyā namaskāraṃ pañcadaśyā pradakṣiṇam |

	ṣoḍaśyodvāsanaṃ kuryāc cheṣakarmāṇi pūrvavat ||

	snāne vastropavīte ca carāvācamanīyakam |

	hutvā ṣoḍaśabhir mantraiḥ ṣoḍaśāntāsya cāhutiḥ ||

	śeṣaṃ nivedayet tasmai dadyād ācamanaṃ tataḥ |

	tataḥ ṣoḍaśabhir mantrair dadyāt puṣpāṇi ṣoḍaśa ||

	tac ca sarvaṃ japed bhūyaḥ pauruṣaṃ sūktam uttamam |

	tataḥ prakakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā nārāyaṇam anāmayam ||

	śaṅkhacakragadāpāṇiṃ dhyātvā viṣṇuṃ samarcayet |

	ṣaṇmāsāt siddhim āpnoti evam eva samarcayan ||

	saṃvatsareṇa tenaiva sāyujyam adhigacchati |

	dhyeyaḥ sadā savitṛmaṇḍalamadhyavartī nārāyaṇaḥ sarasijāsanasaṃniviṣṭaḥ |

	keyūravān makarakuṇḍalavān kirīṭī hārī hiraṇmayavapur dhṛtaśaṅkhacakraḥ ||

kūrmapurāṇe 'pi |

	na viṣṇvārādhanāt puṇyaṃ vidyate karma vaidikam |

	tasmād anādimadhyāntaṃ nityam ārādhayed dharim ||

	tad viṣṇor iti mantreṇa sūktena puruṣeṇa vā |

	naitābhyāṃ sadṛśo mantro vedeṣūktaś caturṣv api ||

	atha vā devam īśānaṃ bhagavantaṃ sanātanam |

	ārādhayen mahādevaṃ bhāvapūto maheśvaram ||

	mantreṇa rudragāyatryā praṇavenātha vā punaḥ |

	īśānenātha vā rudrais tryambakeṇa samāhitaḥ ||

	tathoṃ namaḥ śivāyeti mantreṇānena vā japet || iti |

bodhāyano 'pi |


        athāto mahāpuruṣasyāhar ahaḥ paricaryāvidhiṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ | snātaḥ śuciḥ śucau deśe gomayenopalipya devasya pratikṛtiṃ kṛtvākṣatagandhapuṣpair yathālābham arcayitvā saha puṣpodakena mahāpuruṣam āvāhayet — oṃ bhūḥ puruṣam āvāhayāmi, oṃ bhuvaḥ puruṣaṃ āvāhayāmi, oṃ suvaḥ puruṣaṃ āvāhayāmi, oṃ bhūr bhuvaḥ suvaḥ puruṣam āvāhayāmi, ity āvāhya āyātu bhagavān mahāpuruṣa iti | atha svāgatenābhinandayati svāgatam anu cāgataṃ bhagavate mahāpuruṣāyaitad āsanam upakḷptam atrāstāṃ bhagavān mahāpuruṣa iti | atra kūrcaṃ dadāti | bhagavato 'yaṃ kūrco darbhamayas trivṛddharitaḥ suvarnas taṃ juṣasveti | atra snānādi kalpayati agrataḥ śaṅkhāya kalpayāmi cakrāya kalpayāmi dakṣiṇato gadāyai kalpayāmi vanamālāyai kalpayāmi paścimataḥ śrīvatsāya kalpayāmi garutmate kalpayāmi uttarataḥ śriyai kalpayāmi sarasvatyai kalpayāmi puṣṭyai kalpayāmi tuṣṭyai kalpayāmīti | atha sāvitryā pātram adbhiḥ prakṣālya tiraḥpavitram apa ānīya punas tenaivāpo 'bhimantrya sapavitreṇādityaṃ darśayet om ity ātamitoḥ | tāsām "trīṇi padā vicakrame" iti padyaṃ dadāti | atha vyāhṛtibhiḥ nirmālyaṃ vyapohya "idaṃ viṣṇur vicakrame" ity arghyaṃ dadyāt | "divo vā viṣṇo" ity ācamanīyam | athainaṃ snāpayati "āpo hiṣṭhā mayobhuvaḥ" iti tisṛbhiḥ, "hiraṇyavarṇāḥ śucayaḥ pāvakāḥ" iti catasṛbhiḥ, "pavamānaḥ suvarjanaḥ" ity etenanuvākena, brahmajajñānaṃ vāmadevyarcā yajuḥpavitreṇeti | athādbhis tarpayati — keśavaṃ tarpayāmi nārāyaṇaṃ mādhavaṃ govindaṃ viṣṇuṃ madhusūdanaṃ trivikramaṃ vāmanaṃ śrīdharaṃ hṛṣīkeśaṃ padmanābhaṃ dāmodaraṃ tarpayāmīti | daivatāni vastrayajñopavitācamanīyāni udakena vyāhṛtibhir datvā vyāhṛtibhiḥ pradakṣiṇam udakaṃ pariṣicya praṇavena vāso dadāti sāvitryā yajñopavītam, "idaṃ viṣṇuḥ" ity acamanīyam, "gandhadvārām" iti gandham, "irāvatī" ity akṣatam, "tad viṣṇoḥ" iti puṣpam, savitryā dhūpam, "uddīpyasva" iti dīpam, "devasya tvā savituḥ prasave 'śvinor bāhubhyāṃ pūṣṇo hastābhyāṃ bhagavate mahāpuruṣāya juṣṭaṃ caruṃ nivedayāmi" iti naivedyam, athāsmai dvādaśabhir nāmabhiḥ (keśavādibhir dvādaśa) puṣpāṇi dadyāt | tataḥ śaṅkhāya namaḥ cakrāya namaḥ gadāyai namaḥ vanamālāyai namaḥ śrīvatsāya namaḥ garutmate namaḥ śriyai namaḥ sarasvatyai namaḥ puṣṭyai namaḥ tuṣṭyai namaḥ iti | atha śiṣṭair gandhamālyair brāhmaṇān alaṃkṛtyātiśiṣṭair gandhamālyair ātmānam alaṃkṛtya, athainam ṛgyajuḥsāmātharvabhiḥ stutibhiḥ stuvanti | dhruvasūktaṃ japtvā puruṣasūktaṃ cāthānyāṃś ca vaiṣṇavān mantrān ity eke | oṃ bhūr bhuvaḥ suvar mahar oṃ bhagavate mahāpuruṣāya carum udvāsayāmīti carum udvāsya udvāsanakāle "oṃ bhūḥ puruṣam udvāsayāmi oṃ bhuvaḥ puruṣam udvāsayāmi oṃ suvaḥ puruṣam udvāsayāmi oṃ bhūr bhuvaḥ suvaḥ puruṣam udvāsayāmi" ity udvāsya prayātu bhagavān mahāpuruṣo 'nena haviṣā tṛpto vā punar āgamanāya punaḥ saṃdarśanāya ca iti | pratimāsthāneṣv apsu agnau vāvāhanavisarjanaṃ sarvaṃ samānaṃ mahat savastyayanam ity ācakṣate ity āha bhagavān bodhāyanaḥ || iti |

atra pūjānantaraṃ yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	evaṃ saṃpūjya deveśaṃ kṣaṇaṃ dhyātvā nirañjanam |

	tato 'valokayed arkaṃ haṃsaḥ śuciṣd ity ṛcā |

	sa yāti brahmaṇaḥ sadma dhyātvekṣetānayā tu yaḥ || iti |

evaṃ kurvataḥ phalam āha bhagavān |

	ye 'rcayanti sadā viṣṇuṃ śaṅkhacakragadādharam |

	sarvapāpavinirmuktā brahmāṇaṃ praviśanti te ||

viṣṇurahasye 'pi |

	iti viṣṇvarcanaṃ ye tu prakurvanti narā bhuvi |

	te yānti śāśvataṃ viṣṇor anantaṃ paramaṃ padam || iti |

atra vyāsaḥ |

	sarveṣām eva lokānāṃ gurur nārāyaṇo hariḥ |

	tasya saṃpūjanaṃ kāryaṃ sarvapāpaharaṃ hi yat || iti |

śivārcanaphalaṃ tu śivadharmaśāstre darśitam |

	yaḥ pradadyād gavāṃ lakṣaṃ dogdhrīṇāṃ vedapārage |

	ekāham arcayel liṅgaṃ tasya puṇyaṃ tato 'dhikam ||

	māse mase tu yo 'śnīyād yāvajjīvaṃ dvijottamān |

	yas tv arcayet sakṛl liṅgaṃ samam etan na saṃśayaḥ || iti |

tathākaraṇe 'pi doṣaḥ kūrmapurāṇe darśitaḥ |

	yo mohād atha vālasyād akṛtvā devatārcanam |

	bhuṅkte sa yāti narakān sūkareṣv iha jāyate ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ devatārcanam**

**devatāsnānādiviṣayāṇi**

athānyāny api devatāsnānādiviṣayāṇi vacanāni kānicil likhyante | tatra viṣṇudharme pulastyaḥ |

	gavāṃ śatasya viprāṇāṃ yad dattasya bhavet phalam |

	ghṛtaprasthena tad viṣṇor bhavet snānān na saṃśayaḥ ||

	bhūridyumnena saṃprāptā saptadvīpā vasundharā |

	ghṛtāḍhakena govindapratimāsnapanāt kila ||

	dvādaśyāṃ pañcadaśyāṃ vā gavyena haviṣā hareḥ |

	snāpanaṃ daityaśārdūla mahāpatakanāśanam ||

	ayane cottare prapte yaḥ snapayati keśavam |

	ghṛtaprasthena pāpaṃ sa sakalaṃ vai vyapohati ||

	kapilāṃ vipramukhyāya dadāty anudinaṃ hi yaḥ |

	ghṛtasnānaṃ hi devasya tasmin kāle samaṃ hi yate ||

	snāpyamānaṃ ca paśyanti ye ghṛtenotarāyaṇe |

	te yānti viṣṇusālokyaṃ sarvapāpavivarjitāḥ ||

	dadhyādīnāṃ vikārāṇāṃ kṣīrataḥ saṃbhavo yathā |

	tathaivāśeṣakāmānāṃ kṣīrasnāpanato hareḥ ||

nṛsiṃhapurāṇe 'pi |

	snāpya dadhnā sakṛd viṣṇuṃ nirmalaṃ priyadarśanam |

	viṣṇulokam avāpnoti sevyamānaḥ surottamaiḥ ||

yamo 'pi |

	devamālyāpanayanaṃ devāgārasamūhanam |

	snāpanaṃ sarvadevānāṃ gopradānasamaṃ smṛtam ||

nṛsiṃhapurāṇe |

	kuṅkumāgaruśrīkhaṇḍakardamair acyutākṛtim |

	ālipya bhaktyā rājendra kalpakoṭiṃ vased divi ||

śaṅkho 'pi: "candanakuṅkumamṛganābhibhir jātīphalavarjam anulepanaṃ samādadhyāt" iti | eteṣāṃ saṃbhava iti śeṣaḥ | padmapurāṇe 'pi |

	gandhebhyaś candanaṃ puṇyaṃ candanād agarur varaḥ |

	kṛṣṇāgarus tataḥ śreṣṭhaḥ kuṅkumaṃ tu tato varam ||

nṛsiṃhapurāṇe 'pi |

	aparyuṣitanicchidrair aspṛṣṭaiś cāpi jantubhiḥ |

	ātmārāmodbhavair vāpi puṣpaiḥ saṃpūjayed dharim ||

	daśa datvā suvarṇāni yat phalaṃ labhate naraḥ |

	tat phalaṃ labhate niṣṇor droṇapuṣpapradānataḥ ||

	doṇapuṣpasahasrebhyaḥ khādiraṃ puṣpam uttamam |

	khādirāt puṣpasāhasrāc chamīpatraṃ viśiṣyate ||

	śamīpatrasahasrād dhi bilvapatraṃ viśiṣyate |

	bilvapatrasahasrād dhi bakulaṃ puṣpam uttamam ||

	bakulāt puṣpasāhasrān nadyāvartaṃ viśiṣyate |

	nandyāvartasahasrād dhi karavīraṃ viśiṣyate ||

	karavīrasahasrebhyaḥ pālāśaṃ puṣpam uttamam |

	pālāśapuṣpasāhasrāt kuśapuṣpaṃ viśiṣyate ||

	kuśapuṣpasahasrād dhi vanamālā viśiṣyate |

	vanamālāsahasrād dhi campakaṃ puṣpam uttamam ||

	campakāt puṣpasāhasrād aśokaṃ puṣpam uttamam |

	aśokapuṣpasāhasrāt sevantīpuṣpam uttamam ¦|

	sevantīpuṣpasāhasrād gorjaṭāpuṣpam uttamam |

	gorjaṭāpuṣpasāhasrān mālatīpuṣpam uttamam ||

	mālatīpuṣpasāhasrāt saṃdhyāraktam anuttamam |

	saṃdhyāraktasahasrād dhi kundapuṣpaṃ viśiṣyate ||

	kundapuṣpasahasrād dhi mallikāpuṣpam uttamam |

	mallikāpuṣpasāhasrāj jātīpuṣpaṃ viśiṣyate ||

	jātīpuṣpasahasreṇa yo mālāṃ saṃprayacchati |

	viṣṇave vidhivad bhaktyā tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu ||

	kalpakoṭisahasrāṇi kalpakoṭiśatāni ca |

	vased viṣṇupure śrīmān viṣṇutulyaparākramaḥ ||

viṣṇurahasye 'pi |

	varṇānāṃ tu yathā vipraḥ tīrthānāṃ jāhnavī yathā |

	surāṇāṃ ca yathā viṣṇuḥ puṣpāṇāṃ mālatī tathā ||

	mālatyānudinaṃ devaṃ yo 'rcayed garuḍadhvajam |

	janmamṛtyujarārogair mukto 'sau muktim āpnuyāt ||

	dattamātraṃ hareḥ puṣpaṃ nirmālyaṃ bhavati kṣaṇāt |

	upabhuṅkte tv ahorātraṃ mālatyāḥ kusumaṃ hariḥ ||

	sugandhair mallikāpuṣpair arcayitvācyutaṃ naraḥ |

	sarvapāpavinirmukto viṣṇuloke mahīyate ||

	yo 'rcayet pāṭalīpuṣpaiḥ sarvapāpaharaṃ harim |

	sa puṇyātmā paraṃ sthānaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ vrajate 'malam ||

	sitaraktair mahāpuṇyaiḥ kusumaiḥ karavīrajaiḥ |

	arcayitvācyutaṃ yāti yatrāste garuḍadhvajaḥ ||

	gandhāḍhyair vimalai ramyaiḥ kusumaiḥ kubjakodbhavaiḥ |

	bhaktyābhyarcya hṛṣīkeśaṃ śvetadvīpaṃ vrajen naraḥ ||

	śubhraśuddhair mahāgandhaiḥ kusumaiḥ paṅkajodbhavaiḥ |

	adhokṣajaṃ samabhyarcya naro yāti hareḥ padam ||

	arcayitvā hṛṣīkeśaṃ kusumaiḥ ketakodbhavaiḥ |

	puṇyaṃ tadbhavanaṃ yāti keśavasya nirāmayam ||

	abhyarcya kundakusumaiḥ keśavaṃ kalmaṣāpaham |

	prayāti bhavanaṃ viṣṇor vanditaṃ municāraṇaiḥ ||

	āḍharūpikapuṣpair yaḥ pūjayej jagatāṃ patim |

	sa puṇyavān naro yāti viṣṇos tat paraṃ padam ||

	aśokakusumai ramyair janmaśokabhayāpaham |

	pūjayitvācyutaṃ devaṃ yāti viṣṇum anāmayam ||

	tilakasyojjvalaiḥ puṣpaiḥ saṃpūjya madhusūdanam |

	dhūtapāpo nirātaṅkaḥ kṛṣṇasyānucaro bhavet ||

	nīpārjunakadambaiś ca vakulaiś ca sugandhibhiḥ |

	abhyarcya keśavaṃ puṣpaiḥ puṇyakṛd viṣṇulokabhāk ||

	agastyāmbumayaiḥ puṣpaiḥ kiṃśukaiḥ sumanoharaiḥ |

	samabhyarcya hṛṣīkeśaṃ janmaduḥkhād vimucyate ||

	śatadūrvāmayaiḥ puṣpais tathā kāśakuśodbhavaiḥ |

	bhūdharaṃ samalaṃkṛtya viṣṇulokaṃ vrajen naraḥ ||

	mārutaṃ ketakaṃ puṣpaṃ tathā dāmanakaṃ punaḥ |

	uttamāṃ tu hareḥ prītiṃ karoti śatavārṣikīm ||

	puropavanajaiḥ puṣpair alaṃkṛtya janārdanam |

	yat phalaṃ prāpyate puṃbhir āraṇyais triguṇaṃ tataḥ ||

	bhaktyā dattaṃ phalaṃ puṣpaṃ patraṃ dūrvāṅkuraṃ jalam |

	acirāt pratigṛhṇāti bhaktigrāhyo hi keśavaḥ ||

viṣṇudharmeṣv api |

	bhaktyā dūrvāṅkuraiḥ pumbhiḥ pūjitaḥ parameśvaraḥ |

	harir dadāti hi phalaṃ sarvayajñaiḥ sudurlabham ||

viṣṇurahasye pi |

	sakṛd abhyarcya govindaṃ bilvapatreṇa mānavaḥ |

	muktibhāgī nirātaṅkaḥ kṛṣṇasyānucaro bhavet ||

	ye 'rcayanti śamīpatraiḥ pramādenāpi keśavam |

	te prasanne hṛṣīkeśe narā yānti parāṃ gatim ||

	hariṃ bhṛṅgārajenāpi ye 'rcayanti sureśvaram |

	te 'pi muktā jarārogair narā yānti hareḥ padam ||

	ye 'rcayanti tam ālasya patraiḥ pāpaharaṃ harim |

	dhūtapāpmācyutāvāsaṃ prayāti sukṛtī naraḥ ||

	tulasī kṛṣṇagaurā syāt tayābhyarcya janārdanam |

	naro yāti tanuṃ tyaktvā vaiṣṇavīṃ śāśvatīṃ gatim ||

padmapurāṇe 'pi |

	sugandhatulasīpatraiḥ pratimāyāḥ samantataḥ |

	nicchidram āstared yas tu so 'nantaṃ phalam āpnuyāt ||

	puṣpajātiṣu sarvāsu sauvarṇaṃ puṣpam uttamam |

	tṛṭimātrapradānāt tu śakrārdhāsanam āpnuyāt ||

tṛṭimātram aṇumātram | viṣṇurahasye 'pi |

	svarṇe lakṣādhikaṃ puṇyaṃ mālā koṭiguṇādhikā |

	dattā bhavati kṛṣṇāya narair bhaktisamanvitaiḥ ||

	evaṃ śubhaiḥ sadā puṣpaiḥ pūjanīyo janārdanaḥ |

	niṣiddhair duḥkhadair devaṃ nārcayeta kathaṃcana || iti |

niṣiddhāny api tatraiva darśitāni |

	na śuṣkaiḥ pūjayed devaṃ kusumair na mahīṃ gataiḥ |

	na viśīrṇadalaiḥ siṣṭair nāśubhair nāvikāsibhiḥ ||

	pūtigandhogragandhāni āmlagandhāni varjayet ||

padmapurāṇe 'pi |

	kīṭakeśāpaviddhāni śīrṇaparyuṣitāni ca |

	bhagnapatraṃ ca na grāhyaṃ krimiduṣṭaṃ na cāharet |

	varjayed ūrṇanābhena vāsitaṃ yadi śobhanam |

	sthalajaṃ noddharet puṣpaṃ chedayej jalajaṃ na tu ||

	yāni spṛṣṭāni cāspṛśyair lokāyukaiś ca varjayet ||

hārīto 'pi |

	snānaṃ kṛtvā tu ye kecit puṣpaṃ gṛhṇanti vai dvijāḥ |

	devatās taṃ na gṛhṇanti na ca gṛhṇanti vai dvijāḥ ||

	pitaras taṃ na gṛhṇanti bhasmībhavati kāṣṭhavat ||

etan madhyāhnasnānābhiprāyam | dvitīyabhāgaṃ prakṛtya,

	samitpuṣpakuśādīnāṃ na kālaḥ parikīrtitaḥ |

iti dakṣasmaraṇāt | viṣṇurahasye 'pi |

	ye 'rakapuṣpais trilokeśam arcayanti janārdanam |

	tebhyaḥ kruddho 'kṣayaṃ duḥkhaṃ krodhād viṣṇuḥ prayacchati ||

	unmattakena ye mūḍhāḥ pūjayanti trivikramam |

	unmādaṃ dāruṇaṃ teṣāṃ dadāti garuḍadhvajaḥ ||

	kāñjanāramaiḥ puṣpair ye 'rcayanty asuradviṣam |

	dāridryaṃ duḥkhabahulaṃ tebhyo viṣṇuḥ prayacchati ||

	girikarṇikayā viṣṇuṃ ye 'rcayanty abudhā janāḥ |

	teṣāṃ kulakṣayaṃ ghoraṃ kurute madhusūdanaḥ || iti |

atra hārītaḥ |

	mahiṣākṣakaṇaṃ dārusallakaṃ sāgaraṃ madam |

	śaṅkhajātiphalaṃ śrīmat priyā dhūpā harer ime ||

	ghṛtatailair vinā kiṃcid dīpārthaṃ na samāharet ||

saṃvarto 'pi |

	devāgāre dvijānāṃ ca datvā dīpaṃ catuṣpathe |

	medhāvī jñānasaṃpannaś cakṣuṣmān jāyate naraḥ ||

bhaviṣyottare 'pi |

	prajvālya devadevasya karpūreṇa tu dīpakam |

	aśvamedham avāpnoti kulaṃ caiva samuddharet ||

padmapurāṇe 'pi |

	naivedyapātraṃ vakṣyāmi keśavāya mahātmane |

	hairaṇyaṃ rājataṃ kāṃsyaṃ tāmraṃ mṛṇmayam eva vā ||

	pālāśaṃ padmapatraṃ vā pātraṃ viṣṇor atipriyam |

	haviḥ śālyodanaṃ divyam ājyayuktaṃ saśarkaram ||

	naivedyaṃ devadevāya yāvakaṃ pāyasaṃ tathā |

	naivedyavastvalābhe tu phalāni vinivedayet ||

	phalānām apy abhāve tu tṛṇagulmaiṣadhīr api |

	oṣadhīnām alābhe tu toyāny api nivedayet ||

	tadabhāve tu sarvatra mānasaṃ paramaṃ smṛtam ||

varāhapurāṇe 'pi |

	praṇamya daṇḍavad bhūmau namaskāreṇa yo 'rcayet |

	sa yāṃ gatim āpnoti na tāṃ kratuśatair api ||

nṛsiṃhapurāṇe 'pi |

	namaskāreṇa caikena aṣṭāṅgena hariṃ vrajet | iti |

aṣṭāṅgalakṣaṇaṃ purāṇe darsitam |

	urasā sirasā dṛṣṭyā manasāpi dhiyāpi ca |

	padbhyāṃ karābhyāṃ vācā ca praṇāmo 'ṣṭāṅga ucyate ||

atra brahmā |

	viṣṇor vimānaṃ yaḥ kuryāt sakṛd bhaktyā pradakṣiṇam |

	aśvamedhasahasrasya phalaṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ ||

purāṇe 'pi |

	agniṣṭomasahasrais tu vājapeyaśatair api |

	tat phalaṃ labhate devi viṣṇor naivedyabhakṣaṇāt ||

	hṛdi rūpaṃ mukhe nāma naivedyam udare hareḥ |

	dhārodakaṃ ca nirmālyaṃ mastake yasya so 'cyutaḥ || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ devatāsnānādiviṣayāṇi**

**atha śivārcanam**

tatra bodhāyanaḥ |


        athāto mahādevasyāhar ahaḥ paricaryāvidhiṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ | snātaḥ śuciḥ same deśe gomayenopalipya pratikṛtiṃ kṛtvākṣatagandhapuṣpair yathālābham arcayitvā saha puṣpodakena mahādevam āvāhayet | oṃ bhūr mahādevam āvāhayāmi oṃ bhuvar mahādevam āvāhayāmi oṃ suvar mahādevam āvāhayāmi oṃ bhū bhuvaḥ suvaḥ mahādevam āvāhayāmi | āyātu bhagavān mahādeva iti | atha svāgatenābhinandayati svāgatam anu cāgataṃ bhagavate mahādevāya etad āsanam upakḷptaṃ atrāstāṃ bhagavān mahādeva iti | atra kūrcaṃ dadāti bhagavato 'yaṃ kūrco darbhamayas trivṛd dharitaḥ suvarṇas taṃ juṣasveti | atra sthānāni kalpayati agrato brahmaṇe kalpayāmi viṣṇave kalpayāmi, dakṣiṇataḥ skandāya kalpayāmi vināyakāya kalpayāmi, paścimataḥ śūlāya kalpayāmi mahākālāya kalpayāmi, uttarata umayai kalpayāmi nandikeśvarāya kalpayāmi iti kalpayitvā sāvitryā pātram abhimantrya prakṣālya tiraḥpavitram apa ānīya punas tenaivābhimantrya saha pavitreṇādityaṃ darśayet om ityātamitoḥ | tāsāṃ tvaritarudreṇa pādyaṃ dadyāt | praṇavenārghyam | atha vyāhṛtibhir nirmālyaṃ vyapohya uttarataś caṇḍīśvarāya namaḥ iti | athainaṃ snāpayati "āpo hiṣṭhā mayobhuvaḥ" iti tisṛbhiḥ "hiraṇyavarṇāḥ" iti catasṛbhiḥ "pavamānaḥ svarjanaḥ" ity etenānuvākena | snāpayitvādbhis tarpayati bhavaṃ devaṃ tarpayāmi śarvaṃ devaṃ tarpayāmi īśānaṃ devaṃ tarpayāmi paśupatiṃ devaṃ tarpayāmi rudraṃ devaṃ tarpayāmi ugraṃ devaṃ tarpayāmi bhīmaṃ devaṃ tarpayāmi mahāntaṃ devaṃ tarpayāmi iti tarpayitvā | athaitāni vastrayajñopavītācanīyāny udakena vyāhṛtibhir datvā vyāhṛtibhiḥ pradakṣiṇam udakaṃ pariṣicya namas te rudra manyava iti gandhaṃ dadyāt | īśānaṃ tvā bhuvanānām adhiśriyaṃ ity akṣatān dadyāt | sāvitryā ghūpam, uddīpyakheti dīpaṃ devasya tvā savituḥ prasave 'śvinor bāhubhyāṃ pūṣṇo hastābhyāṃ bhagavate mahādevāya juṣṭaṃ caruṃ nivedayāmīti naivedyam | athāṣṭabhir (?) nāmabhir aṣṭau puṣpāṇi dadyāt bhavāya devāya namaḥ śarvāya devāya namaḥ īśānāya devāya namaḥ paśupataye devāya namaḥ rudrāya devāya namaḥ ugrāya devāya namaḥ bhīmāya devāya namaḥ mahate devāya namaḥ brahmaṇe namaḥ viṣṇave namaḥ skandāya namaḥ vināyakāya namaḥ mahākālāya namaḥ umāyai namaḥ durgāya namaḥ nandikeśvarāya nama iti | caruśeṣeṇāṣṭabhir nāmabhir aṣṭāhutīr juhoti bhavāya devāya svāhetyādibhiḥ | atha śiṣṭair gandhamālyair brāhmaṇāna alaṃkṛtyātmānaṃ cālaṃkṛtya | athainam ṛgyajuḥsāmātharvābhiḥ stutīnta (?) sahasrāṇi sahasraśa ity anuvākaṃ japtvānyāṃś ca raudrān mantrān yathāśaktīty eke | oṃ bhūr bhuvaḥ suvar mahar oṃ bhagavate mahādevāya caturm udvāsayāmīti carum udvāsya udvāsanakāle oṃ bhūr mahādevam udvāsayāmi oṃ bhuvaḥ mahādevam udvāsyāmi oṃ suvar mahādevam udvāsyāmi oṃ bhūr bhuvaḥ suvar mahādevam udvāsayāmi |


        	prayātu bhagavān īśaḥ sarvalokaparāyaṇaḥ |


        	anena haviṣā tuṣṭaḥ punar āgamanāya ca || iti |


        pratimāsthāneṣv apsv agnau vā āvāhanavisarjanavarjaṃ sarvaṃ samānaṃ mahatsv asty ayanam ity ācakṣate mahatsv asty ayanam ity ācakṣata ity āha bhagavān bodhāyanaḥ | iti |

tvaritarudra iti sarvo vai rudra ity anuvākena | evaṃ kurvataḥ phalam āha purāṇe nandikeśvaraḥ |

	yaḥ pradadyād gavāṃ lakṣaṃ dogdhrīṇāṃ vedapārage |

	ekāham arcayel liṅgaṃ tasya puṇyaṃ tato 'dhikam ||

	māse māse tu yo 'śnīyād yāvajjīvaṃ dvijottamān |

	yas tv arcayet sakṛl liṅgaṃ samam etan na saṃśayaḥ || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ śivārcanavidhiḥ**

**atha śivasnānādiviṣayāṇi **

tatra śivadharme nandikeśvaraḥ |

	kalpakoṭisahasrais tu yat pāpaṃ samjpārjitam |

	ghṛtasnānena tat sarvaṃ dahaty agnir ivendhanam ||

	varṣakoṭisahasrais tu yat pāpaṃ samupārjitam |

	ghṛtābhyaṅgena liṅgasya dahet sarvaṃ na saṃśayaḥ ||

	kṛṇāṣṭamyāṃ ghṛtasnānaṃ kṛtvā liṅge sakṛn naraḥ |

	triḥsaptakulam uddhṛtya śivaloke mahīyate ||

	nairantaryeṇa yo māsaṃ ghṛtasnānaṃ samācaret |

	sa trisaptakulopeto labhate padam aiśvaram ||

	ayutaṃ yo gavāṃ dadyād dogdhīṇāṃ vedapārage |

	vastrahemādiyuktānāṃ kṣīrasnānasya tat phalam ||

	dadhnā tu snāpayel liṅgaṃ sakṛd bhaktyā tu yo naraḥ |

	sarvapāpavinirmukto viṣṇuloke mahīyate ||

	dadhnā tu snāpayel liṅgaṃ kṛṣṇāṣṭamyām upoṣitaḥ |

	kulasaptakam uddhṛtya śivaloke mahīyate ||

	madhunā snāpayitvā tu sakṛd bhaktyā tu vai naraḥ |

	pāpakañcukam uddhṛtya vahniloke mahīyate ||

	snānam ikṣurasenāpi yo liṅge sakṛd ācaret |

	labhed vaidyādharaṃ lokaṃ sarvakāmasamanvitam ||

	vastrapūtena toyena yo liṅgaṃ snāpayet sakṛt |

	sarvakāmasutṛptātmā vāruṇaṃ lokam āpnuyāt ||

	kuśodakena yo liṅgaṃ sakṛt snāpayate naraḥ |

	kāñcanena vimānena brahmaloke mahīyate ||

	gandhacandanatoyena snāpayet sakṛd īśvaram |

	gandharvalokam āsādya gandharvaiś ca supūjyate ||

	puṣpodakena sāvitraṃ kauberaṃ hemavāriṇā |

	ratnodakena cāpy aindraṃ lokaṃ prāpya sa modate ||

	kapilāpañcagavyena vidhinā sakṛ ācaret |

	snānaṃ śataguṇaṃ proktam itareṣāṃ na saṃśayaḥ ||

	snānaṃ śataphalaṃjñeyam abhyaṅgaṃ pañcaviṃśatiḥ |

	phalānāṃ dve sahasre tu mahāsnānaṃ prakīrtitam ||

	vāsāṃsi suvicitrāṇi sāravanti mṛdūni ca |

	dhūpitāni śive dadyād vikeśāni navāni ca ||

	yāvat tadvastratantūnāṃ parimāṇaṃ vidhīyate |

	tāvad varṣasahasrāṇi rudraloke mahīyate ||

	trivṛtaṃ śuklapītaṃ vā paṭṭasūtrādinirmitam |

	datvopavītaṃ rudrāya bhaved vedāntapāragaḥ ||

	liṅgasya lepanaṃ kuryād divyagandhaiḥ sugandhibhiḥ |

	varṣakoṭiśataṃ divyaṃ śivaloke mahīyate ||

	gandhānulepanāt puṇyaṃ dviguṇaṃ candanasya tu |

	candanād agaror jñeyaṃ puṇyam aṣṭaguṇānvitam ||

	kṛṣṇāgaror viśeṣeṇa dviguṇaṃ phalam iṣyate |

	tasmāc chataguṇaṃ puṇyaṃ kuṅkumasya vidhīyate ||

	candanāgarukarpūraiḥ ślakṣṇapiṣṭaiḥ sakuṅkumaiḥ |

	liṅgaṃ paryāptam ālipya kalpakoṭiṃ vased divi ||

	saṃvījya tālavṛntena divyagandhair vilepitam |

	varṣakoṭisahasrāṇi vāyuloke mahīyate ||

	māyūraṃ vyajanaṃ datvā śivāyātīva śobhanam |

	varṣakoṭiśataṃ tatra rudraloke mahīyate ||

	puṣpair araṇyasaṃbhūtaiḥ patrair vā girisaṃbhavaiḥ |

	aparyuṣitanicchidraiḥ prokṣitair jantuvaritaiḥ ||

	ātmārāmodbhavair vāpi puṣpaiḥ saṃpūjayec chivam |

	puṣpaātiviśeṣeṇa bhavet puṇyaṃ viśeṣataḥ ||

	arkapuṣpe tu ekasmin śivāya vinivedite |

	śataṃ datvā suvarṇānāṃ yat phalaṃ tad avāpnuyāt ||

	arkapuṣpasahasrebhyaḥ karavīraṃ viśiṣyate |

	karavīrasahasrebhyo bilvapatraṃ viśiṣyate ||

	bilvapatrasahasrebhyaḥ padmam ekaṃ viśiṣyate |

	tathā padmasahasrebhyo vakapuṣpaṃ viśiṣyate ||

	bakapuṣpasahasrebhyaś caikaṃ duttūrakaṃ varam |

	duttūrakasahasrebhyo bṛhatīpuṣpam uttamam ||

	bṛhatīpuṣpasāhasrād droṇapuṣpaṃ viśiṣyate |

	droṇapuṣpasahasrebhyo hy apāmārgaṃ viśiṣyate ||

	apāmārgasahasrebhyaḥ kuśapuṣpaṃ viśiṣyate |

	kuśapuṣpasahasrebhyaḥ śamīpuṣpaṃ viśiṣyate ||

	śamīpuṣpasahasrebhyaḥ śrīman nīlotpalaṃ varam |

	sarvāsāṃ puṣpajātīnāṃ pravaraṃ nīlam utpalam ||

	nīlotpalasahasreṇa yo mālāṃ saṃprayacchati |

	śivāya vidhivad bhaktyā tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu ||

	kalpakoṭisahasrāṇi kalpakoṭiśatāni ca |

	vasec chivapure śrīmān śivatulyaparākramaḥ ||

	śamīpuṣpaṃ bṛhatyāś ca kusumaṃ tulyam ucyate |

	karavīrasamā jñeyā jātīvijayapāṭalāḥ ||

	śvetamandārakusumaṃ sitapadmasamaṃ bhavet |

	nāgacampakapunnāgā duttūrakasamāḥ smṛtāḥ ||

	duttūrakena yo liṅgaṃ sakṛt pūjayate naraḥ |

	sa golakṣaphalaṃ prāpya śivaloke mahīyate ||

	bṛhatīkusumair bhaktyā yo liṅgaṃ sakṛd arjayet |

	gavām ayutadānasya phalaṃ prāpya divaṃ vrajet ||

	mallikotpalapadmāni jātīpunnāgacampakāḥ |

	aśokaś caiva mandārakarṇikārabakāni ca ||

	karavīrārkaduttūraśamīnāgarakesarāḥ |

	kuśāpāmārgakusumakādambadroṇajair api ||

	puṣpair etair yathālābhaṃ yo naraḥ pūjayec chivam |

	sa yat phalam avāpnoti tad ekāgramanāḥ śṛṇu ||

	sūryakoṭipratīkāśair vimānaiḥ sārvakālikaiḥ |

	puṣpamālāparikṣiptair gītavāditranāditaiḥ ||

	tantrīmadhuravādyaiś ca svacchandagamanālayaiḥ |

	rudrakanyāsamākīrṇair devadānavadurlabhaiḥ ||

	dodhūyamānaś camaraiḥ stūyamānaḥ surāsuraiḥ |

	gacchec chivapuraṃ divyaṃ yatra vā rucitaṃ bhavet ||

	śivasyopari yaḥ kuryāt sughanaṃ puṣpamaṇṭapam |

	śobhitaṃ puṣpamālādyair āpīḍāntaṃ pralambitaiḥ ||

	atyāścaryair mahāyānair divyapuṣpopaśobhitaiḥ |

	sarvaiḥ parivṛtaḥ śrīmān gacchec chivapuraṃ sukham ||

	truṭimātraṃ tu yo dadyād dhema liṅgasya mūrdhani |

	indrasyārdhāsane tāvad yāvad indrāś caturdaśa ||

	evam evānusāreṇa phalaṃ jñeyaṃ samāsataḥ |

	sarveṣāṃ maṇipadmānāṃ makuṭārthe viśeṣataḥ ||

	svayam utpāṭya puṣpāṇi yaḥ svayaṃ pūjayec chivam |

	tāni sākṣāt pragṛhṇāti tadbhaktyā satataṃ śivaḥ ||

	alābhe vāpi puṣpāṇāṃ patrāṇy api nivedayet |

	patrāṇām apy alabhe tu tṛṇagulmauṣadhīr api ||

	oṣadhīnām alābhe tu bhaktyā bhavati pūjitaḥ |

	kānanāni kadambāni rātrau deyāni śambhave ||

	divā śeṣāṇi puṣpāṇi divā rātrau ca mallikāḥ |

	nirgandhāny ugragandhāni kusumāni vivarjayet ||

	gandhavanty api patrāṇi yāni tāni vivarjayet |

	gandhahīnam api grāhyaṃ pavitraṃ yat kuśādikam ||

	kīṭakeśopaviddhāni śīrṇaparyuṣitāni ca |

	svayampatitapuṣpāṇi tyajed upahatāni ca ||

	mukulair nārcayed devam apakvaṃ na nivedayet |

	kṛṣṇāgarumalo dhūpas tuṣāgnir iva kāñcanam ||

	śodhayet pāpasaṃyujtaṃ puruṣaṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ |

	kṛṣṇāgarusakarpūrair dhūpaṃ dadyān maheśvare ||

	nairantaryeṇa māsārdhaṃ tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu |

	kalpakoṭisahasrāṇi kalpakoṭiśatāni ca ||

	bhuṅkte śivapure bhogāṃs tasyānte ca mahīpatiḥ |

	gugguluṃ ghṛtasaṃyuktaṃ sākṣād gṛhṇāti śaṅkaraḥ ||

	māsārdhamātradānena śivaloke mahīyate |

	śive kṛṣṇacaturdaśyāṃ yaḥ sājyaṃ gugguluṃ dahet ||

	aparādhasahasraikam ihāmutra kṛtaṃ dahet |

	dve sahasre phalānāṃ tu mahiṣājyasya gugguloḥ ||

	dagdhvā tam ājyasaṃmiśraṃ śivatulyaḥ prajāyate |

	ghṛtadīpapradānena śivāya śatayojanam ||

	yāmyaṃ tadālayaṃ hitvā vimānaiḥ sūryasaṃnibhaiḥ |

	sa tasya devadevasya gāṇāpatyaṃ labhen naraḥ ||

	śālīnāṃ taṇḍulaprasthaṃ kuryād annaṃ susaṃskṛtam |

	śivāya tac caruṃ dadyāc caturdaśyāṃ viśeṣataḥ ||

	yāvantas taṇḍulāḥ tasmin naivedye parisaṃkhyayā |

	tāvadyugasahasrāṇi rudraloke mahīyate ||

	guḍakhaṇḍaghṛtānāṃ ca bhakṣāṇāṃ ca nivedite |

	ghṛtena pācitānāṃ ca dānāc chataguṇaṃ phalam ||

	majjakāpānakānāṃ ca bhakṣārdhaṃ phalam iṣyate |

	tadardhaṃ salilasyāpi vāsitasya viśeṣataḥ ||

	mātuluṅgaphalādīni pakvāni vinivedayet |

	śivāya tatphalaṃ tasya yadbhakṣāṇāṃ nivedane ||

	pañcasaugandhikopetaṃ yas tāmbūlaṃ nivedayet |

	śivāya gurave caiva tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu ||

	sugandhidehas tejasvī sarvāvayavasundaraḥ |

	varṣakoṭiśataṃ divyaṃ śivaloke mahīyate ||

	śivasya purato dadyād darpaṇaṃ cāru nirmalam |

	paryaṅkaśobhitaṃ kṛtvā śvetamālyair alaṃkṛtam ||

	candrāṃśunirmalaḥ śrīmān subhagaḥ kāmarūpadhṛt |

	kalpāyutasahasrāṇi rudraloke mahīyate ||

	sa yāṃ gatim avāpnoti na tāṃ kratuśatair api |

	kṛtvā pradakṣiṇaṃ bhaktyā śivasyāyatane naraḥ |

	aśvamedhasahasrasya sukhena labhate phalam ||

liṅgapurāṇe 'pi |

	pradakṣiṇaṃ tu yaḥ kuryāt sapraṇāmaṃ samantataḥ |

	savyāpasavyanyāyena mṛdugatyā śucir naraḥ ||

	pade pade 'śvamedhasya yajñasya phalam āpnuyāt | iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ śivasnānādiviṣayāṇi**

**atha pañca mahāyajñāḥ**

tatra saṃvartaḥ |

	tataḥ pañca mahāyajñān kuryād ahar ahar dvijaḥ |

	na hāpayeta tān prājñaś śrūyante hi śrutāv api ||

tato devapūjānantaram ity arthaḥ,

	pauruṣeṇa tu sūktena tato viṣṇuṃ samarcayet |

	vaiśvadevaṃ tataḥ kuryād balikarma tathaiv ca ||

iti nārasiṃhapurāṇasmaraṇāt | yamo 'pi |

	pañca sūnā gṛhasthasya vartante 'har ahar sadā |

	khaṇḍinī peṣiṇī cullī jalakumbha upaskaraḥ ||

	etā hi vāhayan vipro badhyate vai muhur muhuḥ |

	etāsāṃ pāvanārthāya pañca yañjāḥ prakalpitāḥ || iti | \
sūnā hiṃsāsthānāni, "atha sūnāṃ vyākhyāsyāmo jaṅgamasthāvarādīn prāṇinaḥ sūdayantīti sūnāḥ" iti hārītasmaraṇāt | khaṇḍiny ulūkhalādiḥ | peṣiṇī dṛṣadādiḥ | cullī pākasthānam | jalakumbha udakabhāṇḍam | upaskaraḥ śūrpādiḥ | etā nirvāhayan tat tat kāryaṃ prāpayan vadhyate pāpena saṃyujyate ity arthaḥ | atra yady api nimittaśravaṇān naimittikatvaṃ pratibhāti, tathāpi nityanimittatvān nityataiveti | ata eva śaṅkhaḥ |

	pañca sūnā gṛhasthasya cullī peṣaṇy upaskaraḥ |

	khaṇḍanī codakumbhaś ca tasya pāpasya śāntaye ||

	pañcayajñavidhānaṃ tu gṛhī nityaṃ na hapayet |

vyāso 'pi |

	āpady api ca kaṣṭāyāṃ pañca yajñān na hāpayet |

te ca yajñā yamena darśitāḥ |

	adhyāpanaṃ brahmayajñaḥ pitṛyajñas tu tarpaṇam |

	homo daivo balir bhauto nṛyajño 'tithipūjanam || iti |

adhyāpanam adhyayanaṃ (?) japalakṣaṇaṃ brahmayajñaḥ,

	yas tu śrutijapaḥ prokto brahmayajñas tu sa smṛtaḥ |

iti kātyāyanasmaraṇāt | tarpaṇaṃ pitṛtarpaṇaṃ pitṛśrāddhaṃ pitṛyajñaḥ | yad āha manuḥ |

	ṛṣayaḥ pitaro devā bhūtāny atithayas tathā |

	āśāsate kuṭumbibhyas tebhyaḥ kāryaṃ vijānatā ||

	svādhyāyenārcayetarṣīn homair devān yathāvidhi |

	pitṝn śrāddhena nṝn annair bhūtāni balikarmaṇā || iti |

atha vā kātyāyanoktaṃ draṣṭavyam |

	adhyāpanaṃ brahmayajñaḥ pitṛyajñas tu tarpaṇam |

	homo daivo balir bhauto nṛyajño 'tithipūjanam ||

	śrāddhaṃ vā pitṛyajñaḥ syāt pitryo balir athāpi vā || iti |

atra yathāsvaśākhaṃ vyavasthā | śrāddham atra nityaśrāddham | tathā ca kūrmapurāṇam |

	ekaṃ tu bhojayed vipraṃ pitṝn uddiśya santatam |

	nityaśrāddhaṃ tad uddiṣṭaṃ pitṛyajño gatipradaḥ || iti |

anenādaivaṃ śrāddham ity uktaṃ bhavati | uktaṃ ca manunā |

	ekam apy āśayed vipraṃ pitrarthaṃ pāñcayajñike |

	na caivātrāśayet kaṃcid vaiśvadevaṃ prati dvijaḥ || iti |

pāñcayajñike pañcayajñāṅgabbhūte | apiśabdāt sati vibhave bahūn api | ata eva mārkaṇḍeyapurāṇam |

	kuryād ahar ahaḥ śrāddham ann ādyenodakena vā |

	pitṝn uddiśya viprāṃs tu bhojayed vipram eva vā || iti |

atra viśeṣam āha hārītaḥ: 

	nityaśrāddham adaivaṃ syād ardhyapiṇḍādivarjitam | iti |

pracetā api |

	nāmantraṇaṃ na homaṃ ca nāhvānaṃ na visarjanam |

	na piṇḍadānaṃ na svadhā nitye kuryād dvijottamaḥ ||

	upaveśyāsanaṃ datvā saṃpūjya kusumādibhiḥ |

	nirdiśya bhojayitvā tu kiṃcid datvā visarjayet ||

purāṇe 'pi |

	nityaśrāddhaṃ tu yan nāma daivahīnaṃ tad ucyate |

	tat tu ṣāṭpuruṣaṃ jñeyaṃ dakṣināpiṇḍavarjitam ||

vyāso 'pi |

	nityaśrāddhe 'rdhyagandhādyair dvijān abhyarcya śaktitaḥ |

	sarvān pitṛgaṇān samyak sahaivoddiśya bhojayet ||

	āvāhanasvadhākārapiṇḍāgnaukaraṇādikam |

	nityaśrāddhe tyajed etān bhojyam annaṃ prakalpayet |

	datvā tu dakṣiṇāṃ śaktyā namaskārair visarjayet ||

	ekam apy āśayed vipraṃ ṣaṇṇām apy anvahaṃ gṛhī ||

atra matsyapurānoktaṃ draṣṭavyam |

	yady ekaṃ bhojayed vipraṃ trīn uddiśya pitṝṃs tathā |

atrānukalpam āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	ekam apy āśayed vipraṃ pitṛyajārthasiddhaye |

	athaivaṃ nāsti ced anyo bhoktā bhojyam athāpi vā ||

	apy uddhṛtya yathāśakti kiṃcid annaṃ yathāvidhi |

	pitṛbhya idam ity uktvā svadhākāram udāharet ||

tac cānnaṃ brāhmaṇāya dadyāt | ata eva pitṛyajñaṃ prakṛtya kūrmapurāṇam |

	uddhṛtya vā yathāsakti kiṃcid annaṃ samāhitaḥ |

	vedatattvārthaviduṣe dvijāyaivopapādayet || iti |

tarrāpy asāmarthye manūktam |

	dadyād ahar ahaḥ śrāddham annādyenodakena vā |

	payomūlaphalair vāpi pitṛbhyaḥ prītim āharan || iti |

homo daiva iti homo vaiśvadevaḥ, sa devayajña ity arthaḥ | tathā ca kūrmapurāṇe |

	śālāgnau laukike vātha jale bhūmyām athāpi vā |

	vaiśvadevas tu kartavyo devayajñaḥ sa vai smṛtaḥ || iti |

śālāgnir gṛhyāgniḥ | tatra bodhāyanaḥ: "ahar ahar devebhyaḥ svāhākuryād ā kāṣṭhād athainaṃ devayajñaṃ samāpnoti" iti | ā kāṣṭhad ity annābhāvaviṣayam | ata eva pracetāḥ: "tasmād ahar ahar juhuyād annābhāve kenacid ā kāṣṭhād devebhyaḥ" iti | balir bhauta iti baliharaṇaṃ sa bhūtayajña ity arthaḥ | tathā ca kūrmapurāṇe |

	devebhyaś ca hutād annac cheṣād bhūtabaliṃ haret |

	bhūtayajñaḥ sa vijñeyo bhūtidaḥ sarvadehinām ||

hārīto 'pi: "vāstupālabhūtebhyo baliharaṇam ahutaḥ" iti | ahuto bhūtayajñaḥ | tatrāpy annābhāve bodhāyanoktam: "ahar ahar bhūtebhyo baliṃ hared ā puṣpebhyo 'thainaṃ bhūtayajñaṃ samāpnoti" iti | nṛyajño 'titipūjanam iti, atithipūjanam atithibhyo 'nnadānaṃ sa manuṣyayajña ity arthaḥ,

	atithibhyo 'nnadānaṃ tu nṛyajñaḥ sa tu pañcamaḥ|

iti yamasmaraṇāt | hārīto 'pi: "yad devebhyo juhoti devalokaṃ tenābhiyajati yat pitṛbhyaḥ pitṛlokaṃ tena yat svādhyāyam adhīte ṛṣilokaṃ tena yad bhūtebhyo baliṃ harati bhūtalokaṃ tena yad brāhmaṇāṃś tarpayati manuṣyalokaṃ tena | tasmād annaṃ pitṛbho datvodīkṣetā godohanāt" iti | mārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe 'pi |

	anityaṃ hi sthito yasmāt tasmād atithir ucyate |

	tasmiṃs tṛpte nṛyajñārthān mucyetarṇād gṛhāśramī ||

atra viśeṣam āha nārāyaṇaḥ |

	niyujyaikam anekaṃ vā śrotriyaṃ prāṅmukhaṃ sadā |

	nivīto tadgatamanā ṛṣīn dhyāyan samāhitaḥ ||

	āsanaṃ cārghyadānaṃ ca bhukte cācamanaṃ tataḥ |

ṛṣīn sanakādīn, teṣāṃ manuṣyatvāt | kārṣṇājanir api |

	manuṣyāṇāṃ tathā kuryāt tarpaṇaṃ pratyahaṃ dvijaḥ |

	hanteti hantakāraṃ tu gṛhasthaḥ pratyahaṃ yajet ||

hanteti kriyate yasmin sa hantakāraḥ | hantety uccārya yajed ity arthaḥ | ata eva kātyāyanaḥ |

	svāhākāravaṣaṭkāranamaskārā divaukasām |

	svadhākāraḥ pitṝṇāṃ tu hantakāras tathā nṛṇām ||

hantetikaraṇaṃ hantakāra ity arthaḥ | atrānukalpam āha nārāyaṇaḥ |

	aśaktāv annam uddhṛtya hantety evaṃ prakalpayet | iti |

bodhāyano 'pi: "ahar ahar brāhmaṇebhyo 'nnaṃ dadyād ā mūlaphalaśākebhyo 'thainaṃ manuṣyayajñaṃ samāpnoti" iti | mukhyakalpānantaraṃ kārṣṇājanir api |

	bhikṣāṃ vā puṣkalaṃ vāpi hantakāram athāpi vā |

	asaṃbhave sadā dadyād udapātram athāpi vā ||

dadyād atithaya iti śeṣaḥ | ata eva manuṣyayajñaṃ prakrtya kūrmapurāṇe |

	hantakāram athāgraṃ vā bhikṣāṃ vā śaktito dvijaḥ |

	dadyād atithaye nityaṃ budhyeta parameśvaram || iti |

bhikṣādilakṣaṇaṃ tu śātātapenoktam |

	grāsamātraṃ bhaved bhikṣā puṣkalaṃ tu caturguṇam |

	puṣkalāni ca catvāri hantakāraṃ vidur budhāḥ ||

manur api |

	grāsamātraṃ bhaved bhikṣā agraṃ grāsacatuṣṭayam |

	agraṃ caturguṇīkṛtya hantakāro vidhīyate || iti |

yadā tu pitṛyajñe bhikṣādāne ca brāhmaṇālābhaḥ tadā pratipattiniyamaḥ kūrmapurāṇe darśitaḥ |

	sarveṣām apy alābhe tu dattaṃ gobhyo nivedayet | iti |

evaṃ ca manvādibhir vaiśvadevabaliharaṇe eva devayajñabhūtayajñāv iti darśitam | āpastambena tu mantrabhedāt saṃjñābhedāt pṛthag evaitad yajñadvayam uktam ity uktaṃ tadbhāṣye | atra bodhāyanaḥ |

	pravāsaṃ gacchato yasya gṛhe kartā na vidyate |

	pañcānāṃ mahatām eṣāṃ sa yajñaiḥ saha gacchati ||

	pravāse kurute caitān yad annam upapadyate |

	na ced utpadyate cānnam adbhir etān samāpayet || iti |

atra kālaniyamam āha dakṣaḥ |

	pañcame ca yathābhāge saṃvibhāgo yathārhataḥ |

	pitṛdevamanuṣyāṇāṃ bhūtānāṃ copadiśyate || iti |

saṃvibhāgo 'nnasya | aṣṭadhā vibhaktasyāhnaḥ pañcamabhāge | ata eva viṣṇuḥ |

	madhyāhne tv atha saṃprāpte baliṃ kṛtvātmano gṛhe |

	devapitṛmanuṣyāṇāṃ śiṣṭaṃ bhuñjīta vāgyataḥ || iti |

evaṃ kurvataḥ phalam āha hārītaḥ |

	devān pitṝn ṛṣīṃś caiva bhūtāni brāhmaṇāṃs tathā |

	tarpayan vidhinā vipro brahmabhūyāya kalpate || iti |

śambhur api |

	yat phalaṃ somayāgena prāpnoti dhanavān dvijaḥ |

	samyak pañcamahāyajñair daridras tad avāpnuyāt ||

athākaraṇe doṣo gargeṇa darśitaḥ |

	sūnānirṇiktadoṣā ye sarve te vṛṣalāḥ smṛtāḥ |

	na teṣām adhikāro 'sti kvacid dharme durātmanām ||

vṛṣalaḥ śūdraḥ | vyāso 'pi |

	pañcayajñāṃs tu yo mohān na karoti gṛhāśramī |

	tasya nāyaṃ ca na paro loko bhavati dharmataḥ ||

viṣṇupurāṇe |

	devādiniśvāsahataṃ śarīraṃ yasya veśmani |

	na tena saṅkaraṃ kuryād gṛhāsanaparicchadaiḥ || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ pañcamahāyajñāḥ**

**atha vaiśvadevavidhiḥ**

tatra nārāyaṇaḥ |

	sabhāryas tu śuciḥ snāto vidhinācamya vāgyataḥ |

	praviśya susamiddhe 'gnau vaiśvadevaṃ samācaret || iti |

susamiddhe 'gnāv avaidike vaidike vā | tathā ca śātātapaḥ |

	laukike vaidike vāpi hutvotsṛṣṭe jale kṣitau |

	vaiśvadevas tu kartavyaḥ pañcasūnāpanuttaye ||

vaidike vaivāhike | yad āha manuḥ |

	vaivāhike 'gnau kurvīta gṛhyakarma yathāvidhi |

	pañcayajñavidhānaṃ ca paktiṃ cānvāhikī gṛhī || iti |

viseṣaś caturviṃśatau darśitaḥ |

	prātarhomaṃ tu nirvartya samuddhṛtya hutāśanāt |

	śeṣaṃ mahānase kṛtvā tatra pākaṃ samācaret || iti |

atha vā laukike 'gnau pākaḥ | tad āha aṅgirāḥ |

	śālāgnau tu paced annaṃ laukike vāpi nityaśaḥ || iti |

śālāgnir gṛhyāgniḥ | yadā tu laukike pākas tadā tasminn eva homaḥ | tad uktaṃ kūrmapurāṇe |

	yadi syāl laukike pākas tato 'nnaṃ tatra hūyate |

	śālāgnau tatra ced annaṃ vidhir eṣa sanātanaḥ || iti |

anenaivābhiprāyeṇa āpastambo 'pi: "aupāsane pacane vā ṣaḍbhir ādyaiḥ pratimantraṃ hastena juhuyāt" iti | atra pacane veti yasya sarvādhānaṃ tadviṣayam eveti vyākhyātaṃ tadbhāṣye | tad uktaṃ ca viṣṇunā |

	ādhānād agnihotrasya āvasathyāt tu bāhyataḥ |

	yasminn agnau paced annaṃ tatra homo vidhīyate || iti |

yasya sarvādhānaṃ tasyāvasathyād bāhyataḥ pṛthag agnihotrasyābhāvāt gṛhyāgnyabhāvena yasmin laukike 'gnau vā pākas tatraiva homa ity arthaḥ | so 'pi katham ity apekṣite śaunakaḥ | "atha sāyaṃprātaḥ siddhasya haviṣyasya juhuyād agnihotradevatābhyaḥ somāya vanaspataye 'gnīṣomābhyāṃ dyāvāpṛthivībhyāṃ dhanvataraya indrāya viśvebhyo devebhyo brahmaṇe svāheti | atha baliharaṇam" iti | haviṣyasya haviryogyasyety arthaḥ | agnihotradevatābhyaḥ sūryāgniprajāpatibhya iti yāvat | āpastambo 'pi: "aupāsane pacane vā ṣaḍbhir ādyaiḥ pratimantraṃ hastena juhuyāt | ubhayataḥ pariṣecanaṃ yathā purastāt" iti | ādyaiḥ agnaye svāhetyādisviṣṭakṛdantaiḥ | ubhayataḥ karmādāv ante cety arthaḥ | gṛhyakātyāyano 'pi: "vaiśvadevād annāt paryukṣya svāhākārair juhuyād brahmaṇe prajāpataye gṛhebhyaḥ kāśyapāyānumataye" iti | gautamo 'pi: "agnāv agnir dhanvantarir viśvedevāḥ prajāpatiḥ sviṣṭakṛd iti homāḥ" iti | atra yathāsvaśākhaṃ vyavasthā,

	saṃskṛtānnair haviṣyair vā haviṣyavyañjanānvitaiḥ |

iti smaraṇāt | kātyāyano 'pi |

	uddhṛtya havir āsicya haviṣyeṇa ghṛtādinā |

	svaśākhāvidhinā hutvā taccheṣeṇa baliṃ haret || iti |

atra havir uddhṛtya haviṣyeṇa ghṛtādināsicyābhighārya (?) tena haviṣā hutveti saṃbandhaḥ | atrādiśabdo dadhyādiparigrahārthaḥ | ata eva vyāsaḥ |

	juhuyāt sarpiṣābhyaktaṃ tailakṣāravivarjitam |

	dadhyaktaṃ payasāktaṃ vā tadabhāve 'mbunāpi vā ||

yadā tu haviṣyadravyālābas tadā viśeṣaś caturviṃśatimate darśitaḥ |

	alābhe yena kenāpi phalaśākodakādibhiḥ (?) |

	payodadhighṛtaiḥ kuryād vaiśvadevaṃ sruveṇa tu ||

	hastenānnādibhiḥ kuryād adbhir añjalinā jale | iti |

yena kenāpi karaṇenety arthaḥ | atrāpi yad aśanīyaṃ tenaiva homaḥ | tad uktaṃ pariśiṣṭe |

	śākaṃ (?) vā yadi vā patraṃ mūlaṃ vā yadi vā phalam |

	saṃkalpayed yadāhāre tenāgnau juhuyād api || iti |

atra āpastambokto viśeṣaḥ | 

	uttānena tu hastena aṅguṣṭhāgreṇa pīḍitam |

	saṃhatāṅgulipāṇis tu vāgyato juhuyād dhaviḥ ||

kātyāyano 'pi |

	yo 'narciṣi juhoty agnau vyaṅgāre caiva mohataḥ |

	mandāgnir āmayāvī ca daridraś copajāyate ||

	tasmāt samiddhe hotavyaṃ nāsamiddhe kathaṃcana |

	ārogyam icchatāyuś ca śriyam ātyantikīṃ tathā ||

śaunako 'pi |

	bahuśuṣkendhane vahnau susamiddhe viśeṣataḥ |

	vidhūme lelihāne (?) ca hotavyaṃ karmasiddhaye ||

kātyāyano 'pi |

	juhuyuś ca bubhuṣuś ca pāṇiśūrpāsyadārubhiḥ |

	na kuryād agnidhamanaṃ na kuryād vyajanādinā ||

	mekhenaiva dhamed agniṃ mukhād eṣo 'bhyajāyata |

atra vyavasthām āha sa eva |

	nāgniṃ mukheneti vaco laukike yojayet tataḥ | iti |

āpastambas tu vaiśvadevādyupakrame vrataviśeṣam āha: "teṣāṃ mantrāṇām upayoge dvādaśāham adhaḥśayyā brahmacaryaṃ kṣāralavaṇavarjaṃ cottamasyaikarātram upavāsaḥ" iti | teṣāṃ vaiśvadevabalyarthānām | uttamasya "ye bhūtāḥ" iti mantrasya | tato vaiśvadevaś caruḥ "vaiśvadeve viśve devāḥ" iti tenaivoktatvāt | vaiśvadeve kartavya tatra yat karma tasmin viśvedevā devatā ity arthaḥ | atra punar āpastambaḥ: "siddhe 'nne tiṣṭhan bhūtam iti svāmine prabrūyāt tat subhūtaṃ virāḍ annaṃ tan mā kṣāyīti prativacanam" iti | tato vaiśvadevādikarma | etac ca sāyaṃ prātaḥ kāryam,

	sāyaṃ prātar vaiśvadevaḥ kartavyo balikarma ca |

	anaśnatāpi kartavyam anyathā kilbiṣī bhavet ||

iti kātyāyanasmaraṇāt | anenātmasaṃskāra ity uktaṃ bhavati | uktaṃ ca pariśiṣṭhe |

	pravased āhitāgniś cet kadācit kālaparyayāt |

	yasminn agnau bhavet pāko vaiśvadevas tu tatra vai ||

	tatrāhutvā tu yo bhuṅkte sa bhuṅkte kilbiṣaṃ naraḥ |

	proṣito 'py ātmasaṃskāraṃ kuryād evāvicārayan ||

gobilo 'pi: "yady etasmin kāle vrīhiyavau prakriyeyātām anyatarasya hutvā kṛtam anyena | yady etasmin kāle punaḥ punar annaṃ pacyeta sakṛd evaikaṃ baliṃ tatra kurvīta | yady ekasmin kāle bahudhānnaṃ pacyeta gṛhapatir mahānasād evaikaṃ baliṃ tatra kurvīta" iti | asyārthaḥ: yady etasmin kāle vrīhiyavādyanekānnapākaḥ tadā ekasmād eva pākād dhomādibaliṃ kurvīta na pratipākam | yady etasmin kāle 'bhyāgatādivaśena punaḥ punar annaṃ pacyeta tadāpy ekasmād eva pākāt sakṛd evaikaṃ baliṃ kuryāt | tathaikāgnyupajīvināṃ bhrātṛputrādīnām etasmin kāle bahudhā pāke 'pi gṛhapatipākāt sakṛd eva kurvīteti | atrānagnikaṃ prakṛtya atriḥ |

	sāgnikaḥ pitṛyajñāntaṃ balikarma samācaret |

	anagnir hṛtaśeṣaṃ tu baliṃ kākabaliṃ haret ||

	puruṣayajñād ṛte nāsti niragnes tu mahāmakhaḥ | iti |

homo 'pi tasya vasiṣṭhena darśitaḥ |

	anagnikas tu yo vipraḥ so 'nnaṃ vyāhṛtibhiḥ svayam |

	hutvā śākalamantraiś ca śiṣṭaṃ kākabaliṃ haret ||

śākalamantrāḥ "devakṛtasyainasaḥ" ityādyāḥ | viṣṇur api |

	annaṃ vyāhṛtibhir hutvā hutvā mantraiś ca śākalaiḥ |

	prajāpater havir hutvā pūjayed atithiṃ tataḥ || iti |

atra yamaḥ |

	akṛtvā vaiśvadevaṃ tu bhuñjate ye dvijādhamāḥ |

	vṛthā tenānnapākena kākayoniṃ vrajanti te || 

vyāso 'pi |

	akṛtvā vaiśvadevaṃ tu yo bhuṅkte 'nāpadi dvijaḥ |

	sa mūḍho narakaṃ yāti kālasūtram avākchirāḥ || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ vaiśvadevavidhiḥ **

**atha baliharaṇam**

tatra kātyāyanaḥ |

	uddhṛtya havir āsicya haviṣyeṇa ghṛtādinā |

	svaśākhāvidhinā hutvā taccheṣeṇa baliṃ haret || iti |
