atra havir uddhṛtya haviṣyeṇa ghṛtādinā havir āsicyābhighārya (?) ten haviṣā hutveti saṃbandhaḥ | atra gobilaḥ: "svayaṃ patrī yāvad vased baliṃ hared api vānyo brāhmaṇaḥ" iti | yāvad gṛhe vaset tāvat svayaṃ vānyo baliṃ hared ity arthaḥ | brāhmaṇagrahaṇaṃ putrādipradarśanārtham | at eva atriḥ |

	putro bhrātātha vā ṛtvikchiṣyaśvaśuramātulāḥ |

	patnīśrotriyayājyāś ca dṛṣṭās te balikarmaṇi || iti |

etat pravāsādiviṣayam | ata eva pariśiṣṭe |

	pravased āhitāgniś cet kadācit kālaparyayāt |

	yasminn agnau bhavet pāko vaiśvadevas tu tatra vai ||

	tatrāhutvā tu yo bhuṅkte sa bhuṅkte kilbiṣaṃ naraḥ |

	proṣito 'py ātmasaṃskāraṃ kuryād evāvicārayan |

	putro bhrātā tathā patnī śiṣyo vāsya baliṃ haret || iti |

patnī ced amantram,

	sāyam annasya siddhasya patny amantraṃ baliṃ haret |

iti manusmaraṇāt | yadā tu gṛhe 'nyaḥ kartā nāsti tadā pravāse 'pi svayam eva kuryāt | tad āha bodhāyanaḥ |

	pravāsaṃ gacchato yasya gṛhe kartā na vidyate |

	pañcānāṃ mahatām eṣāṃ saha yajñaiḥ sa gacchati ||

atra śaunakaḥ: "atha baliharaṇam | etābhyaś caiv devatābhyo 'dbhya oṣadhivanaspatibhyo gṛhāya gṛhadevatābhyo vāstudevatābhya indrāyendrapuruṣebhyo yamāha yamapuruṣebhyo varuṇāya varuṇapuruṣebhyas somāya somapuruṣebhya iti pratidiśaṃ brahmaṇe brahmapuruṣebhya iti madhye viśvebhyo devebhyaḥ sarvebhyo bhūtebhyo divācāribhya iti divā naktaṃcāribhya iti naktaṃ rakṣobhya ity uttarataḥ svadhā pitṛbhya iti prācīnāvītī śeṣaṃ dakṣiṇā ninayet" iti | asyārthaḥ: etabhya iti vaiśvadevadevatānāṃ grahaṇam, tāsāṃ prakṛtatvāt | cakāro vakṣyamāṇadevatāsamuccayārthaḥ | evakāro mā bhūd gṛhyāntaroktānāṃ baliharaṇam iti | etac ca sūryāyety ārabhya vāstudevatābhya ityantaiḥ prāgapavargaṃ yathā prāci vidhir bhavati, "prāñcaś ceṣṭā" iti paribhāṣitatvāt | tatas tasyānte pratidiśam indrādyais teṣāṃ madhye brahmaṇe brahmapuruṣebhya iti | sarvasya pradhānasyottarato viśvebhyo devebhya iti | sarvebhyo bhūtebhya iti madhya eva, tasyādhikārāt | brahmādīnām uttarato rakṣobya iti, teṣāṃ prakṛtatvāt | ata eva teṣāṃ dakṣiṇataḥ svadhā pitṛbhya iti | sarve mantrāḥ svāhāntāḥ | atra ninayed iti vacanaṃ pitṛyajñārtham etat karmāntaraṃ baliharaṇam iti vaktum | karmāntaratvaṃ ca svāhākāranivṛttyartham | karmāntaratve kālāntre 'pi syāt tan mā bhūd iti śeṣagrahaṇam iti | etat sarvaṃ gṛhyavṛttāv uktam | āpastambo 'pi: "apareṇāgiṃ saptamāṣṭamābhyām udgapavargam udapānasannidhau navamena madhye 'gārasya daśamaikādaśābhyāṃ prāgapavargam | uttarapūrvdeśe 'gārasyottaraiś caturbhiḥ | śayyādeśe kāmaliṅgena | dehalyām antarikṣaliṅgenottareṇāpidhānyām | uttarair brahmasadane dakṣiṇataḥ pitṛliṅgena prācīnāv ity avācīnapāṇiḥ kuryāt | raudra uttaro yathā devatābhyaḥ | tayor nānā pariṣecanaṃ dharmabhedāt | naktam evottamena vaihāyanam" iti | asyārthaḥ: uttaraiś caturbhiḥ prāgapavargaṃ tasyādhikārāt | brahmasadane 'gāramadhye | tatrāpi prāgapavargam ity anuvartate | brahmasadanād dakṣiṇataḥ pitṛliṅgena tasya prakṛtatvāt | raudra uttarataḥ paitṛkād iti śeṣaḥ | tayor nānā pariṣecanam ity uttaratra vacanāt | yathā devatābhya iti, yathottānena pāṇinā devatābhyo balidānaṃ tadvad asyāpi na punaḥ paitṛkavad ity arthaḥ | atra balidharmān āha sa eva: "balīnāṃ tasya tasya deśe saṃskāro hastena parimṛjyāvokṣya nyupya paścāt pariṣecanam" iti | ekadeśasamavetānāṃ tu pariṣecanaṃ tantreṇaiva vibhavāt | tad api tenaivoktam: "evaṃ balīnāṃ deśe deśe samavetānāṃ sakṛt sakṛd ante pariṣecanaṃ sati sūpasaṃspṛṣṭena kāryāḥ" iti | asyāpavādaḥ: "tayor nānā pariṣecanaṃ dharmabhedāt" iti | tayoḥ paitṛkaraudrayor ekadeśasamavetatve 'pi nānā pṛthakpariṣecanaṃ prācīnāvītatve 'pi dharmabhedatvād ity arthaḥ | naktam evottamena vaihāyasam iti — vihāyasyākāśe bhavo vaihāyasaḥ tam uttamena "ye bhūtāḥ" it mantreṇa naktam eva dadyād ity arthaḥ| kecid uttamenaiva naktaṃ nānyeneti rātrāv anyamantranivṛttim icchanti | etat sarvaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇoktam | gṛhyakātyāyano 'pi: "maṇike trīn parjanyāyādbhyaḥ (?) pṛthivyai dhātre vidhātre ca dvāryoḥ (?) pratidiśaṃ vāyave diśāṃ ca madhye trīn brahmaṇe 'ntarikṣāya sūryāya viśvebhyo devebhyo viśvebhyaś ca bhūtebhyas teṣām uttarata uṣase  bhūtānāṃ ca pataye paraṃ pitṛbhyaḥ svadhā nama iti dakṣiṇataḥ pitṛbhyas tribhya uttarāparasyāṃ diśi ninayet 'yat kṣema tat te nirṇejanam' " iti | ayam arthaḥ: maṇike udapānasamīpe | pratidiśaṃ vāyave tathā diśāṃ ca | pratidiśam iti śeṣaḥ | atra prācyai diśa ity evaṃ prayogaḥ | "madhye" eteṣām iti śeṣaḥ | trayāṇām uttarato viśvebhya iti dvau | "paraṃ" tayor uttarataḥ uṣase bhūtānāṃ ca pataya iti | trayāṇāṃ dakṣiṇataḥ pitṛbhya iti pātraṃ nirṇijya yat kṣema tat te ity uttarāparasyāṃ diśi ninayet | etat sarvaṃ tadbhāṣyakāreṇoktam | atra namo'ntāḥ sarve mantrāḥ,

	amuṣmai nama ity evaṃ balidānaṃ vidhīyate |

iti kātyāyanasmaraṇāt | atra yathāsvaśākhaṃ vyavasthā,

	na jātu paraśākhoktaṃ dvijaḥ karma samārabhet |

iti vasiṣṭhasmaraṇāt | atra mārkaṇḍeyapurāṇam |

	evaṃ gṛhyabaliṃ kṛtvā gṛhe gṛhapatiḥ śuciḥ |

	āpyāyanāya bhūtānāṃ kuryād utsargam ādarāt || iti |

utsargo 'nnasya | so 'pi katham ity apekṣite viṣṇupurāṇam |

	devā manuṣyāḥ paśavo vayāṃsi siddhāḥ sayakṣoragadaityasaṅghāḥ |

	pretāḥ piśācās taravaḥ samastāḥ ye cānnam icchanti mayā pradattam ||

	pipīlikāḥ kīṭapataṅgakāś ca bhbhukṣitāḥ karmanibandhabaddhāḥ |

	prayāntu te tṛptim idaṃ mayānnaṃ tebhyo nisṛṣṭaṃ sukhino bhavanti ||

	yeṣāṃ na mātā na pitā na bandhuḥ naivānnasiddhir na tathāsti tṛptiḥ |

	tattṛptaye 'nnaṃ bhuvi dattam etat te yāntu tṛptiṃ muditā bhavantu ||

	bhūtāni sarvāṇi tathānnam etad ahaṃ ca viṣṇur na tato 'nyad asti |

	tasmād ahaṃ bhūtahitāya bhūtam annaṃ prayacchāmit bhavāya teṣām ||

	caturdaśo lokagaṇo ya eṣaḥ tatra sthitāye khalu bhūtasaṅghāḥ |

	tṛptyartham annaṃ hi mayā nisṛṣṭaṃ teṣām idaṃ te muditā bhavanti ||

	ity uccārya naro dadyād annaṃ śraddhāsamanvitaḥ |

	bhuvi bhūtopakārāya gṛhī sarvāśrayo yataḥ || iti |

tataḥ śvādibhyo 'nnaṃ dadyāt | tad api tatraivoktam |

	śvacaṇḍālavihaṅgānāṃ bhuvi dadyāt tato naraḥ |

	ye cānye patitāḥ kecid āmapātrāḥ samāgatāḥ ||

manur api |

	śunāṃ ca patitānāṃ ca śvapacāṃ pāparogiṇām |

	vāyasānāṃ krimīṇśṃ ca śanakair nikṣiped bhuvi || 

atra śvavāyasabalimantrau vyāsoktau |

	śvānau dvau śyāmaśabalau vaivasvatakulodbhavau |

	tābhyāṃ piṇḍaṃ pradāsyāmi rakṣetāṃ pathi māṃ sadā ||

	aindravāruṇavāyavyā yāmyanaiṛtikāś ca ye |

	te kākāḥ pratigṛhṇantu bhūmau piṇḍaṃ madarpitam ||

atra patitādīnāṃ dānam anityaṃ teṣām aniyatatvāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">kecit</span> tv āgatānām api dadyād ity āhuḥ | tad āha āpastambaḥ: "sarvān vaiśvadeve bhāginaḥ kurvitā śvacaṇḍālebhyaḥ | nānarhadbhyo dadyād ity eke" iti | anarhadbhyaś caṇḍālādibhyaḥ | atra vyāsaḥ |

	datvānena vidhānena baliṃ paścād upaspṛśet | iti |

evaṃ kurvataḥ phalam āha manuḥ |

	evaṃ yaḥ sarvabhūtāni brāhmaṇo nityam arcati |

	sa gacchati paraṃ sthānaṃ tejomūrtiḥ patharjunā || iti |

āpastambo 'pi: "ya etān avyagro yathopadeśaṃ kurute nityaḥ svargaḥ puṣṭiś ca | agraṃ ca deyam" iti | śrotriyāyeti śeṣaḥ | tathā ca vasiṣṭhaḥ: "gṛhadevatābhyo baliṃ harec chrotriyāyāgraṃ datvā brahmacāriṇe cānantaraṃ pitṛbhyo dadyāt" iti | brahmāriṇe bhikṣāṃ datvety arthaḥ | ata eva yamaḥ |

	bhikṣāṃ ca bhikṣave dadyād vidhivad brahmacāriṇe | iti |

so 'pi vidhir gautamena darśitaḥ: "svasti vācya bhikṣādānam appūrvam" iti | bhikṣamāṇaṃ brahmacāriṇaṃ svastīti vācayitvā taddhaste jalaṃ pradāya bhikṣādānaṃ kāryam ity arthaḥ | yateḥ punar ādyantayor udakadānaṃ kāryam | tathā ca vyāsaḥ |

	yatihaste jalaṃ dadyād bhaikṣaṃ dadyāt punar jalam |

	tad bhaikṣaṃ merutulyaṃ syāt tajjalaṃ sāgaropamam ||

atra vacanadvaye 'pi dadyād ity abhidhānād yatiṃ brahmacāriṇaṃ vā na pratyācakṣīteti gamyate | ata eva āpastambaḥ: "strīṇāṃ ca pratyācakṣāṇānāṃ samāhito brahmacārīṣṭaṃ dattaṃ hutaṃ prajāṃ paśūn brahmavarcasam annādyaṃ vṛṅkte | tasmād u ha vai brahmacārisaṅghaṃ carantaṃ na pratyācakṣīta" | purāṇe 'pi |

	apūjayan hi kākutstha tapasvinam upāgatam |

	duḥkhāśī ca pare loke svāni māṃsāni khādati ||

vyāso 'pi |

	yatiś ca brahmacārī ca pakvānnasvāmināv ubhau |

	tayor annam adatvā tu bhuktvā cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret || iti |

atra parāśaraḥ |

	dadyāc ca bhikṣātritayaṃ parivrāḍbrahmacāriṇām |

	icchayā ca tato dadyād vibhave satyavāritam || iti |

etad api vratādhyayanādiyogaviṣayam,

	satkṛtya bhikṣave bhikṣā dātavyā suvratāya vā |

iti yājñavalkyasmaraṇāt,

	avratā by anadhīyānā yatra bhaikṣacarā dvijāḥ |

	taṃ grāmaṃ daṇḍayed rājā corabhaktaprado hi saḥ ||

iti vasiṣṭhasmaraṇāc ca | yadā tu vaiśvadevād arvāg bhikṣur āgacchati tadā vyāsoktaṃ draṣṭavyam |

	akṛte vaiśvadeve tu bhikṣuke gṛham āgate |

	uddhṛtya vaiśvadevārthaṃ bhikṣāṃ datvā visarjayet ||

	vaiśvadevakṛtaṃ doṣaṃ śakto bhikṣur vyapohitum |

	na hi bhikṣukṛtaṃ doṣaṃ vaiśvadevo vyapohati ||

bhikṣuḥ parivrāṭ | evaṃ brahmacāriṇy api draṣṭavyam | ata eva viṣṇupurāṇam|

	bhikṣāṃ tu bhikṣaver dadyāt parivrāḍbrahmacāriṇām |

	akalpitānnād uddhṛtya sarvavyañjanasaṃyutām (?) ||

bhikṣāṃ prakṛtya yamaḥ |

	hastadattā tu yā bhikṣā salilavyañjanāni ca |

	bhoktā tv aśucitāṃ yāti dātā svargaṃ na gacchati ||

yadā tu bhikṣukālābhas (?) tadā viṣṇunoktam |

	bhikṣukālābhe 'nnaṃ gobhyo dadyād agnau vā prakṣipet | iti |

te ca bhikṣukā vyāsena darśitāḥ |

	brahmacārī yatiś caiva vidyārthī gurupoṣakaḥ (?) |

	adhvagaḥ kṣīṇavṛttiś ca ṣaḍ ete bhikṣukāḥ smṛtāḥ ||

purāṇe 'pi |

	vyādhitasyārthahīnasya kuṭumbāt pracyutasya ca |

	adhvānaṃ vā prapannasya bhikṣācaryā vidhīyate || iti | \
bhikṣādiparimāṇaṃ manunoktam|

	grāsamātrā bhaved bhikṣā agraṃ grāsacatuṣṭayam |

	agraṃ caturguṇīkṛtya hantakārī vidhīyate || iti |

evaṃ kurvataḥ phalam āha yamaḥ |

	satkṛtya bhikṣave bhikṣāṃ yā prayacchati mānavaḥ |

	gopradānasamaṃ puṇyaṃ tasyāha bhagavān yamaḥ ||

brahmapurāṇe 'pi |

	yaḥ pātrapūraṇīṃ bhikṣāṃ yatibhyaḥ saṃprayacchati |

	vimuktaḥ sarvapāpebhyo nāsau durgatim āpnuyāt || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ baliharaṇam**

**athātithipūjā**

tatra viṣṇuḥ | "bhikṣāṃ ca datvātithipūjane paraṃ yat samātiṣṭhet" iti | bhikṣādānānantaram anyatithinirīkṣaṇāya (?) gṛhāṅkaṇe kaṃcit kālaṃ tiṣṭhed ity arthaḥ | tathā ca mārkaṇḍeyapurāṇaṃ |

	ācamya ca tataḥ kuryāt prājño dvārāvalokanam |

	muhūrtasyāṣṭamaṃ bhāgam udvīkṣyo hy atithir bhavet ||

dvāre 'valokanaṃ dvārāvalokanam | brahmagarbho 'pi |

	godohakālaṃ kāṃkṣeta kṛtvā bhūtabaliṃ dvijaḥ | iti |

ayaṃ ca kālaniyamaḥ kālāntare tasya nirīkṣaṇamānāvaśyakam iti vaktum | ata eva viṣṇupurāṇam |

	tato godohamātraṃ vā kālaṃ tiṣṭhan gṛhāṅkaṇe |

	atithigrahaṇārthāya tadūrdhvaṃ vā yathecchayā || iti |

so 'pi kiṃlakṣaṇa ity apekṣite śātātapaḥ |

	priyo vā yadi vā preṣyo mūrkhaḥ paṇḍita eva vā |

	prāptas tu vaiśvadevānte so 'tithiḥ svargasaṅkramaḥ (?) ||

manur api |

	ekarātraṃ tu nivann atithir brāhmaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ |

	anityaṃ hi sthito yasmāt tasmād atithir ucyate ||

mārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe 'pi |

	na mitram atithiṃ kuryān naikagrāmanivāsinam |

	ajñātakulanāmānam annakāla upasthitam ||

	bubhukṣum āgataṃ śrāntaṃ yācamānam akiṃcanam |

	brāhmaṇaṃ prāhur atithiṃ saṃpūjyaḥ śaktito budhaiḥ || iti |

brāhamaṇāgrahaṇaṃ kṣatriyavyudāsārtham | ata eva manuḥ |

	na brāhmaṇasya tv atithir gṛhe rājanya ucyate |

	vaiśyaśūdrau sakhā caiva jñātayo gurur eva ca || iti | \
yat tu vāyupurāṇe |

	na ghoro nāpi saṃkīrṇo navidyo naviśeṣavit |

	na ca santānasaṃbandho na sevanaparo 'tithiḥ || iti |

tad atithivad hutve (?) draṣṭavyam | ata eva śaṅkhaḥ: "yadi tu bahūnāṃ na śaknuyād ekasmā eva dadyād yaḥ prathamam upāgatas tasya yaḥ śrotiryas tasmai dadyād iti vā" | dāne viśeṣo mārkaṇḍeyena darśitaḥ |

	na pṛcched gotracaraṇaṃ svādhyāyaṃ vāpi paṇḍitaḥ |

	śobhanāśobhanākāraṃ taṃ manyet prajāpatim ||

purāṇe 'pi |

	svādhyāyāyagotracaraṇam apṛṣṭvā ca tathā kulam |

	hiraṇyagarbhabuddhyā taṃ manyetābhyāgataṃ gṛhī ||

	tathā prajāpatiḥ śukro vahnir vasugaṇo yamaḥ |

	praviśyātithim evaite bhuñjate 'nnaṃ nareśvaraḥ || iti |

evaṃ bhoktāpi kulaṃ na brūyāt | tad āha viṣṇuḥ |

	deśaṃ gotraṃ kulaṃ vidyām annārthaṃ yo nivedayet |

	vaivasvateṣu dharmeṣu vāntāśī sa tu kīrtitaḥ || iti |

atithau yat kartavyaṃ tad āha manuḥ |

	saṃprāptāya tv atithaye pradadyād āsanodake |

	annaṃ caiva yathāśakti satkṛtya vidhipūrvakam || iti |

udakagrahaṇaṃ pādyādipradarśanārtham, "sa tasya svātatam arghyācamanam āsanaṃ ca pradadyāt" iti hārītasmaraṇāt | parāśaro 'pi |

	atithiṃ tatra saṃprāptaṃ pūjayet svāgatādinā |

	tathāsanapradānena padaprakṣālanena ca ||

	śraddhayā cānnadānena priyapraśnottareṇa ca |

	gacchataś cānuyānena prītim utpādayed gṛhī ||

yamo 'pi |

	cakṣur dadyān mano dadyād vācaṃ dadyāc ca sūnṛtām |

	utthāya cāsanaṃ dadyāt sa dharmaḥ pañcalakṣaṇaḥ ||

uttyāyeti śrotriyātithiviṣayam | ata eva āpastambaḥ: "brāhmāṇāyānadhīyānāyāsanam udakam annam iti deyam | na pratyuttiṣṭhet | abhivādanāyaivottiṣṭhed abhivādyaś cet" iti | atrāsanādidāne viśeṣam āha sa eva: "asamudetaś ced atithir bruvāṇa āgacched āsanam udakam annaṃ śrotriyāya dadāmīty eva dadyāt | evam asya samṛddhaṃ bhavati" | vidyāvittādivihīno 'samudetaḥ | tathāhitāgnāv api viśeṣas tenaiva darśitaḥ: "āhitāgniś ced atithir abhyāgacchet svayam enam abhyudetya brūyāt | vrātya kvāvātsīr iti | vrātyodakam iti | vrātya tarpayaṃstu" iti | vrātya kvāvāksīr iti mantreṇa saṃbhāṣyottareṇa mantradvayenodakam annaṃ ca dadyād ity arthaḥ | atra punar āpastambaḥ: "payaupasecanam annam agniṣṭomasaṃmitaṃ sarpiṣokthyasaṃmitaṃ madhunātirātrasaṃmitaṃ māṃsena dvādaśāhasaṃmitam udakena prajāvṛddhir āyuṣaś ca" (ĀpDh 2.7.4) iti | annābhāve ca tenaivoktam: "kāle svāmināv annārthinaṃ ca pratyācakṣīyātām | abhāve bhūmir udakaṃ tṛṇāni kalyāṇī vāg iti | etāni vai sato 'gāre na kṣīyante kadācana" iti | atithibahutve tu manunoktam |

	āsanāvasathau śayyām anuvrajyām upāsanām |

	uttameṣūttamaṃ kuryād dhīne hīnaṃ same samam ||

annādikaṃ tu samam evaikapaṅktau | yathāha hārītaḥ |

	vidyātapo'dhikānāṃ ca prathamāsanam ucyate |

	paṅktau sahasthitānāṃ tu bhojanādi samaṃ smṛtam || iti |

ata eva viṣamadāne doṣam āha vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	yady ekapaṅktau viṣamaṃ dadāti snehād bhayād vā yadi vārthahetoḥ |

	vedeṣu dṛṣṭām ṛṣibhiś ca gītāṃ tāṃ brahmahatyāṃ munayo vadanti ||

atra mārkaṇḍeyapurāṇam |

	māṃsam annaṃ śākaṃ gṛhe yac copapaditam |

	na vai svayaṃ tad aśnīyād atithiṃ yena nārcayet ||

āpastambo 'pi: "ūrjaṃ puṣṭiṃ prajāṃ paśūn iṣṭāpūrtam iti gṛhāṇām aśnāti yaḥ pūrvo 'tither aśnāti" iti | atithibhojanānantaraṃ vasiṣṭhaḥ: "tato gacchantam āsīnam āsīmāntam anuvrajet | anujñānād vā" | āsīmāntam iti śrotriyadiviṣayam,

	atithiṃ śrotriyaṃ tṛptam āsīmāntam anuvrajet |

iti yājñavalkyasmaraṇāt | evaṃ kurvataḥ phalam āha manuḥ |

	atithiṃ pūjayed yas tu śrāntaṃ cāduṣṭamānasam |

	savṛṣaṃ gośataṃ tena dattaṃ syād iti me matiḥ ||

viṣṇur api |

	svādhyāyenāgnihotreṇa yajñena tapasā tathā |

	nāvāpnoti gṛhī lokān yathā tv atithipūjanāt || iti |

tathā akaraṇe doṣo vyāsena darśitaḥ |

	pathi śrāntam avijñātam atithiṃ kṣutpipāsitam |

	yo na pūjayate bhaktyā tam āhur brahmaghātinam ||

mārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe 'pi |

	atithir yasya bhagnāśo gṛhāt pratinivartate |

	sa datvā duṣkṛtaṃ tasya puṇyam ādāya gacchati ||

devalo 'pi |

	atithir gṛham āgatya yasya pratinivartate |

	asatkṛto nirāśaś ca sa sadyo hanti tatkulam ||

ato na taṃ pratyācakṣīteti bhāvaḥ | evaṃ sūryoḍhe 'pi draṣṭavyam | tathā ca manuḥ |

	apraṇodyo 'tithiḥ sāyaṃ sūryoḍho gṛhamedhinā |

	kāle prāptas tv akāle vā nāsyānaśnan gṛhe vaset || iti |

kāle vaiśvadevakāle prāptaḥ | sūryoḍhe vā anyo vā sāyam atithir apraṇōdyaḥ apratyākhyeya ity arthaḥ | sūryoḍhasya lakṣaṇam āha pracetā |

	yaḥ svayaṃ vaisvadevānte sāyaṃ vā gṛham āgataḥ |

	devavat pūjanīyo 'sau sūryōḍhaḥ so 'tithiḥ smṛtaḥ ||

atrāpi vimukhe 'tithau doṣo viṣṇupurāṇe darśitaḥ |

	devātithau tu vimukhe gate yat pātakaṃ nṛpa |

	tad evāṣṭaguṇaṃ puṃsāṃ sūryoḍhe vimukhe gate ||

ata eva lubdhakāyātithaye 'nnādyabhāve bhojanārthaṃ kapota ātmānam eva pradadau | tathāha vyāsaḥ |

	devatānām ṛṣīṇāṃ ca saṃvādeṣu punaḥ punaḥ |

	śrutapūrvo mayā dharmo mahān atithipūjane ||

	sudūrād āśramāt prāptaḥ kṣuttṛṣṇāśramakarśitaḥ |

	yaḥ pūjyate 'tithiḥ samyag ayūpaḥ kratur eva saḥ ||

	evam uktvā sa dharmātmā prahṛṣṭenāntarātmanā |

	tam agniṃ triḥ parikramya praviveśa svaveśmavat || iti |

yadā tu kṣatriyādir atithirūpeṇāgacchati tadā manūktam |

	yadi tv atithidharmeṇa kṣatriyo gṛham āvrajet |

	bhuktavatsūktavipreṣu kāmaṃ tam api bhojayet ||

	vaiśyaśūdrāv api prāptau kuṭumbe 'tithidharmiṇau |

	bhojayet saha bhṛtyais tāv ānṛśaṃsyaṃ prayojayan || iti |

ānṛśaṃsyam anaiṣṭhuryam | bhṛtyāḥ bharaṇīyāḥ poṣyā ity arthaḥ | śūdreṣu viśeṣam āha āpastambaḥ: "śūdram abhyāgataṃ karmaṇi niyuñjyāt" iti | te ca poṣyā dakṣeṇa darśitāḥ |

	mātā pitā gurur bhāyā prajā dīnāḥ samāśritāḥ |

	abhyātato 'tithiś cāgniḥ poṣyavarga udāhṛtaḥ ||

etac ca bhṛtyabharaṇāvaśakam | anyathā doṣaśravaṇāt | tathā ca atriḥ |

	bharaṇaṃ poṣyavargasya praśastaṃ svargasādhanam |

	narakaḥ pīḍane tasya tasmād yatnena taṃ bharet || iti |

manur api |

	devatātithibhṛtyānāṃ pitṝṇām ātmanaś ca yaḥ |

	na nirvapati pañcānām ucchvasan na sa jīvati ||

yat tu yājñavalkyenoktam,

	bhojayec cāgatān kāle sakhisaṃbandhivāndhavān |

iti, tat svakuṭumbāvirodhena saty anne draṣṭavyam | yad āha āpastambaḥ: "ye nityā bhāktikās teṣām anuparodhena saṃvibhāgo vihataḥ | kāmam ātmānaṃ bhāryāṃ putraṃ voparundhyāt" iti | bhaktam annaṃ tad eṣāṃ te bhāktikāḥ | saṃvibhāgo 'nnasya | manur api |

	bhṛtyānām anuparodhena yaḥ karoty aurdhvadaihikam |

	tad bhavaty asukhodarkaṃ jīvataś ca mṛtasya ca || iti |

ataḥ sadhanasyaivāyaṃ bāndhavādibhojananiyama ity avagantavyam | uktaṃ ca ādipurāṇe |

	jñātir bandhujanaḥ kṣīṇaḥ tathānāthaḥ samāśritaḥ |

	anyo 'pi dhanayuktasya poṣyavarga udāhṛtaḥ ||

asyāpy āvaśyakam eva bharaṇam | yato 'nantaram evoktam |

	abhuktavatsu caiteṣu buñjan bhuṅkte tu kilbiṣam |

	mṛtaś ca gatvā narakaṃ śleṣmabhug jāyate naraḥ ||

mārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe 'pi |

	śrīmantaṃ jñātim āsādya yo jñātir avasīdati |

	sīdatā yat kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tat sarvaṃ pratipadyate || iti |

atithipūjānantaraṃ viṣṇupurāṇam |

	tataḥ suvāsinīduḥkhigarbhiṇīvṛddhabālakān |

	bhojayet saṃskṛtānnena prathamaṃ tu tato gṛhī ||

atra vyāsaḥ |

	gavāhnikaṃ paragave dadyāt saṃvatsaraṃ tu yaḥ |

	akṛtvā svayam āhāraṃ tadvrataṃ sārvakālikam || iti |

atra mantraḥ |

	saurabheyāḥ sarvahitāḥ pavitrāḥ pāpanāśanāḥ |

	pratigṛhṇantu me grāsaṃ gāvas trailokyamātaraḥ || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyām atithipūjā**

**atha prasaṅgād annadānaviṣayāṇi kānicidvacanāni likhyante**

tatra vyāsaḥ |

	grāsam apy ekam annasya yo dadāti dine dine |

	svargalokam avāpnoti narakaṃ ca na paśyati ||

	dvāv imau puruṣau loke sūryasyopari tiṣṭhataḥ |

	annapradātā durbhikṣe subhikṣe hemavastradaḥ ||

	agnau hutvātha dānena yat puṇyaphalam āpyate |

	tena tulyaṃ viśiṣṭaṃ vā brāhmaṇe tarpite phalam ||

	brāhmaṇeṣv akṣayaṃ dānam annaṃ śūdre mahāphalam |

	annadānaṃ hi śūdrasya syād vipre cāviśeṣataḥ ||

viṣṇur api |

	kṛtvā tu pātakaṃ karma yo dadyād annam arthine |

	brāhmaṇāya viśeṣeṇa na sa pāpena lipyate ||

atra devalaḥ |

	aghṛtaṃ bhojayed vipraṃ yo gṛhe sati sarpiṣi |

	paratra nirayaṃ ghoraṃ sa yāty eva na saṃśayaḥ ||

	mṛṣṭam annaṃ svayaṃ bhuktvā paścāt kadaśanaṃ naraḥ |

	brāhmaṇān bhojayen mūkho narake ciram āvaset || iti |

te ca brāhmaṇāḥ śrotriyā eva | yad āha vyāsaḥ |

	vedavidyāvrasnāte śrotriye gṛham āgate |

	krīṣanty oṣadhayaḥ sarvā yāsyāmaḥ parāṃ gatim ||

	saṃdhyāhīne vratabhraṣṭe vipre vedavivarjite |

	dīyamānaṃ rudaty annaṃ kiṃ mayā duṣkṛtaṃ kṛtam ||

manur api |

	vidyātapaḥsamiddheṣu hutaṃ vipramukhāgniṣu |

	tat tārayati durgāc ca mahataś caiva kilbiṣāt || iti |

atrāpi viśeṣam āha yamaḥ |

	apacantam atikramya pacantaṃ yas tu bhojayet |

	bhūṣikāṇāṃ bhaved yonau varṣāṇām adhikaṃ śatam || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyām annadānavidhiḥ**

**atha bhojanavidhiḥ**

tatra manuḥ |

	bhuktavatsu ca vipreṣu bhṛtyeṣv anyeṣu caiva hi |

	bhuñjīyāyāṃ tataḥ paścād vidhasaṃ taṃ tu dampatī ||

vighasaṃ bhuktaśiṣṭam | tathā ca vyāsaḥ |

	vidhasāśī bhaven nityaṃ nityaṃ cāmṛtabhojanaḥ |

	vighasaṃ bhuktaśiṣṭaṃ tu yajñaśiṣṭaṃ tathāmṛtam || iti |

anena na kadācid apy ātmārtham annaṃ paced ity arthād uktaṃ bhavati | uktaṃ ca devalena |

	nātmārthaṃ pacayed annaṃ nātmārthaṃ ghātayet paśūn |

	devārthe brāhmaṇārthe ca pacamāno na lipyate ||

manur api |

	aghaṃ sa kevalaṃ bhuṅkte yaḥ pacaty ātmakāraṇāt |

	yajñaśiṣṭāśanaṃ hy etat satām annaṃ vidhīyate ||

atra diṅniyamam āha sa eva |

	āyuṣyaṃ prāṅmukho bhuṅkte yaśasyaṃ dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ |

	śriyaṃ pratyaṅmukho bhuṅkte ṛtaṃ bhuṅkta udaṅmukhaḥ ||

āyuṣe hitam āyuṣyam | tat prāṅmukho bhuñjīta | yasase hitaṃ yaśasyaṃ dakṣiṇāmukho bhuñjīta | śriyam icchan pratyaṅmukhaḥ | ṛtaṃ satyam | tad icchann udaṅmukha ity arthaḥ | viṣṇur api: "prāṅmukho 'śnīyād dakṣiṇāmukho vā" iti | atra āpastambaḥ: "dakṣiṇāmukho bhuñjīta | anāyuṣyaṃ tv evaṃmukhasya bhojanaṃ mātur ity upadiśanti" iti | etac ca bhojanaṃ rahasi kāryam | tathā ca devalaḥ |

	āhāraṃ tu rahaḥ kuryād vihāraṃ cāpi sarvataḥ |

	gupto hi lakṣmyā yuktaḥ syāt prakāśe hīyate śriyā || iti |

raho guptapradeśaḥ | padmapurāṇe 'pi |

	gupte caiva pradeśe tu prāṅmukho vāpy udaṅmukhaḥ |

	sukhāsane samāsīnaḥ pādau kṛtvā mahītale || iti |

atra viśeṣam āha devalaḥ |

	upalipte śucau deśe pādau prakṣālya vāgyataḥ |

	prāṅmukho 'nnāni bhuñjīta śuciḥ pīṭham adhiṣṭhitaḥ ||

bhaviṣyatpurāṇe 'pi |

	sadyaḥ kṛtopalepe tu bahir ācamya vāgyataḥ |

	udaṅmukhaḥ prāṅmukho vā samyag vidhṛtabhojanaḥ ||

bahirbhojanaśālāta it śeṣaḥ |

	yas tu bhojanaśālāyāṃ bhoktukāma upaspṛśet |

	āsanastho na cānyatra sa vipraḥ paṅktidūṣakaḥ ||

ity āpastambasmaraṇāt | kṛtopalepe gomayeneti śeṣaḥ | tathā ca bodhāyanaḥ |

	mantreṇaiva dvir ācamya gomayenopalepite |

	bhasmanā vāriṇā vāpi kārayen maṇḍalaṃ tataḥ || iti |

atra viśeṣam āha śaṅkhaḥ |

	ādityā vasavo rudrā brahmā caiva pitāmahaḥ |

	maṇḍalāny upajīvanti tasmāt kurvīta maṇḍalam ||

	catuṣkoṇaṃ dvijāgryasya trikoṇaṃ kṣatriyasya tu |

	maṇḍalākṛtiṃ vaiśyasya śūdrasābhyukṣaṇaṃ smṛtam || iti |

atra yamaḥ |

	ārdrapādas tu bhuñjīta nārdrapādas tu saṃviśet |

	ārdrapādas tu bhuñjāno dīrgham āyur avāpnuyāt || iti |

pādagrahaṇam aṅgapañcakopalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva vyāsaḥ |

	pañcārdhro bhojanaṃ kuryāt prāṅmukho maunam āsthitaḥ |

	hastau pādau tathaivāsyam eṣu pañcārdratā matā ||

mārkaṇḍeyo 'pi |

	naikavāsās tathāśnīyād bhinnabhāṇḍena mānavaḥ |

	anārdrapāṇipādaś ca tathaivānārdramastakaḥ || iti |

na bhinnabhāṇḍeneti tāmrādivyatiriktaviṣayam | ata eva paiṭhīnasiḥ: "tāmrarajatasuvarṇaśaṅkhaśuktyaśmasphaṭikānāṃ bhinnam abhinnam iti na doṣaḥ" iti | pracetā api |

	na bhinnabhāṇḍe bhuñjīta na bhāvapratidūṣitaiḥ |

	anyatra tāmraraupyābjasauvarṇād bhājanād dvijaḥ || iti |

abjaṃ śaṅkhādi | bhojanapātraṃ prakṛtya paiṭhīnasiḥ |

	brahmapatre tu yo buṅkte māsam ekaṃ nirantaram |

	triṃśac cāndrāyaṇais tulyaṃ mahāpātakanāśanam ||

	sauvarṇe rājate patre tāmre padmapalāśayoḥ |

	bhojane bhojane caiva trirātrāt palam aśnute ||

brahmapatraṃ palāśapatram | purāṇe 'pi |

	palāśeṣu ca patreṣu madhyameṣu ca bhārata |

	yaḥ karoty aśanaṃ tasya prājāpatyaṃ dine dine ||

	ya icched ūrdhvagāmitvaṃ paraṃ sthānaṃ ca śāśvatam |

	padmapatre tu bhoktavyaṃ māsam ekaṃ nirantaram ||

paiṭhīnasir api |

	eka eva tu yo bhuṅkte vimale kāṃsyabhājane |

	bhojane bhojane caiva trirātraphalam aśnute ||

	eka eva tu yo bhuṅkte vimale kāṃsyabhājane |

	catvāri tasya vardhante āyuḥ prajñā yaśo balam ||

kāṃsyabhājanaṃ yatyādivyatiriktaviṣayam | tad āha pracetāḥ |

	tāmbūlābhyañjane caiva kāṃsyapātre ca bhojanam |

	yatiś ca brahmacārī ca vidhavā ca vivarjayet ||

atra varjyāny āha paiṭhīnasiḥ |

	vaṭārkāśvatthaparṇeṣu kumbhīśryaudumbareṣu ca |

	śrīkāmo naiva bhuñjīta kovidārakarañjayoḥ ||

hārīto 'pi |

	na kārṣṇāyase mṛṇmaye vā pātre 'śnīyāt | iti |

pracetā api |

	mṛṇmaye parṇapṛṣṭhe vā kārpāse tāntave tathā |

	nāśnīyān na pibec caiva na kare na tathāsane || iti |

tathāsanāny api varjyāni tenaiva darśitāni |

	gośakṛnmṛṇmayaṃ bhinnaṃ tathā pālāśam eva ca |

	lohabaddhaṃ sadaivārkaṃ varjayed āsanaṃ budhaḥ || iti |

atra kūrmapurāṇam |

	pañcārdro bhojanaṃ kuryād bhūmau pātraṃ nidhāya tu |

	upavāsena tat tulyaṃ manur āha prajāpatiḥ ||

vyāso 'pi |

	bhūmau pātraṃ pratiṣṭhāpya yo bhuṅkte vāgyataḥ śuciḥ |

	bhojane bhojane caiva trirātraphalam aśnute ||

	nyastapātras tu bhuñjīta pañcagrāsān mahāmune |

	śeṣam uddhṛtya bhoktavyaṃ śrūyatām atra kāraṇam ||

	vipruṣāṃ doṣasaṃsparśaḥ pādacelarajas tathā |

	sukhena bhuṅkte viprendra pitrarthaṃ tu na lipyate || iti | \
pitrarthaṃ bhūmau pātraṃ pratiṣṭhāpya na tal lepanīyam | itaram uddhṛtya tatpātre bhuñjītety arthaḥ | vāgyamanaṃ prakṛtya purāṇe 'pi |

	snāsyato varuṇaḥ śaktiṃ juhvato 'gniḥ śriyaṃ haret |

	bhuñjato mṛtyur āyuṣyaṃ tasmān maunaṃ triṣu smṛtam || iti |

yat tu atriṇoktam,

	maunavrataṃ mahākaṣṭaṃ huṃkāreṇāpi naśyati |

	tathā sati mahān doṣas tasmāt taṃ niyataṃ caret || iti |

tat kāṣṭhamaunābhiprāyam | etac ca grāsād upari veditavyam,

	anindan bhakṣayen nityaṃ vāgyato 'nnam akutsayan |

	pañcagrāsaṃ mahāmaunaṃ prāṇādyāpyāyanaṃ hit tat ||

iti vṛddhamanusmaraṇāt | akutsayan anindann ity arthaḥ | atra śātātapaḥ |

	hastadattāni cānnāni pratyakṣalavaṇaṃ tathā |

	mṛttikābhakṣaṇaṃ caiva gomāṃsāśanavat smṛtam ||

vṛddhavasiṣṭho 'pi |

	ghṛtaṃ vā yadi vā tailaṃ vipro nādyān nakhacyutam |

	yamas tam aśuciṃ prāha tulyaṃ gomāṃsabhakṣaṇe ||

paiṭhīnasir api |

	lavaṇaṃ vyañjanaṃ caiva ghṛtaṃ tailaṃ tathaiva ca |

	lehyaṃ peyaṃ ca vividhaṃ hastadattaṃ na bhakṣayet || iti |

kena tarhi deyam ity apekṣite manuḥ |

	darvyā deyaṃ ghṛtānnaṃ tu samastavyañjanāni ca |

	udakaṃ yac ca pakvānnaṃ yo darvyā dātum icchati |

	sa bhrūṇahā surāpaś ca sa steno gurutalpagaḥ ||

atra bodhāyanaḥ |


        sarvāvaśyakāvasāne suprakṣālitapāṇipādo 'pa ācamya saṃmṛṣṭopalipte deśe prāṅmukha upaviśya tadbhūtam āhriyamāṇaṃ bhūr bhuvaḥ suvar om ity upasthāya vācaṃ yacchet | nyastam annaṃ mahāvyāhṛtibhiḥ pradakṣiṇam udakaṃ pariṣicya savyena pāṇināvimuñcann amṛtopastaraṇam asīti purastād apaḥ pītvā pañcānnena prāṇāhūtīr juhoti prāṇe niviṣṭo 'mṛtaṃ juhomi śivo māviśāpradāhāya prāṇāya svāheti | pañcānnena prāṇāhutīr hutvā tūṣṇīṃ bhūyo vratayet prajāpatiṃ manasā dhyāyan nātisuhito 'mṛtāpidhānam asīti tadupariṣṭhād apaḥ pītvācānto hṛdayadeśam abhimṛśati prāṇānāṃ granthir asi rudro mā viśāntakas tenānnenāpyāyasveti punar ācamya dakṣiṇe pādāṅguṣṭhe pāṇī nisrāvayati, aṅguṣṭhamātraḥ puruṣo 'ṅguṣṭhaṃ ca samāśritaḥ | īśaḥ sarvasya jagataḥ prabhuḥ prīṇāti viśvabhuk || iti |

hutānumantraṇam ūrdhvahastaḥ samācaret | śraddhāyāṃ prāṇe niviśyāmṛtaṃ hutaṃ prāṇam annenāpyāyasveti | evam apānavyānodānasamānābhiḥ pañcabhiḥ | brahmaṇi ma ātmāmṛtatvāyety akṣareṇātmānaṃ yojayet | sarvakratuyājinām ātmayājī viśiṣyata iti | athāpy udāharanti |

	yathā hi tūlam aiṣīkam agnau protaṃ pradīpyate |

	tadvat sarvāṇi pāpāni dahyante hy ātmayājinaḥ || iti |

gobilo 'pi |


        athātaḥ prāṇāhutikalpo vyāhṛtibhir gāyatryābhimantrya ṛtaṃ tvā satyena pariṣiñcāmīti sāyaṃ satyaṃ tvartena pariṣiñcāmīti prātaḥ antaś carasi bhūteṣu guhāyāṃ visvato mukhaḥ | tvaṃ yajñas tvaṃ viṣṇus tvaṃ vaṣaṭkāras tvaṃ brahma tvaṃ prajāpatiḥ āpo jyotīraso 'mṛtaṃ brahma bhūr bhuvaḥ suvar om amṛtopastaraṇam asīty apaḥ pītvā daśhotāraṃ manasānudrutyātvarayan pañcagrāsān gṛhṇīyat prāṇāya svāheti | gārhaptyam etena juhoti | apānāya svāheti | anvāhāryapacanam etena juhoti | vyānāya svāheti | āhavanīyam etena juhoti | udānāya svāheti | sabhyam etena juhoti | samānāya svāheti | āvasathyam etena juhoti || iti |

ete mantrā svāhākārāntāḥ praṇavādyāś ca | tathā ca śaunakaḥ |

	svāhāntāḥ praṇavādyāś ca nāmnā mantrās tu vāyavaḥ |

	juhvann eva grased annaṃ daśanaiś ca saṃspṛśet ||

atra viśeṣam āha sa eva |

	tarjanīmadyamāṅguṣṭhalagnaṃ prāṇāhutau bhavet |

	madhyamānāmikāṅguṣṭhair apāne juhuyād budhaḥ ||

	kaniṣṭhānāmikāṅguṣṭhair vyāne tu juhuyād dhaviḥ|

	tarjanīṃ tu bahiḥ kṛtvā udāne juhuyād budhaḥ |

	samāne sarvahastena samuāyāhutir bhavet ||

viṣṇur api |

	śrūyatām kathayāmīha hūyate ca yathā mukhe |

	bhūmau pātraṃ pratiṣṭhāpya oṃkāreṇaiva saṃyutam ||

	tadannaṃ pañcabhiś caiva aṅgulībhir mukhe kṣipet || iti |

annopakalpanānantaraṃ bhaviṣyatpurāṇam |

	bhojanāt kiṃcid annagraṃ dharmarājāy vai balim |

	datvāth chinnaguptāya dharmarājāya vai balim ||

	yatra kvacana saṃsthānāṃ kṣuttṛṣṇopahatātmanām |

	pretānāṃ tṛptaye 'kṣayyam idam astu yathāsukham || iti |

atra viṣṇupurāṇam |

	aśnīyāt tanmanā bhūtvā pūrvaṃ tu madhuraṃ rasam |

	lavaṇāmlo tathā madhye kaṛutiktādikāṃs tataḥ ||

	prāgdravaṃ puruṣo 'śnīyān madhye tu kaṭhināśanam |

	ante punar dravāśī tu balārogye (?) na muñcati ||

marīcir api |

	bhuktvā dadhnyānupānaṃ tu na kartavyaṃ ca vāriṇā |

	bhuktvā kṣīrodanaṃ paścān nātitṛptaḥ spṛśed budhaḥ ||

vṛddhamanur api |

	pītvāpośanam aśnīyāt pātradattam agarhitam |

	bhāryābhṛtakadāsebhya ucchiṣṭaṃ śeṣayet tataḥ ||

atra keṣucid apavādam āha pulastyaḥ |

	bhojanaṃ tu na niḥśeṣaṃ kuryāt prājñaḥ kathaṃcana |

	anyatra dadhisaktvājyapalalakṣīramadhvapaḥ || iti |

palalaṃ māṃsam | etad api sāyaṃ prataḥ kāryam, "sāyaṃ prātas tv annam abhipūjitam anindan bhuñjīta" gautamasmaraṇāt | anenārthān nāntarā bhuñjītety uktaṃ bhavati | uktaṃ ca manunā |

	sāyaṃ prātar dvijātīnām aśanaṃ śruticoditam |

	nāntarā bhojanaṃ kuryād agnihotrasamo vidhiḥ ||

agnihotrasama ity anena kāladvaye 'pi bhojanam āvaśyakam (?) ity āha | ata eva śrutiḥ: "tasmāt sāyaṃ prātar āvaśyakaṃ bhojanaṃ syāt" iti | bhojanaṃ prakṛtya āpastambaḥ |

	aṣṭau grāsā muner bhakṣāḥ ṣoḍaśāraṇyavāsinaḥ |

	dvātriṃśataṃ gṛhasthasyāparimitaṃ brahmacāriṇaḥ ||

	āhitāgnir anaḍvāṃś ca brahmacārī ca te trayaḥ |

	aśnanta eva siddhyanti naiṣāṃ siddhir anaśnatām || iti |

upavāsādau bodhāyanoktam |

	gṛhastho brahmacārī ca yo 'naśnaṃs tu tapaś caret |

	prāṇāgnihotralopena avakīrṇo bhavet tu saḥ ||

	prāṇāgnihotramantrāṃs tu niruddhe bhojane japet |

	tretāgnihotramantrāṃs tu dravyālābhe yathā japet || iti |

bhojanānantaraṃ devalaḥ |

	bhuktvocchiṣṭaṃ samādāya sarvasmāt kiṃcid ācaman |

	ucchiṣṭabhāgadheyebhyaḥ sodakaṃ nirvaped bhuvi || iti | \
mantras tu |

	raurave 'puṇyanilaye padmārbudanivāsinām |

	arthinām udakaṃ dattam akṣayyam upatiṣṭhatu || iti |

atra gadyavyāsaḥ: "tatas tṛptaaḥ san 'amṛtāpidhānam asi' ity apaḥ prāśya tasmād deśān manāg apasṛtya vidhivad ācāmet" iti | apāṃ prāśane viśeṣam āha sa eva vyāsaḥ |

	hastaṃ prakṣālya gaṇḍūṣaṃ yaḥ pibet pāpamohitaḥ |

	na daivaṃ naiva pitryaṃ ca ātmānaṃ naiva sādhayet ||

	ardhaṃ pītvātha gaṇḍūṣam ardhaṃ tyājyaṃ mahītale |

	rasātalagatān nāgāṃs tena prīṇāti nityaśaḥ ||

atra devalaḥ |

	bhuktvācamya tathoktena vidhānena samāhitaḥ |

	śodhayen mukhahastau ca mṛdbhir gharṣaṇakarair api ||

	ācamya ca tataḥ kāryaṃ dantakāṣṭhasya bhakṣaṇam |

	bhojane dantalagnāṃś ca nirhṛtyācamanaṃ caret ||

	dantalagnam asaṃhāryaṃ lepaṃ manyeta dantavat |

	na tatra bahuśaḥ kuryād yatnam uddharaṇaṃ prati ||

	bhaved aśaucam atyarthaṃ tṛṇavedhād vraṇe kṛte | iti | \
atra vyāsaḥ |

	mā kareṇa karaṃ sprākṣīr mā jaṅghe mā ca cakṣuṣī |

	jānunī spṛśa kaunteya bhartavyas te mahājanaḥ || iti |

śātātapo 'pi |

	ācamya pātram utsārya kiṃcid ārdreṇa pāṇinā |

	mukhyān prāṇān samālabhya nābhiṃ pāṇitalena ca ||

	bhuktvā cāpi pratiṣṭheta na cāpy ārdreṇa pāṇinā |

	pāṇiṃ mūrdhni samādhāya spṛṣṭvā cāgniṃ samāhitaḥ ||

	jñātiśraiṣṭhyam avāpnoti prayogakusalo naraḥ | iti |

āpastambo 'pi: "ācamya cordhvau pāṇī dhārayed ā prodakībhāvāt | tato 'gnim upaspṛśet" (ĀpDh 2.19.12–13) iti | pragatam udakaṃ yābhyāṃ tau prodakau | viṣṇupurāṇe 'pi |

	svasthaḥ praśāntacittas tu kṛtāsanaparigrahaḥ |

	abhīṣṭadevatānāṃ tu kurvīta smaraṇaṃ budhaḥ ||

	agnir āpyāyayatv annaṃ prārthivaṃ pavaneritaḥ |

	dattāvakāśaṃ nabhasā jarayantv astu me mukham ||

	annaṃ balāya me bhūyād apām agnyanilasya ca |

	bhavatv etat pariṇataṃ mamāstv avyāhataṃ sukham ||

	prāṇāpānasamānānām udānavyanayor api |

	annaṃ puṣṭikaraṃ cāstu mamāstv avyāhataṃ sukahm ||

	agastir agnir vaḍavānalaś ca bhuktaṃ mayānnaṃ jarayatv aśeṣam |

	sukhaṃ mamaitat pariṇāmasaṃbhavaṃ yacchatv arogaṃ mama cāsstu dehe ||

	viṣṇuḥ samastendriyadehadehī pradhānabhūto bhagavān yathaikaḥ |

	satyena tenāttam aśeṣam annam ārogyadaṃ me pariṇāmam etu ||

	viṣṇur attā tahaivānnaṃ pariṇāmaś ca vai yathā |

	satyena tena me bhuktaṃ jīryatv annam idaṃ tathā ||

	ity uccārya svahastena parimṛjyātha codaram |

	anāyāsapradāyīni kuryāt karmāṇy atandritaḥ || iti |

mārkaṇḍeyo 'pi |

	bhūyo 'py ācmya kartavyaṃ tatas tāmbūlabhakṣaṇam |

	śravaṇaṃ cetihāsasya tathā rāmāyaṇasya vā ||

kuryād ity adhyāhāraḥ | viṣṇur api |

	bhuktvopaviṣṭo viśrānto brahma kiṃcid vicintayet | 

dakṣo 'pi |

	itihāsapurāṇānābhyāṃ ṣaṣṭhasaptamakau nayet |

	aṣṭame lokayātrā tu bahiḥ saṃdhyā tataḥ punaḥ || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ bhojanavidhiḥ**

**atha bhoktṛniyamāḥ**

tatra hārītaḥ: "mārjanārcanabalikarmabhojanāni daivena tīrthena kuryāt" iti | daivaṃ tīrtham aṅgulyagram | āpastambo 'pi |

	yatnena dhārayed vipraḥ pavitraṃ dakṣiṇe kare |

	bhuñjānas tu viśeṣeṇa annadoṣair na lipyate ||

atrir api |

	brahmayajñe jape caiva brahmagranthir vidhīyate |

	bhojane vartulaḥ proktaḥ evaṃ dharmo na hīyate ||

viṣṇupurāṇe 'pi |

	praśastaratnapāṇis tu bhuñjīta prayato gṛhī |

	bhuñjītoddhṛtasārāṇi na kadācid nareśvara ||

vasiṣṭho 'pi: "na ca mukhaśabdaṃ kuryāt sarvābir aṅglībhir aśnīyāt pāṇiṃ ca nāvadhūnuyāt" iti | mārkaṇḍeyo 'pi |

	āpo'śanaṃ sarvatīrthaṃ yavad annaṃ na laṅghayet |

	bāhunā laṅghitaṃ tv annam abhojyaṃ manur avravīt ||

	yas tu pāṇitale bhuṅkte yaḥ savāyu samaśnute |

	aṅgulīṃ coddhared yas tu gomāṃsāśanavat smṛtam ||

savāyu samaśnute saśabdaṃ grasata ity arthaḥ | brahmapurāṇe 'pi |

	grāmaśeṣaṃ na cāśnīyāt pītaśeṣaṃ piben na tu |

	śākamūlaphalekṣūṇi dantacchedair na bhakṣayet ||

bodhāyano 'pi: "sarvabhakṣāpūpakandamūlaphalamāṃsāni dantair nāvadyāt | nātisuhitaḥ" | nātisuhito 'titṛpta ity arthaḥ | manur api |

	anārogyam anāyuṣyam asvargyaṃ cātibhojanam |

	apuṇyaṃ lokavidviṣṭaṃ tasmāt tat parivarjayet ||

yamo 'pi |

	nocchiṣṭaṃ bhakṣayet kiṃcin na gacchan vā kadācana |

	khaṭvārūḍho na bhuñjīta na pāṇisthaṃ kadācana ||

mārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe 'pi |

	nāsnāto na ca saṃviṣṭo na caivānyamanā naraḥ |

	na caiva śayane norvyām upaviṣṭo na śabdavat ||

	na caikavastro na vadan prekṣatām apradāya ca |

	bhuñjīta puruṣaḥ snātaḥ sāyaṃ prātar yathāvidhi ||

nāśnīyād ity anuvṛttau mārkaṇḍeyo 'pi |

	pādaprasāraṇaṃ kṛtvā na ca veṣṭitamastakaḥ |

uśanāpi |

	nādatvā mṛṣṭam aśnīyān na bahūnāṃ ca paśyatām |

	nāśnīyur bahavaś caiva tathā caikasya paśyataḥ ||

hārīto 'pi: "na ca tad aśnīyād yenānnena devapitṛmanuṣyayajñān na kuryāt" iti | vṛddhamanur api |

	na piben na ca bhuñjīta dvijaḥ savyena pāṇinā |

	naikahastena ca jalaṃ śūdreṇāvarjitaṃ pibet ||

	pibato yat patet toyaṃ bhojane mukhaniḥsṛtam |

	abhojyaṃ tad bhaved annaṃ bhoktā bhuñjīta kilbiṣam ||

	pītāvaśeṣitaṃ kṛtvā brāhmaṇaḥ punar āpibet |

	trirātraṃ tu vrataṃ kuryād vāmahastena vā punaḥ ||

ekahastenāvarjitaṃ jalam ity arthaḥ | caturviṃśatāv api |

	hastād ṛte 'mbu cānyena nāśnan pātrād ṛte pibet |

viṣṇur api |

	nocchiṣṭo ghṛtam aśnīyād aśnīyāc cātijīrṇitaḥ | iti |

ādipurāṇe 'pi |

	nocchiṣṭo grāhayed ājyaṃ jagdhaśiṣṭaṃ na saṃtyajet |

	śūdrabhuktāvaśiṣṭaṃ tu nādyād bhāṇḍasthitaṃ tathā || iti |

devalo 'pi |

	ekavastro na bhuñjīta kavāṭam apidhāya vā |

	yānasthaḥ śakaṭastho vā pādukānikaṭe 'pi vā ||

atrir api |

	āsane pādam aropya (?) yo bhuṅkte brāhmaṇaḥ kvacit |

	mukhena dhamitaṃ cānnaṃ tulyaṃ gomāṃsabhakṣaṇe ||

bodhāyano 'pi |

	bhojanaṃ ca japaṃ dānam upahāraḥ praigrahaḥ |

	na bahir jānu kāryāṇi tadvad ācamanaṃ smṛtam || iti |

bṛhaspatir api |

	na spṛśed vāmahastena bhuñjāno 'nnaṃ kadācana |

	na pādau na śiro vastiṃ (?)na padā bhājanaṃ spṛśet ||

vastir nābher adhaḥ | āpastambo 'pi |

	agnyagāre gavāṃ goṣṭhe devabrāhmaṇasaṃnidhau |

	japye bhojanakāle ca pāduke parivarjayet ||

	notsaṅge bhājanaṃ kṛtvā bhuñjīta snātako dvijaḥ |

	na ca pāṇitale kṛtvā na śayyāyāṃ na cāsane ||

ādipurāṇe 'pi |

	śayanastho na bhuñjīta na cānyāsanasaṃsthitaḥ |

	na saṃdhyayor na madhyāhne nārdharātre kadācana ||

	nārdravāsā nārdraśirā na cāyajñopavitavān |

	na yantrārūḍhapādas tu na ca sārdhaṃ tu bhāyayā ||

	śūnyālaye na cāsnīyān na ca devāgniveśmani |

	mātāpitror athocchiṣṭaṃ bālo bhuñjan bhavet sukhī ||

viṣṇupurāṇe 'pi |

	nāśnīyād bhāryayā sārdhaṃ nākāśe na tathotthitaḥ |

	śayānaḥ prauḍhapādaś ca kṛtvā caivāvasakthikām ||

prauḍhapādaḥ āsanādyāropitapādaḥ | avasakthikā jānvor madhyasya ca vastrādinā bandhanam | yat tu,

	brāhmaṇyā saha yo 'śnīyād ucchiṣṭaṃ vā kadācana |

	na tasya doṣam icchanti nityam eva manīṣiṇaḥ ||

	ucchiṣṭam itaras trīṇāṃ yo 'śnīyād brāhmaṇaḥ kvacit |

	prāyaścittī sa vijñeyaḥ saṃkīrṇo mūḍhacetanaḥ ||

iti, na tat sarvathā doṣābhāvapratipādanaparam, kadācaneti vacanāt | ata eva ādipurāṇe |

	brāhmaṇyā bhāyayā sārdhaṃ kvacid bhuñjīta vādhvani |

	adhovarṇastriyā sārdhaṃ bhuktvā patati tatikṣaṇāt || iti |

atra paiṭhīnasiḥ: "nāniyukto 'grāsanaṃ gacchet" iti | bhoktum iti śeṣaḥ | śaṅkho 'pi: "nāgrāsanasthaḥ pūrvam aśnīyāt" iti | śātātapo 'pi |

	agrāsanopaviṣṭas tu yo bhuṅkte prathamaṃ dvijaḥ |

	bahūnāṃ paśyatāṃ so 'jñaḥ paṅktyā harati kilbiṣam || iti |

gobilo 'pi |

	ekapaṅktyupaviṣṭānāṃ viprāṇāṃ sahabhojane |

	yady eko 'pi tyajet pātraṃ nāśnīyur itare 'py anu ||

	mohāt tu bhuṅkte yas tatra sa sāntapanam ācaret |

	bhuñjāneṣu tu vipreṣu yas tu pātraṃ parityajet |

	bhojane vighnakartāsau brahmahā ca tathocyate ||

ādipurāṇe 'pi |

	ekapaṅktir anutthāya madhe ced ācamet paraḥ |

	tadā śeṣaṃ vihāyaiva tataḥ samyag upaspṛśet ||

	apy ekapaṅktyāṃ nāśnīyād brāhmaṇaiḥ svajanair api |

	ko hi jānāti kiṃ tasya pracchannaṃ pātakaṃ bhavet || iti |

yataḥ sarveṣāṃ pātakaṃ bhavatīty abhiprāyaḥ | ata eva bṛhaspatiḥ |

	ekapaṅktyupaviṣṭānāṃ duṣkṛtaṃ yad durātmanām |

	sarveṣāṃ tatsamaṃ tāvad yāvat paṅktir na bhidyate || iti |

paṅktibhedo 'pi tenaiva darśitaḥ |

	agninā bhasmanā vāpi stambhena salilena vā |

	dvāreṇa caiva mārgeṇa paṅktibhedo budhaiḥ smṛtaḥ ||

hārīto 'pi |

	udakaṃ ca tṛṇaṃ bhasma dvāraṃ panthās tathaiva ca |

	ebhir antaritaṃ kṛtvā paṅktidoṣo na vidyate || iti |

atra atriḥ |

	ācānto 'py aśucis tāvad yāvat pātram anuddhṛtam |

	uddhṛte 'py aśucis tāvad yāvad bhūmir na lipyate ||

	bhūmāv api hi liptāyāṃ tāvat syād aśuciḥ pumān |

	āsanād utthitas tasmād yāvan na spṛśate mahīm || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ bhoktṛniyamāḥ**

**atha bhojananiyamaprasaṅgād anyad api tadviṣayaṃ kiṃcid ucyate**

atra manuḥ |

	candrasūryagrahe nādyād adyāt snātvā vimukayoḥ |

	amuktayor astagayor dṛṣṭvā snātvā pare 'hani || iti |

atra candrasūryagrahaśabdena tadyuktam ahorātraṃ lakṣyate | evaṃ ca candrasūryagrahaṇayukte 'horātre tadvimocanāt pūrvaṃ na bhuñjītety uktaṃ bhavati | uktaṃ ca mārkaṇḍeyena |

	candrasya yadi vā bhānor yasminn ahani bhārgava |

	grahaṇaṃ tu bhavet tatra na pūrvaṃ bhojanakriyā ||

	nācaret sagrahe (?) tasmiṃs tathaivāstam upāgate |

	yāvat syān nodayas tatra nāśnīyāt tāvad eva tu || iti |

tatra tasminn ahorātra ity arthaḥ | atrodayagrahaṇaṃ kathaṃcin muktādarśane 'py udaye sati bhojanaṃ yathā syād ity evaṃ kaiścid vyākhyātam | anenaivābhiprāyeṇa śātātapo 'pi |

	ahorātraṃ tu nāśnīyāc candrasūryagraho yadā |

	muktaṃ dṛṣṭvā tu bhuñjīta snānaṃ kṛtvā vidhānataḥ || iti |

candragrahe tu viśeṣam āha mārkaṇḍeyaḥ |

	grahaṇaṃ tu bhaved indoḥ prathamād adhiyāmataḥ |

	bhuñjītāvartanāt pūrvaṃ prathame prathamād adhaḥ || iti |

prathamād adhi prathamayāmād ūrdhvam ity arthaḥ | āvartanaṃ madhyaṃdinam | anena yasmin yāme grahaṇaṃ tataḥ pūrvaṃ yāmatrayaṃ parihāya bhuñjītety uktaṃ bhavati | sūryagrahe tu smṛtyantarokto viśeṣaḥ |

	sūryagrahe tu nāśnīyāt pūrvaṃ yāmacatuṣṭayam |

	candragrahe tu yāmāṃs trīn bālavṛddhāturair vinā ||

bālavṛddhāturair ity ubhayatra saṃbadhyate | ata eva mārkaṇḍeyaḥ |

	sāyāhne grahaṇaṃ cet syād aparāhṇe na bhojanam |

	aparāhṇe na madhyāhne madhyāhne na tu saṅgave ||

	bhuñjīta saṅgave cet syān na pūrvaṃ bhojanakriyā | iti |

evaṃ ca yad uktaṃ kūrapurāṇe |

	nādyāt sūryagrahāt pūrvam ahni sāyaṃ śaśigrahāt |

	grahakāle tu nāśnīyāt snātvāśnīyād vimuktayoḥ ||

	mukte śaśini bhuñjīta yadi na syān mahāniśā |

	snātvā dṛṣṭvāpare 'hny adyād grastāstamitayos tayoḥ ||

atrāhaḥsāyaṃśabdāv anuvādakau vacanāntaraprāptakālopalakṣaṇārthau vety anusaṃdheyam | atra vyāsaḥ |

	sarvaṃ bhūmisaṃ dānaṃ sarve brahmasamā dvijāḥ |

	sarvaṃ gaṅgāsamaṃ toyaṃ rāhugraste divākare ||

	indor lakṣaguṇaṃ puṇyaṃ raveḥ śataguṇaṃ tataḥ |

	gaṅgātoye tu saṃprāpte indoḥ koṭī raver daśa ||

	indoḥ koṭisahasrasya yat phalaṃ labhate naraḥ |

	tat phalaṃ jāhnavīsnāne rāhugraste divākare ||

	dandrasūryagrahe caiva yo 'vagāheta jāhnavīm |

	sa snātaḥ sarvatīrtheṣu kim artham aṭate mahīm ||

	sūryavāre ravigrāsaḥ some somagrahas tathā |

	vāreṣv anyeṣu yat puṇyaṃ grahaṇe candrasūryayoḥ |

	tat puṇyaṃ koṭiguṇitaṃ grāse cūḍāmaṇau smṛtam ||

ṣaṭtriṃśanmate 'pi |

	sarveṣām eva varṇānāṃ sūtakaṃ rāhudarśane |

	snātvā karmāṇi kurvīta śṛtam annaṃ vivarjayet ||

sūtakagrahaṇaṃ sacelasnānaprāptyartham | ata eva vṛddhavasiṣṭhaḥ |

	sarveṣām eva varṇānāṃ sūtakaṃ rāhusūtake |

	sacelaṃ tad bhavet snānaṃ sūtakānnaṃ ca varjayet ||

sūtakānnaṃ rāhusūtakānnam | atra śātātapaḥ |

	sarvasvenāpi kartavyaṃ śrāddhaṃ rāhusamāgame |

	akurvāṇas tu tac chrādhaṃ paṅke gaur iva sīdati ||

ṛṣyaśṛṅgo 'pi |

	rāhugraste tu vai sūrye yas tu śrāddhaṃ prakalpayet | \
	tenaiva sakalā pṛthvī dattā viprasya vai kare ||

	snānaṃ dānaṃ tapaḥ śrāddham anantaṃ rāhudarśane |

	āsurī rātrir anyatra tasmāt tāṃ parivarjayet ||

rāhudarśanagrahaṇaṃ saṃkrāntyāder api pradarśanārtham,

	rāhudarśanasṃkrāntivivāhātyayavṛdddhiṣu |

	snānadānādikaṃ kuryān niśi kāmyavrateṣu ca ||

iti devalasmaraṇāt | atyayo maraṇam | śrāddhadravyaṃ ca śātātapoktam |

	āpady anagnau tīrthe ca candrasūrgrahe tathā |

	āmaśrāddhaṃ dvijaḥ kuryāc chūdro dadyāt sadaiva hi ||

bodhāyano 'pi |

	annābhāve dvijābhāve pravāse putrajanmani |

	hemaśrāddhaṃ sagrahe ca śūdraḥ kuryāt sadaiva hi || iti |

atra kālaniyamo vṛddhavasiṣṭhena darśitaḥ |

	tridaśāḥ sparśasamaye tṛpyanti pitaras tathā |

	manuṣyā madhyame kāle mokṣakāle tu rākṣasāḥ ||

atra liṅgapurāṇam |

	candrasūryagrahe snāyāt sūtake mṛtake 'pi vā |

	asnāyī mṛtyum āpnoti snāyī pāpaṃ na vindati ||

	sūtake mṛtake caive na doṣo rāhudarśane |

	tāvad eva bhavec chuddhir yāvan mukto na dṛśyate ||

	trirātraṃ samupoṣyaiva grahaṇe candrasūryayoḥ |

	snātvā datvā ca vidhivan modate brahmaṇā saha ||

	ekarātram upoṣyaiva snātvā datvā ca śaktitaḥ |

	kañcukād iva sarpasya niṣkṛtiḥ pāpakośataḥ ||

śātātapo 'pi |

	ayane viṣuve caive candrasūryagrahe tathā |

	ahorātroṣitaḥ snātaḥ sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ||

evaṃ ca yad uktaṃ ṣaṭtriṃśanmate,

	sūryagraho yadā rātrau divā candragrahas tathā |

	tatra snānaṃ na kurvīta dadyād dānaṃ na ca kvacit ||

tad yad būbhāgāvasthitānām uparāgo na dṛśyate tadviṣayam ity avagantavyam ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ grahaṇaviṣayāḥ**

**atha sāyaṃsaṃdhyā**

tatra vyāsaḥ |

	sūrye 'staśikharaṃ yāte pādaśaucakriyānvitaḥ |

	bahiḥ saṃdhyām upāsīta kuśapāṇiḥ samāhitaḥ || iti |

astaśikharaṃ prāpte 'rdhāstamita ity arthaḥ | ata eva saṃvartaḥ |

	prātaḥsaṃdhyāṃ sanakṣatrām upāsīta yathāvidhi |

	sādityāṃ paścimāṃ saṃdhyām ardhāstamitabhāskarām ||

atra viśeṣam āha āpastambaḥ: "saṃdhyayoś ca bahir grāmād āsanaṃ vāgyataś ca vipratiṣedhe śrutilakṣaṇaṃ balīyaḥ" iti | 

ahotrātrasaṃdhyayor grāmād bahir vāgyatasya saṃdhyopāsanaṃ bhavati | yasya tu bahiḥsaṃdhyātve śrutilakṣaṇaviharaṇāṅgabādhas tasya gṛhe 'pi saṃdhyādvayam aviruddham ity arthaḥ | ata eva atriḥ |

	saṃdhyādvayaṃ tu kartavyaṃ dvijenātmaviśuddhaye |

	ubhe saṃdhye tu kartavye brāhmaṇaiḥ svagṛheṣv api || iti |

atra vyāsaḥ |

	bahiḥsaṃdhyā daśaguṇā gartaprasravaṇeṣu ca |

	khyātatīrthe śatuguṇā sahasraṃ jāhnavījale ||

śātātapo 'pi |

	anṛtaṃ madyagandhaṃ ca divāmaithunam eva ca |

	punāti vṛṣalasyānnaṃ bahiḥsaṃdhyābhyupāsitam ||

vasiṣṭho 'pi |

	gṛhe tv ekaguṇā saṃdhyā goṣṭhe śataguṇā smṛtā |

	śatasāhasrikā nadyām anantā viṣṇusaṃnidhau || iti |

atra "anantā śivasaṃnidhau" iti śātātapīyo viśeṣaḥ | atrāyaṃ prayogaḥ: kṛtaprāṇāyāmaḥ sāyaṃsaṃdhyām upāsiṣya iti saṃkalpya pūrvavan mārjanānte "agniś ca" ity apaḥ pibet | tad āhatuḥ krameṇa yājñavalkyaśaunakau |

	prāṇān āyamya saṃprokṣya ṛcenābdaivatena tu |

	sāyam agniś ca mety uktvā prataḥ sūryety apaḥ pibet ||

tasya prakṛtiḥ chandaḥ | sūrya ṛṣiḥ | aginimanumanupatyahāni (?) devatā | sāyaṃsamdhyācamane viniyogaḥ | tato mārjanādi samānam ā gāyatrījapāt | tatra viśeṣam āha vyāsaḥ |

	pratyaṅmukhopaviṣṭas tu vāgayataḥ susamāhitaḥ |

	praṇavavyāhṛtiyutāṃ gāyatrīṃ tu japet tataḥ ||

	akṣasūtraṃ samādāya samyag ā tārakodayāt |

śaṅkho 'pi: "kuśabrusyāṃ samāsīnaḥ kuśottarāyāṃ vā kuśapavitrapāṇir udaṅmukhaḥ sūryābhimukho vā akṣamālām ādāya devatāṃ dhyāyañ japaṃ kuryāt" iti | brusī āsanam | kuśottarā kuśacchannā | devatā cātra gāyatrīpratipadyā, "maunaṃ mantrārthacintanam" iti bṛhaspatismaraṇāt | tataḥ pūrvavad gāyatrīvisarjanāntaṃ kṛtvā svaśākhādhītair mantrair ādityam upatiṣṭheta,

	upasthānaṃ svakair mantrair ādityasya tu kārayet |

ity vasiṣṭhasmaraṇāt | te ca mantrā nārāyaṇena darśitāḥ: "vāruṇībhir ādityam upasthāya pradakṣiṇaṃ kurvan diśo namaskuryād digīśāṃś ca pṛthak pṛthak" iti | vāruṇyaś ca "imaṃ me varuṇa", "tatvā (?) yāmi", "yaccid dhite", "yaktiṃ cedam", "kita vāsaḥ" iti | tāsāṃ prathamāgṛtīyayor gāyatrī chandaḥ | dvitīyāpañcamyos triṣṭub chandaḥ | caturthī jagatī | ādyānāṃ tisṛṇāṃ śunaḥśepha ṛṣiḥ | anantrayoḥ krameṇa vasiṣātrī | varuṇo devatā | ādityopasthāne viniyogaḥ | bodhāyanas tu gāyatrījapānte rātryupasthānam āha: "vāruṇībhyāṃ rātrim upatiṣṭhata imaṃ me varuṇa tat tvā yāmīti dvābhyām" iti | atra aṅgirāḥ |

	ubhe saṃdhye tu yo vipro maunam āste samāhitaḥ |

	divyaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu brahmaloke mahīyate || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ sāyaṃsaṃdhyavidhiḥ**

**atha śayanavidhiḥ**

tatra yājñavalkyaḥ |

	upāsya paścimāṃ saṃdhyāṃ hutvāgnīṃs tān upāsya ca |

	bhṛtyaiḥ parivṛto bhuktvā nātitṛptyātha saṃviset ||

saṃviśet svaped ity arthaḥ | cakāro vaiśvadevāder api samuccyārthaḥ,

	sāyaṃ prātar vaiśvadevaḥ kartavyo balikarma ca |

	anaśnatāpi satatam anyathā kilbiṣī bhavet ||

iti kātyāyanasmaraṇāt | etac ca pākāntarād ādāya kāryaṃ na punar bhuktaśeṣṭena,

	na ca śrāddhasya yac chiṣṭaṃ gṛhe paryuṣitaṃ ca yat |

	dampatyor bhuktaśiṣṭaṃ ca bhuktvā cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret ||

iti tasyābhojyatvasmaraṇāt, "yad āryāṇām abhojanaṃ syān na tena yajeta" ity āpastambasmaraṇāt | ata eva viṣṇupurāṇam |

	punaḥ pākam upādāya sāyam apy avanīpate (?) |

	vaiśvadevanimittaṃ vai patnyā sārdhaṃ baliṃ haret ||

	tatrāpi śvapacādibhyas tathaivānnāpavarjanam |

	atithiṃ cāgataṃ tatra svaśaktyā pūjayet tataḥ ||

	devātithau tu vimukhe gate yat pātakaṃ nṛpa |

	tad evāṣṭaguṇaṃ puṃsāṃ sūryoḍhe vimukhe gate ||

	kṛtapādādiśaucaś ca bhuktvā sāyaṃ tato gṛhī |

	gacchec chayyām asphuṭitāṃ dṛḍhadārumayīṃ nṛpa || iti |

gacchec chayyāṃ śayanārtham iti śeṣaḥ | tat katham ity apekṣite hārītaḥ |


        suprakṣālitacaraṇaḥ sarvato rakṣāṃ kṛtvā udakapūrṇaghaṭādimaṅgalopetaḥ ātmābhirucitām anupahatāṃ "sutrāmāṇam" iti paṭhan śayyām adhiṣṭhāya rātrisūktaṃ japtvā viṣṇuṃ namaskṛtya "sarpāpasarpa bhadraṃ te" ity etc chlokadvayaṃ japtvā iṣṭadevatāsmaraṇaṃ kṛtvā samādhim āsthāya anyāṃś ca vaidikān mantrān sāvitrīṃ japtvāmaṅgalaśrutiṃ śaṅkhaṃ ca śṛṇvan dakṣiṇaśirāḥ svapet | iti |

rakṣā cātra gāruḍair mantriḥ,

	māṅgalyaṃ pūrṇakumbhaṃ ca śiraḥsthāne nidhāya ca |

	vaidikair gāruḍair mantraiḥ rakṣāṃ kṛtvā svapet tataḥ||

iti purāṇasmaraṇāt | rātrasūktam "rātrī svakhyadāyatī" ity aṣṭarcam | dakṣiṇaśirā iti pradarśanārtham,

	prācyāṃ diśi śiraḥśastaṃ yāmyāyām atha vā nṛpa |

	sadaiva svapataḥ puṃso viparītaṃ tu rogadam ||

iti padmapurāṇasmaraṇāt | atra viśeṣam āha vyāsaḥ |

	śucideśaṃ viviktaṃ tu gomayenopalepayet |

	prāgudakpravaṇe caiva saṃviśet tu sadā budhaḥ || iti |

viviktaṃ rahaḥ | gobilo 'pi: "snātaḥ saṃveśanavelāyāṃ vaiṇavaṃ daṇḍam upanidadhāti śayanasamīpe sarvāṃ rātriṃ niścalaṃ svastyayanārtham" iti | purāṇe 'pi |

	rātrisūktaṃ japet smṛtvā devāṃś ca sukhaśāyinaḥ |

	namaskṛtyāvyayaṃ viṣṇuṃ samādhisthaḥ svapen niśi || iti |

sukhaśāyino gobilena darśitā |

	agastyo mādhavaś caiva mucukundo mahābalaḥ |

	kapilo munir āstīkaḥ pañcaita sukhaśāyinaḥ ||

atra mārkaṇḍeyaḥ |

	śūnyālaye śmaśāne ca eko vṛkṣo catuṣpathe |

	mahādevagṛhe vāpi mātṛveśmani na svapet ||

	na yakṣanāgāyatane skandasyāyatane tathā |

	kūlacchāyāsu ca tathā śarkarāloṣṭapāṃsuṣu ||

	na svapec ca tathā darbhe vinā dīkṣāṃ kathaṃcana |

	dhānyagodevaviprāṇāṃ gurūṇāṃ ca tathopari ||

	na cāp bhinnaśayane nāśucau nāśuciḥ svayam |

	nārdravāsā na nagnaś ca nottarāparamastakaḥ ||

	nākāśe sarvataḥ śūnye na ca caityadrume tathā ||

pracetā api: "na saṃdhyāyāṃ śayīta na devasamīpe na devasamāptau nāśucir na nagno na viśīrṇakhaṭvāyāṃ nānyavarṇopaśāyitayāṃ nāśmapīṭhopahitāyāṃ na bhūtayakṣagrahāyataneṣu na śmaśānavalmīkamahāvṛkṣacchāyāsu ca" iti | viṣṇur api: "nārdrapādavāsāḥ svapen na palāśaśayane na pañcadārukṛte na gajabhagnakṛte na vidyuddagdhe nāgnipluṣṭe na ghaṭāsiktadrumaje na śmaśānaśūnyālayadevatāyataneṣu na ca palamadhye na nārīmadhye na dhānyagoguruhutāśanasurāṇām upari nocchiṣṭo na divā" iti | viṣṇupurāṇe 'pi |

	nāviśālāṃ na vā bhagnāṃ nāsamāṃ malināṃ na ca |

	na ca jantumayīṃ śayyām adhitiṣṭhed anāstṛtām || iti |

dakṣo 'pi |

	pradoṣapaścimau yāmau vedābhyāsena tau nayet |

	yāmadvayaṃ śayānas tu brahmabhūyāya kalpate ||

atra kūrmapurāṇam |

	ity etad akhilaṃ proktam ahany ahani vai dvijāḥ |

	brāhmaṇānāṃ kṛtyajātam (?) apavargaphalapradam ||

	nāstikyād atha vālasyād brahmaṇo na karoti yaḥ|

	sa yāti narakān ghorān kākayonau ca jāyate ||

	nānyo vimukta ye panthā muktvāśramavidhiṃ svakam |

	tasmāt karmāṇi kurvīta tuṣṭaye parameṣṭhinaḥ || iti |

**iti śrīsakalavidyāviśārada-śrīkeśavādityabhaṭṭopādhyāyasuta-**

**yājñikadevaṇabhaṭṭopādhyāyaviracitāyāṃ **

**smṛticandrikāyāṃ āhnikakāṇḍaḥ smāptaḥ**
